# cs.CL [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [Sycophancy as Material Failure under Pushback Loading: A Multi-Axis Characterization Across Three Loading Cases and up to Seventeen Material Charges](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16617)
*Ferdinand M. Schessl*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文借助材料科学框架，将对话视为加载下的试样、LLM视为材料，通过多轴力学测量（速度、损伤累积、框架漂移、脆性、方向稳定性）对模型中的“谄媚行为（sycophancy）”进行系统刻画。基于7800个样本和三种加载场景的分析发现，力效模式在辩论场景中由材料本身决定（脆性断裂），而假预设和伦理场景中由负载决定（蠕变），且跨评分者一致性因场景而异。该方法回应了Ye等人（2026）对现有谄媚构念操作化不一致的诊断，提供了一种不依赖特定表层形式的多元表征方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有70余篇论文记录了大型语言模型（LLM）中的谄媚行为（sycophancy），但专家对构念边界的一致性极低（ICC=0.184; Ye et al., 2026），原因在于行为分类依赖于研究者所选用的表层形式（surface form）。亟需一种不依赖特定表层形式的系统性表征方法。

Method: 采用材料科学（materials science）框架：将对话视为承受载荷（load）的试样（specimen），LLM模型视为材料（material charge），反驳（pushback）视为渐进载荷，立场翻转（stance-flip）视为材料失效（material failure）。在三种加载场景（辩论n=1000、假预设n=3400、伦理设定n=3400）共7800个样本中，使用14种轮次级轴测量（含速度、损伤累积、框架漂移、脆性、方向稳定性）及独立管线的3种说话者解析轴进行表征，并采用Hooke类耦合（σ=E·ε模拟）进行分析。

Result: 14种轴测量在三种加载场景中可复现（辩论场景效应量达|r_rb|=0.35）；符号结构揭示伦理场景中速度与累积块发生反转。方差组成呈现两种剖面：辩论场景由材料主导（脆性断裂-like，材料等级决定结果），假预设和伦理场景由话题主导（蠕变-like，负载决定结果）；比率（2.03 vs 0.13/0.17）依赖于估计器，辩论场景中方向亦存在依赖性。跨评分者信度：辩论场景对评分者稳健（Cohen's κ=0.88），假预设场景对评分者敏感（κ=0.36）。

Conclusion: 本文提供了Ye等人（2026）的诊断所要求的方法论转向：一种不依赖于特定构念表层形式的多元轴表征方案。单评分者基准测试应报告评分者敏感性这一注意事项。

Abstract: Sycophancy in LLMs is documented across 70+ papers, but expert agreement on construct boundaries remains low (ICC=.184; Ye et al., 2026). The construct fragments because behavioral classification depends on which surface form is privileged. We adopt a materials-science framing: conversation as test specimen under load, LLM-model as material charge, pushback as progressive load, stance-flip as material failure. We characterize this failure across three loading cases (debate n=1000; false-presuppositions n=3400; ethical-setting n=3400; 10-17 material charges per case; 7800 specimens total) using 14 turn-level axis-measurements spanning velocity, damage accumulation, frame-drift, brittleness, and direction stability, plus three speaker-resolved axes from an independent pipeline. The measurements are Hooke-coupled ($σ= E \cdot \varepsilon$ analog) and reproduce across loading cases with effects up to $|r_{rb}| = 0.35$ on debate; the sign structure adds a second pattern: the ethical-setting case inverts the velocity and accumulation blocks. Variance composition partitions into two profiles: debate is charge-dominated (brittle-fracture-like: the material grade decides), false-presuppositions and ethical-setting are topic-dominated (creep-like: the load decides); the ratios (2.03 vs 0.13/0.17) are estimator-dependent, for debate even in direction. Cross-judge reliability (GPT-4o vs Haiku 4.5) shows debate scoring is judge-robust (Cohen's $κ= 0.88$) while false-presupposition scoring is judge-sensitive ($κ= 0.36$) -- a caveat single-judge benchmarks must report. This is the methodological move Ye et al.'s diagnosis calls for: a multi-axis characterization that does not depend on which surface form of the construct one privileges.

</details>

# math.CO [[Back]](#toc)

### [2] [$C$-networks and the planar Ising inverse problem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15082)
*Yassine Elmaazouz,Terrence George*

Main category: math.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种非递归方法，用于求解圆盘内约化平面图上伊辛模型（Ising model）的反问题，即从边界自旋关联（boundary spin correlations）恢复边耦合常数（edge coupling constants）。该方法基于伊辛版本的腔室猜想（chamber ansatz），该猜想断言逆映射应通过图中某些变量分解，这些变量在伊辛 Y-Δ 变换（Y-$Δ$ move）下遵循离散CKP方程（discrete CKP equation）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 伊辛模型的反问题在统计力学（statistical mechanics）中具有基础重要性，但已有解法（Galashin–Pylyavskyy）是递归的，缺乏简洁的封闭形式。本文旨在提供一种非递归的显式解法。

Method: 方法基于伊辛版本的腔室猜想（chamber ansatz），即逆映射因子化（factor）为图中某些变量的形式，这些变量在伊辛 Y-Δ 变换（Y-$Δ$ move）下满足离散CKP方程（discrete CKP equation）。

Result: 成功给出了圆盘内约化平面图上伊辛模型反问题的非递归解。该解不依赖于递归步骤，而是通过上述因子化结构直接得到。

Conclusion: 该非递归解法为伊辛模型的反问题提供了更简洁的数学框架，并建立了与离散可积系统（discrete integrable system）中CKP方程的联系。

Abstract: We solve the inverse problem for Ising models on reduced planar graphs in a disk, i.e., recovering the edge coupling constants from the boundary spin correlations. A recursive solution to this problem was provided by Galashin--Pylyavskyy. Our solution is non-recursive. It is based on an Ising analog of the chamber ansatz which asserts that the inverse map should factor through variables on the graph that transform under the Ising Y-$Δ$ move according to the discrete CKP equation.

</details>


<div id='physics.plasm-ph'></div>

# physics.plasm-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [3] [Quasiparticles and ion cooling by an electron beam in a strong magnetic field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16126)
*D. M. Popov,A. I. Milstein*

Main category: physics.plasm-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了强磁场中离子与磁化电子束相互作用产生的摩擦力，通过将问题简化为准粒子（quasiparticles，即拉莫尔圆环（Larmor circles））与离子的相互作用，推导了描述该相互作用的哈密顿量（Hamiltonian），并阐明了不同碰撞参数（impact parameters）在离子冷却过程中的作用，同时考虑了正负离子两种情况。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解强磁场环境下离子与磁化电子束之间的摩擦相互作用机制，揭示离子冷却过程背后的物理原理。

Method: 将原始问题简化为准粒子（quasiparticles，即拉莫尔圆环（Larmor circles））与离子的相互作用；推导了描述该相互作用的哈密顿量（Hamiltonian）；分别分析了不同碰撞参数（impact parameters）的影响，并对比了正负离子两种情况。

Result: 推导出了描述拉莫尔圆环与离子相互作用的哈密顿量，并阐明了各类碰撞参数在离子冷却过程中的作用。研究覆盖了正离子与负离子两种情形。

Conclusion: 通过准粒子框架有效描述了强磁场中离子与磁化电子束的摩擦相互作用，为理解离子冷却过程提供了理论依据。

Abstract: The frictional force arising from the interaction of ions with a magnetized electron beam in a strong magnetic field is investigated. The problem is reduced to the interaction of quasiparticles, or Larmor circles, with ions. A Hamiltonian describing this interaction is derived. The role of various impact parameters in the process of ion cooling is elucidated. The cases of both positively and negatively charged ions are considered.

</details>


<div id='quant-ph'></div>

# quant-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [4] [Quantum optimal control of steady orbits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15383)
*Shebha Anandhi Jegadeesan,Yujie Zhao,Robert Hunter,Hassane El Mkami,Maximilian Keitel,Callum Musselwhite,Graham Smith,Guinevere Mathies,Ilya Kuprov*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种针对耗散量子系统中稳态轨道（steady orbit）和频闪稳态（stroboscopic steady state）的高效量子最优控制策略，解决了GRAPE方法因无限循环导致的数值复杂性过高问题，并能在Spinach库中实现与GRAPE同量级的数值复杂度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 周期性驱动的耗散量子系统会进入稳态轨道，其频闪稳态是量子最优控制（quantum optimal control）的有前景目标，但传统方法（如梯度上升脉冲工程，GRAPE）因依赖时域显式数值传播而无法处理无限循环，数值复杂度过高。

Method: 提出一种新的量子最优控制形式，不同于Floquet-Lindblad态工程和有效哈密顿量（effective Hamiltonian）理论，该方法能够找到控制序列，将耗散量子系统驱动至经过用户指定路标点（waypoint）的稳态轨道。软件实现基于Spinach库，数值复杂度与GRAPE相当。

Result: 该方法能高效地设计控制序列，使系统渐进地趋近于重复无限次控制序列后的频闪稳态和极限环（limit cycle），并支持用户指定轨道上的中间路标点。

Conclusion: 该策略克服了GRAPE在稳态轨道控制中的数值瓶颈，为冷却引擎、相干振荡器、精密计量和磁共振等领域的量子设备初始化与控制提供了更高效的优化路径。

Abstract: Periodically driven dissipative systems can settle into steady orbits - fixed loops on their dynamical manifolds. In quantum mechanics, steady orbits occur in cooling engines (used to initialise quantum devices), coherent oscillators (such as lasers and masers), precision metrology devices (atomic clocks, optical and spin magnetometers), and magnetic resonance (steady state free precession, dynamic nuclear polarisation). Steady orbits and stroboscopic steady states are a promising target for quantum optimal control, but the numerical complexity is prohibitive: the infinite loop defeats gradient ascent pulse engineering (GRAPE) which relies on explicit numerical propagation in the time domain.
  Here we propose an efficient quantum control strategy for stroboscopic steady states and limit cycles that are approached asymptotically when a control sequence is repeated infinitely many times. The formalism is different from Floquet-Lindblad state engineering and effective Hamiltonian theories: it finds control sequences that drive a dissipative quantum system towards a steady orbit passing through user-specified waypoints. The software implementation (same numerical complexity scaling as GRAPE) is done for the Spinach library.

</details>


### [5] [A New Definition of Quantum Superposition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15607)
*Stephen Bruce Sontz*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文指出，希尔伯特空间中态叠加的二元运算并不能自然地诱导到射影空间，因而传统的“叠加”定义存在歧义；作者在复射影空间（complex projective space）框架下给出了一个严格的几何定义——两个纯态的叠加是它们在射影空间中所在的那条唯一的复直线（complex line），并对叠加与正交基展开作了比较。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 狄拉克早在1930年就已注意到，希尔伯特空间中纯态（pure state）的求和运算无法直接传递到商空间即射影空间（projective space）上，但学界仍常将叠加视为一种有唯一结果的二元运算。本文旨在为叠加概念提供一个严谨的几何定义，以消除该歧义。

Method: 在复射影空间（complex projective space）的框架下——该空间已被学界认为是量子理论的自然几何相空间（phase space）——将两个纯态视为射影空间中的两个不同点，定义它们的叠加为这两个点所确定的唯一复直线（complex line）。

Result: 新的叠加定义表明，两个纯态（射影空间中的两点）的叠加唯一对应它们所在的那条复直线。此外，文章对“叠加”与“正交基展开”这两个概念进行了比较。

Conclusion: 在复射影空间的几何框架下，可以给出一种严格的叠加定义，从而解决传统描述中的歧义问题；这一工作有助于澄清量子理论中关于态叠加的基本概念。

Abstract: The usual description of the superposition of two (pure quantum) states is ambiguous, since the binary operation of summation in a Hilbert space does not pass down to the quotient projective space. Even though Dirac noted this as early as 1930, it is often asserted that the superposition is a binary operation acting on two states with a value that is a unique state. The goal for this note is to motivate a rigorous, geometrical definition of the superposition of states in the setting of complex projective space, which has been argued elsewhere to be the natural geometric phase space for quantum theory. The upshot is that the new definition of the superposition of two pure states, viewed as two distinct points in the projective space, is the unique (complex) line on which those two points lie. Finally, a comparison is given between superposition and expansion in an orthonormal basis.

</details>


### [6] [A Gauge-Covariant Geometric Framework for Non-Hermitian Quantum Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15922)
*Gargi Das,Sudhanshu Shekhar,Bhabani Prasad Mandal*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文发展了一个用于准厄米（quasi-Hermitian）非厄米量子系统的规范协变几何框架，通过将Dyson映射提升为核心几何对象，构建了Dyson联络，并将其分解为拉伸（stretching）和旋转（rotation）分量，进而导出了非厄米贝里相位、量子几何张量（QGT），并揭示了奇异点（EP）附近几何曲率的发散层级结构，最后在SSH和Hatano-Nelson模型中验证了临界标度律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非厄米量子系统中缺乏一个统一且规范协变的几何框架，难以清晰区分物理的度规形变与规范冗余。本文旨在建立一个由Dyson映射驱动的几何形式体系，以系统描述准厄米区域中的几何量及其在奇异点（exceptional point, EP）附近的发散行为。

Method: 将Dyson映射提升为中心几何对象，由其构造Dyson联络，将该联络分解为厄米（Hermitian）与非厄米部分，分别识别为拉伸（stretching）和旋转（rotation）分量。在此基础上，利用显式规范协变态（manifestly gauge-covariant states）推导非厄米贝里相位和量子几何张量（quantum geometric tensor, QGT），并分析EP附近的几何奇异性。

Result: 非厄米几何曲率源于拉伸分量在算符层面的非对易性。对于一般两能级非厄米模型，量子度规张量（QMT）在EP附近呈现出主导阶发散 $\sim |\varepsilon_\mu|^{-2}$，而贝里曲率则表现出较弱的次主导阶发散 $\sim |\varepsilon_\mu|^{-3/2}$。非厄米Su–Schrieffer–Heeger（SSH）和Hatano–Nelson（HN）模型中的精确解析结果证实了上述临界标度律。

Conclusion: 所建立的规范协变几何框架为理解准厄米非厄米系统中的几何效应提供了统一工具，揭示了EP附近几何量的发散层级结构，并强调了度规形变驱动的非厄米几何特性。

Abstract: We develop a comprehensive, gauge-covariant geometric framework for non-Hermitian quantum systems in the quasi-Hermitian regime, that is, the region of parameter space where the non-Hermitian Hamiltonian admits a real spectrum and a positive-definite metric operator. We build this framework by elevating the Dyson map to a central geometric object. This map is the transformation that converts a non-Hermitian Hamiltonian into an equivalent Hermitian one. From it we construct the Dyson connection and decompose it into Hermitian and anti-Hermitian parts, identified respectively as {\it stretching } and {\it rotation } components. This decomposition cleanly separates the genuine physical metric deformations from the unitary gauge redundancies. Working with manifestly gauge-covariant states, we then derive the complex non-Hermitian Berry phase and the quantum geometric tensor (QGT), and show that the non-Hermitian geometric curvature originates from the non-commutativity of the stretching components at the operator level. We further analyse the geometric singularities near an exceptional point (EP) and uncover a distinct hierarchy of divergences. For a general two-level non-Hermitian model, the quantum metric tensor (QMT) exhibits a leading-order divergence $\sim |ε_μ|^{-2}$, while the Berry curvature shows a weaker, subleading divergence $\sim |ε_μ|^{-3/2}$, with $ε_μ$ denoting the parameter displacement from the EP along an individual parameter axis $μ$. Finally, we examine physical realizations of this model, including the non-Hermitian Su--Schrieffer--Heeger (SSH) and Hatano--Nelson (HN) models, where exact analytical results confirm the predicted critical scaling laws and illustrate the metric-deformation-driven non-Hermitian geometries.

</details>


### [7] [Quantum Measurement and Continuous Markov Processes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15958)
*Chris Jackson*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本篇为2025年秋季在Perimeter Institute开设的关于扩散量子测量仪器（diffusive quantum measuring instruments）的课程讲义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 课程旨在系统讲授扩散量子测量仪器的理论与应用，填补该领域教学材料的空白。

Method: 以系列讲座（lecture）形式呈现，面向线下与线上（录播）听众，采用讲义（lecture notes）作为主要教学载体。

Result: 课程于2025年10月27日至12月11日间完成，共安排多次讲座，授课时间为每周一和周四下午2:30至4:00。

Conclusion: 该讲义为扩散量子测量仪器提供了系统化的教学资源，录播内容已公开可查。

Abstract: These are the lecture notes for a course on diffusive quantum measuring instruments. They were prepared and delivered at the Perimeter Institute on Mondays and Thursdays, from 2:30 to 4:00 PM, beginning October 27th, 2025 and ending December 11th, 2025. These lectures were recorded and can be found at \textbf{https://pirsa.org/c25038}.

</details>


### [8] [Complete Relational Description of Spin in a Quantum Background](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15873)
*Hannah Troger,Ofek Bengyat,Thomas D. Galley,Marios Christodoulou*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过引入两个大自旋量子参考系来取代经典背景，在组平均（group averaging）框架下恢复了标准量子力学（quantum mechanics）中对单个自旋（spin）的完整描述，解决了Poulin原方案仅能得到经典概率混合比特的局限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准量子力学中对自旋状态的描述预设了外部固定的方向——即一个经典背景（classical background）。作者试图探索能否完全通过与其他量子力学系统的关系来定义自旋状态，从而消除对经典背景的依赖。

Method: 重新审视Poulin二十年前提出的组平均（group averaging）方法，该方法对基本自旋与大角动量参考自旋的联合态进行旋转群平均，但仅得到经典概率混合比特。本文将该方案扩展，将量子参考系统（quantum reference system）从单个大自旋增强为两个大自旋，并在大量子数极限下进行分析。

Result: 当参考系统包含两个大自旋时，在参考系统量子数趋于无穷大的极限下，标准量子力学中单个自旋的完整描述得以恢复。

Conclusion: 通过引入两个而非一个大自旋作为量子参考系，可以在无需经典背景的前提下重建量子自旋的完整描述，为量子力学的关系性诠释提供了新的理论依据。

Abstract: The standard description of the state of a spin in quantum mechanics presupposes externally fixed directions -- a classical background. Can a spin be fully described instead in relation to other quantum mechanical systems? Poulin suggested twenty years ago group averaging over rotations the joint state of a fundamental spin and a reference spin with large angular momentum which, however, yields a classical bit in a probabilistic mixture. We revisit this idea and show that when the quantum reference system is augmented to \emph{two} large spins, the standard quantum mechanical description of a spin is recovered in the limit of large quantum numbers for the reference system.

</details>


### [9] [Ultrastrongly coupled open systems and fine grained time](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16634)
*Stefano Marcantoni,Marco Merkli*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过引入与耦合强度倒数成比例的精细缩放时间标度，严格推导了超强耦合（ultrastrong coupling）条件下d能级量子系统与玻色子库（bosonic reservoir）耦合的开放系统动力学，揭示了退相干（decoherence）在此新时间标度下连续展开的过程，并发现非半群（non-semigroup）形式的马尔可夫动力学（Markovian dynamics）自然出现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在强耦合极限下，已知系统会发生瞬时非选择性测量（instantaneous nonselective measurement）并进入幺正芝诺动力学（unitary Zeno dynamics），但这一动力学过程在中间时间尺度上的具体展开方式尚未被解析。

Method: 引入与耦合强度倒数成正比的精细缩放时间标度（fine grained scaling regime of short times），在该超强耦合标度下对开放系统动力学进行严格推导。

Result: 证明了退相干在新的时间标度下是连续发生的，而非瞬时；揭示了该标度下自然出现的马尔可夫动力学并非由半群（semigroup）描述，这与弱耦合理论形成鲜明对比。

Conclusion: 超强耦合下的开放系统动力学可以在精细时间标度下被连续解析，且其马尔可夫性具有不同于传统弱耦合理论的非半群结构。

Abstract: We study the dynamics of a d-level quantum system coupled to a bosonic reservoir when the coupling constant is large. It is known that in the limit of infinite coupling strength, the system undergoes an instantaneous nonselective measurement, resulting in the immediate decoherence in the measurement basis, followed by a unitary Zeno dynamics. Here we resolve this dynamical process by introducing a fine grained scaling regime of short times proportional to the inverse coupling. We provide a rigorous derivation of the open system dynamics in this regime of ultrastrong coupling and demonstrate how decoherence unfolds continuously in the new time scale. We show that Markovian dynamics which are not given by semigroups arise naturally, in contrast to what happens in the weak coupling theory.

### [10] [Morphology-resolved scrambling in a chaotic quantum billiard](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16865)
*Pranaya Pratik Das*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本研究在花生形量子台球（quantum billiard）中，通过形态分辨框架建立了疤痕本征态（scarred eigenstates）与本征态分辨的离序时间关联函数（eigenstate-resolved OTOCs）之间的定量联系，发现强形态重复的本征态具有近乎相同的 OTOC 增长与饱和行为，表明疤痕结构作为算子增长（operator growth）的空间模板，而非仅仅是遍历性破缺的静态标志。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 混沌量子系统可通过疤痕本征态保留空间记忆，但这些静态结构是否控制量子信息的打乱（scrambling）尚不清楚。本文旨在建立疤痕本征态与动力学打乱之间的形态分辨联系。

Method: 在花生形量子台球中，采用尺度归一化密度重叠（scale-normalised density overlap）直接比较概率密度分布，识别具有几乎相同空间形态的正交本征态族。结合微分熵（differential entropy）和连续参与比（continuum participation ratios）等标量局域化诊断，对比这些本征态的完整 OTOC 时间迹。

Result: 中等密度重叠无法给出普适预测，而强形态重复的正交本征态展现出近乎一致的 OTOC 增长与饱和行为。标量局域化诊断能检测反常集中但会丢失空间架构信息。

Conclusion: 疤痕结构作为算子增长的空间模板，不仅仅是遍历性（ergodicity）的静态破缺。该形态分辨框架将本征态形状转化为打乱的定量预测工具，并为量子混沌中的弱遍历性破缺提供尺度可控的诊断。

Abstract: Chaotic quantum systems can retain spatial memory through scarred eigenstates, but whether these static structures control scrambling remains unclear. This work establishes a morphology-resolved connection between scarred eigenstates and eigenstate-resolved OTOCs in a peanut-shaped quantum billiard. Scalar localisation diagnostics, including differential entropy and continuum participation ratios, detect anomalous concentration but discard spatial architecture. A scale-normalised density overlap, in contrast, directly compares probability density profiles, revealing families of orthogonal eigenstates with nearly identical spatial morphology. Comparing the complete OTOC time traces of these orthogonal eigenstates reveals that morphological recurrence has dynamical content: moderate density overlap yields no universal prediction, whereas strongly recurring morphologies exhibit nearly identical OTOC growth and saturation. Thus, scarred structures act as spatial templates for operator growth, not merely static violations of ergodicity. This morphology-resolved framework turns eigenstate shape into a quantitative predictor of scrambling and provides a scale-controlled diagnostic of weak ergodicity breaking in quantum chaos.

### [11] [The Optimal Rate Function in Covariant Quantum State Tomography](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16948)
*Arick Grootveld,Alexander Maloney,Jason Pollack,Peixue Wu*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究量子层析成像（quantum tomography）协议的最优估计问题。通过引入速率函数（rate function）作为协议性能的度量标准，证明了该函数以量子相对熵（quantum relative entropy）为上界且该界是紧的；同时证明了Keyl猜想：在所有协变（covariant）协议中，基于Schur采样的协议具有最大的速率函数，该速率函数是量子相对熵的退火版本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子层析成像的核心问题是从有限拷贝数中估计未知量子态。如何选择多拷贝测量协议以获得最优估计是一个基础性问题。本文旨在建立一套理论框架来比较不同协议的性能，并确定在无先验信息的协变协议中最优的估计方案。

Method: 用速率函数（rate function）刻画协议将概率分配给特定估计态σ的指数衰减速率；该函数是经典相对熵（relative entropy）的量子推广。通过对比量子相对熵（quantum relative entropy）的上界，构造了一个协议族使得速率函数收敛到该上界。针对协变（covariant）协议，基于Schur采样（Schur sampling）协议进行分析，并证明了Keyl猜想。

Result: 速率函数以量子相对熵D(σ∥ρ)为上界，且该界是紧的（sharp）：对任意ρ和σ，存在协议族使其速率函数趋近于D(σ∥ρ)。在协变协议类中，基于Schur采样的协议具有最大的速率函数，证实了Keyl猜想。该速率函数表现为量子相对熵的退火版本（annealed version），原因在于协变量子态层析中学习本征基（eigenbasis）需要额外代价。

Conclusion: 研究从速率函数的角度建立了量子层析协议性能的严格比较框架，证明了量子相对熵是协议速率函数的最佳可达上界，并解决了协变协议类中Keyl猜想的最优性问题。结果揭示了学习未知本征基带来的性能代价，为量子态估计理论提供了基础性理解。

Abstract: The problem of quantum tomography is to estimate an unknown quantum state $ρ$ from a measurement of $n$ copies of $ρ$. One can ask which tomography protocol, i.e.\ which choice of multi-copy measurement, gives the best possible estimate of $ρ$. To do so, we characterize tomography protocols by their \emph{rate function}, which governs the exponential rate at which a protocol assigns probability to a particular estimate $σ$ of the true state $ρ$. This rate function is a quantum mechanical generalization of the classical relative entropy between the true state and its estimate, and depends on the choice of protocol. It is bounded by the quantum relative entropy, and we show that this bound is sharp: for any $ρ$ and $σ$ we construct a family of protocols whose rate functions converge to the quantum relative entropy $D(σ\|ρ)$.
  We consider the family of covariant tomography protocols; these are the basis independent state estimation schemes that assume no prior information about $ρ$ and $σ$. Keyl described a specific tomography protocol based on Schur sampling, and conjectured that among all covariant tomography protocols it has the largest possible rate function for all $σ$ and $ρ$. We prove this conjecture. The resulting rate function is an annealed version of quantum relative entropy, due to the cost of learning the eigenbasis in covariant quantum state tomography.

</details>


### [12] [Magic transfer in quantum spin chains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14855)
*Antonio Palamara,Chad Nelmes,Enrico C. Domanti,Francesco Perciavalle*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了自旋链（spin chain）中量子魔法（quantum magic）的传输问题，通过稳定子范数（stabilizer norm）量化非稳定子态（nonstabilizer state）在自然动力学下的资源输运，发现注入态的几何结构（Bloch半球位置）显著影响传输质量，并可实现魔法放大（magic amplification）效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于自旋链的量子通信协议已被广泛研究，但尚未系统性地考察其对非稳定子资源（nonstabilizer resources）的传输能力。本文旨在填补这一空白，研究量子魔法在自旋链中的输运行为。

Method: 通过将系统初始化于非稳定子态，利用自然动力学实现态传输；采用稳定子范数量化传输的量子魔法资源。分析了三种实验可行的态传输协议（state-transfer protocols），涵盖从噪声传输到（准）完美传输的情形，其中一种可在离子阱（trapped-ion）平台实现。

Result: 注入态的几何结构对传输质量起决定性作用：Bloch下半球（lower Bloch hemisphere）的态获得更高传输质量，而上半球（upper hemisphere）的态需在趋向完美传输的参数超过某阈值后才实现高效魔法传输。该特征对所有协议均具鲁棒性。此外，发现了参数区域中传输的魔法超过初始编码量，表明自旋链可作为魔法放大通道（magic-amplification channel）。

Conclusion: 本文确立了非稳定子资源高效传输的条件，并展示了量子魔法可作为超越布居数动力学（population dynamics）的灵敏量子输运探针。

Abstract: Quantum communication protocols based on spin chains have been extensively studied, yet their ability to transmit nonstabilizer resources has not been systematically addressed. We investigate the transport of quantum magic in spin chains through the natural dynamics of systems initialized in nonstabilizer states, and quantify the transported resource via the stabilizer norm. We analyze three experimentally feasible state-transfer protocols, ranging from noisy to (quasi-)perfect transfer, including one realizable in trapped-ion platforms. We find that the geometry of the injected state strongly influences transport: states in the lower Bloch hemisphere achieve higher transfer quality, whereas states in the upper hemisphere give rise to an efficient magic transport only beyond a threshold value of the parameter controlling the tendency towards perfect transfer. These features are robust across all protocols and identify the Hamiltonian and state properties that favor high-quality transfer. Moreover, we identify a parameter region, relevant to the initial state preparation, in which the transported magic exceeds the initial encoding, indicating that such spin systems can act as magic-amplification channels. Our results establish the conditions for efficient transport of nonstabilizer resources and demonstrate quantum magic as a sensitive probe of quantum transport beyond population dynamics.

### [13] [Finite-Element Matrix Product States for Continuum Models in One Dimension](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14873)
*Akshay Shankar,Karel Van Acoleyen,Jutho Haegeman*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在连续空间中模拟一维量子多体系统时，传统方法通常依赖正交基组，而非正交单粒子基组的使用虽具有灵活性，但会引入复杂的多体重叠算符（many-body overlap operator），需要有效的方法对其进行编码与求解。

Method: 将物理问题映射至辅助计算空间，将多体重叠算符编码为矩阵乘积算符（matrix product operator, MPO），适用于充分局域化的轨道；将变分基态搜索转化为广义本征值问题（generalized eigenvalue problem），采用广义密度矩阵重整化群（generalized DMRG）算法求解；利用一阶有限元（first-order finite-element）展开进行离散化，并引入多重网格优化（multigrid optimization）策略实现晶格精确细化。

Result: 实现了对连续空间中一维量子多体系统的矩阵乘积态（MPS）模拟，并通过Lieb-Liniger气体在非均匀势下的基态性质研究展示了该方法的可行性。

Conclusion: 该框架为在连续空间中使用非正交基组进行矩阵乘积态（MPS）模拟提供了一种通用且可扩展的途径，并为多网格优化等高级数值策略在矩阵乘积态中的应用奠定了基础。

Abstract: We present a matrix product state framework for simulating one-dimensional quantum many-body systems in the continuum using non-orthogonal single-particle basis sets. By mapping the physical problem to an auxiliary computational space, we show that the resulting many-body overlap operator can be efficiently encoded as a matrix product operator for sufficiently localized orbitals, thereby generalizing a construction that first appeared in [arXiv:2405.10285]. This construction recasts the variational ground-state search into a generalized eigenvalue problem, which can be solved using a generalized density matrix renormalization group algorithm. As a primary application, we employ a first-order finite-element expansion to study the ground state properties of the Lieb-Liniger gas in the presence of inhomogeneities. This approach also provides a natural setting for exactly refining the lattice, thereby enabling multigrid optimization strategies for matrix product states.

### [14] [VQE as Initial State Preparation for QPE on Heisenberg Spin-Glass Hamiltonians](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15061)
*Elijah Pelofske,Stephan Eidenbenz*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文通过经典数值模拟，系统评估了变分量子本征求解器（VQE）能否为量子相位估计（QPE）高效制备与真正基态具有显著重叠的初始态。针对最多15个量子比特的无序全连接各向异性海森堡自旋玻璃哈密顿量，研究发现VQE通常无法高效收敛到基态，低能态未必具有大的基态重叠但两者存在相关性，超过三层的VQE拟设（ansatz）不再带来改进，且最佳重叠随系统规模缩放并非强烈指数衰减，暗示VQE有潜力作为QPE的启发式态制备算法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子相位估计（Quantum Phase Estimation, QPE）是计算量子哈密顿量基态能量的核心量子算法，但其有效性高度依赖于初始态与真正基态之间的显著重叠（overlap）。本研究旨在评估NISQ时代的变分量子本征求解器（Variational Quantum Eigensolver, VQE）能否高效制备这种高重叠初始态，从而为QPE在科学和商业价值最高的物理系统基态能量计算中实现超越经典的性能提供可行路径。

Method: 采用经典数值模拟方法，对无序全连接各向异性海森堡自旋玻璃量子哈密顿量（disordered fully-connected anisotropic Heisenberg spin glass quantum Hamiltonians）进行大量计算，系统规模最多至15个量子比特（qubits）。研究考察了VQE制备态与真正基态的重叠程度、VQE收敛行为、拟设（ansatz）层数的影响，以及最佳重叠随系统规模（system size）的缩放行为。

Result: 主要发现包括：(i) VQE通常无法高效收敛到目标哈密顿量的基态，这与广泛持有但鲜有数值验证的认知一致，归因于梯度消失（vanishing gradients）和局部极小值（local minima）等因素；(ii) 低能态（low energy states）不一定具有大的基态重叠，但两者通常存在相关性；(iii) 在VQE拟设中加入超过三层既不改善重叠也不改善能级；(iv) 最佳重叠（best-found overlap）随哈密顿量系统规模的缩放并非强烈指数衰减（strongly exponentially decreasing）。

Conclusion: 尽管VQE在制备高重叠初始态方面存在显著局限（如梯度消失与局部极小值问题），但最佳重叠随系统规模并非强烈指数衰减的发现表明，VQE具有作为QPE启发式（heuristic）态制备算法的潜在价值。不过，该结论仅基于15个量子比特以内的数值实验，其在实际量子计算问题中的推广性仍需进一步验证。

Abstract: Quantum Phase Estimation (QPE) is the quantum algorithmic workhorse for computing ground state energies of quantum Hamiltonians with quantum computers. Ground state energy calculation of physical systems is perhaps the most promising use case for quantum computing in terms of scientific and commercial value with a plausible path to outperformance of classical alternatives. This path, however, hinges on the availability of initial states for QPE with significant overlap with the true ground state. Using extensive (classical) numerical computations, we study whether the NISQ-era algorithm VQE (Variational Quantum Eigensolver) could be used to efficiently prepare high-overlap states of disordered fully-connected anisotropic Heisenberg spin glass quantum Hamiltonians with up to $15$ qubits. We find that (i) -- consistent with widely held, but rarely numerically illustrated beliefs -- VQE is generally unable to efficiently converge to the ground state for our Hamiltonians, which is a well-known issue with VQE due to a variety of factors including vanishing gradients and local minima; (ii) low energy states do not necessarily have large ground-state overlap, but there is typically a correlation between the two measures; (iii) adding more than three layers to the VQE ansatz neither improves overlap nor the energies found; and (iv) the best-found overlap scaling as a function of the Hamiltonian system size is not strongly exponentially decreasing, suggesting potential for VQE to be a heuristic state preparation algorithm for QPE.

### [15] [Discontinuous strong-to-weak symmetry breaking transition from thermal pure states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15062)
*Taiki Haga,Masaya Kunimi,Masaya Nakagawa*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了多体量子系统从热纯态出发经历退相干时，从强自发对称性破缺到弱自发对称性破缺的非平衡动力学，发现系统在临界时间处发生不连续的动力学相变（dynamical phase transition），熵在该时刻饱和至最大值。通过退相干伊辛模型（dephasing Ising model）和硬核玻色子模型（hard-core boson model）的数值模拟，验证了该相变在不同对称性下的普适性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解高度纠缠的纯态在退相干作用下如何演化为混合态，传统观点认为这是一个渐近弛豫过程，但本文旨在检验是否存在非平凡的动力学相变行为。

Method: 从满足体积律纠缠熵（volume-law entanglement entropy）的一般初始纯态出发，解析分析强到弱自发对称性破缺（strong-to-weak spontaneous symmetry breaking）的非平衡动力学；结合退相干伊辛模型和硬核玻色子模型的数值模拟，验证理论预言。

Result: 系统在临界时间处发生不连续的动力学相变，伴随熵的奇异性（singularity），熵在该时刻饱和至最大值。该相变在不同对称性下表现出普适性（universality）。

Conclusion: 从高度纠缠态到退相干混合态的动力学涌现并非渐近松弛过程，而是一场由全局相干性（global coherence）突然崩溃驱动的尖锐相变。

Abstract: We investigate the nonequilibrium dynamics of strong-to-weak spontaneous symmetry breaking in many-body quantum systems undergoing decoherence from thermal pure states. For generic initial pure states with volume-law entanglement entropy, we show that the system undergoes a discontinuous dynamical phase transition at a critical time. This transition is accompanied by a singularity in the entropy of the system, which saturates to its maximum value at the same critical time. Through numerical simulations of the dephasing Ising and hard-core boson models, we establish the universality of this transition across different symmetries. Our results reveal that the dynamical emergence of a decohered mixed state from a highly entangled state is not a gradual asymptotic relaxation, but rather a sharp phase transition driven by a sudden collapse of global coherence.

### [16] [Connecting entanglement growth with local integrals of motion in the disordered Fermi-Hubbard model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15481)
*Ahad Nokhostin Helm,Brandon Leipner-Johns,Rachel Wortis*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究无序费米-哈伯德模型（Fermi-Hubbard model）中电荷与自旋自由度对纠缠增长（entanglement growth）的贡献。通过将哈密顿量展开为一组最优局域守恒量（optimally localized conserved quantities），发现电荷-自旋耦合远弱于电荷-电荷和自旋-自旋耦合。这种解耦效应仅在电荷与自旋无序强度不同导致特征时间尺度分离时才明显。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解量子系统在无序（disorder）作用下纠缠动力学的行为，特别是相互作用局域化系统中电荷与自旋自由度对纠缠增长的不同贡献及其耦合机制。

Method: 研究费米-哈伯德模型中电荷无序与自旋无序强度相等和不相等两种场景下的纠缠增长。通过将哈密顿量展开为一组具有独立电荷和自旋特征的最优局域守恒量，分别确定电荷与自旋自由度对纠缠的贡献。

Result: 电荷-自旋耦合显著弱于电荷-电荷耦合和自旋-自旋耦合；这种解耦效应在电荷与自旋无序强度不同导致特征时间尺度（characteristic timescales）分离时才显现。

Conclusion: 在无序费米-哈伯德模型中，电荷与自旋自由度的纠缠贡献在时间尺度上可分离，该解耦效应依赖于两个扇区无序强度的差异。

Abstract: Generically a quantum system initialized in an unentangled state will, under unitary dynamics, rapidly become entangled, a process closely related to information transport and to thermalization. Disorder can suppress the growth of entanglement and result in memory of initial conditions. In non-interacting systems this arises from localization of single-particle states, the occupancy of which is fixed by the initial condition. In interacting systems similar localized conserved quantities persist, but with the added feature that they are coupled, resulting in entanglement growth which is distinct from both non-interacting localized systems and from generic ergodic systems. The Fermi-Hubbard model has two degrees of freedom per site -- charge and spin -- and disorder may be present in both of these. We study the growth of entanglement in two scenarios -- disorder in charge equal and unequal to that in spin, and determine the distinct contributions of charge and spin degrees of freedom by expanding the Hamiltonian in terms of a set of optimally localized conserved quantities with separate charge and spin character. We find that coupling between charge and spin is significantly weaker than charge-charge and spin-spin coupling. While this decoupling is present in all our results, it is only apparent when the strength of the disorder in the two sectors is different such that there is a separation between the characteristic timescales of the contributions to entanglement made by charge and by spin.

</details>


### [17] [Suppressing Intrinsic Spin-Phonon Errors in Trapped-Ion Quantum Simulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15518)
*Dylan Sheils,James Wang,Or Katz*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过在离子阱量子模拟器中采用帧变换序列，有效抑制了由声子总线（phonon bus）引入的自旋-声子固有误差，使得非对易哈密顿量（noncommuting Hamiltonians）的可编程模拟精度得到数量级提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在离子阱量子模拟器中，声子介导相互作用（phonon-mediated interactions）虽能实现可编程自旋模型，但当哈密顿量包含非对易项时，声子总线会产生固有自旋-声子误差（spin-phonon errors），这些误差受自旋相关声子运动的完整时间历史支配，标准闭环控制（loop-closing control）无法消除，严重限制了模拟精度。

Method: 作者采用一系列帧变换（frame transformations）来分离残余误差动力学，并证明这种固有误差可以在保持可编程伊辛耦合（Ising couplings）的同时被强烈抑制。

Result: 多离子链的全自旋-玻色子模拟（full spin-boson simulations）表明，该方法的误差比恒定驱动（constant-drive）和传统闭环控制协议低数个数量级。

Conclusion: 该工作消除了离子阱模拟量子模拟中的一个核心精度障碍，使得非对易多体哈密顿量和动力学协议（dynamical protocols）的可编程精确模拟成为可能。

Abstract: Trapped-ion quantum simulators realize programmable spin models through phonon-mediated interactions. For Hamiltonians with noncommuting terms, however, the same phonon bus generates intrinsic spin-phonon errors that strongly distort the target dynamics. Because these errors are governed by the full time history of the spin-dependent phonon motion, they survive standard loop-closing control and limit simulation accuracy. Using a sequence of frame transformations, we isolate the residual error dynamics and show that this intrinsic error can be strongly suppressed while preserving programmable Ising couplings. Full spin-boson simulations of multi-ion chains demonstrate orders-of-magnitude lower error than both constant-drive and conventional loop-closing protocols. These results remove a central precision barrier in trapped-ion analog quantum simulation and enable accurate programmable simulation of noncommuting many-body Hamiltonians and dynamical protocols.

</details>


### [18] [Experimental Observation of Dynamical Phase Transitions in a Dephased Photonic Quantum Walk](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15935)
*Xiaojian Huang,Lei Xiao,Bingzi Huo,Xiaowei Wang,Stefano Longhi,Peng Xue*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过离散时间光子量子行走（photonic quantum walk）实验，研究了开放量子系统中的动力学相变（dynamical phase transition），揭示了可调合成规范通量（synthetic gauge flux）与退相干（dephasing）如何控制细致平衡（detailed balance）特性，从而在一阶与二阶动力学相变之间实现切换，并追踪了向量子相干（quantum-coherent）区域的交叉行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解开放量子系统中非平衡态向稳态弛豫的动力学相变机制，并实验验证Liouvillian谱拓扑（Liouvillian spectral topology）与弛豫临界性（relaxation criticality）之间的关联。

Method: 在三节点图（three-node graph）上实现离散时间光子量子行走，通过可调合成规范通量控制时间反演对称性（time-reversal symmetry），并通过标定退相干调节有效马尔可夫动力学（Markovian dynamics）的细致平衡特性。

Result: 在满足细致平衡时，观察到由实Liouvillian本征值交叉标志的一阶动力学相变；打破细致平衡后，在本征值与本征向量同时合并的例外点（exceptional point）处观察到二阶动力学相变。逐步降低退相干强度可追踪向量子相干区域的交叉，且相变在有限阈值以下依然存在。

Conclusion: 实验结果建立了Liouvillian谱拓扑与弛豫临界性之间的联系，并展示了一种可用于工程化耗散动力学（engineered dissipative dynamics）的可控实验平台。

Abstract: Dynamical phase transitions in open quantum systems govern how non-equilibrium states relax toward a stationary state. We study these transitions experimentally using a discrete-time photonic quantum walk on a three-node graph. A tunable synthetic gauge flux and calibrated dephasing allow us to control time-reversal symmetry and the detailed balance properties of the effective Markovian dynamics. With detailed balance, we observe a first-order dynamical phase transition marked by a crossing of real Liouvillian eigenvalues. When detailed balance is broken, we observe a second-order dynamical phase transition at an exceptional point where eigenvalues and eigenvectors coalesce. By progressively reducing the dephasing strength, we track the crossover toward the quantum-coherent regime and determine that the transitions persist down to a finite threshold. Our results link Liouvillian spectral topology to relaxation criticality and demonstrate a controllable platform for engineered dissipative dynamics.

### [19] [Learning ground state observables from quantum computing experiments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15983)
*Ben Jaderberg,Freya Shah,Minjun Jeon,M. Emre Sahin,Christa Zoufal,Kunal Sharma*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然理论已建立机器学习模型可从量子生成数据中高效预测能隙局域哈密顿量（gapped local Hamiltonians）的基态性质，但先前实验受限于小系统或高度结构化态。本文旨在克服制备多体基态的困难，在大规模相互作用系统中实现量子数据学习的实验验证。

Method: 在二维海森堡XXZ模型的反铁磁相中，使用多达115个量子比特的近似基态生成实验量子数据。构建的数据集包含单点期望值（single-site expectation values）、两点关联函数（two-point correlations）和12体环关联函数（12-body loop correlations）。随后在此数据上训练神经网络。

Result: 训练后的神经网络能够准确预测未见过的哈密顿量参数下的空间分辨可观测量（spatially resolved observables），包括训练分布内和接近相边界（phase boundary）的分布外（out-of-distribution）区域。

Conclusion: 实验结果证明了在可扩展的相互作用二维多体系统中，利用量子数据进行学习的实际可行性，为量子处理器提供超越经典近似方法能力的训练数据铺平了道路。

Abstract: Recent theoretical progress has established conditions under which machine learning models can efficiently predict ground-state properties of gapped local Hamiltonians when trained on quantum-generated data. Previous experimental demonstrations in this paradigm, however, have largely been limited to small systems or highly structured states, due to the difficulty of preparing many-body ground states on quantum processors. In this work, we demonstrate learning from experimental quantum data generated from approximate ground states of the two-dimensional Heisenberg XXZ model with system sizes up to 115 qubits. We construct a dataset of single-site expectation values, two-point correlations, and 12-body loop correlations across the antiferromagnetic phase. We then train neural networks on this data and show that they can accurately predict spatially resolved observables for previously unseen Hamiltonian parameters, both within the training distribution and in an out-of-distribution regime approaching the phase boundary. Our results demonstrate the practical realization of learning from quantum data for an interacting two-dimensional many-body system at scale, motivating a path toward regimes where quantum processors could provide training data beyond the reach of classical approximation methods.

### [20] [Quantum Algorithm for Open-System Battery Cathodes by Modeling Multiple Strongly Coupled Holstein Polarons with Chain-Mapped Caldeira-Leggett Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16017)
*Joshua M. Courtney*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种容错量子算法，通过幺正链映射的Caldeira-Leggett嵌入将电化学开放系统（battery cathode lithiation）转化为可Trotter化的幺正动力学，从而计算开路电压与微分容量等开放系统可观测量。该算法在强耦合下验证了与层级运动方程（HEOM）的一致性，在弱耦合下验证了Lindblad极限，并在LiFePO₄和LiMn₂O₄上分别实现了±5 mV和17%误差内的电压曲线复现，给出了368个逻辑量子比特、每步约3×10⁵ T门的资源估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 阴极锂化（cathode lithiation）涉及紧束缚轨道、窄带宽和强电子-晶格耦合的化学区域，其核心电化学可观测量（开路电压与微分容量）属于开放系统、库平衡量，无法通过封闭哈密顿量量子模拟产生。因此需要发展一种能够处理电子、Li⁺和声子浴交换的容错量子算法。

Method: 提出一种容错量子算法，通过幺正链映射的Caldeira-Leggett嵌入（unitary chain-mapped Caldeira-Leggett embedding）将浴系统转化为可Trotter化的形式，从而在容错量子计算机上模拟开放系统动力学。采用四阶Trotter步长，其T门计数与系统规模呈多项式关系。在强耦合下用层级运动方程（hierarchical equations of motion, HEOM）验证，在弱耦合下用Lindblad极限验证。

Result: 对于单载流子橄榄石LiFePO₄，单个电压锚点结合DFT固定哈密顿量可将微分容量峰定位在±5 mV实验平台可重复性内。对于多载流子尖晶石LiMn₂O₄（1:1 Mn³⁺/Mn⁴⁺填充），同一核得到两个电压平台，分裂为125 mV，与观测值150 mV相差17%。端到端资源估计：368个逻辑量子比特，每步约3×10⁵ T门，完整电压曲线约1.7×10¹² T门（可并行化至约10³条轨迹）。

Conclusion: 该算法内核在不修改的情况下还能复现宏观量子相干性、两带超导性及Mikheyev-Smirnov-Wolfenstein共振，表明动态电池化学（dynamical battery chemistry）及类似哈密顿量已纳入容错量子模拟的适用范围。生产规模的动力学运行仍有待未来硬件发展。

Abstract: Cathode lithiation occupies a chemical regime of tightly localized orbitals, narrow bandwidths, and strong electron-lattice coupling. The defining electrochemical observables (open-circuit voltage and differential capacity) are open-system, reservoir-equilibration quantities that closed-Hamiltonian quantum simulation cannot produce, set by exchange with electron, Li$^+$, and phonon baths. We present a fault-tolerant quantum algorithm that recovers them through a unitary chain-mapped Caldeira-Leggett embedding, rendering the baths Trotterizable. The resulting fourth-order Trotter step has a T-gate count polynomial in system size, validating its open-system dynamics against hierarchical equations of motion (HEOM) at strong coupling and the Lindblad limit at weak coupling. For single-carrier olivine LiFePO$_4$, a single voltage anchor on an otherwise DFT-fixed Hamiltonian places the differential-capacity peak within the $\pm5$ mV reproducibility of the experimental plateau. For multi-carrier spinel LiMn$_2$O$_4$, whose $1{:}1$ Mn$^{3+}$/Mn$^{4+}$ filling makes the inter-site Coulomb repulsion dynamically active, the same kernel yields a two-plateau voltage curve with a $125$ mV split, within $17\%$ of the observed $150$ mV. We deliver an end-to-end fault-tolerant resource estimate for such a multi-carrier, three-reservoir observable: $368$ logical qubits and $\sim3\times10^5$ T-gates per step, or $\sim1.7\times10^{12}$ T-gates for a full voltage curve (parallelizable over $\sim10^3$ trajectories), leaving the production-scale dynamical run as a milestone for future hardware. The same kernel reproduces macroscopic quantum coherence, two-band superconductivity, and the Mikheyev-Smirnov-Wolfenstein resonance without modification, placing dynamical battery chemistry and similar Hamiltonians within scope for fault-tolerant quantum simulation.

### [21] [Reconstruction of detector error model for quantum error correction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16288)
*Cheng Ye,Pan Zhang*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出基于相关性分析的超图重构算法（CAHR），通过全局一致的代数框架直接从实验纠错码综合征统计量中恢复离散物理超图（fault hypergraph），避免了传统贪婪推理的统计失真和虚假正例问题，并在表面码与颜色码上验证了其无虚假正例的拓扑恢复能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 容错量子计算（fault-tolerant quantum computing）依赖对电路级噪声（circuit-level noise）的准确刻画以优化解码算法，但提取复杂多体错误关联（multi-body error correlations）仍然困难；现有贪婪推理算法存在统计失真，既丢弃真实物理机制又引入大量非物理的虚假正例（false positives）。

Method: CAHR算法将实验纠错码综合征统计量（experimental syndrome statistics）直接反演为离散物理超图（discrete physical hypergraphs），其核心是将精确代数关联方程（exact algebraic correlation equations）与自上而下的并发剪枝策略（top-down concurrent-pruning strategy）相结合。

Result: 在基准测试中，CAHR对d=5旋转表面码（rotated surface codes）和密集8体2D颜色码（dense 8-body 2D color codes）均实现了无虚假正例的故障拓扑（fault topology）恢复。此外，研究发现在密集码中精确连续参数提取受限于“方差级联效应”（variance cascade），即绝对统计方差从高维机制向低维机制线性累积。

Conclusion: 该工作提出了两阶段推理范式（two-stage inference paradigm）：先利用CAHR提取故障拓扑，再进行连续概率优化（continuous probability optimization），为实际量子硬件中高关联噪声的表征与解码提供了实用方案。

Abstract: Fault-tolerant quantum computing fundamentally relies on the accurate characterization of circuit-level noise to optimize decoding algorithms. However, extracting complex multi-body error correlations remains challenging. Contemporary greedy inference algorithms can suffer from statistical distortion, discarding true physical mechanisms while introducing many unphysical false positives. Here, we introduce the Correlation-Analysis-based Hypergraph Reconstruction (CAHR) algorithm, a globally consistent framework to invert experimental syndrome statistics directly into discrete physical hypergraphs. By coupling exact algebraic correlation equations with a top-down concurrent-pruning strategy, CAHR recovers the fault topology without false positives for both $d=5$ rotated surface codes and dense 8-body 2D color codes in our benchmark settings. Furthermore, we show that exact continuous parameter extraction in dense codes is limited by a \textit{variance cascade}, where absolute statistical variance accumulates linearly from high- to low-degree mechanisms. This motivates a two-stage inference paradigm: utilizing CAHR to extract the fault topology, followed by continuous probability optimization. This provides a practical approach for characterizing and decoding highly correlated noise in realistic quantum hardware.

### [22] [3D Ising criticality with Platonic lattice superconducting qubits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16854)
*Liyang Sui,Hong-Hao Song,Sainan Huai,Yufan Li,Zhiwen Zong,Kunliang Bu,Xiaopei Yang,Xingrui Liu,Wenyan Jin,Bowen Chen,Xutao Zhang,Jianlan Wu,Yicong Zheng,Shengyu Zhang,Gang v. Chen,Yi Yin*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本研究利用基于共形场论（conformal field theory）态-算子对应的数字量子模拟，在具有柏拉图晶格几何的多连通9量子比特超导量子处理器上，通过扩展变分量子本征求解器（extended variational quantum eigensolver）与基于傅里叶变换的能谱提取，成功制备了三维（3D）伊辛模型（Ising model）的低能本征态，并精确测得了临界指数Δε=1.5850和ν=0.7067，与理论值高度吻合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 三维伊辛模型是统计物理（statistical physics）与临界现象（critical phenomena）中的基础模型，但由于其解析不可解性，长期以来难以精确确定普适临界指数（universal critical exponents）。尽管经典数值方法和共形自举（conformal bootstrap）技术已给出高精度估计，但直接对三维伊辛临界性进行量子模拟仍面临非平凡连接性、足够系统尺寸和高谱分辨率的挑战。

Method: 借助共形场论（conformal field theory）中的态-算子对应（state-operator correspondence），在一个具备柏拉图晶格（Platonic lattice）几何的多连通9量子比特超导量子处理器上进行数字量子模拟。采用配备基于相位的损失函数（phase-based loss function）的扩展变分量子本征求解器（extended variational quantum eigensolver），在编码于8量子比特寄存器的立方柏拉图晶格上的横向场伊辛模型（transverse-field Ising model）中变分制备低能本征态。通过傅里叶变换分析（Fourier-transform analysis）和高精度数值拟合提取四个最低本征能量，其与精确对角化（exact diagonalization）值的偏差在±0.001以内。

Result: 实验得到的标度维度（scaling dimension）Δε=1.5850和临界指数（critical exponent）ν=0.7067与理论预测吻合良好。

Conclusion: 该工作展示了利用数字量子模拟方法精确测量三维伊辛模型临界指数的可行性，验证了基于超导量子处理器和变分量子算法研究强关联统计力学系统的潜力。

Abstract: The three-dimensional (3D) Ising model is a foundational model in statistical physics and critical phenomena, yet its analytical intractability has long impeded the precise determination of universal critical exponents. While high-precision estimates have been obtained through classical numerical methods and conformal bootstrap techniques, a direct quantum simulation of the 3D Ising criticality remains challenging, requiring nontrivial connectivity, sufficient system size, and high spectral resolution. In this work, assisted by the state-operator correspondence of conformal field theory, we perform a digital quantum simulation of the 3D Ising critical exponents using a multiply-connected 9-qubit superconducting quantum processor with a Platonic lattice geometry. Employing an extended variational quantum eigensolver equipped with a phase-based loss function, we variationally prepare the low-energy eigenstates of the transverse-field Ising model on a cubic Platonic lattice encoded in an 8-qubit register. The four lowest eigenenergies are extracted via Fourier-transform analysis and high-precision numerical fitting, agreeing with the exact diagonalization values up to +/- 0.001. The resulting scaling dimension Delta_epsilon = 1.5850 and critical exponent nu = 0.7067 match well with theory.

### [23] [Bath memory as a precision resource in quantum transport](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17026)
*José Molina,Sheikh Parvez Mandal,Mahasweta Pandit,Javier Prior*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出利用结构化浴（structured bath）的存储效应，在非相互作用量子点链中实现相干费米子输运的精度增强。通过推导双阻抗匹配条件（dual impedance-matching condition），使导体模式分裂、边界耗散与浴带宽同步，从而在传输窗口内维持多模相长干涉，最小化电流Fano因子（Fano factor），并将热力学与动力学精度系数提升至马尔可夫极限（Markovian limit）之上，为量子点阵列等介观平台提供了实用的精度增强输运设计方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管结构化浴能够重塑介观量子器件中的输运涨落，但缺乏预测何种条件下可增强精度的判据。本文旨在提出一种利用浴存储效应（bath memory）实现相干费米子输运精度优势的理论路径。

Method: 基于Landauer-Büttiker形式（Landauer-Büttiker formalism），推导出双阻抗匹配条件，使导体模式分裂、边界耗散和浴带宽三者同步。通过精确的非平衡格林函数（nonequilibrium Green's function, NEGF）计算，验证了洛伦兹（Lorentzian）、高斯（Gaussian）和Newns谱密度下的最优浴带宽解析预测。

Result: 解析预测的最优浴带宽与NEGF数值计算高度一致。在该最优带宽下，电流Fano因子被最小化，热力学与动力学精度系数同时超越马尔可夫极限。最优精度区间与实验可测的电流Fano因子最小值对齐。

Conclusion: 本文提出的方案为半导体量子点阵列（semiconductor quantum-dot arrays）和超冷费米子通道（ultracold fermionic channels）等介观平台提供了实用的精度增强输运设计策略。

Abstract: Structured baths can reshape transport fluctuations in mesoscopic quantum devices, yet a predictive criterion for when this enhances precision has been lacking. We propose a route towards such precision advantages by utilizing bath memory in coherent fermionic transport through a noninteracting quantum-dot chain. Using the Landauer-Büttiker formalism, we derive a dual impedance-matching condition that synchronizes the conductor mode splitting, boundary dissipation, and bath bandwidth, and sustains constructive multimode interference across the transmission window. The analytical predictions for the optimal bath bandwidths show excellent agreement with exact nonequilibrium Green's function calculations of the transport for Lorentzian, Gaussian, and Newns spectral densities. The prescription yields an optimal bath bandwidth at which the current Fano factor is minimized and the thermodynamic and kinetic precision coefficients are simultaneously enhanced beyond their Markovian limits. The alignment of the optimal precision regime with the experimentally accessible current Fano factor minimum thus provides a practical strategy for designing precision-enhanced transport in mesoscopic platforms such as semiconductor quantum-dot arrays and ultracold fermionic channels.

</details>

### [24] [Machine learning enables roughness-driven inverse design of milling processes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16032)
*Hadi Bakhshan,Sima Farshbaf,Fernando Rastellini,Josep Maria Carbonell*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于机器学习（ML）的逆设计（inverse design）框架，用于表面铣削（surface milling）过程，以表面粗糙度（surface roughness）为设计目标。该框架通过深度神经网络（DNN）和随机森林（RF）集成模型的前向训练，并结合贝叶斯优化（Bayesian optimization, BO）解决多对一映射带来的多解性问题，最终模型平均相对误差低于5%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 制造业中对数据驱动方法的需求日益增长，尤其是在映射复杂高维关系方面；然而，逆设计（inverse design）范式面临数据集有限和鲁棒性不足的挑战。本文旨在提出一种基于机器学习（ML）的框架，解决表面铣削过程中逆设计的多解性问题（multiplicity problem）。

Method: 采用计算仿真框架生成高保真合成数据集（synthetic dataset），用于训练前向模型：深度神经网络（deep neural network, DNN）和随机森林（random forest, RF）集成。将训练好的模型集成到贝叶斯优化（Bayesian optimization, BO）流程中，以克服数据集内在的多对一映射（many-to-one mapping）导致的多解性问题。

Result: 所提模型在参考结果对比下平均相对误差低于5%，证明了方法的鲁棒性（robustness）和可靠性。该方法能够从完整解空间中识别出考虑工艺参数和刀具参数的最优铣削工艺配置。

Conclusion: 本文提出的基于机器学习的逆设计框架能够有效解决表面铣削过程中因多对一映射引起的多解性问题，并在有限数据集条件下展现出良好的鲁棒性和预测精度。

Abstract: Interest in applying data-driven approaches in manufacturing has grown significantly, particularly for mapping complex, high-dimensional relationships. The milling process is one area where predictive models can link influential parameters to surface roughness metrics prior to in situ operations. While this approach offers clear advantages, it faces challenges due to limited datasets and robustness issues in inverse design paradigms. To address these challenges, this paper proposes a machine learning (ML)-based framework for the inverse design of the surface milling process, with a focus on surface roughness as the design objective. The framework employs forward training of two ML models, a deep neural network (DNN) and a random forest (RF) ensemble, both developed using a high-fidelity synthetic dataset generated from a computational simulation framework. These trained models are integrated into a Bayesian optimization (BO) procedure to overcome the multiplicity problem arising from the many-to-one mapping inherent in the dataset. The approach identifies top-performing milling process configurations, considering both process and tool parameters, and presents them from the full solution space. The models achieve average relative errors below 5% when compared to reference results, thereby demonstrating the robustness and reliability of the proposed methodology.

### [25] [Time-of-flight photon spectroscopy for scanning tunneling microscopy luminescence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16936)
*Lebin Yu,Jiří Doležal,Maximilian Rödel,Amandeep Sagwal,Benjamin Frölich,Martin Švec,Fabian Donat Natterer*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 本文构建并调试了一种用于扫描隧道显微镜发光（STML）的时间飞行光子光谱仪（TOFS），利用长色散光纤的波长相关折射率将光子到达时间转换为波长信息，实现了近红外范围内低成本、高性能的光谱测量，并可与超导纳米线单光子探测器等兼容以扩展光谱范围。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为扫描隧道显微镜发光（STML）技术提供一种便捷、低成本的光谱测量方案，以克服传统光栅光谱仪在近红外波段及系统集成上的局限性。

Method: 利用长色散光纤的波长相关折射率将光子到达时间转换为波长信息：蓝光光子延迟大于红光光子；采用脉冲激发源（激光脉冲或电压脉冲）将光子从隧道结激发至单光子探测器；TOFS校准可在独立台式实验中完成并转移至STML装置。

Result: 通过与常规光栅光谱仪同步记录Ag-Ag(111)等离激元发光进行验证，结果表明TOFS在近红外范围内性能良好，可作为STML系统的直接、经济有效的补充模块。

Conclusion: TOFS可作为一种便捷的低成本升级方案集成到现有STML系统中；其设计支持单光子探测器的即插替换（如超导纳米线单光子探测器或热辐射计），有望将可用光谱范围扩展至当前STML装置的能力之外。

Abstract: We build and commission a time-of-flight photon spectrometer (TOFS) for scanning tunneling microscopy luminescence (STML). We obtain the spectrum by exploiting the wavelength dependent refractive index of a long dispersive optical fiber that converts photon arrival times into wavelength information; blue photons are delayed more than red photons. The setup uses a pulsed excitation source, either laser flashes or voltage pulses, to launch the photons from the junction into a single photon detector. The TOFS calibration can be performed and transferred to the STML setup from a separate benchtop experiment using pulsed light sources with known wavelength. We verify the TOFS during STML operation by simultaneously recording luminescence from the Ag-Ag(111) plasmon using a conventional grating spectrometer. Our experiments show that the TOFS is a straightforward and cost-effective addition to existing STML setups with good performance in the near-infrared range. The TOFS is compatible with a drop-in replacement of the single photon detector such as a superconducting nanowire single photon detector or even bolometers that may expand the useful spectral range beyond the abilities of current STML setups.

### [26] [Ultralow-Energy Measurements using the Startpoint of $β$ Decays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15014)
*Daniel Kodroff,Michael R. Williams*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于低温固态探测器技术的β衰变新测量方法，利用β动能起点（startpoint）作为探测弱核物理的独特窗口。该技术可搜索keV–MeV能区重惰性中微子（sterile neutrino），灵敏度超越当前最优约束；同时，反冲子核（recoiling daughter ion）能谱可用于校准亚GeV暗物质探测中的核反冲响应。论文还概述了利用中子活化在硅衬底中原位产生³²P的实验方案，并评估了相关灵敏度与校准前景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: β衰变的动能起点（β startpoint，即β动能为零之处）在实验上尚未被利用，但其为弱核物理（weak nuclear physics）提供了独特的探测手段。现有方法对keV–MeV能区重惰性中微子（sterile neutrino）的搜索灵敏度有限，且亚GeV暗物质探测（sub-GeV dark matter searches）中核反冲响应的校准存在关键假设亟待检验。

Method: 采用低温固态探测器（low-temperature solid-state detector）技术进行β衰变测量；通过中子活化（neutron activation）在硅衬底中原位（in situ）产生³²P作为β源；利用β动能起点信号搜索惰性中微子，并分析反冲子核（recoiling daughter ion）的能谱来校准核反冲响应。

Result: 基于当前技术，该方法对惰性中微子与电子耦合的灵敏度可超越现有最佳约束（current best constraints）。论文给出了针对惰性中微子的预计灵敏度，并评估了核反冲校准（nuclear recoil calibration）的可行性。

Conclusion: 该测量方案同时服务于两种物理目标：在keV–MeV能区搜索重惰性中微子，以及为亚GeV暗物质实验提供核反冲响应的校准手段。未来可通过进一步优化实验设计来提升灵敏度。

Abstract: We propose a novel measurement of $β$ decays using low-temperature solid-state detector technologies. The $β$ startpoint, where the $β$ kinetic energy is zero, offers a unique probe of weak nuclear physics that has not yet been exploited experimentally. We describe how this technique enables searches for heavy sterile neutrinos in the keV--MeV energy range and show that, with current technologies, sensitivities to sterile neutrino coupling to electrons can be achieved that exceed the current best constraints. The spectrum produced by the recoiling daughter ion also offers a calibration of the nuclear recoil response, addressing key assumptions in sub-GeV dark matter searches. We outline a potential experimental scheme using neutron activation to produce $^{32}$P $\textit{in situ}$ in a silicon substrate, discuss projected sensitivities to sterile neutrinos, and evaluate the prospects for nuclear recoil calibrations.

### [27] [CKM determination from $W$ decays with jet flavor tagging at CEPC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15773)
*Zhao-Ling Zhang,Li-Bo Liao,Jia-Rong Li,Jia-Bao Gong,Wei-Min Song,Gang Li*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本研究利用CEPC模拟的$e^+e^- \to W^+W^- \to μν\bar{q}q^\prime$样本（积分亮度$21.6\,\mathrm{ab}^{-1}$，质心能量$\sqrt{s}=240\,\mathrm{GeV}$），分析了CEPC对半轻子$W$对衰变中CKM矩阵元$|V_{ij}|$的灵敏度（排除$|V_{ub}|$）。预测的统计精度分别达到$|V_{cb}|$为$0.59\,\%$、$|V_{cs}|$为$0.01\,\%$，表明CEPC能够从强子$W$衰变中提供直接、高精度且很大程度上模型无关的CKM矩阵元测定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高精度测量CKM矩阵元（CKM matrix elements）是检验标准模型（Standard Model, SM）带电电流味结构（charged-current flavor structure）并探寻可能的新物理（new physics）效应的关键途径。

Method: 使用CEPC模拟的$e^+e^- \to W^+W^- \to μν\bar{q}q^\prime$样本（积分亮度$21.6\,\mathrm{ab}^{-1}$，$\sqrt{s}=240\,\mathrm{GeV}$），通过对半轻子$W$对衰变（semileptonic $W$-pair decays）进行模拟分析来研究CKM矩阵元$|V_{ij}|$的灵敏度；$|V_{ub}|$因贡献可忽略而被排除。

Result: 投影统计精度：$|V_{cb}|$可达$0.59\,\%$，$|V_{cs}|$可达$0.01\,\%$。

Conclusion: CEPC能够从强子$W$衰变中提供直接、高精度且大体上模型无关（largely model-independent）的CKM矩阵元测定。这些测量将为SM带电电流味结构提供严格的相容性检验，并通过观测与SM预期的偏差，为可能的新物理效应提供灵敏探针。系统性不确定度主要来源已讨论，进一步的改进预期来自实验和理论两方面，包括专用数据驱动的探测器响应标定、喷注味标记（jet flavor tagging）性能优化以及更高阶电弱和QCD修正计算。

Abstract: This study investigates the sensitivity of the CEPC to CKM matrix elements $|V_{ij}|$ in semileptonic $W$-pair decays using simulated $e^+e^- \to W^+W^- \to μν\bar{q}q^\prime$ samples corresponding to $21.6\,\mathrm{ab}^{-1}$ at $\sqrt{s}=240\,\mathrm{GeV}$, with $|V_{ub}|$ excluded because of its negligible contribution. The projected statistical precisions reach $0.59\,\%$ for $|V_{cb}|$ and $0.01\,\%$ for $|V_{cs}|$, indicating that the CEPC can provide direct, high-precision, and largely model-independent determinations of CKM matrix elements from hadronic $W$ decays. The main sources of systematic uncertainty are discussed, and further improvements are expected from both experimental and theoretical developments, including dedicated data-driven calibrations of detector response and jet flavor tagging performance, as well as more precise higher-order calculations of the relevant electroweak and QCD corrections. Such measurements would provide stringent consistency tests of the Standard Model charged-current flavor structure and offer sensitivity to possible new physics effects through deviations from the Standard Model expectations.

Abstract: Heavy quarks are produced in the early stages of heavy ion collisions due to their large mass, and subsequently traverse the entire QCD medium evolution. In the LHCb experiment, fixed-target collisions cover an unexplored energy range that lies above that of previous fixed-target experiments but below the top RHIC energy for AA collisions. Abstract: Using more than 600 thousand $K_{S}^{0}\toπ^{+}π^{-}$ decays from the $e^{+}e^{-}\toφ(1020)\to K_{S}^{0}K_{L}^{0}$ reaction, the neutral kaon mass has been measured with the CMD-3 detector at the VEPP-2000 collider. Using the beam energies control by the back-scattering laser light photons, and a calibration to the world average $φ$-meson mass, the neutral kaon mass is determind to be m($K^0$) = 497.587 $\pm$ 0.004(stat.) $\pm$ 0.008(syst.) $\pm$ 0.009(calibr.) \mevcc, where the first uncertainty is statistical, the second is systematic, and the third is the uncertainty from the energy calibration.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 核反应堆产生低能量高通量的电子反中微子，为在全相干区间研究弹性中微子-原子核散射（νA_el）提供了理想平台，因此需要利用实验数据对该散射截面进行精确约束。

Method: 使用TEXONO实验中的两个电制冷p型点接触锗探测器（p-type point-contact Germanium detectors），质量分别为523 g和1434 g，在Kuo-Sheng反应堆中微子实验室采集数据；总曝光量为404 kg·天（反应堆开启）和813.7 kg·天（反应堆关闭），电子等价阈值（electron-equivalent threshold）为200 eV_ee；采用Lindhard模型描述电离产额的抑制，其中淬灭因子（quenching factor）由单一参数k参数化。

Result: 在基准值k=0.162下，观测截面与标准模型（Standard Model, SM）预测截面之比ρ<2.0（90%置信水平）；k>0.205的区域在90%置信水平下被排除；从中微子-原子核散射导出的中微子磁矩（neutrino magnetic moment）上限为μ_ν<5.9×10^{-10} μ_B（90%置信水平）。

Conclusion: TEXONO实验利用大质量p型点接触锗探测器在反应堆中微子源下获得了对νA_el截面的改进约束，同时给出了对中微子磁矩的竞争性上限，展示了该实验平台在低能中微子散射研究中的有效性。

Abstract: The low energy and intense flux of electron anti-neutrinos from nuclear reactors provide the perfect stage to study elastic neutrino-nucleus scattering ($νA_{el}$) in the fully coherent regime. We report results from the TEXONO experiment using electro-cooled $p$-type point-contact Germanium detectors with masses of 523~g and 1434~g at the Kuo-Sheng Reactor Neutrino Laboratory. We report improved constraints on the $νA_{el}$ cross section with a combined exposure of 404(813.7)~kg-days of Reactor ON(OFF) data at an electron-equivalent threshold of 200~eV$_{ee}$. The Lindhard model, in which the quenching factor is parameterized by a single parameter k, is adopted to describe the suppression of ionization yield. At the benchmark value of k=0.162, a limit of $ρ<$2.0 at 90\% confidence level (CL) is derived, where $ρ$ represents the ratio of the observed to the predicted Standard Model cross section. Moreover the region k$>$0.205 is excluded at 90\% CL using the SM-predicted $νA_{el}$ rate. A bound on the neutrino magnetic moment from $νA_{el}$ at $μ_ν {<} 5.9 \times 10^{-10}~μ_B$ at 90\% CL is also derived.

</details>

### [32] [Efficient Multi-Precision Computation of Bessel Functions for Real Orders and Complex Arguments with Fortran Implementation -- Part II: The Modified Bessel Function of the Second Kind, $K_ν(z)$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14839)
*Mofreh R. Zaghloul,Steven G. Johnson*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种高效、自包含的计算第二类修正贝塞尔函数K_ν(z)（复参数、实阶数）的算法，通过自适应选择幂级数、大|z|渐近展开、大|ν|一致渐近展开及数值稳定的前向递推关系，并提供了支持双精度和四精度的Fortran实现，在精度和计算速度上均优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为修正贝塞尔函数族（K_ν(z)）开发一种可靠、高效且覆盖广泛参数域（复参数、实阶数）的数值算法，弥补现有方法在数值稳定性或计算效率上的不足。

Method: 算法自适应地在多种解析表示（analytic representations）间切换，包括幂级数（power series）、大|z|渐近展开（large-|z| asymptotics）、大|ν|一致渐近展开（uniform asymptotics for large |ν|）以及带有区域边界优化的数值稳定前向递推关系（forward recurrence）。实现语言为Fortran，支持双精度（double precision）和四精度（quadruple precision）计算。

Result: 四精度扩展了可靠计算域并改善了困难参数区间的稳定性。精度以高精度Maple结果为基准进行了验证。基准测试显示，该算法运行时间显著优于文献中的已有方法，且避免了这些方法在多个参数数量级区间内的数值失效问题。

Conclusion: 结合姊妹篇Part~I（针对I_ν），本工作为{I_ν, K_ν}在广泛参数范围内提供了一套全面的多精度数值计算工具集。

Abstract: This paper, the second in a series, presents an efficient, self-contained algorithm for computing the modified Bessel function of the second kind, \(K_ν(z)\) for complex argument and real orders, building on Part~I (for \(I_ν\)). The method adaptively selects among analytic representations such as power series, large-\(|z|\) asymptotics, uniform asymptotics for large \(|ν|\), and numerically stable forward recurrence with region boundaries tuned for accuracy and efficiency. A robust \texttt{Fortran} implementation supports double precision and quadruple precision. The use of quadruple precision extends the reliable computational domain and improves stability in challenging regimes. Accuracy is validated against high-precision \texttt{Maple} results, and benchmarks show runtimes significantly superior to those of established methods, in the literature, while avoiding their numerical failure modes across several decades of the parameter domain. Together with Part~I, this work provides a comprehensive, multiple-precision toolkit for \(\{I_ν,K_ν\}\) across wide parameter ranges.

</details>


### [33] [Efficient Multi-Precision Computation of Bessel Functions for Real Orders and Complex Arguments with a Fortran Implementation -- Part III: Regular Bessel Functions of the First and Second Kinds $J_ν(z)$ and $Y_ν(z)$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14937)
*Mofreh R Zaghloul,Steven G. Johnson*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本论文提出并实现了针对实阶复自变量贝塞尔函数 J_nu(z) 与 Y_nu(z) 的数值稳定、高效算法，支持双精度与四精度 Fortran 实现。在双精度下性能显著优于 Algorithm 644，且相比 Algorithm 912 在四精度下精度更高、计算成本极低（仅数千分之一到数百分之一）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为弥补现有算法（如 Algorithm 644 仅支持双精度、Algorithm 912 适用范围受限）的不足，开发数值稳定且高效、支持高精度（四精度）与更广泛参数域（实阶复自变量）的贝塞尔函数（Bessel functions）计算方法。

Method: 提出针对贝塞尔函数 J_nu(z) 与 Y_nu(z) 的稳定高效算法，支持正负实阶（real orders）和复自变量（complex arguments）；在双精度（double precision）与四精度（quadruple precision）下实现多精度 Fortran 程序。

Result: 双精度下，本算法执行时间约为 Algorithm 644 的 35–67%（J_nu）和 44–72%（Y_nu），且在 Algorithm 644 失效时仍能产生可靠结果；相比 Algorithm 912，双精度精度相当，四精度精度显著更高，计算成本仅为 Algorithm 912 的千分之几到百分之几。本算法在全部测试域内稳定准确，而 Algorithm 912 仅适用于 (Re(nu), z) 平面的有限区域。

Conclusion: 本论文所提算法在数值稳定性、计算效率、精度和适用范围上均优于或至少不弱于现有主流算法（Algorithm 644 与 Algorithm 912），尤其在高精度计算（四精度）和极端参数区域具有显著优势。

Abstract: This paper is the final part in a series devoted to the development of numerically stable and efficient algorithms, together with multi-precision Fortran implementations, for computing Bessel functions with real orders and complex arguments. Parts~I and~II presented stable and efficient algorithms for the modified Bessel functions I_nu(z) and K_nu(z); here we treat Bessel functions J_nu(z) and Y_nu(z). The proposed algorithms support complex arguments for both positive and negative real orders and are implemented in native double and quadruple precision. Quadruple precision substantially increases dynamic range and accuracy (by roughly an order of magnitude in reliably computable |nu| and |z|), thereby extending applicability to problems requiring 20-30 digits. Comprehensive accuracy and performance comparisons are carried out against both the widely used Algorithm~644, restricted to double-precision arithmetic, and the more recent Algorithm~912, which supports both double- and quad-precision arithmetic as well as complex orders. In double precision, the present implementation consistently outperforms Algorithm~644, achieving execution times of approximately 35-67% for J_nu(z) and 44-72% for Y_nu(z), while also producing reliable results where Algorithm~644 fails. In comparison with Algorithm~912, the present algorithm achieves comparable accuracy in double-precision computations and significantly higher accuracy in quad-precision calculations. At the same time, it requires only a small fraction of the computational cost (from a few thousandths to a few hundredths) of the time taken by Algorithm~912, depending on the precision and parameter regime. Furthermore, unlike Algorithm~912, whose applicability is restricted to a limited region of the (Re(nu),z) plane, the present algorithm remains stable and accurate over the full tested domain for which reliable reference values are available.

</details>

### [34] [Semiclassical Gravity Efficiently Solves $\mathsf{NP}$-Complete Problems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14806)
*Matthew Fox,Chaitanya Karamchedu,Sotirios Mygdalas*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文证明，在引力场为经典且通过半经典爱因斯坦场方程与量子场耦合的假设下，一个大质量非相对论性量子比特的弱场动力学能够在多项式时间内解决一个NP完全问题，表明这种半经典引力设定违反物理扩展丘奇-图灵论题，从而间接支持引力量子化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨半经典引力（semiclassical gravity）——即引力场保持经典、通过半经典爱因斯坦场方程（semiclassical Einstein field equations）与量子场耦合——是否会导致超出标准量子计算框架的计算能力，并以此检验物理扩展丘奇-图灵论题（Physical Extended Church–Turing Thesis）以及引力量子化（quantization of gravity）的必要性。

Method: 分析一个大质量且非相对论性的量子比特（qubit）在弱场极限下的动力学，假设其引力场由半经典爱因斯坦场方程描述。

Result: 证明在该假设下，该量子比特的动力学原则上可以在多项式时间内求解一个NP完全（NP-complete）问题。

Conclusion: 这种巨大的计算能力源自半经典爱因斯坦场方程提供的非线性动力学（non-linear dynamics），而上述两个假设（经典引力与半经典耦合）直接导致物理扩展丘奇-图灵论题被违反。作者将此视为引力必须被量子化的证据。

Abstract: Assuming the gravitational field is classical and that it couples to quantum fields via the semiclassical Einstein field equations, we show that the weak-field dynamics of a massive and non-relativistic qubit can in principle be used to solve an $\mathsf{NP}$-complete problem in polynomial time. We attribute this vast computational power to the non-linear dynamics afforded by the semiclassical Einstein field equations. Consequently, the above two assumptions entail a violation of the Physical Extended Church--Turing Thesis, which we regard as evidence for the quantization of gravity.

</details>


### [35] [Perturbative and Non-Perturbative Contributions to Black Hole Thermodynamics with String Clouds and Dark Matter Backgrounds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14815)
*Kumar Sambhav Upadhyay,Sudhaker Upadhyay,Bhabani Prasad Mandal*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本研究系统分析了在反德西特时空中、受到完美流体暗物质背景和弦云包围的黑洞在微扰与非微扰量子修正下的热力学性质，发现对数型熵修正可导致稳定相变，而指数型修正仅在小半径区域显著，且两类修正下均未在物理允许域内找到类范德瓦尔斯临界点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有黑洞热力学研究多基于半经典贝肯斯坦-霍金熵，而量子引力效应（如热涨落修正）对暗物质背景中黑洞的影响尚不明确，亟需系统分析微扰与非微扰修正对该系统的热力学稳定性与相结构的作用。

Method: 以贝肯斯坦-霍金熵（Bekenstein-Hawking entropy）为半经典基线，分别引入小热涨落的对数型修正（perturbative logarithmic correction）和指数型修正（non-perturbative exponential correction）；推导修正后的熵、质量、亥姆霍兹自由能（Helmholtz free energy）、吉布斯自由能（Gibbs free energy）、热容（heat capacity）和压强；通过热容符号判定稳定性，通过检查压强对热力学体积的一阶和二阶导数同时为零的条件搜索类范德瓦尔斯临界点（van der Waals-like critical point）。

Result: 对数型修正下系统出现从热力学不稳定到稳定相的转变；指数型修正对大黑洞可忽略，但随视界半径趋近普朗克尺度（Planck regime）而变得显著；两类修正下均未在物理允许域内找到类范德瓦尔斯临界点。

Conclusion: 对数型与指数型熵修正在对黑洞热力学稳定性与相结构的调控中发挥不同作用；非微扰效应仅在小尺度下重要，微扰修正则主导大尺度稳定行为；该系统中不存在类范德瓦尔斯相变。

Abstract: We investigate the effects of perturbative and non-perturbative quantum corrections on the thermodynamics of black holes immersed in a perfect fluid dark matter (PFDM) background with a cloud of strings (CoS) in asymptotically anti-de Sitter spacetime. Starting from the Bekenstein-Hawking entropy as the semiclassical baseline, we incorporate two distinct classes of corrections arising from small thermal fluctuations about thermodynamic equilibrium. In the perturbative sector, we derive the logarithmically corrected entropy and systematically compute the resulting modifications to the mass, Helmholtz free energy, Gibbs free energy, heat capacity, and pressure. The stability structure of the system is analyzed through the sign behavior of the heat capacity, which reveals a transition from a thermodynamically unstable to a stable phase. In the non-perturbative sector, we introduce exponential corrections to the entropy and carry out a parallel analysis of all thermodynamic quantities. We demonstrate that non-perturbative effects are negligible for large black holes but become significant as the horizon radius shrinks toward the Planck regime. In both sectors, we investigate the equation of state and search for a van der Waals-like critical point by examining the simultaneous vanishing of the first and second pressure derivatives with respect to thermodynamic volume; no such inflection point is found within the physically admissible domain. Our results illuminate the contrasting roles of logarithmic and exponential entropy corrections in governing the thermodynamic stability and phase structure of PFDM black holes with a CoS.

</details>


### [36] [An inductive approach to $f(R)$ gravity and its application to extended sources](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14859)
*Federico Scali*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文基于一个先前构建的归纳式$f(R)$引力拉格朗日量（Lagrangian）族，批判性地回顾了其构建方法，着重分析了该方法的普适性及其在不同修正引力框架（modified gravity frameworks）中的适用性；同时推导了扩展源（extended source）在该模型下产生的修正牛顿势（modified Newtonian potential），并讨论了牛顿极限（Newtonian limit）的自洽性，进而指出其在星系动力学（galactic dynamics）中的应用前景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 延续前期工作中仅利用太阳系物理（Solar System physics）归纳构造$f(R)$引力拉格朗日量的思路，进一步检验该模型的合理性，并探索其向更大尺度（如星系动力学）拓展的可能性。

Method: 首先，对前期工作中在史瓦西背景（Schwarzschild background）下微扰求解修正爱因斯坦方程（modified Einstein equations）并后验重建拉格朗日量的方法进行批判性回顾；然后，在该归纳式$f(R)$模型中推导扩展源所产生的修正牛顿势。

Result: 证明了该归纳式构建方法具有普适性，可适用于不同的修正引力框架；获得了扩展源下的修正牛顿势表达式，并验证了牛顿极限的一致性。

Conclusion: 该归纳式$f(R)$模型不仅在太阳系尺度上自洽，其修正牛顿势也为应用于星系动力学提供了有趣的理论视角。

Abstract: In a previous work (Phys. Rev. D 110, 064042), a new family of $f(R)$ gravitational Lagrangians was constructed inductively using only Solar System physics. Specifically, the modified Einstein equations were solved perturbatively on a Schwarzschild background, and the corresponding Lagrangian was reconstructed a posteriori from the solution. Classical Solar System tests were then employed to constrain the fundamental length scale quantifying the deviation from general relativity. In the first part of this work, the construction of the model is critically reviewed, emphasizing the generality of the approach and the applicability to different modified gravity frameworks. In the second part, the modified Newtonian potential produced by an extended source is derived within the new inductive $f(R)$ model, discussing the consistency of the Newtonian limit. In this context, the application to galactic dynamics emerges as an intriguing perspective.

</details>


### [37] [Tidal Stripping of Matter Bound to the Secondary in Extreme Mass-Ratio Inspirals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14894)
*Sreejith Nair,Sayak Datta*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了极端质量比旋近（EMRI）中绑定在次级恒星质量天体上的环境物质（如气体或暗物质）在LISA频段旋近过程中被潮汐剥离的效应，发现该过程会显著改变引力波相位，即使环境质量仅为~10⁻³ M☉，累积相位偏移也可大于1，亚太阳质量情形下可达约10³弧度，忽略此效应会严重偏折EMRI参数推断，并提供了探测亚天文单位尺度行星至亚太阳质量环境的新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有EMRI环境研究几乎全部聚焦于主黑洞周围的环境物质，而忽略了绑定在次级天体上的物质（如气体或暗物质）。本文旨在揭示这类绑定物质在旋近过程中被潮汐剥离对引力波（gravitational-wave, GW）信号的影响，并评估其可观测性及物理信息提取潜力。

Method: 从解析和数值角度分析了绑定在次级天体上的环境物质在LISA频段旋近过程中逐步被潮汐剥离的动力学过程，计算了由此导致的引力波相位修正，并与恒定质量波形模板进行相位残差对比。

Result: 绑定物质被剥离会改变旋近天体的绑定质量，从而在次级质量的领头阶修正引力波相位。即使环境质量仅为~10⁻³ M☉，相对于带初始绑定质量波形的累积相位偏移（dephasing）也可大于1；亚太阳质量情形下，相对相位偏移可达O(10³) rad。忽略此效应会导致EMRI参数推断产生与频带内绑定质量分数变化相当的偏误。

Conclusion: 潮汐剥离现象携带了绑定物质的质量和致密性信息，为探测恒星质量黑洞周围亚天文单位尺度、行星至亚太阳质量级别的环境物质提供了新手段。该方法有望在LISA时代成为研究EMRI环境的新途径。

Abstract: Environmental studies of extreme mass-ratio inspirals (EMRIs) have focused almost entirely on matter surrounding the primary supermassive black hole. We instead consider matter bound to the stellar-mass secondary (e.g., gas or dark matter); which can be progressively tidally stripped during the LISA-band inspiral. This changes the bound mass of the inspiraling object, modifying the gravitational-wave (GW) phase at leading order in the secondary mass. Furthermore, as the signal interpolates from an initially dressed inspiral to a nearly bare one, it can produce a characteristic inflection in the residual phase with constant mass waveform templates. Even for an environmental mass $\sim 10^{-3}\,M_{\odot}$, the cumulative dephasing relative to in band initial bound mass waveform can be larger than unity. In subsolar mass cases, the relative dephasing can reach $O(10^3)\, \rm rad$. Neglecting this effect may bias inferred EMRI parameters at the level of the fractional change in the in-band bound mass. The tidal stripping phenomena carry information about the mass and the compactness of the bound matter, enabling probes of sub-AU, planetary- to subsolar-mass environments surrounding stellar-mass black holes.

</details>


### [38] [Eccentricity in Disguise? Insights from GW231123 and Numerically Simulated Binary Black Hole Merger Signals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15150)
*Koustav Chandra,Johann Fernandes,Akshita Mittal,Gregorio Carullo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: GW231123 是一个来自总质量约为 250 M☉ 的双黑洞并合（black hole binary merger）的引力波信号，是 LIGO-Virgo-Kagra 合作组织迄今探测到的最重大信号。该事件在标准先验下显示出极快的自旋（spin）分量（χ₁,₂ ≳ 0.7，90% 一维置信度），但这一推断可能因忽略了非圆形轨道（non-circular）修正的波形模型而产生偏差；环冈（ringdown）分析及偏心（eccentric）数值相对论（numerical-relativity）模板的再分析表明，准球形（quasi-spherical）模板仍更受数据青睐，但偏心解释具有潜在可能性，最终群体（population）分析确认了该事件在当前双黑洞群体中的特殊性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: GW231123 是迄今探测到的最大质量双黑洞并合事件，且推断出自旋极高，这对现有层级并合（hierarchical merger）模型构成挑战，亟需验证其物理性质是否受波形模型偏差影响。

Method: 采用缺少并合-环冈阶段（merger-ringdown stage）偏心修正的波形模型进行推断，并利用可用偏心数值相对论目录（eccentric numerical-relativity catalogues）进行再分析；同时进行双星无关的环冈分析（binary-agnostic ringdown analysis）以及基于群体信息参数先验（population-informed parametric priors）的分析。

Result: 偏心模板虽能良好拟合数据，但准球形模板仍更受青睐；环冈分析确认了与大偏心值相关的次级似然峰（secondary likelihood peak）；基于群体先验的分析确认了该事件在现有双黑洞群体（black hole binary population）中的特殊性。

Conclusion: 保留显著偏心率的双星在忽略非圆形修正时可能被误判为近极端自旋（near-extremally spinning）系统；波形的偏心修正对准确推断类似事件至关重要，而改进的偏心波形模型（eccentric model）是评估该解释可靠性的前提。

Abstract: GW231123 is a gravitational-wave signal originating from the merger of a black hole binary with total mass $\sim 250 M_{\odot}$, the largest ever detected by the LIGO-Virgo-Kagra Collaboration. Remarkably, under standard priors, the system features among the fastest-spinning binary components confidently measured in binary mergers, $ χ_{1,2} \gtrsim 0.7$ at $90\%$ one-dimensional credibility, according to the most accurate model employed. As typical binary mergers result in remnants with $χ\sim 0.7$, such spin values are challenging to obtain even from previous (hierarchical) mergers. These inferred properties rely on waveform models lacking eccentric corrections in the merger-ringdown stage. Here, we show that binaries retaining significant eccentricity up to merger can be misinterpreted as near-extremally spinning when non-circular corrections are neglected. Binary-agnostic ringdown analysis instead provides unbiased estimates of the remnant properties, provided that a robust estimate of the signal peak can be obtained. We re-analyse GW231123 using available eccentric numerical-relativity catalogues, finding that although eccentric templates can provide a good fit to the data, quasi-spherical templates are still favoured. Ringdown analyses confirm a secondary likelihood peak correlated with large eccentricity values, but improved eccentric models will be required to assess the reliability of this interpretation. Finally, analysing GW231123 under population-informed parametric priors confirms the exceptional nature of this event within the current black hole binary population.

</details>


### [39] [General Relativity and Background Independence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15224)
*Antonio Vassallo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文系统分析了经典时空物理学中背景独立性（background independence）的多种形式化策略，并探讨了量子引力（quantum gravity）等后继理论是否应继承广义相对论（General Relativity, GR）的背景独立性。文章主张背景独立性更应被视为一种诊断与比较工具，而非必要的物理要求。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 背景独立性被广泛视为广义相对论相对于牛顿理论和狭义相对论的关键概念进步，但其精确形式化定义及物理与哲学意义仍存在争议，这促使本文进行系统分析。

Method: 本文采用系统分析的方法，梳理了经典时空物理学中捕捉背景独立性的多种策略，并结合当代争论与一系列案例研究展开论证。

Result: 文章论证了背景独立性更宜被理解为一个诊断与比较工具，而非一个必要的物理要求；这一视角既凸显了消除背景结构（background structures）的概念优点，也揭示了其解释代价。

Conclusion: 本文的结论有助于解释为何背景独立性在当代基础研究中仍然是一个未解决问题（open problem），并为后续的量子引力研究提供了概念框架上的反思。

Abstract: General Relativity (GR) is widely regarded as a paradigmatic example of a background independent theory, a feature often taken to mark a decisive conceptual advance over its Newtonian and special relativistic predecessors. Yet the notion of background independence admits multiple formalizations, and its precise physical and philosophical significance remains contested. This chapter offers a systematic analysis of the strategies that have been proposed to capture background independence in classical spacetime physics. The discussion then turns to a central open question: whether, and in what sense, a successor theory of GR -- such as a theory of quantum gravity -- should be expected to inherit GR's background independence. Drawing on contemporary debates and a range of case studies, the chapter argues that background independence is best understood as a diagnostic and comparative tool rather than as a necessary physical requirement. The resulting perspective highlights both the conceptual virtues and the interpretive costs of eliminating background structures, and helps to explain why background independence remains an open problem in contemporary foundational research.
