Method: 采用第一性原理（first-principles）筛选方法，识别非中心对称QFP材料；结合带分辨贝利相位（band-resolved Berry-phase）分析，研究光学跃迁中瓦尼尔中心（Wannier center）位移与位移矢量之间的关系。

Result: 发现 $\mathrm{InNbBr}_6$ 和 $\mathrm{InPS}_3$ 等材料具有巨大SHG响应。其主导光学跃迁连接占据态和低能未占据态，这些态的瓦尼尔中心位于不同的分数威科夫位置（fractional Wyckoff positions），产生大的跃迁分辨瓦尼尔中心位移（transition-resolved Wannier-center displacement），进而形成大的位移矢量及其对静态SHG磁化率的带内贡献（intraband contribution）。

Conclusion: 对称性量子化形式极化可以通过分数瓦尼尔中心扇区之间的跃迁变得光学活跃，提供了一种对称性引导的路径，用于实现巨SHG和位移电流响应。

Abstract: Electric polarization is a static ground-state Berry-phase property, whereas second-harmonic generation (SHG) and shift current are dynamical optical responses. Their connection is encoded in the shift vector, whose Brillouin-zone average is governed by the band-resolved Berry-phase polarization difference between the optically connected initial and final states. Here we exploit this geometric relation in quantized formal polarization (QFP) crystals, where symmetry-quantized formal-polarization branches correspond to fractional Wannier-center sectors. First-principles screening identifies noncentrosymmetric QFP materials with giant SHG responses, including $\mathrm{InNbBr}_6$ and $\mathrm{InPS}_3$. Band-resolved Berry-phase analysis shows that their dominant optical transitions connect occupied and low-lying unoccupied states whose Wannier centers lie at distinct fractional Wyckoff positions, producing a large transition-resolved Wannier-center displacement. This displacement gives rise to a large shift vector and a dominant shift-vector-related intraband contribution to the static SHG susceptibility. Our results show that symmetry-quantized formal polarization can become optically active through transitions between fractional Wannier-center sectors, providing a symmetry-guided route to giant SHG and shift-current responses.

### [87] [Collective relaxation eigenmodes and anisotropic magnon thermal transport in $α$-MnTe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16129)
*Rui-Jie Yao,Lei Wang,Bo-Ye Sun*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过求解含四磁子碰撞矩阵的三维线性化玻尔兹曼输运方程，研究了交错磁体α-MnTe中本征磁子热输运，发现完整线性化玻尔兹曼方程结果在低温下比弛豫时间近似高一个数量级以上，并揭示出显著的输运各向异性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了超越弛豫时间近似（relaxation-time approximation），更准确地理解交错磁体（altermagnet）中本征磁子（magnon）热输运的微观机制，特别是动量相关零模（zero modes）的弛豫行为和各向异性的物理起源。

Method: 求解三维线性化玻尔兹曼输运方程（linearized Boltzmann transport equation），并显式包含四磁子碰撞矩阵（four-magnon collision matrix）。通过对碰撞矩阵进行对角化，直接获取弛豫本征模（relaxation eigenmodes）。

Result: Umklapp散射（Umklapp scattering）解除了Normal散射碰撞算符中的动量相关零模，显著修正了低能弛豫谱。完整线性化玻尔兹曼方程结果在低温下比弛豫时间近似高一个数量级以上，且表现出强输运各向异性（transport anisotropy）：面外热导率在研究温度范围内始终大于面内分量。主导热载模保留了来自Normal散射零模的动量类特征，面外热导率较大主要源于更强的面外群速度（group-velocity）贡献，而非弛豫寿命（relaxation lifetime）的显著差异。

Conclusion: 在交错磁体α-MnTe中，弛豫时间近似严重低估了磁子热导率，且无法正确描述低温下的输运行为与各向异性；基于完整碰撞矩阵的玻尔兹曼方程方法提供了更准确的描述，揭示了群速度各向异性是各向异性热输运的主导因素。

Abstract: The intrinsic magnon thermal transport in the altermagnet $α$-MnTe is studied by solving the three-dimensional linearized Boltzmann transport equation with the four-magnon collision matrix. Diagonalizing the collision matrix gives direct access to the relaxation eigenmodes beyond the relaxation-time approximation. We show that Umklapp scattering lifts the momentum-related zero modes of the Normal-only collision operator and substantially modifies the low-lying relaxation spectrum. Using the same collision matrix, we compute the magnon thermal conductivity tensor. The full linearized Boltzmann transport equation result exceeds the relaxation-time approximation by more than an order of magnitude at low temperature and reveals a strong transport anisotropy, with the out-of-plane thermal conductivity remaining larger than the in-plane component over the studied temperature range. A mode-resolved analysis shows that the dominant heat-carrying modes retain momentum-like character inherited from the Normal-only zero modes, and that the larger out-of-plane conductivity mainly originates from the stronger out-of-plane group-velocity contribution, rather than from a large difference in relaxation lifetimes.

### [88] [InvDesMobility: a reliability-gated first-principles feedback framework for closed-loop materials discovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16133)
*Wen-Kao Li,Ze-Feng Gao,Peng-Jie Guo,Wei Ji,Zhong-Yi Lu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出InvDesMobility，一个基于可靠性门控（reliability-gated）的第一性原理（first-principles）反馈框架，用于逆向材料设计（inverse materials design），重点关注载流子迁移率（carrier mobility）的闭环发现。该框架通过多智能体自动化密度泛函理论（DFT）、证据分层、生成式结构提议、获取排名和可审计发布等模块，在多个迭代中筛选了240万个结构，最终保留了86个可靠门控的生成通道，主要贡献是一个可迁移的反馈契约（feedback contract），使闭环逆向设计在从昂贵的计算属性中学习时既有用又可审计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在逆向材料设计中，从目标功能出发搜索可实现的结构具有重要价值，但闭环发现的效果不仅取决于预测性能，更取决于昂贵的第一性原理结果是否经过独立验证、记录来源（provenance-recorded），并在证据充分时才作为反馈被接受。特别是对于载流子迁移率这类复合性质，最终的标量值往往隐藏了中间量、拟合质量、收敛历史和工作流假设等关键信息。

Method: InvDesMobility是一个可靠性门控的第一性原理反馈框架，集成了多智能体自动化DFT、证据分层（evidence stratification）、生成式结构提议（generative structure proposal）、获取排名（acquisition ranking）和可审计发布（auditable release）五大模块。工作流对来自2DMatPedia的516个候选材料进行处理，经过通道级可靠性门控后，将通过的记录分成两类反馈对象：松弛结构用于更新生成模型，保留的迁移率通道用于训练获取模型并设定验证优先级。

Result: 工作流产生了280个质量检验通过的材料和573个保留的载流子方向通道。经过多次迭代，InvDesMobility筛选了240万个结构，向DFT验证提交了102个候选材料，最终在41个化学式中保留了86个经过可靠性门控的生成通道。

Conclusion: 本文的主要贡献并非一个固定的高迁移率材料清单，而是一个可迁移的反馈契约，使得闭环逆向设计在从昂贵的计算属性中学习时既保持实用性又具有可审计性。所有源数据、保留的反馈记录和工作流均已开源发布。

Abstract: Inverse materials design starts from target functionality and searches for structures that can realize it. Its value in closed-loop discovery depends not only on prediction performance, but also on whether expensive first-principles results are independently validated, provenance-recorded, and admitted as feedback only when evidence is sufficient. This is especially important for composite properties such as carrier mobility, where a final scalar value hides intermediate quantities, fit quality, convergence history, and workflow assumptions. Here we present InvDesMobility, a reliability-gated first-principles feedback framework that integrates multi-agent automated DFT, evidence stratification, generative structure proposal, acquisition ranking, and auditable release. Using 516 2DMatPedia-derived candidates, the workflow produced 280 QC-passed materials and 573 retained carrier-direction seed channels after channel-level reliability gating. These records were split into two feedback objects: relaxed structures updated the generative model, while retained mobility channels trained the acquisition model and set validation priority. Over multiple iterations, InvDesMobility screened 2.4 x 10^6 structures, submitted 102 candidates for DFT validation, and retained 86 reliability-gated generated channels across 41 formulas. Overall, the main contribution is not a fixed list of high-mobility materials, but a transferable feedback contract that makes closed-loop inverse design both useful and auditable when learning from expensive calculated properties. All source data, retained feedback records, and workflows are available at https://github.com/DreamLufei/invDesMobility, with an accompanying evidence website at https://dreamlufei.github.io/invDesMobility/.

### [89] [Dynamically suppressed lattice rotations in SrTiO$_3$ as a basis for photo-induced ferroelectricity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16267)

Result: 在低温四方相中，观察到平衡态反铁畸变旋转角（antiferrodistortive rotation angle）出现长寿命的减小。该结果与高温立方相中的现象形成互补。

Conclusion: 该统一理论能够同时描述高温立方相与低温四方相中的动力学行为，为理解SrTiO₃中光致铁电性提供了统一的物理基础。

Abstract: Photo-induced ferroelectricity in the quantum paraelectric SrTiO$_3$ involves the dynamical interplay between a coherently driven Ti-O stretching vibration and multiple structural degrees of freedom, including antiferrodistortive rotations, strain, and the polar mode instability. In the high-temperature cubic phase, in the absence of average antiferrodistortion, time-resolved X-ray diffuse scattering has evidenced a correlation between a photo-induced reduction in antiferrodistortive fluctuations and the emergence of ferroelectric order. Here, we complement these measurements with time-resolved elastic X-ray diffraction in the low-temperature tetragonal phase, in which antiferrodistortive fluctuations are small but a finite average rotation has set in. In this phase, we observe a long-lived reduction of the equilibrium antiferrodistortive rotation angle. A unified theory of the nonlinear lattice dynamics based on first-principles calculations describes the dynamics in both high-temperature cubic and low-temperature tetragonal phases, providing a basis for light-induced ferroelectricity in SrTiO$_3$.

### [90] [Implementation of rotational invariance for first-principles phonons and application to low-dimensional materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16320)
*Benoit Van Troeye,Xavier Gonze,Geoffrey Pourtois*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出两种基于倒易空间（reciprocal-space）的修正方案，通过在布里渊区中心强制施加旋转不变性（rotational invariance）条件，校正密度泛函理论（DFT）中低维材料声学弯曲（声子）模式的二次色散偏离问题，并在ABINIT软件包中实现。研究发现静电相互作用的常规处理在构型上不满足旋转不变性，这对力常数（IFCs）二阶导数的修正尤为关键。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 低维材料的声学弯曲（flexural）声子模在布里渊区（Brillouin zone）中心附近应呈现二次色散（quadratic dispersion），但密度泛函理论（DFT）计算中常因旋转对称性（rotational invariance）破缺而偏离该行为，现有校正方法有限。因此有必要重新审视并发展有效的校正方案。

Method: 基于倒易空间（reciprocal-space）施加旋转不变性条件，修正布里渊区中心处的原子间力常数（interatomic force constants, IFCs）及其相对于声子波矢（phonon wavevector）的一阶和二阶导数。提出两种短程IFC校正方案：一种基于Moore-Penrose伪逆（Moore-Penrose pseudoinverse），在ABINIT软件包中实现；另一种直接修改动力学矩阵（dynamical matrix）对波矢一阶导数的在位反对称部分。

Result: 研究了不同体系维度和赝势（pseudopotential）下施加旋转不变性对计算结果的影响。发现静电相互作用（electrostatics）的常规处理在构型上不满足旋转不变性，该问题在校正IFC二阶导数时尤为严重。

Conclusion: 旋转不变性条件可通过倒易空间方法有效施加，但长程静电贡献的固有非旋转不变性需要额外关注，尤其是对IFC二阶导数的修正而言。

Abstract: The acoustic flexural (phonon) modes of low-dimensional materials should show a quadratic dispersion close to the Brillouin zone center. Any departure from this behavior in Density Functional Theory calculations is typically associated with a breaking of the rotational invariance, with few methods available to correct it. In this work, we reexamine this issue based on a reciprocal-space imposition of this condition, with corrections on the zone-center IFCs and their first and second derivatives with respect to the phonon wavevector. We propose two correction schemes for the short-range part of the interatomic force constants, one based on the Moore-Penrose pseudoinverse, that we implement in the ABINIT software package, and one based on the straight modification of the on-site antisymmetric part of the first-order derivative of the dynamical matrix with respect to the wavevector. We investigate the impact of imposing rotational invariance for different system dimensionalities and pseudopotentials. Finally, we discuss rotational invariance in the context of long-range electrostatics contribution to the IFCs. We observe that the usual treatment of electrostatics is by construction not rotationally invariant. This is found especially critical when correcting the second derivatives of the IFCs.

</details>


### [91] [Melt-Quench Failures and Practical Solutions for Universal Machine-Learning Interatomic Potentials in Amorphous Structure Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16385)
*Shuwei Li,Yuqi An,Xingyu Guo,Wenqiang Yang,Zhenbin Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文以非晶IrO₂为诊断案例系统评估了8种通用机器学习原子间势（universal machine-learning interatomic potentials, uMLIPs）在熔融淬火非晶结构生成中的可靠性，发现所有模型均产生严重密度偏低的非物理膨胀结构。研究指出仅靠准确的能量与力不足以确保NPT动力学稳定，正确能量-体积响应与压强预测同样关键。提出的两种实用改进方案（压强靶向微调、修正的NVT淬火/NPT平衡协议）无需额外从头算训练数据即可恢复与从头算分子动力学（ab initio molecular dynamics, AIMD）一致的密度与局域结构，且该体积膨胀问题在30种化学多样材料中具有普遍性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从头算第一性原理熔融淬火分子动力学生成实验相关非晶结构的计算成本极高，通用机器学习原子间势（uMLIPs）虽有加速潜力，但它们在非平衡条件下的可靠性尚不明确，亟需系统性诊断与验证。

Method: 以电催化相关氧化物非晶IrO₂为诊断案例，评估8种主流uMLIPs在常规熔融淬火协议下的性能；将结果与AIMD参考值对比，分析能量-体积响应与压强预测对NPT动力学稳定性的影响；提出压强靶向微调与修正的NVT淬火/NPT平衡协议两种实用改进，并在30种化学多样材料中检验体积膨胀问题的普遍性及修正协议的效果。

Result: 所有8种uMLIP在常规熔融淬火协议下生成的IrO₂密度仅为1–4 g/cm³，远低于AIMD参考值10.04 g/cm³；准确的能量与力不足以保证NPT动力学稳定；两种改进方案均能恢复与AIMD一致的密度与局域结构；该体积膨胀问题在30种材料中普遍存在，修正协议使AIMD参考的平均绝对误差（MAE）从2.46降至0.35 g/cm³。

Conclusion: 本研究确立了通用机器学习原子间势（uMLIP）驱动非晶结构生成的实用验证准则与模拟策略，证明现有模型在非平衡熔融淬火场景中存在系统性体积膨胀偏差，并提供了无需额外从头算训练数据的有效修复方案。

Abstract: Generating experimentally relevant amorphous structures via melt-quench molecular dynamics is prohibitively expensive at the first-principles level. Universal machine-learning interatomic potentials (uMLIPs) could accelerate such simulations, but their reliability under non-equilibrium conditions remains unclear. Here, we examine eight leading uMLIPs for generating amorphous IrO2, using this electrocatalytically relevant oxide as a diagnostic case. Under the conventional melt-quench protocol, all models yield unphysically expanded structures with densities of 1-4 g/cm3, far below the ab initio molecular dynamics (AIMD) reference value of 10.04 g/cm3. Comparisons against ab initio references show that accurate energies and forces alone do not ensure stable NPT dynamics; correct energy-volume responses and pressure predictions are also essential. We identify two practical remedies: pressure-targeted fine-tuning and a revised NVT-quench/NPT-equilibration protocol that avoids unphysical volume expansion without additional ab initio training data. Both recover IrO2 densities and local structures consistent with AIMD. Across 30 chemically diverse materials, the volume-expansion failure proves general, and the revised protocol substantially improves density predictions, reducing the AIMD-referenced MAE from 2.46 to 0.35 g/cm3. This work establishes practical validation criteria and simulation strategies for robust uMLIP-driven amorphous structure generation.

Abstract: The bulk photovoltaic effect in non-centrosymmetric materials provides an alternative mechanism for the conversion of light into a current response compared to p-n junctions. Here, we investigate the evolution of the shift current response in mono-, bi-, and trilayer H-MoS2, as well as in twisted moiré bilayers and trilayers. The resulting electronic structures and shift-current responses are compared with density functional theory calculations and Wannier-interpolated results to verify the accuracy of the approach. The model accurately reproduces the electronic structure near the band edges and captures the main spectral features of the shift current conductivity. We show that twisting breaks the crystal symmetry and activates additional conductivity tensor components that are forbidden in untwisted structures, leading to new tunable in-plane photocurrent components. Analysis of the shift distance reveals a direct connection between the twist-induced modification of the electronic wavefunctions and the increase of the nonlinear response. Our results establish the twist angle as an effective parameter for engineering shift current generation in multilayer transition-metal dichalcogenide base systems and demonstrate that tight-binding approaches provide a practical route for exploring nonlinear optical phenomena in large-scale moiré materials beyond the limits of conventional first-principles calculations.

### [94] [Lattice Matching Dictates the Growth Mode and Quality of Deuterium Crystallization in Confined Spherical Shells](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16550)
*Peng Bi,Yu-Shen Wan,Wei Zhang,Jian Chen,Yong Yi,Qi-Feng Chen*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 以氘（D₂）为模型燃料，采用Feynman-Hibbs修正的Silvera-Goldman势能描述低温核量子效应，进行大规模分子动力学（molecular dynamics）模拟，将衬底晶格常数从3.1 Å变化至3.9 Å以系统研究晶格匹配的影响。

Conclusion: 衬底晶格匹配是调控受限固体生长和结晶质量的关键因素，应作为ICF低温靶烧蚀壳内表面工程的核心设计原则，为生长高质量单晶氘氚（DT）燃料层提供了原子尺度的指导。

Abstract: Cryogenic hydrogen isotope fuel layers with high structural integrity and atomic-scale smoothness are prerequisites for symmetric implosion and ignition in inertial confinement fusion (ICF). Using deuterium (D$_2$) as model fuel, we perform large-scale molecular dynamics simulations with a Feynman-Hibbs corrected Silvera-Goldman potential to describe nuclear quantum effects at low temperatures, systematically investigating D$_2$ crystallization inside spherical ablator capsules. By varying substrate lattice constant from 3.1 angstrom to 3.9 angstrom, we demonstrate that lattice matching dictates the transition from coherent epitaxial growth to polycrystalline formation, establishing it as the primary design principle for high-performance targets. When the substrate lattice closely matches the equilibrium hexagonal-close-packed (HCP) spacing of cryogenic D$_2$ (approximately 3.5 angstrom), D$_2$ forms coherent layer-by-layer epitaxial growth consistent with Ostwald's stepwise nucleation theory, yielding HCP-dominated near-single crystals with minimal dislocations and ultra-smooth inner surfaces. In contrast, large lattice mismatch destabilizes coherent growth and causes island-like growth, producing polycrystalline structures with mixed HCP/FCC phases, elevated defects, and greatly increased surface roughness. Radial stress analysis shows that interfacial stress from mismatch localizes within 2-3 molecular layers near the interface, triggering subsequent defect-mediated growth. These findings highlight substrate lattice matching in regulating confined solid growth and crystallization quality, establish it as a key principle for ablator inner-surface engineering in ICF cryogenic targets, and offer atomic guidance for growing high-quality single-crystal deuterium-tritium (DT) fuel layers with optimal smoothness.

### [95] [Moiré trapping of quadrupolar excitons in van der Waals trilayers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16557)
*Indrajit Maity,Arash A. Mostofi,Ángel Rubio,Johannes Lischner*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过在大尺度原子框架内求解贝特-萨佩特方程（Bethe-Salpeter equation），揭示了扭转WSe2/WS2/WSe2三层结构中四极激子（quadrupolar excitons）的原子尺度结构，发现小扭转角下的大原子弛豫会导致两种不同的四极激子被囚禁在莫尔晶格格点处，并指出莫尔囚禁（Moiré trapping）对其多激子相至关重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 四极激子为探索奇异多体物理以及量子传感和光子器件提供了新颖平台，但其内部结构、对称性和实空间局域化仍然未知，亟需高分辨率的原子尺度表征。

Method: 采用大规模原子框架求解贝特-萨佩特方程，对扭转WSe2/WS2/WSe2三层结构中的四极激子进行原子尺度的结构与对称性分析。

Result: 小扭转角下的大原子弛豫导致两种四极激子：一种为电子密度关于空穴呈方位角对称、密度在空穴处最大；另一种为电子密度呈三重对称、在空穴处出现节点。无莫尔囚禁时，四极激子转变为二分方格点阵上的反平行偶极激子；有莫尔囚禁时，偶极子被限制在三角格点上并产生几何阻挫（geometric frustration）。

Conclusion: 四极激子具有高度非平凡的本质，莫尔囚禁对其多激子相的形成至关重要，为在全可调激子平台上模拟阻挫量子磁性（frustrated quantum magnetism）提供了直接途径。

Abstract: Quadrupolar excitons in van der Waals heterostructures - quantum superpositions of anti-aligned dipolar excitons - offer a novel platform to explore exotic many-body physics, with applications to quantum sensing and photonic devices. Yet their internal structure, symmetry, and real-space localisation remain largely unknown. Here, we reveal the atomic-scale structure of quadrupolar excitons in twisted WSe2/WS2/WSe2 trilayers by solving the Bethe-Salpeter equation within a large-scale atomistic framework. We discover that large atomic relaxations at small twist angles give rise to two distinct quadrupolar excitons trapped at moiré lattice sites, differing in the in-plane symmetry of the electron density about the hole: one azimuthally symmetric, with the density maximal at the hole, and one threefold symmetric, with a node at the hole. Moiré trapping, neglected in commonly used models of quadrupolar exciton formation, is critical to their many-exciton phases. Without moiré trapping, quadrupolar excitons transition into anti-parallel dipolar excitons on a bipartite square lattice, while with trapping, the same dipoles are confined to a triangular lattice and experience geometric frustration. Our study uncovers the highly non-trivial nature of quadrupolar excitons, with direct implications for simulating frustrated quantum magnetism in a fully tunable excitonic platform.

### [96] [Activated Migration of Localized Ligand-Field Excitons in Atomically Thin CrCl3](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16702)
*Hyesun Kim,Renlong Liu,Sangho Yoon,Hyunjong Lim,Takashi Taniguchi,Kenji Watanabe,Jonghwan Kim,Changgu Lee,Sunmin Ryu*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Two-dimensional crystals with densely packed atoms exhibit a range of emerging properties, particularly a wide variety of excitonic behaviors. Thickness-variable layered chromium trihalides with finite surface recombination sites provide an ideal system for understanding how excitons confined in octahedral ligand fields migrate on nanometer length scales, a regime that defies conventional transport probes. In this work, we demonstrate that Cr3+-derived photoluminescence in CrCl3 is spectrally thickness-independent, but its relaxation dynamics are strongly sensitive to thickness and temperature, thereby indicating significant activated migration. A diffusion-coupled surface recombination model reveals an effective out-of-plane diffusivity of 4.5 x 10-6 cm2/s for the ligand-field excitons and a diffusion activation energy of 130 meV. The latter is comparable to the reorganization energy independently estimated from optical Stokes shifts, suggesting that exciton transport is coupled to local lattice relaxation. Furthermore, we show that the relaxation dynamics can be systematically tuned by either enhancing or suppressing surface recombination through controlled surface reactions or encapsulation. This work not only reveals the nanoscopic transport of localized ligand-field excitons but also establishes a spectroscopic transport probe applicable to various 2D materials.

### [97] [GaN Nucleation Landscape on Patterned Sapphire Shaped by the Growth Temperature of Directly Grown Boron-Compound Masks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16706)
*Yunjin Heo,Donghoi Kim,Hyeonoh Jo,Aelim Ha,Soohyung Park,Jaewu Choi,Chinkyo Kim*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文研究了在图形化蓝宝石衬底上直接生长的硼化合物掩膜的生长温度如何通过改变蓝宝石表面的局部可及性，进而调控GaN的外延横向过生长初期成核景观。研究发现掩膜生长温度系统性地改变了GaN的优先成核位置，并通过动力学蒙特卡洛模拟证实了温度控制掩膜对基底表面可及位点空间分布的调节机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索直接生长在图形化蓝宝石衬底上的硼化合物掩膜的生长温度对后续GaN成核行为的影响机制，寻找通过掩膜生长温度调控GaN成核景观（nucleation landscape）的实用途径。

Method: 采用不同温度（700–750°C及更高温度）生长的氨硼烷衍生的硼化合物掩膜，在圆形SiO₂开口内进行GaN外延横向过生长（epitaxial lateral overgrowth）实验；通过定量分析GaN面积分数、孤立畴数量和畴中心径向分布表征成核行为；并利用动力学蒙特卡洛（Kinetic Monte Carlo）模拟再现实验趋势。

Result: 低温（700–750°C）掩膜导致GaN呈现显著的边缘偏聚分布，高温掩膜则使GaN向开口内部迁移且空间分布稀疏；GaN覆盖率和空间排列均受掩膜生长温度影响；孤立畴数量的非单调变化源于横向合并减少与有效基底可及性降低之间的竞争。

Conclusion: 硼化合物掩膜的生长温度可通过控制GaN前驱物到达下方蓝宝石表面的局部路径的空间分布和有效性，从而重塑开口内的GaN成核景观，为器件制备提供一种实用的调控手段。

Abstract: The growth temperature of directly grown boron-compound masks on patterned sapphire can modify the local accessibility of the underlying sapphire surface and thereby alter the subsequent nucleation behavior of GaN. In this work, we investigate how ammonia-borane-derived boron-compound masks grown at different temperatures shape the GaN nucleation landscape within circular SiO$_2$ openings during the initial stage of epitaxial lateral overgrowth. The preferential nucleation position of GaN changes systematically with mask growth temperature: masks grown at 700--750$^\circ$C produce pronounced edge-biased distributions, whereas higher-temperature masks lead to more inward-shifted and spatially sparse GaN domains. Quantitative analysis of the GaN areal fraction, the number of visibly isolated domains, and the radial distribution of domain centers shows that the mask growth temperature affects both the amount of GaN coverage and the spatial arrangement of GaN domains within each opening. The nonmonotonic change in the number of visibly isolated domains is interpreted as a consequence of competition between reduced lateral merging and reduced effective substrate accessibility, rather than as a direct measure of the number of active nucleation sites. Kinetic Monte Carlo simulations reproduce the essential experimental trends by varying the effective density and radial distribution of substrate-accessible sites. These results suggest that the growth temperature of directly formed boron-compound masks provides a practical means of reshaping the intra-opening GaN nucleation landscape by controlling the spatial distribution and effectiveness of local pathways through which GaN precursors can access the underlying sapphire surface.

### [98] [Data-Driven Micromechanical Characterization and Mapping of Shale Rocks Using High Speed Nanoindentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16812)
*Shaziya Ahmed Banu,Xukai Zhang,Samah A. Mahgoub,Christopher C. Walker,George M. Pharr,Arash Noshadravan,Sara Abedi*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究提出一种基于高速纳米压痕（high-speed nanoindentation）与无监督统计学习技术相结合的数据驱动方法，实现对非均质岩石（heterogeneous rocks）的微观力学表征（micromechanical characterization），在降低化学分析依赖性的同时提升工作流程效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的微观力学表征需要结合化学分析（如元素图谱技术）进行物相识别，但这一过程增加了实验复杂性。因此，本研究旨在发展一种主要依赖力学数据、减少对化学分析依赖的数据驱动方法。

Method: 利用高速纳米压痕技术测量Mancos页岩（Mancos shale）的微观力学性质，随后应用多种无监督统计学习方法——包括UMAP结合k-means聚类、高斯混合模型（Gaussian Mixture Model, GMM）、狄利克雷过程混合模型（Dirichlet Process Mixture Model, DPMM）以及基于密度的噪声应用空间聚类（DBSCAN）——对压痕数据进行分析。此外，还开发并测试了一种自动化图像处理与分割技术。

Result: 使用加权误差（weighted error）和空间误差（spatial error）两种指标，将各方法的结果与传统化学-力学方法进行系统比较。结果表明，UMAP结合k-means聚类是最优方法，而DBSCAN、DPMM及图像分割技术更适合作为辅助手段。

Conclusion: 该研究证实了高速纳米压痕与机器学习（machine learning）技术相结合的能力，能够在降低分析复杂性、减少化学分析依赖的同时，实现有效的微观力学表征并改善工作流程效率。

Abstract: This study investigates the potential of high-speed nanoindentation in collaboration with data analytics and phase volume fractions to achieve micromechanical characterization of heterogeneous rocks. While micromechanical characterization can be performed using mechanical testing alone, integrating chemical analysis-such as elemental mapping techniques-provides essential phase identification. This enables more accurate interpretation of phase-specific mechanical properties. However, incorporating chemical analysis increases the complexity of the process. Hence, this study proposes data-driven micromechanical characterization and mapping of heterogeneous rocks based primarily on mechanical data and limited dependence on chemical analysis. In this study, Mancos shale rock is analyzed using high-speed nanoindentation to determine the mechanical properties at the microscale. Subsequently, a suite of unsupervised statistical learning techniques, such as Uniform Manifold Approximation and Projection (UMAP) with k-means Clustering, Gaussian Mixture Model (GMM), Dirichlet Process Mixture Model (DPMM), and Density-Based Spatial Clustering of Applications with Noise (DBSCAN), are applied to the nanoindentation data. Additionally, an automated image processing and segmentation technique was developed and tested. The results from each technique have been systematically compared against the conventional chemo-mechanical approach using two metrics: weighted error and spatial error. Based on the results, UMAP with k-means clustering is the most appropriate technique, while DBSCAN, DPMM, and image segmentation techniques are more suitable as secondary approaches. This study demonstrates the capability of high-speed nanoindentation combined with machine learning techniques for micromechanical characterization with reduced analytical complexity and improved workflow efficiency.

### [99] [High-entropy Fe$_2$VAl-based thermoelectric modules with improved conversion efficiency](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16851)
*Michael Parzer,Geoffrey Roy,Fabian Garmroudi,Pawel Ziolkowski,Thomas Konegger,Ernst Bauer,Pascal J. Jacques*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过高熵工程（high-entropy engineering）优化低成本、强韧的Fe₂VAl基全赫斯勒（full-Heusler）化合物的热电（thermoelectric, TE）性能，实现了极低的晶格热导率（κ_L~2.3 W m⁻¹ K⁻¹）和提升的平均热电优值（zT_ave≈0.3，300–500 K）。基于优化合金制备的(6×6)腿热电模块（TEM）在300–673 K宽温区内展示了迄今Fe₂VAl基发电机中最高的输出功率和最高的能量转换效率之一，验证了该材料体系在大规模热电能量收集中的应用潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 热电材料（thermoelectric materials）可将热能直接转化为电能，在可持续能源应用中具有吸引力。实际部署要求材料兼具高效率、低成本、无毒性和可规模化制备。Fe₂VAl基全赫斯勒化合物虽然成本低且强韧，但其热电性能仍需进一步优化，以推动实际应用。

Method: 采用高熵工程策略，协同结合重元素掺杂（heavy-element doping）与可控的非化学计量比（off-stoichiometry），在所有晶格位点上引入替代无序（substitutional disorder），从而触发极低的晶格热导率。优化后的合金通过热压（hot pressing）实现规模化批次合成，并采用直接钎焊（brazing）将热电腿与铜电极连接，完成模块组装。

Result: 实现了全赫斯勒体系中迄今最低的晶格热导率之一（κ_L~2.3 W m⁻¹ K⁻¹），在300–500 K温度范围内平均热电优值zT_ave≈0.3。规模化合成材料的热电性能与实验室小样高度一致，仅电阻率略有升高。(6×6)腿模块在300–673 K宽温区内展现出Fe₂VAl基发电机中迄今最高的输出功率和最高的转换效率之一。

Conclusion: 高熵工程有效优化了Fe₂VAl基全赫斯勒化合物的热电性能，所制备的热电模块具有良好的可重复性和技术相关性，彰显了该材料体系在大规模热电能量收集中的潜力。

Abstract: Thermoelectric (TE) materials enable the direct conversion of heat into electricity and are attractive for sustainable energy applications. For practical deployment, TE materials must combine high efficiency with low cost, non-toxicity, and scalability. In this work, we optimize the TE performance of low-cost and robust Fe$_2$VAl-based full-Heusler compounds through high-entropy engineering: a synergistic combination of heavy-element doping and controlled off-stoichiometry results in substitutional disorder on all lattice sites, triggering one of the lowest lattice thermal conductivities, $κ_\text{L}\sim2.3$ W m$^{-1}$ K$^{-1}$, reported so far for full-Heusler systems. The resulting materials exhibit improved values of the average figure of merit $zT_\text{ave}\approx 0.3$ from $300-500$ K. To demonstrate reproducibility and technological relevance, a full TE module (TEM) based on the optimized alloys was fabricated and characterized. Scaled-up material batches were synthesized by hot pressing, exhibiting TE properties in excellent agreement with laboratory-scale samples, with only slightly increased resistivities in absence of post-annealing treatments. Owing to the excellent mechanical workability of Fe$_2$VAl-based materials, the TEM legs were directly brazed onto copper electrodes, enabling robust module fabrication. A ($6\times 6$)-leg TEM was assembled and systematically characterized. The device exhibits the highest output power and one of the highest conversion efficiencies reported to date for Fe$_2$VAl-based generators over the broad temperature range of $300-673$ K, underscoring the potential of this material system for scalable TE energy harvesting.

### [100] [Evolution of Nonlinear Ion Transport in Nanopore Arrays: Ionic Conductance, Current Rectification, and Osmotic Power](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17012)
*Chih-Yuan Lin,Marija Drndić*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本论文通过实验制备直径小于3 nm和小于20 nm、孔数量从数个到约10000个的纳米孔阵列（nanopore arrays, NPAs），系统研究了离子电导、离子电流整流（ion current rectification）和渗透能转换的缩放行为。实验发现，随着孔数增加，表面电荷主导的电导与整流效应逐渐减弱甚至消失；在亚3 nm密堆积阵列中，电导呈现反常幂律依赖关系；渗透功率密度在缩放过程中可下降三个数量级。结合3D建模，作者揭示了非线性行为源于孔口浓度极化（concentration polarization）和阵列中电场的抑制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解纳米孔阵列（NPAs）中离子输运（ionic transport）及其缩放行为（scaling behaviors），是连接基础离子物理与蓝色能源（blue energy）应用的关键环节。现有研究多集中于单纳米孔，尚缺乏对阵列中多孔协同效应与缩放规律的系统认识。

Method: 制备了亚3 nm和亚20 nm两种直径的NPAs，孔数从数个到约10000个；系统测量了离子电导（ionic conductance）、离子电流整流（ion current rectification）和渗透能量转换（osmotic energy conversion）等关键指标；并构建了3D数值模型用于机制分析。

Result: 离子电导随孔数增加呈现非线性缩放，低盐浓度下非线性更显著。表面电荷主导的电导和离子电流整流随N增大而减弱，在N约10000时几乎消失。亚3 nm密堆积阵列（间距约25 nm）中，电导对浓度的依赖呈现反常幂律关系，与单纳米孔特性明显不同。渗透功率密度在缩放中下降达三个数量级。

Conclusion: NPAs中的非线性离子输运缩放行为源于孔口浓度极化（concentration polarization）和阵列中电场的抑制。该工作揭示了单纳米孔与纳米孔阵列之间输运现象的根本差异，为离子输运缩放规律提供了新的认识。

Abstract: Understanding the ionic transport and scaling behaviors in nanopore arrays is essential for bridging fundamental ion physics and blue energy applications. By fabricating sub-3 nm and sub-20 nm diameter nanopore arrays (NPAs) spanning from few pores to N ~ 10000, we systematically investigate ionic conductance, ion current rectification, and osmotic energy conversion. We report the ionic conductance scaling laws and nonlinearity with nanopore number, with stronger deviations from linearity at lower salt concentrations. Experimental evidence reveals that surface-charge-governed conductance and ion current rectification progressively weaken with increasing N and even vanish as the NPA scales up to N ~ 10000, resulting in an underestimation of surface charge density. In a sub-3 nm densely packed array (separation ~ 25 nm), the conductance exhibits an anomalous power-law dependence on concentration, deviating markedly from the single nanopore characteristics, attributed to the strong pore interactions. Furthermore, osmotic power harvesting measurements reveal a substantial reduction in power density upon scaling, with decreases of up to three orders of magnitude over the same range. To elucidate the underlying mechanism, we developed rigorous 3D modeling showing that the nonlinear behavior originates from concentration polarization at pore entrances and suppressed electric field across NPAs, collectively hindering ion transport. Our work provides insight into nonlinear ion-transport scaling and reveals fundamental differences between transport phenomena in single nanopores and nanopore arrays.

</details>

### [101] [GPT-Based Fast Simulation of CLAS12 Detector Hits via Conditional Autoregressive Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16035)
*Cole Granger,James Giroux,Richard Tyson,Maurizio Ungaro,Cristiano Fanelli*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于GPT风格自回归Transformer（autoregressive transformer）的快速替代模型，用于托马斯·杰斐逊国家加速器设施（Thomas Jefferson National Accelerator Facility）CLAS12实验的电磁量热器（calorimeter）模拟。模型以入射动量为条件，自回归生成所有九个量热器层的探测器击中序列（包含条、ADC和TDC令牌），在保持物理保真度的同时，在单GPU上实现每秒超过700事件的推理速度，大幅优于传统Geant4模拟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代粒子物理实验对快速、高保真度探测器模拟（detector simulation）的需求日益增长，因为探测器组件性能提升而计算资源逼近极限。传统蒙特卡罗方法（Monte-Carlo methods）计算开销过大，亟需更高效的替代方案。

Method: 采用GPT风格的自回归Transformer作为快速替代模型，以入射动量（incident momentum）为条件，将量热器各层的探测器击中数据建模为序列，包含条（strip）、ADC和TDC三种令牌（token），并自回归地逐层生成所有九个量热器层的击中序列。

Result: 模型能够忠实地再现击中多重性（hit multiplicity）、空间分布（spatial distributions）、能量沉积（energy deposits）以及电磁量热器的能量-动量响应（energy-momentum response）。在单GPU上推理速率超过每秒700事件，相比传统Geant4模拟实现了显著的加速。

Conclusion: 该自回归Transformer生成器在保持必要的物理保真度的前提下，提供了大幅的速度提升，适用于高亮度实验（high-luminosity experimental programs）对快速模拟的需求。

Abstract: Modern particles physics experiments have demonstrated an increasing need for fast, high-fidelity detector simulation as detector components have improved and subsequent computational requirements approach the limits of available resources. Recently, deep generative models have emerged as a promising alternative to traditional Monte-Carlo methods, with recent works drawing inspiration from large language models (LLMs) and self-supervised next-token prediction methods. In this work, we present an application of a GPT-style autoregressive transformer as a fast surrogate model for the calorimeter inside the CLAS12 experiment at the Thomas Jefferson National Accelerator Facility. The model is conditioned on incident momentum and generates realistic detector hits autoregressively across all nine calorimeter layers as sequences of strip, ADC, and TDC tokens. We demonstrate that the model faithfully reproduces hit multiplicity, spatial distributions, energy deposits, and the energy-momentum response of the electromagnetic calorimeter. The generator achieves inference rates exceeding 700 events per second on a single GPU, providing a substantial speedup over traditional Geant4-based simulations while maintaining physics fidelity essential for high-luminosity experimental programs.

### [102] [Revisiting Trade-sign Long-memory and Square-root Law price impact](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16269)
*Chris Angstmann,Tim Gebbie*

Main category: q-fin.TR

TL;DR: 本文从耦合的离散反应-扩散（reaction-diffusion）公式出发，推导出两种经典的市场微观结构规律：Lillo-Mike-Farmer（LMF）理论中的交易符号长记忆性，以及元订单（meta-order）冲击的平方根律（square-root law, SQRL）。通过将LMF律重新解释为事件时间（event-time）下的符号记忆陈述，将平方根律重新解释为物理时间（physical-time）下的可行性陈述，揭示了事件等待时间的非均匀性通过映射与插值影响日历时间（calendar-time）冲击轨迹的机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在从统一的微观框架出发，将交易符号的长记忆性（LMF理论）与元订单冲击的平方根律这两种已知的市场规律联系起来，并厘清二者在时间尺度解释上的本质差异。

Method: 采用耦合的离散反应-扩散公式描述照明订单簿（lit order book）与潜在订单簿（latent order book），引入非均匀采样的事件时间和元订单源项。利用局部线性订单簿（locally linear order book）和恒定参与率（constant participation-rate）执行的前沿动力学（front dynamics），将系统约化为Volterra方程（Volterra equation）。通过领先阶解得到凹形冲击轨迹，并利用重尾Pareto分布的元订单长度通过界面源项（interface source term）导出幂律交易符号自相关。

Result: 推导出元订单冲击的凹形轨迹与完成冲击（completion impact）正比于元订单大小的平方根；同时导出元订单长度的重尾Pareto分布导致交易符号的幂律自相关。

Conclusion: LMF律本质上是事件时间下的符号记忆陈述，而平方根律是物理时间下的可行性陈述；非均匀事件等待时间通过映射和插值方式影响日历时间冲击轨迹，两种规律在时间解释维度上存在根本区别。

Abstract: Starting with a coupled discrete reaction--diffusion formulation for the lit and latent order books with non-uniformly sampled event times and meta-order source terms we show how two familiar market-microstructure regularities can emerge from this framework: the long-memory of trade signs associated with the Lillo--Mike--Farmer (LMF) theory and the square-root law (SQRL) of meta-order impact. This uses the well known locally linear order book and constant participation-rate execution in the front dynamics to reduce the dynamics to a Volterra equation whose leading-order solution then yields the well know result of concave impact trajectory, and a completion impact proportional to the square root of the meta-order size. We then re-derive the heavy-tailed Pareto-distributed meta-order lengths induce a power-law trade-sign autocorrelation through the interface source term to discuss the interface representation. These are familiar derivations, what is slightly different here is that we reinterpret these known derivations to make it clear that LMF law is an event-time sign-memory statement, whereas the square-root law is a physical-time viability statement where non-uniform event waiting times can alter the calendar-time impact trajectories depending on the mappings and interpolation used to set continuum operational time.

</details>

### [103] [A Reverse Hard-Core Model in $\mathbb{A}_2$: an Application of the Pirogov-Sinai Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14903)
*A. Mazel,I. Stuhl,Y. Suhov*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用Pirogov–Sinai理论，在单位三角晶格（triangular lattice）A₂上分析了一类统计力学（statistical mechanics）粒子模型。该模型由粒子活度（activity）u∈(0,1)和Löschian数t两个参数刻画；作者证明了模型的周期基态（periodic ground state）由占据位点构成特定边长的三角子晶格，并在活性u足够小时，部分周期基态生成极值Gibbs（DLR）测度，进而描述了相关的相结构（phase structure）与纯相（pure phases）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在统计力学中，理解具有几何约束（如空位周围必须存在占据位点）的粒子模型的基态结构与相变行为是重要的理论问题。本文旨在对一类由活度参数u和Löschian数t控制的粒子模型，利用Pirogov–Sinai理论严格刻画其周期基态，并分析在低温（小u）条件下的极值吉布斯测度（extreme Gibbs measures）存在性与相结构。

Method: 采用Pirogov–Sinai理论（一种用于分析具有多个基态的格点统计力学模型的经典方法）对模型进行解析研究。首先确定使哈密顿量（Hamiltonian）与可容许性条件（admissibility condition）达到最优平衡的周期基态，即占据位点形成特定边长d_*(t)的三角子晶格的结构；随后在活性参数u充分小时的低温区域，分析哪些周期基态能够生成极值Gibbs（DLR）测度，并据此描述相结构。

Result: 证明了模型的周期基态由占据位点构成三角子晶格，其平方边长d_*(t)可显式由t确定。对于足够小的活性u，部分（但非全部）周期基态生成极值Gibbs（DLR）测度；作者进一步描述了由此产生的相结构，并刻画了与稳定基态（stable ground states）相关联的纯相（pure phases）。

Conclusion: 在统计力学的三角晶格粒子模型中，周期基态具有明确的三角子晶格结构，且在低温极限下，部分基态对应的极值吉布斯测度存在，从而呈现丰富的相结构。该结果为理解带有几何排斥约束的粒子系统的基态选择与相变提供了严格的理论基础。

Abstract: In this paper we use the Pirogov--Sinai theory to analyze a class of particle models of Statistical Mechanics on the unit triangular lattice $\mathbb{A}_2$. The models are specified by two parameters: the particle activity $u\in(0,1)$ and a positive Löschian number $t$ interpreted as a maximal squared clearing radius. Admissible configurations are those in which every empty lattice site has an occupied site within squared distance at most $t$, thereby forbidding empty disks of radius exceeding or equal $t$. The Hamiltonian favors configurations with as few occupied sites as possible, while the admissibility condition enforces a positive density of particles.
  We prove that the periodic ground states of the model, i.e., the configurations achieving an optimal balance of two tendencies, are the ones whose occupied sites form triangular sublattices of explicitly determined squared side-length $d_*(t)$. Furthermore, for sufficiently small values of the activity parameter $u$, some (but not necessarily all) periodic ground states generate extreme Gibbs (DLR) measures. We describe the resulting phase structure and characterize the pure phases associated with stable ground states.

### [104] [Structure-Informed Neural Operators for Long-Time Prediction of Parametric Hamiltonian PDEs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14913)
*Victory C. Obieke,Christopher Chukwuemeka,Emmanuel E. Oguadimma*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 提出一种能量投影傅里叶神经算子（EP-FNO），通过在标准FNO时间步进更新后添加不变量投影（invariant projection），提升哈密顿偏微分方程长时间预测的稳定性和准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准傅里叶神经算子（FNO）在自回归滚动预测中无法保持哈密顿偏微分方程（Hamiltonian PDEs）的守恒量（如质量、动量、哈密顿能量），导致守恒量漂移、相位误差和定性精度下降。因此需要一种结构感知的算子学习架构来改进长时间预测可靠性。

Method: 提出能量投影傅里叶神经算子（Energy-Projection Fourier Neural Operator, EP-FNO），其核心结构是在残差FNO时间步进更新之后，附加一个不变量投影（invariant projection）步骤，使预测结果满足守恒量约束。同时提供了算子逼近效率的理论分析和稳定性估计（stability estimate）。

Result: 在Zakharov–Kuznetsov、Kadomtsev–Petviashvili和sine–Gordon方程上的数值实验表明，EP-FNO相比标准FNO基线，在长时间稳定性（long-time stability）和孤子（soliton）及相干波结构（coherent wave structures）的传播精度上均有提升。

Conclusion: 不变量投影（invariant projection）能够有效提升学习型代理模型（learned surrogates）在哈密顿偏微分方程长时间模拟中的可靠性。

Abstract: Hamiltonian partial differential equations (PDEs) often exhibit long-time dynamics governed by conserved quantities such as mass, momentum, and Hamiltonian energy. Standard Fourier neural operators (FNOs) provide efficient data-driven approximations of solution operators, but may not preserve these invariants during autoregressive rollout, and can develop drift in conserved quantities, phase error, and loss of qualitative accuracy. We propose an energy-projection Fourier neural operator (EP-FNO), a structure-informed operator learning architecture that combines a residual FNO time-stepping update with an invariant projection for long-time prediction of parametric Hamiltonian PDEs. We also provide a theoretical analysis showing that EP-FNO can approximate operators associated with PDEs efficiently, we also suggest a stability estimate.
  We evaluate the approach on the Zakharov--Kuznetsov, Kadomtsev--Petviashvili, and sine--Gordon equations. Numerical experiments show that the projected model improves long-time stability, and gives more accurate propagation of soliton and coherent wave structures compared with a standard FNO baseline. Our results demonstrate that invariant projection improves the reliability of learned surrogates for long-time Hamiltonian PDE simulation.

</details>


### [105] [Dynamic Doppler Effects on Dirac Spinor Fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14952)
*Bryce M. Barclay,Alex Mahalov*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文推导了非惯性观测者运动对狄拉克旋量场（Dirac spinor field）产生的动态多普勒效应（dynamic Doppler effects），揭示了固有加速度、固有急动度、路径曲率、挠率和超挠率如何修正自由粒子的惯性量子描述，并发现旋量场中存在标量克莱因-戈登场（Klein-Gordon field）所不具备的自旋诱导特征。

Abstract: We derive the dynamic Doppler effects of noninertial observer motion on Dirac spinor fields, characterizing how proper acceleration, proper jerk, observer path curvature, torsion, and hyper-torsion modify the inertial quantum description of free particles. We quantify the nonlinear behavior of the amplitude and phase of the Dirac spinor wave field and isolate the spin-induced signatures that have no counterpart in the scalar Klein-Gordon field. For worldlines with constant proper jerk the amplitude scales super-exponentially as $\exp(j_0τ^2/4)$. ### [107] [The Standard Model Gauge Group from the Exceptional Jordan Algebra](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15235)
*John C. Baez,Paul Schwahn*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过八元数例外若尔当代数 $\mathfrak{h}_3(\mathbb{O})$ 及其自同构群 $\text{F}_4$，构造出了标准模型规范群（Standard Model gauge group）。具体而言，$\text{F}_4$ 作用于两类嵌套的若尔代子代数对 $X \subset B \subset \mathfrak{h}_3(\mathbb{O})$，其中 $X \cong \mathfrak{h}_2(\mathbb{C})$、$B \cong \mathfrak{h}_3(\mathbb{C})$；对于任意这样的对，$X$ 的稳定子群与 $B$ 的稳定子群的单位连通分支的交集，同构于标准模型规范群。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索如何从数学上统一描述基本粒子物理中的规范对称性，特别是利用八元数（octonion）与例外单群 $\text{F}_4$ 的结构来推导标准模型规范群，为量子场论与高维代数结构之间建立深层联系。

Method: 采用例外若尔当代数 $\mathfrak{h}_3(\mathbb{O})$ 及其自同构群 $\text{F}_4$ 作为数学框架。考虑 $\text{F}_4$ 在嵌套的若尔代子代数对 $X \subset B \subset \mathfrak{h}_3(\mathbb{O})$ 上的作用，其中 $X \cong \mathfrak{h}_2(\mathbb{C})$（量子比特的观测量若尔当代数）、$B \cong \mathfrak{h}_3(\mathbb{C})$（量子三比特的观测量若尔当代数）。计算 $X$ 的稳定子群与 $B$ 的稳定子群单位连通分支的交集。

Result: 该交集的群结构同构于标准模型规范群。因此，标准模型规范群可被视为“八元数三比特（octonionic qutrit）”的对称性群中，限制在普通三比特（qutrit）内且进一步限制在量子比特（qubit）上作用为酉算子（unitary operator）的那部分子群。

Conclusion: 标准模型规范群可以从八元数例外若尔当代数的对称性结构中自然导出，这为理解标准模型的代数基础提供了一个新的视角，并可能为后续统一理论（如大统一理论）的几何与代数构建提供线索。

Abstract: We construct the Standard Model gauge group using the exceptional Jordan algebra $\mathfrak{h}_3(\mathbb{O})$ and its automorphism group $\text{F}_4$. The group $\text{F}_4$ acts on pairs of Jordan subalgebras $X \subset B \subset \mathfrak{h}_3(\mathbb{O})$ with $X \cong \mathfrak{h}_2(\mathbb{C})$ and $B \cong \mathfrak{h}_3(\mathbb{C})$, and for any such pair the stabilizer of $X$ intersected with the identity component of the stabilizer of $B$ is isomorphic to the Standard Model gauge group. Since $\mathfrak{h}_2(\mathbb{C})$ is the Jordan algebra of observables of a qubit and $\mathfrak{h}_3(\mathbb{C})$ is the Jordan algebra of observables of a qutrit, we could say $\mathfrak{h}_3(\mathbb{O})$ is the Jordan algebra of observables of an 'octonionic qutrit'. In this language our result says roughly that the Standard Model gauge group is the group of symmetries of an octonionic qutrit that restrict to act as unitary operators on an ordinary qutrit and, within that, a qubit.

### [108] [Generalized symmetries, invariant solutions and conservation laws in the Jaynes-Cummings model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15538)
*Luis M. Piñuelas,Pablo C. López Vázquez,Alexander Yakhno*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用李对称分析（Lie symmetry analysis）和守恒律理论（conservation-law theory）研究Jaynes-Cummings模型（JCM），通过将冯·诺依曼方程投影到原子自由度并用特征函数表示场模式，将动力学表述为偏微分方程组。除恢复传统缀饰态动力学外，还获得了一类以Heun多项式表达径向依赖的新解；利用生成函数方法导出了包含原子布居、相干性、约化态纯度及场特征函数矩的局部守恒律，并发现了一个与原子-场耦合及纠缠动力学相关的平衡方程，以及无限层次的守恒律层级结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从对称性和守恒律的新视角分析Jaynes-Cummings模型，以揭示其更丰富的数学结构与物理内容，特别是超越传统缀饰态解的新解类型以及原子-场耦合相关的守恒律和纠缠动力学。

Method: 将冯·诺依曼方程（von Neumann equation）投影到原子自由度上，并使用特征函数（characteristic function）表示场模式，将问题表述为偏微分方程组（partial differential equations）；采用李对称分析方法（Lie symmetry analysis）确定允许的点对称性（point symmetries）和广义对称性（generalized symmetries），并构造满足量子力学物理条件的规范不变量解；利用生成函数方法（generating functions methodology）推导局部守恒律（local conservation laws）。

Result: 恢复了传统的缀饰态动力学（dressed-state dynamics），并得到了一类新的解，其径向依赖性通过Heun多项式（Heun polynomials）表达；除恢复总激发数守恒外，还获得了涉及原子布居（atomic populations）、相干性（coherence）、约化态纯度（reduced-state purity）以及场特征函数矩（moments of the field characteristic function）的额外守恒流；导出了一个联系原子纯度与相干性的平衡方程，其演化受原子-场耦合控制并与原子-场关联及纠缠动力学（entanglement dynamics）相关；对称性结构生成了广义对称性和无限层次的守恒律（infinite hierarchy of conservation laws）。

Conclusion: 李对称分析与守恒律理论为Jaynes-Cummings模型提供了更深刻的数学框架，揭示了超越传统缀饰态的新解分支以及丰富的守恒律结构，其中新发现的平衡方程直接关联到原子-场纠缠动力学，为量子光学中的纠缠与关联研究提供了新的守恒律工具。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate the Jaynes--Cummings model (JCM) using Lie symmetry analysis and conservation-law theory. The dynamics is formulated as a system of partial differential equations by projecting the von Neumann equation onto the atomic degrees of freedom and representing the field mode through its characteristic function. We determine the admitted point and generalized symmetries and construct invariant solutions satisfying the physical conditions imposed by quantum mechanics. The conventional dressed-state dynamics is recovered while a second class of solutions with radial dependence expressed through Heun polynomials is obtained for coupled atom--field configurations.
  We also apply the generating functions methodology to derive local conservation laws of the JCM differential system. Besides recovering the conservation of the total number of excitations, we obtain additional conserved currents involving atomic populations, coherence, reduced-state purity, and moments of the field characteristic function. In particular, we derive a balance equation for a combination of atomic purity and coherence whose evolution is controlled by the atom--field coupling and is linked to atom--field correlation and entanglement dynamics. The symmetry structure further generates generalized symmetries and an infinite hierarchy of conservation laws.

### [109] [A High-Order Nyström Method for Coupled Boundary Integral Equations in Oblique-Incidence Scattering by Impedance Cylinders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15616)
*Haochen Liu,Qinghao Yu*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文针对斜入射（oblique incidence）下无限长阻抗圆柱（impedance cylinder）的电磁散射问题，构建了一种基于Kress型对数核分解、周期乘积求积、傅里叶微分及块对角预条件子的高阶Nyström数值求解方法，并通过多种数值实验验证了该方法的稳定性与高精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 斜入射下无限长阻抗圆柱的电磁散射问题中，轴向电场与磁场分量满足一对耦合的二维亥姆霍兹方程（Helmholtz equations），且Leontovich阻抗条件通过切向导数实现耦合，对应的边界积分系统同时包含对数核（logarithmic kernels）和主值切向导数项，现有数值方法在处理此类耦合阻抗系统时面临精度和稳定性挑战，因此需要构建一种高阶收敛的数值求解方案。

Method: 方法基于已有的斜入射柱体散射耦合积分方程公式，采用Kress型对数核分解（Kress-type logarithmic kernel decomposition）处理对数奇异核，利用周期乘积求积（periodic product quadrature）进行边界积分离散，通过傅里叶微分（Fourier differentiation）计算切向导数贡献，并引入与标量阻抗子问题关联的块对角预条件子（block diagonal preconditioner）改善迭代求解性能。

Result: 数值实验包括制造解的傅里叶-贝塞尔基准测试（Fourier-Bessel benchmark）、平面波圆截面柱验证、光滑非圆边界测试、条件数与GMRES迭代对比，以及指定后向角扇区内变阻抗散射截面缩减算例。结果表明该方法作为耦合阻抗系统的稳定高精度正向求解器具有良好性能。

Conclusion: 在连续散射问题解唯一性和均匀离散稳定性假设下，本文建立了边界密度和远场模式（far-field patterns）的高阶收敛框架。该方法提供了一种稳定的高精度正向求解器，而非提出新的物理模型。

Abstract: We study the numerical solution of electromagnetic scattering by an infinitely long impedance cylinder under oblique incidence. After separation of the axial phase factor, the axial electric and magnetic components satisfy a pair of coupled two-dimensional Helmholtz equations. The Leontovich impedance condition couples these components through tangential derivatives, and the associated boundary integral system contains both logarithmic kernels and principal-value tangential derivative terms. Building on existing coupled integral-equation formulations for oblique-incidence cylinder scattering, we construct a high-order Nystrom implementation based on Kress-type logarithmic kernel decomposition, periodic product quadrature, Fourier differentiation for the tangential derivative contribution, and a block diagonal preconditioner associated with the scalar impedance subproblem. Under uniqueness of the continuous scattering problem and a uniform discrete stability assumption, we formulate a high-order convergence framework for the boundary densities and far-field patterns. Numerical experiments include a manufactured Fourier-Bessel benchmark, a plane-wave circular-cylinder validation, a smooth non-circular boundary test, condition-number and GMRES comparisons, and a variable-impedance scattering-width reduction example in a prescribed backward angular sector. The results indicate that the method provides a stable high-accuracy forward solver for the coupled impedance system, rather than a new physical model.

### [110] [Flowing to Normality and the Fate of the Single Ring Theorem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15791)
*Joshua Feinberg,Roman Riser,Richard Scalettar,Anthony Zee*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了一类从满足单环定理（Single Ring Theorem）的非厄米随机矩阵系综流向正态矩阵（normal matrix）分布的模型，通过调节惩罚非正态性的参数，数值发现单环定理在流过程中被打破，并确定了临界参数值；同时观察到奇异值的能级间距统计从Wigner-Dyson排斥连续演变为泊松统计（Poissonian），但该统计变化与单环定理的破坏并非直接相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随机非厄米矩阵（random non-Hermitian matrix）的双侧旋转不变系综在大矩阵极限下服从单环定理，其特征值分布支撑集为圆盘或圆环；而旋转不变的正规随机矩阵（random normal matrix）系综可在复平面上支撑于任意多个同心环。为桥接这两种截然不同的行为，作者引入并研究了一个从单环定理系综流向正规矩阵分布的非厄米矩阵模型。

Method: 通过引入一个惩罚非正态性（non-normality）的可调参数，构建从一般非厄米矩阵分布到正规矩阵分布的流（flow）；采用数值模拟与解析分析相结合的方式，研究该流过程中平均特征值分布支撑集的变化以及奇异值（singular values）的行为。

Result: 数值上观察到单环定理在模型流向正态性的过程中被打破，并确定了该转变发生的临界参数值；奇异值在流参数较小时呈现Wigner-Dyson排斥，在流参数渐近大时（正规矩阵端点）呈现泊松统计，且两种统计之间连续插值；但统计类型的变化与单环定理的破坏并非直接相关，后者在Wigner-Dyson统计区域内很早便已发生。

Conclusion: 本文揭示了一个从单环定理行为到正规矩阵行为的连续流转变，其中特征值支撑拓扑结构的转变与奇异值能级统计的转变发生在不同的参数阶段；此外，作者引入了一个与该气体相关的随机置换系综，并给出关于如何利用其在$N$大极限下从奇异值平均密度近似重建复特征值平均密度的猜想。

Abstract: Random non-hermitian matrix ensembles with double-sided rotation invariance obey, in the limit of large matrix size, the Single Ring Theorem, which states that the support of the mean eigenvalue distribution in the complex plane is either a disk or an annulus. In contrast, rotational-invariant random normal matrix ensembles can have mean eigenvalue densities supported over any number of concentric annuli in the complex plane. In this paper we introduce and investigate, both analytically and numerically, a non-hermitian matrix model which flows from a generic matrix distribution obeying the Single Ring Theorem to a distribution of normal matrices by tuning a parameter which penalizes non-normality.
  We observe numerically breakdown of the Single Ring Theorem as the model flows towards normality, and determine the critical value of the parameter at which the transition occurs. We also study in detail the behavior of the singular values of these matrices under the flow. These singular values form a Fermi gas confined to the positive half-line. In particular, we find that at small values of the flow parameter, the interparticle spacings in the gas exhibit Wigner-Dyson repulsion, whereas for asymptotically large values of the flow parameter, at the normal matrix endpoint of the flow, the spacing statistics is Poissonian. The flow interpolates continuously between these two types of statistics. However, this change in statistics is not related directly to breaking of the Single Ring Theorem, which occurs very early-on along the flow, in the regime of Wigner-Dyson statistics. Finally, we introduce a certain ensemble of random permutations associated with the gas, and make a conjecture on how to use it in order to reconstruct approximately the average density of complex eigenvalues from that of the singular values in the large-$N$ limit.

### [111] [N-transform and factorization of the DN-map](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15895)
*M. I. Belishev,D. V. Korikov*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文在三维光滑紧致黎曼流形（Riemannian manifold）上定义了N-变换（N-transform），证明了其酉性（unitary），并利用该变换给出了DN映射（Dirichlet-to-Neumann map）逆算子的因式分解 $Λ^{-1}=V^*V$，探讨了该分解在从DN映射反演流形结构中的潜在应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在建立N-变换这一新工具，用以分解DN映射（Dirichlet-to-Neumann map）的逆算子，从而为从边界测量数据反演流形内部几何结构（即确定 $(Ω,g)$）提供新的理论途径。

Method: 论文定义了空间 $\mathscr P$（势向量场空间，potential vector fields）和 $\mathscr L_λ$（平行于 $\nablaτ$ 的向量场空间），并基于流形到边界的距离函数 $τ$ 将区域分层切片，由此构造逐层定义的N-变换（N-transform）。通过证明该变换是酉算子（unitary operator），进一步建立了DN算子逆的因式分解结构。

Result: 证明了N-变换是一个酉算子，并基于该变换得到了DN映射的逆算子的因式分解 $Λ^{-1}=V^*V$。

Conclusion: N-变换为DN映射的逆提供了明确的因式分解结构，这一分解有望用于从边界DN映射数据反演流形 $(Ω,g)$ 的几何结构。

Abstract: Let $(Ω,g)$ be a smooth compact 3D Riemannian manifold with the smooth boundary $Γ$, $τ(x):={\rm dist\,}(x,Γ)$, $x\inΩ$; $Ω^τ:=\{x\inΩ\,|\,\,{\rm dist\,}(x,Γ)<τ$\}, $Γ^τ:=\{x\inΩ\,|\,\,{\rm dist\,}(x,Γ)=τ$\}, $τ\geqslant 0$. For the sake of technical simplicity, we deal with $Ω$ diffeomorphic to a ball in $\Bbb R^3$.
  Let $\mathscr P:=\{\nabla p\,|\,\,p\in H^1(Ω)\}$ be the space of the potential vector fields, and let $\mathscr L_λ:=\{\varkappa\nablaτ\,|\,\,\varkappa\in L_2(Ω)\}$ be the space of the vector fields parallel to $\nablaτ$. The N-transform is a map from $\mathscr P$ to $\mathscr L_λ$ defined layer-wise (in accordance with $Ω=\cup_{τ\geqslant 0}Γ^τ$) by $$ Nh\,\big|_{Γ^τ}:=(P^τh)\big|_{Γ^{τ-0}}, \qquadτ>0, $$ where $P^τ$ are the projections in $\mathscr P$ onto the subspaces $\mathscr P^τ:=\{h\in\mathscr P\,|\,\,{\rm supp\,}h\subset\overline{Ω^τ}\}$. We show that $N$ is a unitary operator.
  Let $p=p^f(x)$ be a solution to the Dirichlet problem: $Δ_g p=0$ in $Ω\setminusΓ$, $p=f$ on $Γ$. The DN-map $Λ$ is defined by $Λf:=-\langle\nabla p^f,\nablaτ\rangle$ on $Γ$. We show that the N-transform provides a certain factorization $Λ^{-1}=V^*V$ and discuss its possible usefulness for determination of $(Ω,g)$ from $Λ$.

### [112] [A generalized Stieltjes system with polynomial source](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15916)
*D. Masoero,B. Shapiro*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了一类与任意首一多项式 Q 相关的代数方程组，证明了其解的数目不超过二项式系数 binom(N+M, N)，并在 Zariski 开集上达到该上界；此外描述了当 Q 的一次项系数很大时，系统退化为 M+1 个弱耦合的经典 Stieltjes 系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典 Stieltjes 系统（对应 M=0 情况）与 Hermite 多项式的零点相关，而该文将其推广到任意首一多项式 Q（次数 M+1），旨在探明更一般情形下解的个数上界与代数结构。

Method: 通过建立代数方程组与关联的首一 Stieltjes 多项式系数方程之间的联系，利用代数几何中的总相交重数（total intersection multiplicity）来界定解的数目。

Result: 解的数目不超过 binom(N+M, N)；系数方程的总相交重数恰好等于该二项式系数，因此上界在非空 Zariski 开集上可达。当 Q 的一次项系数充分大时，系统分裂为 M+1 个弱耦合的经典 Stieltjes 系统，分别位于 Q 的每个零点附近。

Conclusion: 该上界对几乎所有 Q 均为紧确，且在大系数极限下系统呈现可分解的渐近行为。

Abstract: Let $Q$ be a monic polynomial of degree $M+1$. We study the algebraic system \[
  \sum_{j\ne i}\frac{1}{x_i-x_j}=Q(x_i),\qquad i=1,\ldots,N, \] for pairwise distinct complex numbers $x_1,\ldots,x_N$, modulo permutations of these numbers. The case $M=0$ is, after a translation, the classical Stieltjes system for the zeros of a Hermite polynomial. We prove that, for arbitrary $Q$, the number of solutions is at most $\binom{N+M}{N}$, and that the coefficient equations for the associated monic Stieltjes polynomial have total intersection multiplicity exactly $\binom{N+M}{N}$. Consequently the bound is attained for all $Q$ in a non-empty Zariski open subset of the affine space of monic polynomials of degree $M+1$. We also describe the solutions when the coefficient of the linear term of $Q$ is large: the system splits into $M+1$ weakly coupled classical Stieltjes systems, one near each zero of $Q$.

</details>


### [113] [$q$-Deformed Topological Recursion, Weight Vectors and Algebraic Structures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16441)
*Fridolin Melong,Raimar Wulkenhaar*

TL;DR: 本论文将Belliard-Bouchard-Kramer-Nelson的移位拓扑递推（shifted topological recursion）进行$q$-形变扩展至量子代数（quantum algebras）领域，通过研究$q$-形变$\mathcal{W}$-代数表示中的最高权向量（highest weight vectors），推导出拓扑递推的$q$-类比（$q$-analogue），并证明其可生成$q$-形变量子曲线（$q$-deformed quantum curves）。该框架统一了量子可积性（quantum integrability）的多种研究途径，并为$q$-形变模空间（moduli spaces）的几何结构提供了新见解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究（Belliard-Bouchard-Kramer-Nelson）构建了移位拓扑递推，但尚未在量子代数的框架下进行$q$-形变推广。

Method: 通过研究$q$-形变$\mathcal{W}$-代数表示中的最高权向量，推导拓扑递推的$q$-类比。

Result: 成功推导出拓扑递推的$q$-类比，并证明该递推可生成$q$-形变量子曲线。

Conclusion: 该框架统一了量子可积性的多种研究途径，并为$q$-形变模空间的几何结构提供了新见解。

Abstract: We investigate a $q$-deformation of the shifted topological recursion, extending the construction of Belliard-Bouchard-Kramer-Nelson to the context of quantum algebras. Through the study of highest weight vectors in $q$-deformed of $\mathcal{W}$-algebra representations, we derive a $q$-analogue of the topological recursion and show it yields $q$-deformed quantum curves. This framework unifies various approaches to quantum integrability and provides new insights into the geometry of $q$-deformed moduli spaces.

### [114] [Boundary monopole bubbling and Macdonald kernels for non-minuscule 't Hooft lines in $\mathcal N=4$ SYM](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16660)
*Ruiliang Li*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文研究了具有正规Nahm-pole边界条件的四维$\mathcal N=4$ $U(N)$超杨-米尔斯理论中，非极小磁荷的半BPS边界't Hooft线。与极小磁荷不同，非极小边界't Hooft线存在磁单极气泡贡献。通过计算单行磁荷的泡利修正缺陷半指标，将其与球面双仿射赫克代数元素联系起来，并通过差子算符展开和Macdonald核证明了与S-对偶Neumann Wilson线半指标的等价性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究集中于极小磁荷（minuscule charges）的边界't Hooft线，但对于非极小（non-minuscule）磁荷的't Hooft线，尤其是其磁单极气泡（monopole bubbling）效应尚缺乏系统理解。本文旨在弥补这一空白，为任意单行磁荷的情况建立严格的数学框架。

Method: 采用正规Nahm-pole边界条件（regular Nahm-pole boundary condition）构造边界't Hooft线；使用缺陷半指标（defect half-index）计算包含磁单极气泡贡献的配分函数；引入球面双仿射赫克代数（spherical double affine Hecke algebra, DAHA）元素$\mathbf e h_r(Y)\mathbf e$来识别边界't Hooft算符；利用差子算符展开（difference-operator expansion）和Macdonald核（Macdonald kernel）建立与S-对偶（S-dual）Neumann Wilson线的等价性；通过边界不动点公式（boundary fixed-point formula）实现系数计算。

Result: 对于单行磁荷$\lambda=(r,0,\ldots,0)$，得到了泡利修正后的缺陷半指标；证明了边界't Hooft算符与球面DAHA元素$\mathbf e h_r(Y)\mathbf e$等价；通过差子算符展开得到了筛选磁扇区（screened magnetic sectors）；利用Macdonald核证明了与S-对偶Neumann Wilson线半指标的相等性；对$U(2)$的所有主导磁荷建立了恒等式；通过边界不动点公式给出了秩二和秩三的具体非极小例子。

Conclusion: 非极小边界't Hooft线在正规Nahm-pole边界条件下可由球面DAHA精确描述，其半指标与S-对偶Wilson线完全等价，从而在数学上严格建立了边界磁算符与差子算符之间的联系。这为理解超杨-米尔斯理论中磁单极气泡效应的代数结构提供了新视角。

Abstract: We study half-BPS boundary 't Hooft lines of non-minuscule magnetic charge in four-dimensional $\mathcal N=4$ $U(N)$ super Yang--Mills theory with the regular Nahm-pole boundary condition. In contrast to minuscule charges, non-minuscule boundary 't Hooft lines receive monopole bubbling contributions. For all one-row charges $λ=(r,0,\ldots,0)$ we compute the bubbling-corrected defect half-index and identify the boundary 't Hooft operator with the spherical DAHA element $\mathbf e h_r(Y)\mathbf e$. Its difference-operator expansion gives the screened magnetic sectors, while the Macdonald kernel proves equality with the S-dual Neumann Wilson-line half-index. As a consequence we obtain the identity for all dominant magnetic charges of $U(2)$. The boundary fixed-point formula realizes the same coefficients and gives explicit non-minuscule examples in ranks two and three.

### [115] [The Algebra of Units: From Buckingham's Pi-grec Theorem to Latent-Variable Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16737)
*Mauro Valorani*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种数据驱动的自动无量纲化方法，利用对数变换后缩放测量的低维流形几何，通过奇异值分解（SVD）和整数指数搜索，无需先验物理知识即可从数据中发现巴克汉姆Pi定理（Buckingham Pi theorem）中的无量纲群，并在合成压缩机数据集上验证了数值精度与物理解释性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上，确定无量纲群（dimensionless groups）依赖专家经验和物理洞察，缺乏自动化的数据驱动方法。因此，本文旨在从数据中自动发现无量纲群，无需事先知道支配物理定律。

Method: 对同一系统不同缩放下测量的数据进行对数变换（logarithmic transformation），使数据落在由底层无量纲群决定的低维流形上；利用奇异值分解（singular value decomposition, SVD）直接识别该流形；随后通过整数指数组合搜索恢复候选无量纲量，并使用重复变量过滤（repeating-variable filter）保留由机器特征尺度构造的群。

Result: 在包含16,000个测量点的合成压缩机数据集上，该方法在无物理输入条件下恢复了正确的无量纲群（如流量系数、扬程系数和马赫数），排除了等价的低可解释性替代方案；复现的压缩机性能图误差低于0.01%。

Conclusion: 该工作揭示了经典量纲分析（dimensional analysis）与现代数据驱动学习之间的深层代数结构联系，为构建兼具可解释性、可扩展性和数据效率的物理模型提供了新思路。

Abstract: Engineers often measure many quantities-speed, pressure, temperature, length-expressed in different physical units. The Buckingham Pi-grec theorem states that these variables can always be combined into a smaller set of dimensionless numbers whose values fully determine the system's behaviour.
  Identifying the appropriate dimensionless groups has traditionally required expert knowledge and physical insight. This paper shows that they can instead be discovered automatically from data, without prior knowledge of the governing physics.
  The key observation is that, after logarithmic transformation, measurements collected under different scalings of the same system lie on a low-dimensional manifold whose geometry is determined by the underlying dimensionless groups. Singular value decomposition (SVD) identifies this manifold directly from data. A subsequent search over integer-exponent combinations recovers candidate dimensionless quantities, while a repeating-variable filter retains only those constructed from the machine's characteristic scales. This procedure recovers familiar engineering groups, including the flow coefficient, head coefficient, and Mach number, while excluding equivalent but less interpretable alternatives.
  The method is demonstrated on a synthetic compressor dataset containing 16,000 measurements. Starting from raw dimensional variables and no physics input, it recovers the correct dimensionless groups to numerical precision and reproduces the compressor performance map with an error below 0.01%.
  More broadly, the work reveals a close connection between classical dimensional analysis and modern data-driven learning. Both rely on the same underlying algebraic structure, suggesting new approaches for building physical models that are simultaneously interpretable, scalable, and data-efficient.

</details>

### [117] [Sharp freezing time estimates for the subcritical Facilitated Exclusion Process](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15233)
*Oriane Blondel,Clément Erignoux,Seonwoo Kim,Sanha Lee*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文研究了一维环面上促进排斥过程（FEP）的精确瞬态时间（transience time），分别给出了亚临界密度和近临界密度情形下的标度律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: FEP在亚临界密度区域$(0,1/2)$会在有限时间内冻结，理解其瞬态时间（即冻结时间）的标度行为对于刻画活性/非活性相变（active/inactive phase transition）的动力学特性至关重要。

Method: 通过估计初始分布中局部超临界区间的典型大小（亚临界情形下为$\Theta(\log N)$，近临界情形下为$N^{1 \wedge (2\alpha)}$），将静态估计与动态去相关不等式结合，推导出冻结时间的精确标度。

Result: 亚临界密度情形下，瞬态时间的精确标度为$\Theta(\log^3 N)$；近临界情形$\rho \simeq 1/2 - N^{-\alpha}$下，瞬态时间呈现多项式标度$N^{1 \wedge (2\alpha)}$。

Conclusion: FEP的冻结时间在亚临界区域由初始分布中局部超临界区间的对数尺度主导，而在近临界区域则需要额外的动态去相关分析来将静态估计转化为冻结时间上界。

Abstract: We investigate the exact transience time of the Facilitated Exclusion Process (FEP) on the one-dimensional torus with $N$ sites. The FEP exhibits an active/inactive phase transition at critical density $1/2$, such that in the subcritical density regime $(0,1/2)$, it becomes frozen after a finite time period -- the transience time or freezing time. We first show that for the FEP starting from a Bernoulli product measure of marginal density $ρ\in (0,1/2)$, the transience time has exactly the scale of $Θ(\log^3 N)$. Secondly, we prove that in the near-critical case $ρ\simeq 1/2 - N^{-α}$ for $α\in (0,1)$, the transience time is polynomial and has a scale of $N^{1 \wedge (2α)}$. The key idea is to estimate the typical size of locally supercritical intervals of the initial distribution, which has order $\log N$ in the subcritical case and $N^{1 \wedge (2α)}$ in the near-critical case. In the subcritical case this is enough, whereas in the near-critical case we need additional dynamical decorrelation inequalities to apply this static result to estimate the freezing time.

### [119] [Eyring-Kramers asymptotics for infinite-dimensional stochastic gradient systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16083)
*Morris Brooks,Giacomo Di Gesù*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文针对一类无穷维可逆随机演化方程，在小噪声极限下推导了生成元第一非零特征值的渐近公式，建立了无穷维Eyring-Kramers定律（infinite-dimensional Eyring-Kramers law），其中指数速率由通信高度（communication height）决定，前因子由相关极小点和鞍点处的局部二次行为决定。该方法将有限维Eyring-Kramers分析提升至无穷维随机梯度系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 考虑形如 $dX_t=-A\nabla F(X_t)\,dt+\sqrt{2β^{-1}A}\,dW_t$ 的可逆随机演化方程，其中 $F$ 为正则多阱势，$A$ 为自伴迁移算子（selfadjoint mobility operator），$W$ 为柱形布朗运动（cylindrical Brownian motion），$β$ 为逆噪声强度。该框架覆盖有界区间上的随机Allen-Cahn方程和随机Cahn-Hilliard方程。

Result: 在双阱势（double-well）情形下，推导了生成元第一非零特征值的精确渐近公式，给出了无穷维Eyring-Kramers定律：指数速率由通信高度决定，前因子由相关极小点和鞍点处的局部二次行为决定。

Conclusion: 提出了将有限维Eyring-Kramers分析提升至无穷维随机梯度系统（stochastic gradient systems）的一般性策略。

Abstract: We study small-noise asymptotics for a class of reversible stochastic evolution equations in infinite dimensions. The dynamics are of the form \[ dX_t=-A\nabla F(X_t)\,dt+\sqrt{2β^{-1}A}\,dW_t, \] where $F$ is a regular multi-well potential, $A$ is a selfadjoint mobility operator, $W$ is a cylindrical Brownian motion and $β\gg 1$ is the inverse noise strength. The invariant measure is a Gibbs perturbation of a Gaussian reference measure, and the resulting framework covers, in particular, the stochastic Allen-Cahn and stochastic Cahn-Hilliard equations on bounded intervals. In the double-well case, we derive a sharp asymptotic formula for the first nonzero eigenvalue of the generator. This gives an infinite-dimensional Eyring-Kramers law for the spectral gap, with exponential rate determined by the communication height and leading prefactor determined by the local quadratic behavior at the relevant minima and saddle points. Our approach provides a general strategy for lifting finite-dimensional Eyring-Kramers analysis to infinite-dimensional stochastic gradient systems.

### [121] [Distilling latent electrostatics from foundation machine learning interatomic potentials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15001)
*Xiaoyu Wang,Bingqing Cheng*

Main category: physics.comp-ph

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基础机器学习原子间势（foundation MLIPs）虽能覆盖广泛的化学与材料空间，但许多模型计算成本高且缺乏显式静电场描述（explicit electrostatics），限制了其在长程相互作用和电响应主导体系中的应用。

Method: 使用隐式埃瓦尔德求和（Latent Ewald Summation, LES）方法，从教师模型（teacher model）预测的能量与力中提取潜藏的静电特征，训练轻量级LES增强的学生MLIP（student MLIP），并可选择性地在额外密度泛函理论（DFT）数据上进行微调（fine-tuning）。

Result: 从UMA、MACE、Orb、eSEN、GemNet-OC、PET和EquiformerV2等多种基础MLIPs中成功提取出静电响应。基准测试发现，训练教师模型所使用的底层DFT水平和数据集对静电与光谱精度的影响大于模型架构本身。对于TiO2-水界面，少量高精度DFT数据微调可改善结构与红外光谱预测。

Conclusion: 基于LES的知识蒸馏（LES-based distillation）提供了一条将基础MLIPs转化为高效、具有电响应能力的模型的实用路径，同时也可用于检验基础模型中编码的物理保真度（physical fidelity）。

Abstract: Foundation machine learning interatomic potentials (MLIPs) have enabled atomistic simulations across broad regions of chemical and materials space, but many remain computationally expensive and lack explicit electrostatics, limiting their use for systems governed by long-range interactions and electrical response. Previously, we introduced Latent Ewald Summation (LES), which learns latent atomic charges and long-range electrostatics from density functional theory (DFT) energy and force labels alone. Here, we use LES to extract electrostatics that are latent in foundation models: energies and forces predicted by a teacher model are used to train a lightweight LES-augmented student MLIP, with optional fine-tuning on additional DFT data. The resulting models reduce computational cost while providing access to Born effective charge tensors, and infrared spectra. We benchmark student models distilled from a broad set of foundation MLIPs, including UMA, MACE, Orb, eSEN, GemNet-OC, PET, and EquiformerV2-based models, against experimental infrared spectra for liquid water, concentrated hydrochloric acid, and the anatase TiO2(101)-water interface. Across these systems, electrostatic response can be extracted from most foundation MLIPs. The benchmark further shows that the underlying DFT level and dataset used to train the teacher model play a larger role than architecture in determining electrostatic and spectroscopic accuracy. For the TiO2-water interface, fine-tuning with a modest amount of higher-level DFT data improves structural and infrared predictions. LES-based distillation therefore provides a practical route for converting foundation MLIPs into efficient, electrically responsive models, while also testing the physical fidelity encoded in foundation models.

</details>

### [122] [Generalized likelihood ratio test for magnetic anomaly detection: a geometrical approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15343)
*C. Chenevas-Paule,S. Zozor,L. -L. Rouve,O. J. J. Michel,O. Pinaud,R. Kukla*

Main category: eess.SP

TL;DR: 本研究证明磁异常检测（magnetic anomaly detection）中基于广义似然比检验（GLRT）的信号实际上被约束在一个半代数空间（semi-algebraic space）内——对于偶极子模型而言为一个锥形（cone）区域——并通过将参数估计限制在该空间内，显著提升了检测性能，其效果接近最优接收机。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前最先进的磁异常检测方法依赖于基于广义似然比检验的参数化模型，但模型生成的信号空间中存在未被充分利用的物理约束。

Method: 首先证明在给定测量配置下，信号仅演化于函数基所生成空间的一个受限子集中；然后将该信号参数表示识别为一个半代数空间，针对本文采用的偶极子模型，该空间为一个锥形区域。

Result: 数值模拟显示，所提方法不仅优于当前最先进的方法，而且其结果可接近清晰观测（clear-seeing）最优接收机的检测性能。

Conclusion: 在广义似然比检验中利用半代数空间约束信号参数，能够有效提升磁异常检测的性能。

Abstract: State-of-the-art approaches to magnetic anomaly detection rely on the generalized likelihood ratio test (GLRT). These approaches are based on the formulation of a parametric model of the source to be detected, expressed in a suitable functional basis. One of the primary objectives of this study is to demonstrate that, for a given measurement configuration, the signal is constrained to evolve within a restricted subset of the space generated by these functional bases. The parametric representation of the signal is identified as a semi-algebraic space which, for the dipole model used in this article, turns out to be a cone outside of which the estimated signal does not satisfy the physical equations. Thus, a second objective is to exploit this property to constrain the signal parameters in the GLRT to belong to the semi-algebraic space, in order to improve detection performance. The performance gain of the proposed algorithm is compared to the one of conventional approaches; numerical simulations show that the proposed approach not only outperforms state-of-the-art methods but can even provide results close to those of the clear-seeing (optimal) receiver.

</details>

### [123] [Optical Creation of Synthetic Microgravity for Quantum Degenerate Gases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14985)
*Catie LeDesma,Kendall Mehling,Tristan Rojo,Murray Holland*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文通过光学力景观实现了对量子简并气体的合成微重力（synthetic microgravity），达到毫g级别的地球引力补偿，并展示了物质波分束和布洛赫能带原子干涉仪，显著抑制了相互作用诱导的退相干，恢复了近√N的干涉灵敏度标度关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统微重力环境仅能在落塔、探空火箭和太空实验室等专用设施中实现，限制了超冷原子实验的连续运行和广泛应用。本文旨在通过光学手段在地面实验室中合成微重力环境，以克服上述限制。

Method: 利用动态绘制（dynamically painted）的光学偶极势（optical dipole potentials）生成光学力景观，补偿地球引力至毫g水平，同时保持对原子系综的连续约束。通过垂直光晶格中的布洛赫振荡（Bloch oscillations）进行原位校准，精确控制残余加速度。

Result: 实现了臂间距达数百微米的物质波分束（matter-wave beam splitting），并展示了布洛赫能带原子干涉仪（Bloch-band atom interferometer），其中相互作用诱导的退相通过合成微重力势中的受控三维膨胀被强烈抑制。对于大型量子简并系综，平均场效应的减弱使干涉灵敏度恢复接近√N标度。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了一个在地面实验室中利用囚禁量子气体实现合成微重力的多功能平台，将微重力实验的优势引入连续运行系统，为量子传感、物质波干涉测量和精密测量开辟了新机遇。

Abstract: Microgravity environments provide unique opportunities for ultracold-atom experiments by enabling long interrogation times and reduced acceleration-induced dynamics. However, their realization has largely been restricted to specialized facilities such as drop towers, sounding rockets, and space-based laboratories. Here we realize synthetic microgravity for quantum degenerate gases using optically engineered force landscapes that compensate Earth's gravity to the milli-g level while maintaining continuous confinement of the atomic ensemble. These force landscapes are generated by dynamically painted optical dipole potentials and calibrated in situ through Bloch oscillations in a vertical optical lattice, enabling precise control of the residual acceleration. We use this capability to demonstrate matter-wave beam splitting with arm separations of several hundred microns. We further implement a Bloch-band atom interferometer in which interaction-induced dephasing is strongly suppressed through controlled three-dimensional expansion in the synthetic microgravity potential. This reduction of mean-field effects restores near-$\sqrt{N}$ scaling of interferometric sensitivity for large quantum degenerate ensembles. Our results establish a versatile platform for realizing synthetic microgravity with trapped quantum gases in terrestrial laboratories, bringing the advantages of microgravity experiments to continuously operating systems and opening new opportunities for quantum sensing, matter-wave interferometry, and precision measurements.

</details>


### [124] [Programmable Gauge-Field Textures with Ultracold Atoms in Momentum Space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15124)
*Hongru Wang,Hang Li,Yichen Pan,Yuyan Luo,Bryce Gadway,Tao Chen,Bo Yan*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本研究利用超冷原子在二维动量态晶格中实现了具有局域Peierls相位控制的高度可编程合成规范场，展示了从弹道输运到磁场抑制动力学的转变，并通过设计合成电场观察到霍尔横向漂移，以及沿磁通畴壁的各向异性传播，将冷原子规范场工程从均匀磁场推进至可编程规范纹理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有超冷原子体系中对Harper-Hofstadter模型的实现主要局限于空间均匀的磁通量（spatially uniform magnetic fluxes），缺乏对规范场（gauge field）结构的局域调控能力。本研究旨在突破这一局限，实现具有可编程局域Peierls相位模式的合成规范场，以探索更丰富的规范纹理（gauge textures）和拓扑界面输运现象。

Method: 实验构建了一个高度可编程的二维动量态晶格（two-dimensional momentum-state lattice），利用超冷原子实现对Peierls相位模式（Peierls phase pattern）的局域控制，从而直接实现具有可调谐和空间结构化合成规范场的Harper-Hofstadter哈密顿量。通过在格点上引入与位置相关的能量梯度，进一步合成了电场，并设计了磁通畴壁（flux domain wall）结构。

Result: 观察到从弹道输运（ballistic transport）到强磁通抑制动力学（strongly flux-modified bulk dynamics）的输运交叉。在合成电场与磁场共同作用下，观测到了霍尔型横向漂移（Hall-type transverse drift）。在磁通畴壁界面处，观测到沿界面的各向异性传播（anisotropic propagation）。

Conclusion: 该工作将冷原子规范场工程从均匀磁场背景推进至可编程设计的规范纹理，为跨越可编程拓扑界面的输运研究提供了实验平台。

Abstract: Synthetic gauge fields with ultracold atoms offer a route to quantum matter in which electromagnetic environments can be designed rather than merely imposed. While the Harper-Hofstadter model has been realized in several cold-atom systems, existing implementations are largely limited to spatially uniform magnetic fluxes. Here we experimentally realize a highly programmable two-dimensional momentum-state lattice of ultracold atoms with local control over the Peierls phase pattern, enabling direct implementation of Harper-Hofstadter Hamiltonians with tunable and spatially structured synthetic gauge fields. We observe a crossover from ballistic to strongly flux-modified bulk dynamics with suppressed transport. By introducing a synthetic electric field through site-dependent energy gradients, we further demonstrate Hall-type transverse drift arising from the interplay between electric and magnetic fields. In addition, we engineer a synthetic flux domain wall separating regions with opposite magnetic fluxes and observe anisotropic propagation guided along the interface. These results move cold-atom gauge-field engineering from uniform magnetic backgrounds toward designer gauge textures, providing an experimental setting for transport across programmable topological interfaces.

</details>


### [125] [Interaction-enabled topological pumping of Rydberg electrons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15126)
*Chenxi Huang,Tao Chen,Kaden R. A. Hazzard,Jacob P. Covey,Bryce Gadway*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文实验展示了在合成晶格中通过可控的偶极交换相互作用实现关联里德伯电子的拓扑泵浦，观察到相互作用导致的拓扑奇点移动以及由此产生的量子化输运的出现与破坏，并得到了有效Rice-Mele模型的描述支持。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拓扑泵浦（topological pumping）是能带系统中量子化输运的范式实现，但其在强关联区域（尤其是长程相互作用下）的行为尚不清楚，本文旨在实验探索这一未解决的问题。

Method: 在合成晶格（synthetic lattice）中构建关联里德伯电子（correlated Rydberg electrons）体系，利用偶极交换相互作用（dipolar exchange interactions）调控参数空间中的拓扑奇点（topological singularity）位置，并通过固定泵浦轨迹随相互作用强度变化驱动拓扑相变。

Result: 实验观察到相互作用可诱导拓扑奇点发生可控移动，使固定泵浦轨迹能通过连续拓扑相变（topological transitions），从而产生或破坏量子化输运；观测结果与包含相互作用重整化格点势（interaction-renormalized onsite potentials）的有效Rice-Mele模型一致，并且展示了绝热性（adiabaticity）和对控制轨迹不完美性的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 该结果为在微扰区域之外探索相互作用控制的拓扑输运（interaction-controlled topological transport）建立了实验平台，并为在合成量子系统中工程化关联拓扑物质（correlated topological matter）开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Topological pumping is a paradigmatic realization of quantized transport in band systems, yet its fate in strongly correlated regimes, especially with long-range interactions, remains largely unexplored. Here we report the experimental observation of interaction-enabled topological pumping of correlated Rydberg electrons in a synthetic lattice. We show that dipolar exchange interactions induce a controllable shift of the underlying topological singularity in parameter space, such that a fixed pumping trajectory can be driven through successive topological transitions by tuning the interaction strength alone. This leads to the emergence and breakdown of quantized transport. The observations are consistent with an effective Rice-Mele description with interaction-renormalized onsite potentials and are supported by characterizing the adiabaticity and robustness to control trajectory imperfections. Our results establish a platform for exploring interaction-controlled topological transport beyond perturbative regimes and open a route toward engineering correlated topological matter in synthetic quantum systems.
