### [126] [Dressed Floquet scars from protected zero modes in a Rydberg chain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15605)
*Saptadip Roy,Bhaskar Mukherjee,K. Sengupta,Arnab Sen*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文在周期驱动（periodically driven）的里德伯原子（Rydberg atoms）环上构造了两个近似的零准能量量子多体疤痕（zero quasienergy quantum many-body scars），它们在有限尺寸下对驱动振幅和频率具有鲁棒性。指数定理（index theorem）保证了Floquet哈密顿量（Floquet Hamiltonian）中存在指数级（按系统尺寸）数量的精确零能模，而这两个疤痕态区别于大多数随驱动参数连续变化的零模，保留了特定量子态的“记忆”。通过Floquet微扰论（Floquet perturbation theory）和精确对角化（exact diagonalization），研究提供了对其存在性和鲁棒性的解析与数值理解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索周期驱动相互作用系统中受保护零模（protected zero modes）的结构，特别是理解为何在大量零能模中，特定量子多体疤痕态能够抵抗驱动参数变化而保持记忆。

Method: 采用Floquet微扰论进行解析构造，并结合有限系统的精确对角化验证非微扰区域（beyond the perturbative regime）的鲁棒性。

Result: 成功构造了两个零准能量量子多体疤痕态，分别对应里德伯真空（Rydberg vacuum）和体积律疤痕（volume-law scar）的幺正旋转变体的“修饰版本”（dressed versions），它们在有限尺寸下对驱动振幅和频率保持稳定。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了相互作用Floquet系统中受保护零模的结构特征，为理解周期性驱动多体系统中的非热化（non-thermalization）行为提供了新视角。

Abstract: In this Letter, we present an approximate analytic construction of two zero quasienergy quantum many-body scars in a periodically driven model of Rydberg atoms on a ring, which persist over a range of driving amplitudes and frequencies for finite sizes. An index theorem protects an exponentially large number (in system size) of exact zero energy modes of the Floquet Hamiltonian in this setting. Unlike most of these zero modes which continuously change with drive parameters, these two quantum many-body scars retain the memory of particular states. They can be expressed as {\it dressed versions} of two contrasting states, the Rydberg vacuum and a unitarily rotated variant of a volume-law scar [Ivanov and Motrunich, Phys. Rev. Lett. {\bf 134}, 050403 (2025)], respectively. We provide an analytic understanding of their existence using a Floquet perturbation theory and show their resilience beyond the perturbative regime using exact diagonalization in finite systems. Our study provides insight into the structure of protected zero modes in interacting Floquet settings.

### [127] [Adiabatic preparation of a fractional quantum Hall fluid by coherently pumping atoms from a Bose-Einstein condensate](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15951)
*Alberto Tabarelli de Fatis,Christof Weitenberg,Alexander Schnell,André Eckardt,Iacopo Carusotto*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文提出一种利用含时相干耦合大稀薄玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（Bose-Einstein condensate）与强相互作用原子态，绝热制备多粒子分数量子霍尔流体（fractional quantum Hall fluid）的玻色超冷原子协议，其通过在Fock空间中避开拓扑相变（topological phase transitions）来保持可观的绝热能隙，数值评估表明方案效率可远超当前实验水平。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有数守恒方案依赖有限尺寸诱导的拓扑能隙（finite-size-induced topological gaps），在制备多粒子分数量子霍尔流体时面临绝热能隙过小、难以扩展至大粒子数的困难。本文旨在设计一种非数守恒的绝热路径，避免跨越拓扑相变（topological phase transitions），从而在大粒子数下仍保持可观的绝热能隙，提升制备效率与可扩展性。

Method: 协议采用含时依赖的相干耦合，将强相互作用的原子态与一个大的稀薄玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（Bose-Einstein condensate）耦合。初始从空云团出发，利用具有拉盖尔-高斯（Laguerre-Gauss）轮廓的拉曼光束（Raman beams），将具有确定角动量（angular momentum）的原子相干泵浦到流体中。该方案在Fock空间中识别一条避免穿越拓扑相变（topological phase transitions）的绝热路径。

Result: 在典型实验参数下对协议效率进行数值评估，结果显示可处理的粒子数远超当前实验技术水平（state-of-the-art）。此外，研究强调了包含非简谐约束（anharmonic confinement）对方案具有关键优势。

Conclusion: 提出的非数守恒绝热制备协议通过避免拓扑相变（topological phase transitions）保持大能隙，有望实现大粒子数分数量子霍尔流体（fractional quantum Hall fluid）的玻色超冷原子制备，且非简谐约束（anharmonic confinement）的引入是提升方案性能的关键因素。

Abstract: We propose a protocol to adiabatically prepare a many-particle fractional quantum Hall fluid of bosonic ultracold atoms exploiting a time-dependent coherent coupling of a strongly interacting atomic state with a large dilute Bose-Einstein condensate. Starting from an empty cloud, atoms with well-defined angular momentum are coherently pumped into the fluid by Raman beams with a Laguerre-Gauss profile. Compared to number-conserving schemes which rely on finite-size-induced topological gaps, we identify an adiabatic path in the Fock space which avoids crossing topological phase transitions and thus maintains a sizable adiabatic gap open at all times. The efficiency of our preparation protocol is numerically assessed for typical experimental parameters up to particle numbers that largely exceed the experimental state-of-the-art. The crucial advantage of including an anharmonic confinement is finally highlighted.

</details>


### [128] [Asymmetric binary Bose mixtures: a Functional Renormalisation Group study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16029)
*Boris Krippa*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 利用功能重整化群（functional renormalisation group, FRG）框架研究零温下具有质量和种内耦合不平衡的二元玻色混合物，发现双不对称性导致量子涨落在组分间自发重新分配，引起准粒子残差（quasiparticle residue）显著发散，并预测密度通道声速随不对称性增加而系统性地降低，与标准 Bogoliubov 理论定性矛盾。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索二元玻色混合物中质量和种内耦合（intraspecies coupling）双重不对称性对系统量子涨落、准粒子性质和集体激发的非微扰影响，揭示平均场（mean-field）理论无法捕捉的强关联效应。

Method: 采用功能重整化群（functional renormalisation group, FRG）这一非微扰（non-perturbative）框架，分析零温下具有质量和种内耦合不平衡的二元玻色混合物。

Result: 双不对称性诱导量子涨落在组分间自发再分配，导致两种组分的准粒子残差（quasiparticle residue）出现显著发散；密度通道声速随不对称性增大而系统性降低，与标准 Bogoliubov 理论的预测定性相反；提出重整化因子（renormalisation factor）比值可作为多体关联与涨落转移的定量探针。

Conclusion: 该 FRG 分析为解释异质混合物（heterogeneous mixtures）的未来实验提供了一个一致的非微扰框架。

Abstract: Zero-temperature binary Bose mixtures with mass and intraspecies couplings imbalances are studied using the functional renormalisation group (FRG) framework. We find that this dual asymmetry induces a spontaneous redistribution of quantum fluctuations between the components. This effect leads to a significant divergence in the quasiparticle residues of the two species, a phenomenon not captured in mean-field treatments. Critically, our FRG analysis predicts a systematic reduction of the density-channel sound velocity with increasing asymmetry -- a result that qualitatively contradicts the behaviour predicted by standard Bogoliubov theory. The ratio of the renormalisation factors is proposed as a robust quantitative probe of many-body correlations and fluctuation transfer. These findings provide a consistent non-perturbative framework for interpreting future experiments on heterogeneous mixtures.

</details>


### [129] [Luttinger liquid parameters in one-dimensional Rydberg arrays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16128)
*Shu-Ao Liao,Li-Ping Yang,Jin Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文利用Luttinger液体参数K（通过Friedel振荡和交叉帽方法提取），研究了一维里德伯链中的Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless（BKT）相变，确定了公度周期五线和非公度浮动相中的BKT临界点，并验证了两种方法在多种模型中的一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解一维里德伯原子链中Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless（BKT）相变的普适性质，特别是公度（commensurate）晶体序熔化与非公度（incommensurate）浮动相（floating phase）的描述，需要准确提取Luttinger液体参数K这一核心量，但现有方法在适用范围和可靠性上仍有局限。

Method: 利用Friedel振荡（Friedel oscillations）和近期在Phys. Rev. Lett. 134, 076501 (2025)中提出的交叉帽方法（crosscap method）提取Luttinger液体参数K；在Friedel振荡分析中采用多谐波拟合方案（multi-harmonic fitting scheme）；通过有限尺寸外推（finite-size extrapolation）和能量隙标度（energy-gap scaling）以及Binder累积量（Binder cumulant）分析进行验证。

Result: 交叉帽方法在Z₃对偶硬核玻色子链和自旋1 XY链中获得的BKT转变点与已有结果一致；在公度周期五线上，正弦-戈登理论（sine-Gordon theory）预测的临界K值揭示了无序相、临界相和Z₅晶体相之间的两次BKT相变；Friedel振荡与交叉帽方法的结果相互一致，并得到能量隙标度和Binder累积量分析的进一步支持；在非公度线上，Friedel振荡得到的BKT点与纠缠熵（entanglement entropy）提取的结果一致，且两种方法在非公度浮动相内得到的K值相互吻合。

Conclusion: 交叉帽方法和多谐波拟合的Friedel振荡方法均能可靠地提取Luttinger液体参数K，从而有效刻画一维里德伯链中的BKT相变，并在公度和非公度两种情形下均得到一致且互为验证的相图描述。

Abstract: We investigate Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless (BKT) transitions in one-dimensional Rydberg chains, where commensurate critical regimes associated with the melting of crystalline orders with period larger than five and incommensurate floating phases are both described by Luttinger liquid theory. The central quantity is the Luttinger liquid parameter $K$, which characterizes the universal low-energy theory and controls the relevance of perturbations driving BKT transitions. We extract $K$ using Friedel oscillations and the recently developed crosscap method introduced in Phys. Rev. Lett. 134, 076501 (2025). As benchmarks, we first apply the crosscap method to a $\mathbb{Z}_3$ dual hard-core boson chain and a spin-1 XY chain with single-ion anisotropy, obtaining BKT transition points consistent with previous results after finite-size extrapolation. We then compute $K$ in the Rydberg chain along lines with fixed correlation-oscillation period near BKT transitions. Along the commensurate period-five line, the critical values of $K$ predicted by sine-Gordon theory reveal two BKT transitions separating the disordered phase, the critical phase, and the $\mathbb{Z}_5$ crystalline phase. The results from Friedel oscillations and the crosscap method agree with each other and are further supported by energy-gap scaling and Binder-cumulant analysis. To obtain reliable values of $K$ from Friedel oscillations, we use a multi-harmonic fitting scheme throughout the analysis. Along incommensurate lines, the BKT points obtained from Friedel oscillations agree with those extracted from entanglement entropy. Finally, we show that the values of $K$ obtained from the two methods are mutually consistent inside the incommensurate floating phase.

</details>


### [130] [Ultracold atomic lattice systems for simulating topological phases: A review](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16598)
*Bei-Bei Wang,Xiao-Dong Lin,Jinyi Zhang,Long Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文综述了超冷原子晶格系统在拓扑相量子模拟中的最新实验进展，涵盖光晶格、合成晶格、Floquet工程晶格和光镊阵列四类平台，总结了代表性拓扑模型、探测技术及未来方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超冷原子晶格系统在拓扑相模拟领域正处于从成熟范式向通用可编程量子模拟器演进的关键阶段，亟需系统梳理不同平台的最新实验突破与技术能力，以推动量子模拟前沿的拓展。

Method: 本文采用综述方法，按四大平台类别（光晶格、合成晶格、Floquet工程晶格和光镊阵列）组织内容，分别介绍其代表性实验进展、已实现的拓扑模型（topological models）以及先进的探测与表征技术。

Result: 四类平台各自展示了独特的拓扑物质实现与探测能力：光晶格借助激光辅助隧穿和光学拉曼晶格实现拓扑模型；合成晶格在动量或内态空间中构造人工维度；Floquet工程晶格通过周期驱动产生拓扑能带；光镊阵列提供高度可编程的原子排布。这些互补路径共同拓展了量子模拟的边界。

Conclusion: 文章指出强关联和非平衡拓扑相是新兴研究方向，并对未来超冷原子量子模拟器的发展前景进行了展望。

Abstract: Owing to rapid recent progress, ultracold atomic lattice systems for simulating topological phases are now at a pivotal stage, evolving from established paradigms into increasingly versatile and programmable quantum simulators. In this review, we survey recent experimental advances across four major classes of platforms: optical lattices, including optical lattices with laser-assisted tunneling and optical Raman lattices; synthetic lattices in momentum or internal-state space; Floquet-engineered lattices; and optical tweezer arrays, all of which offer distinct capabilities for realizing and probing topological matter. For each class, we highlight representative experimental breakthroughs, the topological models that have been realized, and the advanced detection and characterization techniques employed, emphasizing how these complementary approaches collectively expand the frontier of quantum simulation. We also discuss emerging directions in strongly correlated and nonequilibrium topological phases, and conclude with an outlook on future prospects.

</details>


### [131] [Band-minimum degeneracy is not enough: density-of-states control of low-density ferromagnetism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16912)
*Jinghao Wang,Pierbiagio Pieri*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文使用 T-矩阵近似（T-matrix approximation）研究几何可调谐费米-哈伯德晶格（geometrically tunable Fermi–Hubbard lattice）中铁磁序（ferromagnetism）在宽密度范围内的稳定性，发现低密度铁磁相的大小依赖性取决于能带底部态密度奇异性（density-of-states singularity）的强弱。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期超冷原子实验在中间密度下观察到几何可调谐费米-哈伯德晶格中的铁磁关联，后续理论研究将该模型低密度极限与流动铁磁性的 Mueller–Hartmann 机制联系起来。本文旨在系统考察该模型在广泛密度范围内铁磁序的稳定性。

Method: 采用 T-矩阵近似（T-matrix approximation）这一在稀薄极限下可控的方法，结合有限尺寸分析与热力学极限计算，系统比较两类不同几何构型（单对角线跳跃晶格与双对角线方形晶格）的哈伯德模型。

Result: 再现了实验观察到的中间密度铁磁区间；低密度下单对角线跳跃晶格中的铁磁相随体系尺寸增大而显著抑制，在热力学极限下消失；而双对角线方形晶格中的低密度铁磁相保持稳健。能带最小值简并本身不能解释这一差异，其根源在于能带底部态密度奇异性的不同：弱发散不足以稳定铁磁序，而准一维强奇异性支持完全极化基态。

Conclusion: 能带最小值简并并非低密度铁磁性的充分条件；能带底部态密度奇异性的性质最终决定了铁磁序的稳定性。

Abstract: Recent ultracold-atom experiments have observed ferromagnetic correlations in a geometrically tunable Fermi--Hubbard lattice at intermediate densities. Motivated by subsequent theoretical work that connected the low-density limit of the same model to the Mueller--Hartmann mechanism for itinerant ferromagnetism, we investigate the stability of ferromagnetism across a broad density range using the T-matrix approximation, a controlled approach in the dilute limit. We reproduce the ferromagnetic regime observed experimentally at intermediate densities and systematically compare finite-size and thermodynamic-limit calculations in the dilute regime. We find that the low-density ferromagnetic phase reported for the one-diagonal hopping lattice is strongly suppressed with increasing system size and disappears in the thermodynamic limit, indicating that it originates from finite-size effects. By contrast, low-density ferromagnetism remains robust in the square-lattice Hubbard model with hopping along both diagonal directions. We show that this qualitative difference cannot be explained by the degeneracy of the band minima alone, which occurs in both models. Instead, it is controlled by the singular behavior of the density of states at the band bottom: a weak divergence is insufficient to stabilize ferromagnetism, whereas a much stronger quasi-one-dimensional singularity supports a fully polarized ground state even in the dilute limit. Our results demonstrate that band-minimum degeneracy alone is not sufficient for low-density ferromagnetism and that the nature of the band-bottom density-of-states singularity ultimately controls its stability.

</details>


### [132] [Adiabatic realization of anomalous Floquet topological systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16942)
*Luca Asteria,Marcel N. Kosch,Henrik P. Zahn,Jonathan Bracker,André Eckardt,Klaus Sengstock,Christof Weitenberg*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文通过绝热（adiabatic）协议在超冷原子六角晶格中实现了反常弗洛凯拓扑相（anomalous Floquet topological phases），避免了共振驱动带来的加热问题，并展示了其在存在平均场相互作用下的鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统反常弗洛凯拓扑相依赖于与系统带宽近共振的周期调制（near-resonant periodic modulation），这会在相互作用系统中引发显著的弗洛凯加热（Floquet heating）效应，限制其实用性。本文旨在探索一种无需共振驱动的替代实现方案。

Method: 采用绝热协议，使系统始终处于参数空间闭合路径的瞬时基态（instantaneous ground state），类似于索利斯电荷泵（Thouless charge pump）。实验上利用超冷原子（ultracold atoms）在六角晶格（hexagonal lattice）中，通过绝热调制晶格几何结构（包括子晶格偏移）实现该拓扑相。使用实空间微运动面积（micromotion area in real-space）作为缠绕数（winding number）的替代指标来推断拓扑性质。

Result: 成功实现了反常弗洛凯拓扑相，避免了共振弗洛凯加热（resonant Floquet heating）和目标态不完全加载（imperfect loading）的问题。即使在平均场相互作用（mean-field interactions）强度与其他所有能量尺度相当时，仍能观察到反常拓扑相，证明了绝热构造的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 绝热协议为更鲁棒地工程化新型拓扑态（topological states）提供了有前景的途径，有望克服传统共振驱动方案在相互作用系统中的加热等核心问题。

Abstract: Topology has emerged as a central concept for classifying phases of matter. The situation is especially rich in periodically driven systems, where anomalous Floquet topological phases break the usual bulk-boundary correspondence between Chern number and edges modes of two-dimensional systems. These phases were so far realized by periodic modulation of the tunneling elements at frequencies near-resonant with respect to the system's bandwidth, a regime where Floquet heating plays a significant role in interacting systems. Here we show that such anomalous Floquet topological phases can also be realized by means of an adiabatic protocol, where the system is always in the instantaneous ground state of the cyclic path in parameter space, like in a Thouless charge pump. We experimentally realize such a state using ultracold atoms in a hexagonal lattice where we adiabatically modulate the lattice geometry, including the sublattice offset. To infer the topology, we use the micromotion area in real-space, which was recently identified as a proxy for the winding number. This way of realizing anomalous phases avoids resonant Floquet heating and imperfect loading into the target state. We demonstrate the robustness of the adiabatic construction by observing the anomalous phase even in the presence of mean-field interactions of magnitude comparable to all other energy scales. These findings are promising for engineering novel topological states in a more robust way.

</details>

### [133] [Ising Dirac fermions across a topological phase transition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14829)
*Aoqian Zhang,Yaqi Ma,Yifei Jin,Nan Zhang,Wentao Jiang,Tianyu Qiao,Ivana Wang,Ulf Lampe,Kenji Watanabe,Takashi Taniguchi,Tze Kin Cheung,Junwei Liu,Shilin Huang,Xi Dai,Hoi Chun Po,Ning Wang,Kaifei Kang*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文报道在扭曲双层WSe₂的伊辛莫尔体系中，通过量子自旋霍尔相变实现了六重简并狄拉克费米子。在3.65°转角器件中观察到量子自旋霍尔相（电阻接近h/(2e²)）和狄拉克半金属相，磁输运测量显示半整数量子化朗道扇序列，并绘制出完整相图，确定了量子自旋霍尔与狄拉克半金属之间的相边界为临界转角3.3°。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 狄拉克费米子（Dirac fermions）因其相对论性色散关系及其与拓扑物理的紧密联系而备受关注，但在具有强伊辛自旋轨道耦合（Ising spin-orbit coupling）的二维体系中通常预期是有能隙的，因此在这类材料中实现狄拉克费米子是一个突出挑战。

Method: 制备不同转角的扭曲双层WSe₂（twisted WSe₂）器件，在3.65°器件中通过电场调控实现量子自旋霍尔相变，并利用磁输运测量（magnetotransport measurements）和温度依赖测量分析狄拉克相的输运行为。

Result: 在3.65°器件的高电场区观察到量子自旋霍尔相（quantum spin Hall phase），电阻接近h/(2e²)；在零电场附近观察到狄拉克半金属相（Dirac semimetal phase）。狄拉克相的磁输运显示半整数量子化朗道扇（half-integer Landau fan）序列，空穴掺杂侧六重简并，电子掺杂侧二重简并。温度依赖呈现弱金属行为，转角依赖测量确定了临界转角为3.3°。

Conclusion: 该工作通过拓扑相变（topological phase transition）在强自旋轨道耦合的莫尔体系（moire system）中实现了狄拉克费米子，为高迁移率自旋电子学（spintronics）提供了有前景的平台。

Abstract: Dirac fermions have attracted significant interest due to their relativistic dispersions and close connections to topological physics, yet they are generally expected to be gapped in two-dimensional systems with strong Ising spin orbit coupling, making their realization in such materials an outstanding challenge. Here we report the emergence of six fold degenerate Dirac fermions in an Ising moire system across a quantum spin Hall transition in twisted WSe2. In a 3.65 degree device, we observe a quantum spin Hall phase at high electric fields with nearly quantized resistance h/(2e2), and a Dirac semimetal phase over a broad range of electric fields near zero field. Magnetotransport measurements of the Dirac phase exhibit a half-integer Landau fan sequence, characteristic of Dirac fermions, with six-fold degeneracy on the hole-doped side and two fold degeneracy on the electron-doped side. Temperature dependence shows weakly metallic behavior consistent with a semimetallic state. Our twist-angle-dependent transport measurements map out a complete phase diagram and identify a critical twist angle of 3.3 degree, establishing the phase boundary between the quantum spin Hall and Dirac semimetal regimes. Our work establishes a new route to realizing Dirac fermions in strongly spin orbit coupled moire systems through a topological phase transition, providing a promising platform for high mobility spintronics.

</details>


### [134] [Dominant spin Hall torque and negligible orbital Hall torque in α-W/ferromagnet heterostructures with artifacts-free angular momentum detectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14872)
*Taiyang Zhang,Lujun Zhu,Qianbiao Liu,Lijun Zhu*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过开发两种无伪影扭矩的角动量探测器（Cu/Ni/Cu和Cu/FeCoB/Cu），澄清了W薄膜的电流诱导扭矩主要源于自旋霍尔效应（spin Hall effect），而非轨道霍尔效应（orbital Hall effect），并在整个厚度范围内观察到负阻尼类扭矩，否定了α-W中轨道电流的非局域角动量源假设。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理论预测α相钨（α-phased W）同时具有负的自旋霍尔电导率（spin Hall conductivity）和正的轨道霍尔电导率（orbital Hall conductivity），导致电流诱导扭矩的物理起源成为未解决的关键问题。本文旨在区分自旋霍尔效应与轨道霍尔效应对扭矩的贡献。

Method: 开发了两种无伪影扭矩（如自诱导扭矩和自旋-涡量扭矩）的角动量探测器：Cu/Ni/Cu和Cu/FeCoB/Cu。通过测量不同W厚度下的阻尼类扭矩（damping-like torque）变化，分析其与结构相变的关系。

Result: 两种探测器均显示W贡献的自旋轨道扭矩（spin-orbit torque）为负，且主要来自自旋霍尔效应。当W厚度超过5 nm时，阻尼类扭矩单调衰减，归因于β-W到α-W的结构相变。整个厚度范围内扭矩为负，表明α-W中轨道霍尔扭矩（orbital Hall torque）和轨道电流可忽略。

Conclusion: 实验结果与基于简化能带结构计算的轨道霍尔效应并非非局域角动量源的理论一致，暗示轨道电流缺乏普遍性，甚至可能普遍不存在。

Abstract: α-phased W was theoretically predicted to have a negative spin Hall conductivity and a positive orbital Hall conductivity at the same time, leaving the physical origin of the current-induced torque a critical open question. Here, we develop two angular momentum detectors of Cu/Ni/Cu and Cu/FeCoB/Cu that are free of artifacts torques (e.g., self-induced torque and spin-vorticity torque) and clarify that the spin-orbit torque contributed by W remains negative and predominantly from the spin Hall effect in the entire thickness regime. With both detectors, the damping-like torque exhibits a monotonic decay as the W thickness increases above 5 nm, which results from the structural phase transition from \b{eta}-W to α-W. The negative torque in the entire thickness regime suggests negligible orbital Hall torque and orbital current from the α-W. This result is consistent with the theory that the orbital Hall effect from simplified band structure calculations is not a non-local angular momentum source. These findings suggest poor generality or even universal absence of orbital current.

</details>


### [135] [Valley Valves at Domain Walls in Symmetry-Broken Rhombohedral Graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14878)
*Vo Tien Phong,Elsa Prada,Pablo San-Jose,Francisco Guinea,Eugene J Mele*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文揭示了菱方多层石墨烯（rhombohedral multilayer graphene）中谷畴壁（valley domain wall）在金属态下是电子输运的不可穿透势垒，必须通过谷间相互作用（intervalley interaction）实现透射；在超导态中，谷间混合（intervalley mixing）对支撑通过相反手性超导区之间的约瑟夫森结（Josephson junction）的超流至关重要，强调了谷间杂化（intervalley hybridization）对畴壁输运性质的决定性作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实验上，在时间反演对称性破缺（time-reversal-symmetry-breaking）的菱方多层石墨烯体系中，磁成像和输运测量在金属相和超导相中都暗示存在畴壁（domain walls），但畴壁对输运的具体影响机制尚不明确，需要理论阐明。

Method: 从对称性分析（symmetry analysis）出发，推导对称性允许的谷间相互作用项；结合微观数值模拟（microscopic numerical simulations），验证电子在谷畴壁上的透射机制；并在超导相中构建 SNS' 约瑟夫森结模型，研究谷间混合对超流的影响。

Result: 金属态下，谷畴壁对输运不可穿透，透射完全依赖于谷间相互作用的介导；数值模拟证实了该机制可使电子穿越畴壁。超导态中，谷间混合是支持相反手性超导区之间产生可观超流的关键条件。

Conclusion: 本研究阐明了菱方多层石墨烯中畴壁的物理本质，并强调了谷间杂化在调控这类体系输运性质中的关键作用，为理解相关实验现象提供了理论框架。

Abstract: Rhombohedral multilayer graphene polarized by a moderate perpendicular displacement field hosts a time-reversal-symmetry-breaking valley-and-spin-polarized metallic phase that may condense into a chiral superconductor. Recent magnetic imaging and transport measurements in this unconventional system suggest the presence of domain walls both in the metallic and superconducting phases. In this work, we show that valley domain walls are impenetrable barriers to transport in the metallic regime. Transmission through such a domain wall must therefore be mediated by intervalley interactions. We derive the symmetry-allowed terms and show via microscopic numerical simulations that they enable the transmission of electrons across the domain wall. In the superconducting phase, we find that intervalley mixing is crucial for supporting an appreciable supercurrent through a SNS' Josephson junction that connects opposite-chirality superconducting regions. Taken together, our work elucidates the nature of domain walls in these experimentally relevant multilayer systems and emphasizes the critical role of intervalley hybridization plays in governing their transport properties.

</details>


### [136] [Oxidation-induced ultrafast spin-to-orbital conversion at heavy-metal interfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15128)
*Xiaoxue Zeng,Tianyi Zhang,Yaokai Niu,Qiye Wen,Zhiyong Zhong,Zhi-Min Liao,Peng Yan,Xiufeng Han,Lichuan Jin*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文报告了一种由重金属界面氧化驱动的高效自旋-轨道转换（spin-to-orbital conversion）机制。在W/Co/SiO₂异质结中，太赫兹发射的时间延迟与W层厚度呈线性关系，表明主导起源为轨道电流（orbital-current）输运。该发射振幅约为Co/Pt双层膜的3倍，显示自旋角动量向轨道角动量的高效转换。通过系统变化Co层厚度、化学计量比及界面构型，证实该效应源于W/Co界面处W层的氧化对界面轨道纹理（orbital texture）的调控。该机制在多种重金属中具有普适性，且与自旋-轨道耦合强度（spin-orbit coupling strength）呈正比。研究确立了氧化作为工程化自旋-轨道转换的有效手段，并为轨道电子学（orbitronics）太赫兹发射器提供了通用路线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 氧化工程（oxidation engineering）提供了控制轨道自由度（orbital degrees of freedom）的途径，但其在自旋-轨道转换（spin-to-orbital conversion）中的作用尚未被充分探索。本文旨在揭示这一机制并探索其在太赫兹发射中的应用潜力。

Method: 构建W/Co/SiO₂异质结（heterostructures），测量太赫兹（terahertz, THz）发射的时间延迟与振幅；系统变化Co层厚度、化学计量比（stoichiometry）及界面构型（interface configuration）；对比不同重金属（heavy metals）体系，考察与自旋-轨道耦合强度（spin-orbit coupling strength）的关联性。

Result: 太赫兹发射的时间延迟与W层厚度呈线性关系，表明轨道电流（orbital-current）输运为主导起源；发射振幅约为Co/Pt双层膜的3倍，揭示高效自旋-轨道角动量转换；效应来源为W/Co界面处W层的氧化对界面轨道纹理（orbital texture）的调控；该机制在多种重金属中具有普适性，且与自旋-轨道耦合强度呈正比。

Conclusion: 氧化可以作为工程化自旋-轨道转换（spin-to-orbital conversion）的有效调控手段，并为轨道电子学（orbitronics）太赫兹发射器提供一条通用实现路线。

Abstract: Oxidation engineering provides a route to control orbital degrees of freedom, yet its role in spin-to-orbital conversion remains largely unexplored. Here, we report an efficient spin-to-orbital conversion mechanism driven by interfacial oxidation at heavy-metal interfaces. In W/Co/SiO2 heterostructures, terahertz emission exhibits a time delay that scales linearly with the W thickness, identifying orbital-current transport as the dominant origin. The emission amplitude is approximately three times larger than that of Co/Pt bilayers, indicating highly efficient conversion from spin to orbital angular momentum. Systematic variation of Co thickness, stoichiometry, and interface configuration reveals that the effect originates from oxidation of the W layer at the W/Co interface, which modulates the interfacial orbital texture. We further show that this mechanism is generic across different heavy metals and scales with their spin-orbit coupling strength. These results establish oxidation as an effective handle to engineer spin-to-orbital conversion and provide a general route toward orbitronic terahertz emitters.

### [137] [Creation and motion of antiferromagnetic skyrmions by edge manipulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15212)

Abstract: Magnetic racetrack architectures that use topological magnetic particles to store information are one of the most promising concepts for future storage applications. Antiferromagnetic racetracks are particularly appealing as they are not susceptible to external magnetic fields. State-of-the-art racetracks use magnetic fields, spin-transfer and spin-orbit torques caused by electric currents to move the bits across the entire circuit. However, the application of currents in many antiferromagnetic racetracks is limited because many of them are insulating. Recently, however, a concept for ferromagnetic racetrack memories that are free of global driving forces has been proposed. It has been demonstrated that various topological entities can be generated and transported over long distances solely through local magnetization rotation at the sample boundaries, independent of global driving forces. Here, we demonstrate that the local rotation of magnetization at the boundary of an antiferromagnetic sample can be exploited in racetracks to efficiently generate and transmit antiferromagnetic skyrmions. Additionally, we demonstrate that local switching of staggered magnetization at the edge of an antiferromagnetic racetrack can be even more successful than the rotational procedure. A comparison of ferromagnetic and antiferromagnetic processing of skyrmionic bits, together with energy considerations, shows that this procedure is fairly efficient in antiferromagnets.

### [138] [Interaction and non-Hermiticity controlled transmission in extended Su-Schrieffer-Heeger models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15245)
*Syeda Rafisa Rahaman,Shreekantha Sil,Nilanjan Bondyopadhaya*

Abstract: We study the transport characteristics of an extended version of the Su-Schrieffer-Heeger (SSH) model with next-nearest-neighbor (NNN) interactions and non-Hermitian onsite energies. We observed that transport in such a system is significantly modified by the NNN interaction and the non-Hermitian terms. The transmission coefficient exhibits oscillatory behavior as the strength of the NNN interaction varies in a fixed-length chain. Moreover, the transmission coefficient also shows oscillation with system size for a fixed strength of the NNN interaction. We find that novel oscillatory behavior of the transmission coefficient, arising form the NNN interaction, is a unique feature of such a model and has not been reported previously. The presence of the non-Hermitian terms also enhances/reduces the transmission coefficient depending on the values of the other system parameters like intra-, inter- and NNN hopping. It appears from our study that both the NNN interaction and the non-Hermiticity introduce significant changes in the transport properties of the extended SSH chain, which are not observed in the standard Hermitian nearest-neighbour variant of the SSH model.

### [139] [Floquet-Sambe Bottleneck and Frequency-Selective Localization in a Driven Synthetic Spin Chain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15293)
*J. Cao,K. L. Zhang,R. Wang,X. Z. Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究一维有限Floquet自旋链中由周期性旋转SU(2)自旋辅助跳跃与均匀近邻跳跃共存导致的局域化现象，发现Floquet本征态的平均反参与率（MIPR）对驱动频率呈非单调依赖：低、高频下态为扩展态，中间频率下达到最大局域化。通过开放系统的Floquet-Sambe格林函数反参与率诊断，证实了相同的非单调局域化趋势，并揭示了边界瓶颈与频率可调局域化在超导量子电路中的潜在应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建有限Floquet链模型，包含均匀近邻跳跃与周期性旋转的SU(2)自旋辅助跳跃；在封闭系统中计算Floquet本征态的平均反参与率（mean inverse participation ratio, MIPR）；在开放系统中构建Floquet-Sambe格林函数反参与率（Green-function inverse participation ratio），通过注入散射态的空间密度分析局域化性质。

Result: 封闭系统下Floquet本征态的MIPR对驱动频率ω呈非单调依赖：低频和高频下态为扩展态，在中间频率ω_peak ≈ μ_{-s} = √(2s)处达到最大局域化，该标度由第一个边界瓶颈控制。开放系统诊断恢复相同的非单调局域化趋势，唯峰值因静态带宽和电极自能（lead self-energy）向高频移动。

Conclusion: 受驱动的合成自旋链提供了直接可实现的频率可调平台，用于相干信息存储与检索；其机制根植于Floquet-Sambe虚通道、边界控制的局域化以及频率选择性输运之间的相互作用，适用于新兴的多级超导电路架构。

Abstract: We study a finite Floquet chain in which a uniform nearest-neighbor hopping coexists with a periodically rotating, \textrm{SU(2)}-dictated spin-assisted hopping profile. The resulting coupling is spatially inhomogeneous -- weakest at the chain boundaries and strongest in the bulk -- and produces a frequency-dependent Floquet-Sambe bottleneck. In the closed system, the mean inverse participation ratio (\textrm{MIPR}) of the Floquet eigenstates exhibits a striking nonmonotonic dependence on the driving frequency $ω$: the states remain extended at both low and high frequencies, but become maximally localized at an intermediate frequency. We demonstrate that this localization maximum occurs at $ω_{\mathrm{peak}}\sim μ_{-s}=\sqrt{% 2s}$, a scale controlled by the first boundary bottleneck. To connect these spectral properties to measurable transport, we construct an open-system Floquet-Sambe Green-function inverse participation ratio from the spatial density of the injected scattering state. This open-system diagnostic recovers the same nonmonotonic localization trend as its closed-system counterpart, with the peak shifted to higher frequencies by the static bandwidth and the lead self-energy. These findings establish the driven synthetic spin chain as a directly realizable, frequency-tunable platform for coherent information storage and retrieval, rooted in the interplay of Floquet-Sambe virtual channels, boundary-controlled localization, and frequency-selective transport in emerging multi-level superconducting circuit architectures.

### [140] [Topological Surface Charge Detection via Terahertz Time-domain Spectroscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15371)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: The topological magnetoelectric effect (TME) in three-dimensional topological insulators manifests as a quantized surface charge accumulation proportional to an applied magnetic field. Here we demonstrate an optical method using terahertz time-domain spectroscopy (THz-TDS) to detect surface charge accumulation in a chromium-doped (Bi,Sb)$_2$Te$_3$ thin film under oblique incidence, achieving sub-milliradian Faraday rotation precision. Unlike transport probes that require ultralow longitudinal conductivity, this optical technique is robust against finite $σ_L$, degrading by less than $0.3\%$ even when $σ_L \sim σ_T$. We extract the charge accumulation $η/B_z$ from the measured Faraday rotation and show results at $45^\circ$ and $60^\circ$ coincide within experimental uncertainty. Extending this to axion insulators, we predict that the TME produces an imaginary Faraday rotation linear in frequency, whose slope directly reflects the single-surface charge density. With improved sample thickness and precision, this optical scheme provides a viable pathway toward direct verification of the TME and four-dimensional quantum Hall effect.

### [141] [Mapping the Stability of Spin Qubits in Superconducting Pseudogap Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15711)
*Chen-How Huang,Miguel A. Cazalilla*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文分析超导赝隙体系中量子杂质基态（Yu-Shiba-Rusinov 自旋二重态）的稳定性，发现随着赝隙指数 $r$ 增大，临界 Kondo 耦合 $J_c$ 增加，而 Andreev 反射在所有 $r>0$ 下稳定单重态；粒子-空穴对称性破缺可恢复较低 $J_c$ 下的相变，表明大赝隙指数增强自旋量子比特稳定性。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用有效场论（effective field theory）和数值重整化群（numerical renormalization group）方法，针对具有赝隙隧穿态密度 $ρ(ε) \sim |ε|^r$ 的超导宿主体系，绘制了随赝隙指数 $r>0$ 及粒子-空穴对称性破缺扰动变化的相图。

Result: 在粒子-空穴对称性下，增大 $r$ 使触发自旋二重态到单重态转变的 Kondo 耦合临界值 $J_c$ 增大。与无能隙赝隙 Kondo 体系不同，Andreev 反射在所有 $r>0$ 下稳定单重态基态。粒子-空穴对称性破缺（如势散射或化学势改变）可在较低 $J_c$ 下恢复转变。

Conclusion: 结果表明，耦合到大赝隙指数（large pseudogap exponents）的超导宿主可在强 Kondo 耦合下增强自旋量子比特的稳定性。

Abstract: Superconducting spin qubits, realized as Yu-Shiba-Rusinov spin-doublet states in quantum-dot-superconductor systems, represent a cornerstone of current research in quantum technologies. We analyze these ground states of quantum impurities in superconducting pseudogap systems, namely systems with a pseudogap tunneling density of states $ρ(ε) \sim |ε|^r$ for energies $|ε|\gg Δ$ ($Δ$ being a $s$-wave pairing potential). For $r=1$, these hosts are realized as Dirac materials (graphene or 3D topological insulator surfaces) in proximity to conventional superconductors, or as $d+i s$ superconductors. Using effective field theory and numerical renormalization group, we map the phase diagram against the pseudogap exponent $r > 0$ and particle-hole symmetry-breaking perturbations. At particle-hole symmetry, increasing $r$ also increases the critical value, $J_c$, of the Kondo coupling that triggers the transition from spin doublet to singlet. Unlike the gapless pseudogap Kondo systems, numerical and analytical evidence suggest that Andreev reflection stabilizes a singlet ground state at $J$ for all $r > 0$. Breaking particle-hole symmetry -- by potential scattering or chemical potential -- eventually restores the transition at lower $J_c$. Our results indicate that coupling to superconducting hosts with large pseudogap exponents enhances the stability of spin qubits at large Kondo coupling.

We focus on the properties of the doublet-singlet transition at large Kondo coupling. The effective field theory for the singlet phase is inferred from a strong coupling expansion in the Kondo coupling. For $Δ\neq 0$, it contains a local pairing term which drives the system into a spin-singlet phase with enhanced paring correlations. We study how the singet-doublet phase boundary is affected by particle-hole symmetry breaking perturbations such as a scattering potential and/or the chemical potential. ### [143] [Spin-dependent electron transfer through a ring-wire coupled junction: Role of in-plane electric field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15776)
*Prabhab Patra,Santanu K. Maiti*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究了一种混合磁系统中与反铁磁（AFM）介观环侧耦合的非磁性（NM）导线的自旋相关输运，利用紧束缚（TB）框架和非平衡格林函数（NEGF）方法计算了两种耦合结型（单耦合与双耦合）的输运性质，发现面内电场可显著增强或诱导自旋极化（SP），在低偏压区域使SP接近100%，且该效应在有限温度和不同系统尺寸下保持稳健，表明该结构可用于实现外部可控的自旋电子学器件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在低维混合磁系统中，研究如何通过外部电场实现对自旋极化（spin polarization）的高效调控，探索无需外磁场即可打破自旋对称性（spin symmetry）的机制，以推动外部可控自旋电子学（spintronic）器件的发展。

Method: 采用紧束缚（tight-binding, TB）框架对系统进行建模，并使用非平衡格林函数（non-equilibrium Green's function, NEGF）形式计算输运性质。考虑两种线-环耦合构型：单耦合结（single-coupled junction）和双耦合结（double-coupled junction），并考察面内电场（in-plane electric field）以及有限温度（finite temperature）和不同系统尺寸对自旋极化（SP）的影响。

Result: 在单耦合构型中，耦合几何本身即可打破自旋对称性，即使无外场也存在有限自旋极化（SP）；面内电场进一步增强对称性破缺，在低偏压区域使SP接近100%。在双耦合构型中，无外场时自旋对称性保持，电场作为唯一的对称性破缺来源，同样产生较大的SP。有限温度和系统尺寸变化不影响上述关键特征，不同参数集下的结果保持一致。

Conclusion: 该混合磁结构在低维系统中具有实现外部可控自旋电子学器件的潜力，通过电场可高效调控自旋极化，且其关键性质对温度变化和系统尺寸具有鲁棒性（robustness）。

Abstract: We study spin-dependent transport in a hybrid magnetic system, where a non-magnetic (NM) wire is coupled to a side-attached antiferromagnetic (AFM) mesoscopic ring, placed between two non-magnetic electrodes subject to an in-plane electric field oriented perpendicular to the NM wire. The system is described within a tight-binding (TB) framework, and transport properties are computed using the non-equilibrium Green's function (NEGF) formalism. We consider two junction configurations distinguished by the wire-ring coupling: a single-coupled junction and a double-coupled junction. In the single-coupled configuration, the coupling geometry alone breaks the spin symmetry, yielding a finite spin polarization (SP) even without any external field. The in-plane electric field further enhances the symmetry breaking in both configurations, serving as an efficient tuning parameter that drives the SP nearly $100\%$ in the low-bias region. In the double-coupled configuration, spin symmetry is preserved in the absence of the external field, and the electric field acts as a sole source of symmetry breaking, producing a large SP. Finite temperature effects and different system sizes are examined, confirming the robustness of the observed features. To validate the findings over a wide parameter space, we considered different sets of parameters and found that the key signatures remain unchanged. Our results demonstrate that such hybrid structures are promising candidates for realizing an externally controllable spintronic device in low-dimensional systems.

</details>


### [144] [Quantum Information Geometry of Multicomponent Superconducting Fluctuation Transport](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15928)
*Zi-Ting Sun,Ying-Ming Xie,Naoto Nagaosa*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文证明超导涨落输运可直接探测集体多体物质中的混合态量子信息几何（mixed-state quantum information geometry），通过将纵向导电率与量子Fisher信息（quantum Fisher information）、异常霍尔效应与平均Uhlmann曲率（mean Uhlmann curvature）建立对应，并在菱面体多层石墨烯（rhombohedral multilayer graphene）中的手征超导涨落体系中加以验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用高斯涨落区间的多分量含时金兹堡-朗道理论（multicomponent time-dependent Ginzburg-Landau theory），将平衡态涨落库珀对的密度矩阵（density matrix）识别为静态对传播子（static pair propagator），从而在动量空间中定义正定混合态流形（positive mixed-state manifold）。

Result: 纵向量纲电导率（paraconductivity）由超导涨落模的量子Fisher信息主导；涨落异常霍尔效应由平均Uhlmann曲率主导。在菱面体多层石墨烯中的手征超导涨落体系中，对称性允许的Lifshitz不变量生成有限平均Uhlmann曲率，并在临界温度以上对数增强了异常霍尔电导率。

Conclusion: 集体超导涨落可作为混合态量子信息几何的一种实验上可访问的输运探针，并揭示了正定配分函数空间几何与可观测输运响应之间的普适联系。

Abstract: Quantum geometry underlies many electronic responses, but its transport signatures have so far been established mainly for pure single-particle Bloch states. Whether collective many-body fluctuations possess a measurable quantum geometry remains largely unexplored. Here we show that superconducting fluctuation transport provides a direct probe of quantum information geometry in collective many-body matter. Starting from a multicomponent time-dependent Ginzburg-Landau theory in the Gaussian fluctuation regime, we identify the equilibrium density matrix of fluctuating Cooper pairs as the static pair propagator, which defines a positive mixed-state manifold in momentum space. The geometry of this manifold is directly measurable through paraconductivity: the longitudinal paraconductivity is governed by the quantum Fisher information of superconducting fluctuation modes, while the fluctuational anomalous Hall effect is governed by the mean Uhlmann curvature, the mixed-state counterpart of Berry curvature. This correspondence further yields geometric bounds between these two transport components, with no direct analogue in normal electronic transport. Applied to chiral superconducting fluctuations in quarter-metal systems motivated by rhombohedral multilayer graphene, a symmetry-allowed Lifshitz invariant generates finite mean Uhlmann curvature and logarithmically enhances the anomalous Hall conductivity above the critical temperature. Our results establish collective superconducting fluctuations as an experimentally accessible transport probe of mixed-state quantum information geometry.

Here, we develop a tensor-network framework that combines quantics tensor cross interpolation with the kernel polynomial method, enabling compact representations of large non-Hermitian tight-binding Hamiltonians and direct calculations of real-space spectral functions for systems exceeding one billion lattice sites. Abstract: We investigate magnetotransport in a van der Waals heterostructure composed of monolayer graphene and the insulating helical antiferromagnet NiI$_2$. ### [151] [Optical vortex probe of loop-current chirality in moiré materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16676)
*Nobuhiko Yokoshi,Akihito Kato*

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种对称性分辨（symmetry-resolved）的光学探测方法，用于测量莫尔材料（moiré materials）中内禀的环路电流手性（intrinsic loop-current chirality），以扭转双层石墨烯（twisted bilayer graphene）为代表实现。该方法利用光学涡旋光束（optical vortex beams）的轨道角动量差（Δℓ）来隔离贝里曲率（Berry curvature）中经 C₃ 对称性选定的角谐波，从而在 Δℓ=3 通道的螺旋度依赖直流光电流（helicity-dependent dc photocurrent）中提取内禀几何手性贡献。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 莫尔材料中的手性环路电流内禀几何特性缺乏直接的实验探测手段，现有的非线性光学响应通常难以将内禀几何贡献与外在对称性破缺效应分离。

Method: 基于双层间干涉产生三角晶格位点上的手性电子环流，利用轨道角动量差 Δℓ 的光学涡旋光束作为探测工具，通过分析 C₃ 对称性约束下贝里曲率的角谐波（angular harmonic）选择性，在螺旋度依赖直流光电流的不同 Δℓ 通道中区分内禀与外在贡献。

Result: 当莫尔 C₃ 对称性保持时，内禀几何手性贡献仅出现在 Δℓ=3 通道的螺旋度依赖直流光电流中；而 C₃ 对称性破缺的扰动会激活其他 Δℓ 通道。

Conclusion: 角动量分辨的非线性光学（angular-momentum-resolved nonlinear optics）为探测莫尔材料及其他对称性工程量子材料中的几何手性（geometric chirality）提供了一条可行路径。

Abstract: We propose a symmetry-resolved optical probe of intrinsic loop-current chirality in moiré materials, with twisted bilayer graphene as a representative realization. Interlayer interference generates chiral electronic circulation on triangular plaquettes, giving rise to an intrinsic geometric chirality that enters the second-order response through a $C_3$-selected angular harmonic of the Berry curvature and can be isolated by the orbital-angular-momentum difference $Δ\ell$ of interfering optical vortex beams. When moiré $C_3$ symmetry is preserved, the intrinsic contribution appears in the $Δ\ell=3$ channel of the helicity-dependent dc photocurrent, whereas $C_3$-breaking perturbations activate additional channels. These results establish angular-momentum-resolved nonlinear optics as a route to probing geometric chirality in moiré and other symmetry-engineered quantum materials.

### [152] [Distinguishing between Direct and Parametric Driving in Nanomechanics Using a Vibrating Carbon Nanotube](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16884)
*Sam Dicker,Patrick Steger,Deepanjan Das,Saba M. Khan,Edward A. Laird*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 通过独立于驱动频率的谐振频率测量，分辨了碳纳米管谐振器中参量驱动（parametric driving）的直接运动与参量运动（parametric motion），并观测到高阶参量激发。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准直流电读出不直接揭示运动频率，导致参量驱动在纳米机械谐振器（nanomechanical resonators）中的特征存在歧义。

Method: 将碳纳米管（carbon nanotube）用作机电混频器（electromechanical mixer），利用低噪声超导放大器（low-noise superconducting amplifier）检测微波边带（microwave sidebands），实现独立于驱动频率的谐振频率测量。

Result: 频率分辨读出来区分了一阶泛音（first overtone）的直接运动与基模（fundamental）的参量运动；进一步通过驱动功率依赖性将两种机制分离；观测到了在 $2f_0$、$3f_0$ 和 $4f_0$ 处的响应，对应于与非线性刚度项相关的高阶参量激发（high-order parametric excitation）。

Conclusion: 频率分辨读出技术有效消除了参量驱动信号的歧义，并揭示了超出常规参量共振（parametric resonance）的高阶驱动效应。

Abstract: Parametric driving is a powerful route to amplification and nonlinear control in nanomechanical resonators, but its signatures can be ambiguous because standard dc electrical readout does not directly reveal the frequency of motion. Here we resolve this ambiguity by measuring the motional frequency of a vibrating carbon nanotube independently of the drive frequency. We operate the nanotube as an electromechanical mixer and detect microwave sidebands using a low-noise superconducting amplifier. This frequency-resolved readout distinguishes direct motion of the first overtone from parametric motion of the fundamental, even when the corresponding drive frequencies nearly coincide. The two mechanisms are further separated by their drive-power dependence. Beyond conventional parametric resonance at $2f_0$, we observe responses to driving at $3f_0$ and $4f_0$, consistent with high-order parametric excitation associated with nonlinear stiffness terms.

Conclusion: 所建立的超快光谱平台能够有效整合极端条件与强场光源，为复杂材料中涌现相的低能集体模式研究提供了强有力的实验手段，尤其是在太赫兹波段实现了对多参数相空间内超快动力学的探测。

Abstract: Elucidating and manipulating emergent phases in complex materials requires direct access to their low-energy collective modes. Terahertz (THz) time-domain and ultrafast optical spectroscopies have emerged as indispensable experimental tools, enabling the probing of intrinsic electrodynamics and the coherent control of non-equilibrium states. At the Synergetic Extreme Condition User Facility (SECUF), we have developed a suite of intense ultrashort light sources covering the near-infrared, mid-infrared, and THz spectral ranges. By integrating these strong-field pulses with extreme sample environments, such as low temperatures, strong magnetic fields, and high pressures, we have established several state-of-the-art spectroscopy platforms. In this article, we outline the technical specifications of each setup and highlight representative user experiments. The presented results underscore the exceptional capability of the THz experimental unit (A4-2) to explore ultrafast dynamics across a multi-parameter thermodynamic phase space.

### [154] [Adiabatic response in the Migdal Effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14845)
*Stefan Nellen Mondragón,Josef Pradler,Mukul Sholapurkar*

Main category: hep-ph

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于孤立原子进行第一性原理计算（first-principles calculation），不引入额外的临时假设，直接从散射振幅（scattering amplitude）出发描述电离行为。

Result: 确立了电离受抑制的绝热交叉（adiabatic crossover）区域；证明该抑制行为完全由散射振幅编码；绘制了相关的参数空间，发现暗物质探测实验位于未受抑制的参数区域。

Conclusion: 该工作首次从第一性原理层面验证了米格达效应在暗物质探测相关参数范围内的有效性，并为该效应的适用范围提供了严格的理论边界。

Abstract: The Migdal effect-the prompt ionization induced by a sudden nuclear recoil-is widely used in direct dark matter searches, yet its validity beyond the impulse approximation has remained unresolved. We present the first first-principles calculation for isolated atoms, establishing the adiabatic crossover where ionization is suppressed. We show that this behavior is fully encoded in the scattering amplitude, without ad hoc assumptions, and map the relevant parameter space, finding that dark matter searches lie in the unsuppressed regime.

### [156] [Production of high-orbital kaon excited states in the $K^{-}p$ reaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15736)
*Ting-Yan Li,Zi-Yue Bai,Xiang Liu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在有效拉格朗日量方法（effective Lagrangian approach）框架下，系统研究了K⁻p反应中高轨道激发（high-orbital-excitation）K介子的产生。通过单可调参数校准t道（t-channel）过程模型，成功再现了K₃*(1780)、K₂(1820)、K₂(1770)和K₄*(2045)等态的测量截面，并预测了其他高轨道K介子的产生截面。结果显示出较大的截面和前向峰角分布（forward-peaked angular distribution），表明其在未来实验中的可观测量潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高轨道激发K介子（如K₃*(1780)、K₂(1820)等）的产生机制尚不清晰，现有实验数据有限。本文旨在通过有效拉格朗日量方法系统研究K⁻p反应中这些态的产生过程，并预测尚未观测的高轨道K介子的产生截面，为未来实验提供理论指导。

Method: 采用有效拉格朗日量方法（effective Lagrangian approach）构建K⁻p反应的相关t道（t-channel）过程。模型通过单一可调参数（single adjustable parameter）进行校准，该参数由现有实验数据确定。

Result: 模型成功再现了K₃*(1780)、K₂(1820)、K₂(1770)和K₄*(2045)态的测量产生截面。对其他高轨道K介子的截面预测显示这些态具有较大的产生截面，并呈现前向峰角分布（forward-peaked angular distribution），这是t道交换（t-channel exchange）的典型特征。

Conclusion: 高轨道K介子在K⁻p反应中具有可观的产生截面和特征性的前向峰角分布，表明其具有很高的未来实验观测潜力。

Abstract: In this work, a systematic investigation of the production of high-orbital-excitation kaons in $K^{-}p$ reactions is carried out within an effective Lagrangian approach. The relevant $t$-channel processes are constructed, and the model is calibrated using a single adjustable parameter determined from existing experimental data. With this parameter, the measured production cross sections for the $K_3^*(1780)$, $K_2(1820)$, $K_2(1770)$ and $K_4^*(2045)$ states are successfully reproduced. Employing the same framework, the production cross sections for other high-orbital kaons are predicted. The results indicate that these states possess sizable cross sections and exhibit characteristically forward-peaked angular distributions, which is a typical feature of $t$-channel exchange, highlighting their great potential for observation in future experiments.

### [157] [Why fluctuations of conserved charges in the confining regime above $T_{ch}$ behave as if the quarks were free?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15798)
*L. Ya. Glozman*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文解释为何在手征交叉（chiral crossover）以上温度，守恒荷（conserved charges）的涨落表现如同自由夸克，而介子关联子（mesonic correlators）却显示出不同的性质。作者提出弦流物质（stringy fluid matter）的微观图像：重叠的强相互作用的色单态团簇（color singlet clusters）中，泡利不相容原理驱动的夸克交换使夸克呈准自由（quasifree）态，从而解释了上述矛盾。该现象与零温下e+e-→强子过程中夸克-强子二象性（quark-hadron duality）一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 澄清在手征交叉温度以上、退禁闭温度（deconfinement temperature T_d）以下区域，守恒荷涨落与介子关联子表现出截然不同物理行为的深层原因。实验观测显示守恒荷涨落如同自由夸克，被许多学者视为退禁闭的证据，但同一温度下的介子关联子却揭示出传播自由度是质量为零的夸克通过色电弦（chromoelectric confining string）连接成的色单态，这与自由夸克气体存在本质差异，因此需要统一的物理解释。

Method: 通过对比全QCD（full QCD）中介子传播子（mesonic propagators）与自由夸克圈（free quark loop）的差异，以及守恒荷数密度在时间与空间方向上的传播行为，并结合零温条件下e+e-→强子过程中夸克-强子二象性的已有结论，提出弦流物质模型。该模型将介质描述为重叠的强相互作用的色单态团簇，团簇之间的夸克交换由泡利不相容原理（Pauli principle）驱动，使夸克呈现准自由态。

Result: 全QCD中T>220 MeV时，夸克数密度空间传播子（spatial propagator）非常接近自由夸克圈；而同一温度下全QCD的介子传播子与自由夸克圈截然不同。守恒荷的涨落不“看到”禁闭，介子关联子则相反。这一差异与零温下e+e-→强子反应中，上述禁闭区域在不变质量>2 GeV时由自由夸克圈加小量微扰修正表示的经验规律一致。

Conclusion: 在手征交叉温度以上但低于退禁闭温度的区域，守恒荷涨落与介子关联子的差异并非矛盾，而是可以通过弦流物质图景获得统一理解：介质由重叠的强相互作用的色单态团簇构成，泡利不相容原理导致的夸克交换使夸克在守恒荷涨落中表现准自由，但在介子传播中仍体现禁闭效应。

Abstract: Some cumulants of the fluctuations of conserved charges soon above the chiral crossover behave as if the quarks were free. This was taken by many as evidence of deconfinement. At the same temperatures the mesonic correlators reveal the chiral spin and SU(4) symmetries, indicating that the propagating degrees of freedom are massless quarks connected into color singlets by the chromoelectric confining string. These correlators are qualitatively different from the free quark gas. Here we clarify the reason for the difference. The conserved quark number densities do not propagate in time but do propagate in spatial directions. The mesonic propagators calculated in full QCD differ radically from the free quark loop (quark gas) above T_ch. In contrast, the quark number density spatial propagator in full QCD at T > 220 MeV is very close to the free quark loop.
  In other words, the conserved charges do not see confinement, in contrast to the mesonic correlators. This is consistent with the well understood quark-hadron duality at T=0 in e^+e^- -> hadrons, where at invariant masses above 2 GeV the cross-section in the confining regime is represented by the free quark loop plus small perturbative corrections. All these features above T_ch but below the deconfinement temperature T_d can be combined within the following microscopic picture of the stringy fluid matter. It is a medium of the overlapping strongly interacting color singlet clusters. The quark interchanges between the clusters, required by Paili principle, make the quarks quasifree, which is reflected in fluctuations of conserved charges.

</details>


### [158] [Determining the Spin Density Matrix via Its Rank and Probing the Quantum Entanglement and Bell Non-Locality at the Lepton Colliders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16365)
*Liwei Liu,Xiqing Hao,Dianwei Wang,Lina Wu,Tianjun Li*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究在正负电子对撞机（$e^+e^-$ collider）上，通过单标量或光子交换产生的两费米子（$F_a F_b$）产生与衰变过程，证明自旋密度矩阵（spin density matrix）的秩（rank）等于中介粒子（mediator）的自由度数。标量交换对应纯态（pure state）且秩为一，可确定自旋分析能力（spin analyzing powers）并探测CP破坏；光子交换对应混合态（mixed state）且秩为二，可重建自旋密度矩阵、探测量子纠缠（quantum entanglement）与贝尔非定域性（Bell non-locality），并规避no-go定理。研究还猜想，在轻子对撞机上，满足$r_ρ \le N-2$的$N\times N$自旋密度矩阵可被普遍重建。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 动机在于通过对两费米子产生与衰变过程中自旋密度矩阵秩的分析，建立其与中介粒子自由度数的关联，从而提供一种系统方法来确定自旋分析能力、探测CP破坏、检验量子纠缠与贝尔非定域性，并尝试规避现有理论中的no-go定理。

Method: 理论分析基于正负电子对撞机上单标量或单光子交换的两费米子产生与衰变过程，通过计算自旋密度矩阵的秩，建立其与中介粒子自由度数之间的对应关系，并分别讨论纯态（秩一）与混合态（秩二）条件下的自旋分析能力确定问题。

Result: 标量交换下自旋密度矩阵秩为一（纯态），可确定自旋分析能力并探测CP破坏；光子交换下秩为二（混合态），可重建自旋密度矩阵、探测量子纠缠与贝尔非定域性，并规避no-go定理。以BESIII实验的$\eta_c \to Λ\barΛ$、$Λ\barΛ$产生与衰变以及LHC的Higgs $\to ττ$为例进行了说明。

Conclusion: 自旋密度矩阵的秩等于中介粒子自由度数这一结论具有普遍性，并推测在轻子对撞机上，满足$r_ρ \le N-2$条件的$N\times N$自旋密度矩阵均可被重建。

Abstract: Considering two-fermion $F_a F_b$ productions and decays via one scalar or photon exchange at the $e^+e^-$ collider, we show that the rank $r_ρ$ of spin density matrix $ρ$ is equal to the number of degrees of freedom of the mediator. For one generic scalar exchange, the spin density matrix is rank one for a pure state. With rank-one condition, we can determine the spin analyzing powers for $F_a$ and $F_b$ and their product if the CP symmetry is violated and conserved, respectively, and probe the CP violation. These results can be applied to the $η_c \to Λ{\bar Λ}$ at the BESIII experiment and the Higgs $\to ττ$ at the LHC. For one photon exchange, the spin density matrix is rank two for a mixed state. Considering the $Λ\bar Λ$ productions and decays at the BESIII experiment as an example, we show that the spin analyzing powers for $F_a$ and $ F_b$ can be determined by the rank-two conditions in details. Therefore, we can reconstruct the spin density matrices, probe the quantum entanglement and Bell non-locality, and evade the no-go theorem. Furthermore, we conjecture that the $N\times N$ spin density matrix with $r_ρ \le N-2 $ can be reconstructed at the lepton colliders in general.

</details>


### [159] [Chiral-odd structure of the $N \to Δ$ transition: tensor form factors from QCD light-cone sum rules](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16433)
*Ulaş Özdem*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 利用QCD光锥求和规则（QCD light-cone sum rules）首次直接计算了核子到Δ共振的张量跃迁形状因子（tensor transition form factors, TFFs），在时空区域1 ≤ Q² ≤ 10 GeV²内得到四个独立的形状因子，并分析了其味结构及与电磁、引力跃迁的互补性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 张量流算符在核子-Δ共振跃迁中的矩阵元尚未被直接计算，而该信息对于理解夸克横向自旋结构、补充电磁和引力跃迁的叉称性（chiral-odd）观测具有重要意义。本研究旨在填补这一空白，提供模型无关的输入以用于未来横向度（transversity）相关跃迁可观测量分析。

Method: 基于QCD光锥求和规则（QCD light-cone sum rules），利用核子分布振幅（nucleon distribution amplitudes）展开为不同扭曲度（twist）波函数，在时空区域1 ≤ Q² ≤ 10 GeV²内计算四个独立的张量跃迁形状因子，并通过多极拟合函数（multipole fit functions）外推到静态极限。

Result: 四个TFFs在味分解中展现出三种不同的模式：F₁和F₂中d夸克占主导（|F^d| ≫ |F^u|），与核子对角张量荷中u夸克主导的情形相反；F₃呈现反对称味结构（F^u ≈ -F^d），自然解释了该形状因子缺乏稳定同位旋标量求和规则；F₄的味贡献大小相当但符号相反，同位旋标量组合被压低。

Conclusion: 张量跃迁形状因子提供了与电磁和引力N→Δ跃迁互补的叉称性信息，可为未来横向度相关跃迁可观测量分析提供模型无关的输入，并需通过格点QCD（lattice QCD）和其他唯象学方法进行检验。

Abstract: We present the first direct calculation of the tensor transition form factors (TFFs) of the $N \to Δ$ transition using the QCD light-cone sum rules. The matrix element of the tensor current sandwiched between the nucleon and $Δ$ states is parametrized in terms of four independent form factors, derived from Lorentz covariance, Hermiticity, parity, time-reversal, and the Rarita--Schwinger constraints. The natural-parity character of the $1/2^+ \to 3/2^+$ channel combined with the spin-$1$ polarization content of the Rarita--Schwinger spinor imposes a trailing $γ_5$ in the parametrization, in analogy with the gravitational $N \to Δ$ case. Using the nucleon distribution amplitudes expanded in wavefunctions of different twists, we compute the four TFFs in the spacelike range $1 \leq Q^2 \leq 10$~GeV$^2$ for two sets of light-cone input parameters, and extrapolate to the static limit through multipole fit functions. A flavor decomposition into $u$- and $d$-quark contributions reveals three qualitatively distinct patterns among the four TFFs: $d$-quark dominance with $|F^d| \gg |F^u|$ for $F_1$ and $F_2$ -- in marked contrast to the diagonal nucleon tensor charges where the $u$-quark dominates; an antisymmetric flavor structure $F^u \approx -F^d$ for $F_3$, which naturally explains the absence of a stable isoscalar sum rule for this form factor; and comparable but opposite-sign flavor contributions to $F_4$, with a suppressed isoscalar combination. The TFFs provide chiral-odd information complementary to the electromagnetic and gravitational $N \to Δ$ transitions and offer model-independent input for future analyses of transversity-related transition observables, to be checked against lattice QCD and other phenomenological approaches.

</details>


### [160] [Modern Determination of Pion and Kaon Fragmentation Functions from SIA and High-Precision COMPASS SIDIS Multiplicities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16754)
*HAPS Collaboration,Maryam Soleymaninia,Hamzeh Khanpour,Hubert Spiesberger,Majid Azizi,Michael Klasen,Hadi Hashamipour*

Method: 在NLO和NNLO微扰QCD（perturbative QCD）框架下，联合SIA数据与HERMES和COMPASS提供的电荷分离SIDIS多重数数据，利用公开的MontBlanc框架进行全局拟合，生成FF副本集并以LHAPDF格式发布。

Abstract: We present a combined determination of charged-pion and charged-kaon fragmentation functions (FFs), denoted HAPS-PiFF1.0 and HAPS-KaFF1.0, at next-to-leading order (NLO) and within a next-to-next-to-leading-order (NNLO) perturbative QCD setup. The analysis combines single-inclusive electron-positron annihilation (SIA) data with charge-separated semi-inclusive deep-inelastic-scattering (SIDIS) multiplicities from HERMES and COMPASS. A central goal of this work is to incorporate the modern COMPASS SIDIS input, namely the COMPASS 2025 proton-target multiplicities and the COMPASS 2026 revised isoscalar-target multiplicities, into a common charged-pion and charged-kaon FF analysis and to assess their role in the resulting flavor separation. The revised isoscalar data supersede the earlier COMPASS measurements used in previous global fits. The charge-separated pion multiplicities provide important constraints on favored and unfavored light-quark fragmentation, while the kaon measurements enhance the sensitivity to light-quark, unfavored, and strange-to-kaon fragmentation channels. In both analyses, the gluon FF remains indirectly constrained in the present SIA+SIDIS framework and should be interpreted with appropriate caution. The extractions are carried out using the publicly available MontBlanc framework, and the resulting HAPS-PiFF1.0 and HAPS-KaFF1.0 replica sets are provided in the standard LHAPDF format.

### [161] [Threshold cusp effects to measure masses of radiatively decaying hadrons: The $B_{s0}^*$ mass from the $Υφ$ spectrum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16976)
*Hai-Long Fu,Xu Zhang,Feng-Kun Guo,Christoph Hanhart,Ulf-G. Meißner,Mao-Jun Yan*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种普适且模型无关的方法，通过目标强子与已知质量伴随粒子间的S波吸引相互作用产生的阈值尖点（cusp）来间接探测主要衰变到含光子末态的强子质量；作为概念验证，利用粒子-二聚体（particle-dimer）计算重现了X(4274)结构，并成功提取出D_{s0}^*的质量，进而将该方法推广到底部能区，预言了B_{s0}^*末态在~11.09 GeV处的类似结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在强子对撞机上，主要衰变到含光子末态的强子（如尚未观测到的B_{s0}^*和B_{s1}）极难直接探测；这些强子预期表现出超出传统夸克模型（quark-model）预言的奇特性质，亟需一种替代性探测方案。

Method: 当目标强子与一个质量精确已知的伴随强子之间存在吸引性S波相互作用时，合适末态的不变质量谱会在对阈值处产生尖点（cusp），若吸引足够强形成束缚态则会在阈值下方产生峰；通过减去伴随强子质量即可反推目标强子质量。作为概念验证，对D\bar D_s K三体系统进行领头阶粒子-二聚体（particle-dimer）计算。

Result: 该计算重现了LHCb实验中从B\to K J/ψφ提取的J/ψφ分布中的X(4274)结构，将其解释为由一个邻近虚态极点驱动的D_{s0}^*\bar D_s阈值尖点，得到m_{D_{s0}^*}=(2322±6) MeV，与实验测量值一致，并倾向于X(4274)的J^{PC}=0^{-+}量子数。将弹性三体相互作用转移到底部能区后，预言在~11.09 GeV处B_{s0}^*\bar B_s阈值附近存在类似结构。

Conclusion: 该方法能够利用已有的精确测量数据间接探测衰变到光子末态的难探测强子质量，且模型无关；LHC上Υφ不变质量分布可作为B_{s0}^*质量的干净探针。

Abstract: Hadrons that decay predominantly into final states containing photons are notoriously difficult to detect at hadron colliders. Prominent examples are the yet-unobserved $B_{s0}^*$ and $B_{s1}$, the bottom partners of the $D_{s0}^*(2317)$ and $D_{s1}(2460)$, which are expected to exhibit exotic properties deviating from the conventional quark-model predictions of $\bar b s$ mesons. We propose a general, model-independent method to overcome this problem: when the target hadron has an attractive $S$-wave interaction with a companion hadron of precisely known mass, the line shape of a suitable final state develops a cusp at the pair threshold, or a peak just below it if the attraction binds, so that subtracting the companion mass returns the target mass, up to the binding energy in the latter case. As a proof of concept, a leading-order particle-dimer calculation of the $D\bar D_s K$ three-body system reproduces the $X(4274)$ structure in the LHCb $J/ψφ$ distribution extracted from $B\to K J/ψφ$, as a $D_{s0}^*\bar D_s$ threshold cusp driven by a nearby virtual-state pole, yielding $m_{D_{s0}^*}=(2322\pm6)$ MeV in agreement with its measured value and favoring $J^{PC}=0^{-+}$ for the $X(4274)$. Transferring the elastic three-body interaction to the bottom sector, we predict an analogous structure at the $B_{s0}^*\bar B_s$ threshold near $11.09$ GeV, making the $Υφ$ invariant-mass distribution at the LHC a clean probe of the $B_{s0}^*$ mass.

Abstract: The neutrino sky below 165\,keV is yet to be explored. This region provides a unique probe of stellar cooling mechanisms through the detection of thermal solar neutrinos and the low-energy tail of the $pp$ solar cycle. Here, we investigate prospects for probing this regime via neutrino capture on tritium. Analyzing KATRIN public data, we set the first experimental bound on the thermal solar neutrino flux $Φ/Φ_{\mathrm{SSM}} < 1.86 \times 10^{18}$ at 95\%~CL ($1.58\times10^{18}$ at 90\%~CL), and show that a $100\;\text{kg}\cdot\text{yr}$ exposure would constrain the thermal solar neutrino component to $Φ/Φ_{\mathrm{SSM}} \lesssim 10^4$ and detect the low-energy $pp$ flux at the Standard Solar Model (SSM) level. ### [163] [Towards a consistent perturbation theory at finite temperature](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14863)
*Passant Ali,Peter Lowdon,Owe Philipsen*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于非微扰谱学（non-perturbative spectral）的热粒子（thermoparticle）微扰理论，通过推广Gell-Mann-Low关系来解决有限温度量子场论中标准微扰方法存在的壳上发散和红外发散等问题，并在φ⁴理论中通过两圈计算与数值晶格模拟的对比验证了该框架的精确预测能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 有限温度量子场论（finite-temperature quantum field theories）的标准微扰方法存在若干严重问题：实时形式（real-time formulation）中会出现定义不良的在壳（on-shell）贡献，无质量理论中则存在红外发散（infrared diverges）问题。先前研究表明，这些问题均源于Gell-Mann-Low关系在热场中的不一致推广，而这种不一致性又来自于该关系使用了在相互作用热理论中并不存在的自由散射态（free scattering states）。因此，亟需建立一种自洽的有限温度微扰框架。

Method: 基于非微扰谱学（non-perturbative spectral）的见解，提出有限温度下的散射态可由阻尼但稳定的类粒子激发——即热粒子（thermoparticles）——来描述，并据此推广了Gell-Mann-Low关系。该推广关系的微扰展开产生的贡献拓扑结构与标准方法完全相同，但其中的传播子（propagators）不再是自由场传播子，而是依赖于理论动力学的热粒子传播子。

Result: 热粒子微扰理论（thermoparticle perturbation theory）解决了标准方法中已知的发散问题。在质量φ⁴理论（massive φ⁴ theory）中，通过比较两圈水平的虚时计算（imaginary-time calculations）与两点关联函数（two-point correlation functions）的数值晶格模拟（numerical lattice simulations），明确展示了该框架能够像真空情况一样给出精确预测，这与标准方法的性能形成鲜明对比。

Conclusion: 热粒子微扰理论为有限温度量子场论提供了自洽且精确的微扰框架，有效克服了标准方法中的发散问题，并具备与真空微扰论相当的预测精度。

Abstract: The standard approach to perturbation theory for finite-temperature quantum field theories has several issues, including the appearance of ill-defined on-shell contributions in the real-time formulation, and infrared diverges in massless theories. Earlier studies indicate that these issues all stem from the inconsistent thermal generalisation of the Gell-Mann-Low relation, which forms the foundation of perturbation theory in vacuum. This inconsistency arises from the use of free scattering states in the relation, which are known not to exist in interacting thermal theories. In this work, we propose a generalisation of the Gell-Mann-Low relation for scalar theories based on non-perturbative spectral insights, namely that finite-temperature scattering states can be described by damped but stable particle-like excitations, so-called thermoparticles. The perturbative expansion of this generalised relation gives rise to contributions with exactly the same topology as the standard finite-temperature approach, except that now the propagators appearing in this expansion are not those of a free field but of thermoparticles, which depend on the dynamics of the theory. We demonstrate that thermoparticle perturbation theory resolves the known problems of the standard approach. Furthermore, by comparing imaginary-time calculations at two-loop level with numerical lattice simulations of two-point correlation functions in massive $φ^{4}$ theory, we explicitly show that this framework gives rise to precise predictions, as in the vacuum case, in stark contrast to the standard approach.

Abstract: We derive thermodynamic currents for a perfect fluid of massive spin-1 particles obeying Bose-Einstein statistics within the Wigner-function approach. We find that the approach yields a unified description of relativistic spin hydrodynamics independent of statistics and spin representation. *Nathaniel Craig,Amalia Madden*

TL;DR: 该论文提出五维’t Hooft-Polyakov单极弦（monopole strings）在核心恢复非阿贝尔规范对称性（non-abelian gauge symmetry）时，可成为额外维轴子（extra-dimensional axions）的轴子弦（axion strings），并论证弦张力与量子引力（quantum gravity）标度之间的参数化分离允许高质量轴子暗物质（axion dark matter）在暴胀后宇宙学（post-inflationary cosmology）中成立。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索高质量轴子暗物质在暴胀后宇宙学中的可行构建方案，解决轴子弦与量子引力标度之间的张力问题。

Method: 利用五维’t Hooft-Polyakov单极弦模型，通过核心区域恢复非阿贝尔规范对称性，将弦映射为额外维轴子的轴子弦。

Result: 弦张力与量子引力标度之间存在参数化分离（parametric separation），这使得高质量轴子暗物质在暴胀后宇宙学中具有可行性。

Conclusion: 五维单极弦可作为一种有效的轴子弦实现机制，为高质量轴子暗物质在暴胀后宇宙学中的存在提供理论支持。

Abstract: Five-dimensional 't Hooft-Polyakov monopole strings whose cores restore a non-abelian gauge symmetry become axion strings for extra-dimensional axions. The parametric separation between the string tension and the scale of quantum gravity admits a viable post-inflationary cosmology for high-quality axion dark matter.

### [168] [A scaling non-compact QCD axion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17019)
*Georgios K. Karananas,Mikhail Shaposhnikov*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种动力学机制，通过早期指数势（exponential potential）驱动非紧致QCD轴子（non-compact QCD axion）进入宇宙学标度吸引子（scaling cosmological attractor），从而擦除暴胀过程中产生的等曲率扰动（isocurvature perturbations），并开启动能错位（kinetic misalignment）机制，同时引入可探测的残余CP破缺（residual CP violation）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 暴胀期间产生的等曲率扰动（isocurvature perturbations）对宇宙微波背景辐射（CMB）观测形成严格约束，尤其对于轴子这类在暴胀期间有效质量为零的场。现有机制难以有效擦除这些扰动，因此需要提出新的动力学擦除方案。

Method: 通过在暴胀后引入一个早期指数势（early-time runaway exponential potential），将轴子驱动到标度宇宙学吸引子（scaling cosmological attractor）上。一旦进入吸引子，轴子便追踪宇宙主导成分——辐射，从而擦除等曲率模式。当QCD势能开启时，轴子携带非零速度，动能错位（kinetic misalignment）机制随之启动。

Result: 指数势机制成功擦除了暴胀等曲率扰动；轴子进入吸引子后追踪辐射主导成分；QCD势能开启后轴子具有非零速度，使得动能错位得以运作；指数势引入了残余CP破缺（residual CP violation），可能被未来的电偶极矩（electric dipole moment）实验探测到。

Conclusion: 该机制要求轴子在暴胀后演化所涉及的行星范围（field range）内有效为非紧致（non-compact）。该方案不仅解决了等曲率扰动问题，还为动能错位和CP破缺探测提供了新的理论路径。

Abstract: We present a dynamical mechanism for the erasure of inflationary isocurvature perturbations of the non-compact QCD axion. The key ingredient is an early-time runaway exponential potential, which drives the axion onto the well-known scaling cosmological attractor after inflation. Once on the attractor, the axion tracks the dominant component of the Universe, radiation, and isocurvature modes are erased even if the field is effectively massless during inflation. When the QCD potential turns on, the axion carries nonzero velocity, and kinetic misalignment can become operative. The exponential potential induces residual CP violation, potentially accessible to future electric dipole moment searches. This mechanism requires that the axion be effectively non-compact over the field range relevant for its post-inflationary evolution.

</details>
