### [169] [Plateau Gaps of Poisson Correctors Encode Metastable Reaction Rates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14789)
*Sang Yang,Zhixin Peng*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出一种直接从占位时间泊松校正器（occupation-time Poisson corrector）的平稳间隙提取亚稳态反应速率（metastable reaction rates）的方法，无需预定义过渡态表面，并在过阻尼与欠阻尼双阱动力学中恢复Kramers、Grote-Hynes和Pollak-Grabert-Hänggi速率层级，同时通过校正器-鞅分解揭示贡献于跃迁的随机力密度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统推断亚稳态反应速率的方法依赖于过渡态通量、平均首次通过时间或拟合动力学模型，这些方法通常需要预定义一个过渡态表面（transition-state surface）。本文旨在建立一种无需预定义过渡态表面、直接从生成元（generator）、稳态测度（stationary measure）和亚稳态划分（metastable partition）出发提取反应速率的新框架。

Method: 方法核心是构造一个居中的盆地观测量（centered basin-occupation observable）的占位时间泊松校正器，该校正器在反应物和产物盆地中形成亚稳态平台（metastable plateaus），平台之间的间隙直接决定正向和反向跃迁速率。该方法仅需要生成元、稳态测度和亚稳态划分，无需预设过渡态表面。进一步通过校正器-鞅分解（corrector-martingale decomposition）导出反应噪声密度（reactive-noise density）。

Result: 在过阻尼（overdamped）和欠阻尼（underdamped）双阱动力学（double-well dynamics）中，该平台间隙速率恢复Kramers、Grote-Hynes以及Pollak-Grabert-Hänggi的层级理论。校正器-鞅分解给出了反应噪声密度，揭示了构型空间或相空间中随机力对跃迁的贡献位置。

Conclusion: 亚稳态反应速率及其涨落源信息可以从单一的校正器场（corrector field）中同时提取，该框架为无需过渡态表面假设的速率计算提供了新途径。

Abstract: Metastable reaction rates are commonly inferred from transition-state fluxes, mean first-passage times, or fitted kinetic models. We show that they are directly encoded in the plateau gap of an occupation-time Poisson corrector. For a centered basin-occupation observable, the Poisson corrector develops metastable plateaus in the reactant and product basins, and their separation determines the forward and backward transition rates. This construction requires only the generator, stationary measure, and metastable partition, and therefore does not rely on a predefined transition-state surface. In overdamped and underdamped double-well dynamics, the plateau-gap rate recovers the Kramers, Grote-Hynes, and Pollak-Grabert-Hänggi hierarchy. The same corrector-martingale decomposition yields a reactive-noise density, revealing where stochastic forcing contributes to transitions in configuration or phase space. Thus, reaction rates and their fluctuation sources emerge from a single corrector field.

</details>


### [170] [Quasiparticle Diffusion for the Toda Fluid in Equilibrium](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15131)
*Seema Chahal,Alberto Brollo,Indranil Mukherjee,Abhishek Dhar,Anupam Kundu,Herbert Spohn*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文针对Toda流体（Toda fluid），提出了一种基于Lax矩阵（Lax matrix）时变特征向量来追踪准粒子（quasiparticle）轨迹的数值方案，数值验证了准粒子的布朗运动（Brownian motion），并确认了标记粒子（tagged particle）的扩散常数与热力学贝特假设（thermodynamic Bethe ansatz, TBA）预测一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多体可积系统（many-body integrable systems）可理解为准粒子气体，其弹道传播驱动大规模输运，但除硬杆系统（hard rods system）外，尚未有数值工具能够追踪此类准粒子轨迹。

Method: 以Toda流体为研究对象，该系统的可积性依赖于Lax对的存在；作者利用Lax矩阵的时变特征向量，设计了一种数值方案来追踪准粒子的运动轨迹。

Result: 在热平衡态下模拟Toda流体，数值追踪方案确认了准粒子的布朗运动；同时模拟了标记粒子的运动，其扩散常数（diffusion constant）与一种新颖的热力学贝特假设预测结果吻合。

Conclusion: 该数值方案有望推广至其他具有Lax矩阵的经典多粒子模型。

Abstract: Many-body integrable systems can be understood as a gas of quasiparticles. They propagate ballistically and drive large-scale transport. However, with the exception of the hard rods system, no tools have been available to numerically track such quasiparticles. Focusing on the Toda fluid, whose integrability relies on the availability of a Lax pair, we present a numerical scheme to track quasiparticle trajectories as determined by the time-dependent eigenvectors of the Lax matrix. Simulating the Toda fluid in thermal equilibrium, this tracking scheme is used to numerical confirm Brownian motion of a quasiparticle. Simulated is also the motion of a tagged particle. Our numerical results for the diffusion constant matches with a novel TBA prediction. We believe our numerical scheme can be extended to other classical many-particle models possessing a Lax matrix.

</details>


### [171] [Self-Consistent Closure of Fractal Dimension, Nonextensive Statistics, and Non-Markovian Dynamics in Critical Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15750)
*O. Sotolongo-Costa,J. Weberszpil,M. E. Mora-Ramos*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过相空间自洽性推导出自组织临界系统中三个宏观特征参数（Tsallis指数q、Hausdorff维数D、记忆指数α）之间的封闭代数关系：α = D/(2D - 1)，并结合q = 1 + 1/D导出α = 1/(3 - q)。该"三重关系"（Troika relation）不含自由参数，并在八个独立实验系统中得到验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自组织临界系统（self-organized critical systems）通常同时表现出三个宏观特征：非广延热力学（由Tsallis指数q量化）、结构分形性（由Hausdorff维数D衡量）和非马尔可夫动力学（由记忆指数α表征）。历史上这些参数被视为相互独立，只能逐案例进行经验拟合，缺乏统一的理论关联。

Method: 通过相空间自洽性（phase-space self-consistency）分析，推导出α = D/(2D - 1)的代数封闭关系。结合分形支撑上Tsallis熵的广延性条件导出的q = 1 + 1/D，进一步得到α = 1/(3 - q)。该封闭关系不含自由参数，并满足物理边界条件：α(1) = 1（欧氏空间中的弹道输运）和D→∞时α→1/2（最大亚扩散极限）。

Result: 在八个独立实验系统中验证了该"三重关系"（Troika relation），包括：地震活动、电磁前兆、脑电图（EEG）、城市网络、植物结构以及空间等离子体。所有实测值均落在理论预测的误差范围内，证明了该封闭关系的普适性（universality）。

Conclusion: 相空间自洽性将自组织临界系统的三个关键参数——q、D、α——统一为一个不含自由参数的封闭关系，从而将以往独立拟合的变量纳入同一理论框架。该关系已在多种自然与人工系统中得到实验确认，表明自组织临界性具有更深层的结构普遍性。

Abstract: Self-organized critical systems often exhibit three macroscopic features simultaneously: nonextensive thermodynamics (quantified by the Tsallis index $q$), structural fractality (measured by the Hausdorff dimension $D$), and non-Markovian dynamics (characterized by the memory exponent $α$). Historically, these parameters have been treated as independent, to be empirically fitted case by case. Here we demonstrate that phase-space self-consistency imposes a unique algebraic closure: $α=D/(2D-1)$. This relation, together with $q=1+1/D$ derived from the extensivity of Tsallis entropy on fractal supports, yields the known result $α=1/(3-q)$ as a consequence, not as an independent assumption. The closure contains no free parameters and satisfies the physical boundary conditions $α(1)=1$ (ballistic transport in Euclidean spaces) and $α\to1/2$ as $D\to\infty$ (maximally subdiffusive regime). We validate the Troika relation across eight independent experimental systems, including seismicity, electromagnetic precursors, EEG, urban networks, botanical architectures, and space plasma. All measured values fall within error bars of the theoretical prediction, establishing the universality of the closure.

</details>


### [172] [Geometric decomposition of the $d$-dimensional hard-sphere partition function](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16483)
*Luke K. Davis*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文引入了一种硬球（hard-sphere）配分函数（partition function）的几何分解方法，通过基于密堆（close-packing）的可用插入体积几何上界（经局部密度认证后严格成立），建立了构型积分（configurational integral）的参考上界 Q*。将 Q* 从Speedy统计几何配分函数中分解出来，得到d维配分函数的新形式 Q = Q* exp(-N J)，其中J仅依赖于空隙的边界-体积比及密堆密度。该工作深化了对硬球体系的统计几何理解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 硬球体系是统计力学（statistical mechanics）中的核心模型，但其配分函数的几何结构尚未被充分揭示。本文旨在通过几何分解方法，建立配分函数与密堆几何量之间的严格关系，从而深化对硬球体系统计几何的理解。

Method: 引入基于密堆思想的几何上界约束可用插入体积（available insertion volume），并在具备局部密度证书（local density certificate）时使其严格成立，从而建立构型积分的一个参考上界 Q*。将Q*从Speedy的统计几何配分函数中分解出来，得到新的配分函数形式。

Result: 得到d维硬球配分函数的新表达式 Q(N,V,T)=Q* exp(-N J)，其中J严格依赖于空隙的边界-体积比（boundary-to-volume ratio）和密堆密度（close-packing density）。

Conclusion: 该工作通过几何分解方法，建立了硬球配分函数与密堆几何量之间的显式联系，增进了对硬球体系统计几何（statistical geometry）的理解。

Abstract: We introduce a geometric decomposition of the hard-sphere partition function. Using a close-packing-inspired geometric bound on the available insertion volume, made rigorous when a corresponding local density certificate is available, we establish a reference upper bound $Q^\ast$ on the configurational integral. Factoring this upper bound out of the statistical geometric partition function of Speedy yields a new form for the $d$-dimensional partition function, $Q(N,V,T)=Q^\ast \exp(-N \mathcal{J})$, where $\mathcal{J}$ depends strictly on the boundary-to-volume ratio of the voids and the close-packing density. Overall, this work deepens our statistical geometric understanding of the hard-sphere system.

</details>


### [173] [Extracting Boundary Conformal Data from Periodic Non-Hermitian Critical Chains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16785)
*Yifan Liu,Haruki Shimizu,Dongchang Liu,Kohei Kawabata*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种周期链投影-配分函数谱学方法（periodic-chain projected-partition-function spectroscopy），通过非厄米体临界量子链直接提取边界共形场论（BCFT）的普适数据，无需构造微观开边界，并成功应用于非厄米Ising模型与五态Potts链，获得了Affleck-Ludwig边界熵等非幺正边界临界量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 边界共形场论（boundary conformal field theory, BCFT）包含的普适数据通常需在格点上施加空间边界才能微观获取，但非厄米系统中的细微边界效应使这一途径面临挑战。作者希望发展一种仅依赖体临界系统知识、无需构建显式开边界的方法来提取非幺正BCFT的边界普适量。

Method: 引入周期链投影-配分函数谱学方法（periodic-chain projected-partition-function spectroscopy），利用短程纠缠边界制备（short-range-entangled boundary preparation）及其红外相容的左对偶（infrared-compatible left dual），从非厄米体临界量子链中直接得到边界量。

Result: 在PT对称Ising实现（实非幺正杨-Lee CFT）中，提取了最小边界投影系数，并恢复了非平凡负激发-基态比。在非厄米五态Potts链（真正复不动点）中，解析了本质复数的边界系数，并再现了Kramers-Wannier对偶所要求的精确关系。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了仅凭体临界系统知识获取非幺正BCFT普适数据的路径，为研究非厄米边界临界现象打开了窗口。

Abstract: Boundary conformal field theory (BCFT) contains universal data that are usually accessed microscopically by imposing spatial boundaries on the lattice. Here, we introduce a periodic-chain projected-partition-function spectroscopy that extracts universal boundary quantities directly from non-Hermitian bulk-critical quantum chains, avoiding the need to engineer microscopic open boundaries and circumventing subtle boundary effects in non-Hermitian systems. Using a short-range-entangled boundary preparation and its infrared-compatible left dual, we obtain the Affleck-Ludwig boundary entropy in non-Hermitian systems. We demonstrate this construction for two representative non-Hermitian infrared structures. For a $\mathcal{PT}$-symmetric Ising realization of the real nonunitary Yang-Lee CFT, we extract the minimal-boundary projected coefficient and recover a nontrivial negative excited-to-ground ratio. For the genuinely complex fixed points of the non-Hermitian five-state Potts chain, we resolve intrinsically complex boundary coefficients and reproduce the exact relation required by the Kramers-Wannier duality. Our results establish a route to nonunitary BCFT universal data via only knowledge of the bulk critical system, opening a window into non-Hermitian boundary criticality.

</details>


### [174] [Entropic Necks, Dynamic Crossovers, and Fragility in Supercooled Liquids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15557)
*Biman Bagchi*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文基于Zwanzig熵瓶颈图像（entropic-neck picture）的组态空间（configuration-space）扩展，结合Mori–Zwanzig记忆函数形式（memory-function formalism），构建了一个理论框架来解释过冷液体（supercooled liquids）中的动力学交叉，特别是从Rosenfeld过剩熵标度（Rosenfeld excess-entropy scaling）到Adam–Gibbs关系的转变。核心思想是结构弛豫受限于连接亚稳盆地（metastable basins）的组态路径的收缩，降温时颈缩导致熵亏缺，从而产生活化动力学（activated dynamics）。脆性（fragility）在此图像中获得了几何解释：脆性液体对应有效组态颈的快速坍缩，强液体则对应缓慢演化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 过冷液体的动力学急剧减慢伴随着一系列动力学交叉，其中从高温碰撞主导输运到低温活化结构弛豫的转变，以及从Rosenfeld过剩熵标度到Adam–Gibbs关系的跨越尤为显著。现有理论尚缺乏一个统一的动力学与几何框架来解释这些交叉现象。

Method: 将Zwanzig熵瓶颈图像扩展到组态空间（configuration space），并与Mori–Zwanzig记忆函数形式（Mori–Zwanzig memory-function formalism）相结合。从描述盆地内运动（intrabasin motion）和颈涨落（neck fluctuations）的耦合慢变量出发，推导出约化广义朗之万描述（reduced generalized Langevin description），通过消除颈坐标产生长寿命记忆核（memory kernel）。

Result: 高温下瓶颈宽且易达，得到由局部结构熵（local structural entropy）主导的Rosenfeld型输运；冷却时瓶颈逐渐收缩，产生熵亏缺，导致Adam–Gibbs行为和活化弛豫。脆性获得几何解释：脆性液体有效组态颈随温度快速坍缩，强液体则缓慢演化。

Conclusion: 该框架提供了过冷液体动力学交叉的动力学与几何解释，但不从微观相互作用计算组态熵、失配罚分（mismatch penalty）或协作长度（cooperative length），其目标在于提供一种动力学的几何诠释。

Abstract: The dramatic slowdown of dynamics in supercooled liquids is accompanied by a sequence of dynamical crossovers, most notably the transition from high-temperature collision-dominated transport to low-temperature activated structural relaxation. A particularly striking manifestation of this change is the crossover from Rosenfeld excess-entropy scaling to the Adam--Gibbs relation. In this work we develop a theoretical framework based on a configuration-space extension of Zwanzig's entropic-neck picture and combine it with a Mori--Zwanzig memory-function formalism to address anomalies of supercooled liquids. The central idea is that structural relaxation is controlled by the narrowing of configurational pathways connecting metastable basins of the inherent-structure landscape. Starting from coupled slow variables describing intrabasin motion and neck fluctuations, we derive a reduced generalized Langevin description in which elimination of the neck coordinate generates a long-lived memory kernel and naturally leads to entropy-controlled activated dynamics. At high temperatures the neck is broad and readily accessible, yielding Rosenfeld-type transport governed primarily by local structural entropy. Upon cooling, progressive neck constriction produces an increasing entropy deficit, leading to Adam--Gibbs behavior and activated relaxation. Within this picture, fragility acquires a simple geometric interpretation: fragile liquids are characterized by a rapid collapse of the effective configurational neck with decreasing temperature, whereas strong liquids exhibit a much slower evolution of accessible pathways. The framework does not by itself compute the configurational entropy, mismatch penalty, or cooperative length from microscopic interactions; its aim is to provide a dynamical and geometrical interpretation.

</details>


### [175] [Exact solution of the Glauber-Ising model on the finite-length semi-open chain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16848)
*Malte Henkel*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文解析地推导了淬火至零温的一维半开有限格点Glauber-Ising模型的精确时空关联函数，进而导出其对偶一维周期环上凝聚-扩散过程的精确空区间概率，并重现了粒子浓度的长时间衰减行为。上述结果与动力学有限尺寸标度理论的普适预期一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究一维Glauber-Ising模型在零温淬火下的精确动力学行为，特别是有限尺寸系统中的时空关联函数，以检验动力学有限尺寸标度理论的普适性。

Method: 采用解析方法，在大小为N的半开格点（semi-open lattice）上推导淬火至零温的一维Glauber-Ising模型的精确时间-空间关联函数（time-space correlation function）；并通过对偶关系（duality）将其映射到一维周期环上的凝聚-扩散过程（coagulation-diffusion process），从而获得精确空区间概率（empty-interval probability）。

Result: 获得了半开有限格点上一维Glauber-Ising模型在零温淬火下的精确时空关联函数，以及其对偶过程中周期环上的精确空区间概率，并成功再现了粒子浓度的长时间衰减行为。

Conclusion: 所得结果与动力学有限尺寸标度（dynamical finite-size scaling）理论的普适预期相一致，从而为该标度理论的正确性提供了精确的解析验证。

Abstract: The exact time-space correlation function of the $1D$ Glauber-Ising model, quenched to temperature $T=0$ and on a semi-open lattice of finite size $N$, is obtained. This also allows to deduce the exact empty-interval probability of the dual $1D$ coagulation-diffusion process on a periodic finite ring and to reproduce the long-time decay of the particle concentration. These results are consistent with the generic expectations of dynamical finite-size scaling theory.

### [176] [Wavelet Localisation and Local Modulation Freezing in MRW Unwrapping](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15929)

Method: 基于局部乘性调制冻结假设，推导对数小波振幅的近似可加分解，将MRW解缠重新表述为局域化多尺度算子问题；通过分析支撑几何、尺度依赖重叠及残差多尺度混合，刻画有限尺度偏差与协方差畸变的结构形式。

Abstract: We develop a localised wavelet formulation of multifractal random walk unwrapping based on the local multiplicative modulation freezing. The validity of the approximation depends explicitly on support geometry, scale-dependent overlap, and residual multiscale mixing generated by internal modulation variability. We show that these effects naturally produce finite-scale deviations from ideal logarithmic covariance scaling and lead to structured covariance distortions whose form depends on the interaction between the modulation field and the geometry of the wavelet representation. Numerical investigations using orthonormal wavelet decompositions support the proposed interpretation and demonstrate the emergence of scale-dependent freezing regimes, residual covariance mixing, and finite-support breakdown effects consistent with the theory. The proposed framework suggests a broader connection between wavelet localisation, local regularity organisation, and finite-support multiscale stochastic operators. Wavelet localisation becomes an operational mechanism for probing localised multiscale structure.

### [177] [Universality in the target arrival statistics of non-conservative search processes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16025)
*José Giral-Barajas,Samantha Linn,Paul C. Bressloff*

TL;DR: 本文揭示了非保守随机搜索过程（non-conservative stochastic search）与排队论（queueing theory）之间的自然映射关系，推导出目标到达时间分布的完整时间依赖形式，并发现稳态下到达间隔时间分布（inter-arrival time distribution）具有普适的指数形式，不受搜索过程细节的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用非保守随机搜索与排队论之间的自然映射（natural mapping），在极少的底层搜索过程假设下推导目标到达时间的完整时间依赖分布。

Result: 稳态下到达间隔时间分布精确为指数分布（exponential distribution），不受搜索过程细节影响，展现出从排队框架中直接产生的稳健普适性（robust universality）。非保守搜索过程的到达统计量比固定搜索者数量的序贯搜索-捕获过程（sequential search-and-capture processes）更简单。

Abstract: Stochastic search processes in which searchers are continuously introduced to and removed from a target search domain are fundamental to a wide class of physical and artificial systems. The theory of such non-conservative search processes is, however, much less developed than for search processes with a fixed number of particles. Here we exploit a natural mapping between non-conservative stochastic search and queueing theory to derive the full time-dependent distribution of target arrivals under minimal assumptions on the underlying search process. Remarkably, we find that the steady-state inter-arrival time distribution is exactly exponential, regardless of the details of the search process, showing a robust universality that emerges directly from the queueing framework. Thus, counterintuitively, the arrival statistics of a non-conservative search process are much simpler than sequential search-and-capture processes involving a fixed number of searchers. This has major implications for target resource accumulation, where the delivery of resources is counter-balanced by their downstream consumption.

Result: 成功得到了该模型的精确自由能表达式；该结果将Onsager自由能和含虚场的Lee-Yang自由能作为特例涵盖其中，并通过连续参数建立了它们之间的联系；同时揭示了虚磁场$iπ/2$与对偶晶格中受阻正方形的一一对应关系。

### [179] [Foundations of entropy in complex systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16312)
*Jan Korbel*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文综述了熵（entropy）的基础理论及其向复杂系统（complex systems）的推广，涵盖广义熵公式、统计分布、公理化体系及标度关系，强调应根据系统的结构与物理性质选择适当的熵形式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典玻尔兹曼-吉布斯（Boltzmann-Gibbs）熵在复杂系统（如长程相互作用、非遍历系统）中面临局限性，亟需建立更具普适性的熵理论框架。

Method: 采用综述性方法：首先从玻尔兹曼公式、重分（multiplicity）、粗粒化（coarse-graining）与香农熵（Shannon entropy）的关系出发，引入Rényi、Tsallis及Burg等广义熵；随后考察三种经典统计分布（Maxwell–Boltzmann、Bose–Einstein、Fermi–Dirac）以及结构形成系统、样本空间约化过程（sample-space reducing processes）、波利亚罐（Pólya urns）和非线性动力学；接着梳理Shannon–Khinchin公理、Tempesta群可组合性（group-composability）、Hanel–Thurner渐近标度、Shore–Johnson相容性公理以及Lieb–Yngvason公理；最后讨论校准不变性（calibration invariance）、线性平均与伴随平均（escort averages）之间的Hanel–Thurner–Gell-Mann对偶性及Kolmogorov–Nagumo平均。

Result: 相同的概率分布可以由不同的熵、约束条件或动力学机制导出；公理化框架揭示了熵函数的选择与系统渐近标度行为及可组合性结构之间的内在关联。

Conclusion: 熵的选择并非任意，而应由系统的底层结构与物理特性（如相空间几何、相互作用范围、遍历性程度）来引导；上述理论工具为复杂系统的统计描述提供了统一且灵活的形式化基础。

Abstract: This chapter reviews the foundations of entropy and their extensions to complex systems. We first discuss the relation between Boltzmann's formula, multiplicity, coarse-graining, and Shannon entropy, before introducing generalized entropies such as Rényi, Tsallis, and Burg entropy. We then examine Maxwell--Boltzmann, Bose--Einstein, and Fermi--Dirac statistics, structure-forming systems, sample-space reducing processes, Pólya urns, and nonlinear dynamics. Axiomatic approaches are presented through the Shannon--Khinchin axioms, Tempesta group-composability, Hanel--Thurner asymptotic scaling, Shore--Johnson consistency axioms, and Lieb--Yngvason axioms. Finally, we discuss calibration invariance, Hanel--Thurner--Gell-Mann duality between linear and escort averages, and Kolmogorov--Nagumo averages, showing how the same distribution can arise from different entropies, constraints, or dynamics. These results emphasize that the choice of entropy should be guided by the structure and physical properties of the system.

We augment this model by specifying the duration of the isothermal process as a monotonic decreasing function of the temperature difference between the working substance and the reservoir. As an illustration, we analyze the machine's operation in the low-dissipation regime in which the entropy production in each isothermal branch is inversely proportional to the duration of the process. The modified model is able to determine the optimal durations of isothermal processes as well as heat and work per cycle, while retaining the optimal power conditions of the CA model.

Abstract: Thermodynamic Uncertainty Relations (TURs) impose universal bounds linking current precision to entropy production in nonequilibrium systems. In this work, we derive a generalized entropic bound for current fluctuations in renewal-reward processes. By utilizing a rigorous variance decomposition within the framework of renewal-reward theory, we obtain a model-independent bound that is not only rigorous but tighter than the standard PV relation. Notably, in the linear-response regime, our bound correctly scales with the renewal rate and identifies a precision penalty arising from cycle-length fluctuations. ### [182] [Persistence Properties of a Phase-ordering System with Competing Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16443)
*Shubham Thwal,Suman Majumder*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该论文通过零温蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）模拟，研究了二维伊辛模型（Ising model）在竞争性非守恒自旋翻转（spin-flip）与守恒自旋交换（spin-exchange）动力学下的持续性质（persistence properties）。研究发现总持续概率（total persistence probability）与自旋翻转持续概率（spin-flip persistence probability）具有相同的幂律衰减行为，其持续指数（persistence exponent）θᵢ ≈ 0.225，且满足标度关系（scaling relation）d-d_fⁱ = θᵢ/αᵢ；而复合持续概率（composite persistence probability）虽也呈幂律衰减，但其持续指数θ_c与分形维数（fractal dimension）d_f^c强烈依赖于自旋翻转相对概率p_r，导致标度关系失效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究对纯非守恒或纯守恒动力学下的持续性质已有较多关注，但实际体系常涉及两种动力学的竞争。该工作旨在填补对竞争性非守恒与守恒动力学共存下持续性质的理解空白。

Method: 采用零温蒙特卡洛模拟，研究二维伊辛模型在竞争性非守恒自旋翻转与守恒自旋-exchange动力学下的相序（phase ordering）过程。分别测量了总持续概率、自旋翻转持续概率和复合持续概率三种持续量，并分析了它们的幂律衰减行为及对应的标度关系。

Result: 总持续概率与自旋翻转持续概率在渐近区域表现出相同的幂律衰减，持续指数θᵢ ≈ 0.225，与纯非守恒动力学下的结果一致；两者均满足标度关系d-d_fⁱ = θᵢ/αᵢ，其中αᵢ ≈ 1/2。复合持续概率虽也呈幂律衰减，但其指数θ_c和分形维数d_f^c均对p_r有强依赖性，且标度关系被破坏。

Conclusion: 竞争动力学下，总持续概率和自旋翻转持续概率的行为与纯非守恒动力学一致，表现出普适性；而复合持续概率因同时受两种动力学影响，不再具备普适标度行为。

Abstract: We investigate the persistence properties during phase ordering in the two-dimensional ($d=2$) Ising model evolving under competing nonconserved spin-flip and conserved spin-exchange dynamics by means of Monte Carlo simulations at zero temperature. We examine three distinct persistence probabilities: (i) the total persistence probability, defined as the probability that a lattice site has never experienced a change in the sign of the spin residing there; (ii) the spin-flip persistence probability, which exclusively measures the fraction of sites that have never undergone a spin-flip event; and (iii) the composite persistence probability, defined as the fraction of sites that have experienced neither a spin-flip nor a spin-exchange event. In the asymptotic regime, both the total and spin-flip persistence probabilities exhibit identical power-law decay, irrespective of the relative occurrence probability of the spin-flip move $p_r$. The corresponding persistence exponent $θ_i \approx 0.225$, is found to be consistent with the value reported for systems evolving purely under nonconserved dynamics. We further demonstrate that both persistence measures satisfy the scaling relation $d-d_f^i=θ_i/α_i$, where $d_f^i$ is the fractal dimension of the corresponding persistence lattice and $α_i\approx 1/2$ characterizes the asymptotic power-law growth of spatially correlated regions of non-persistent spins. In contrast, although the composite persistence probability also exhibits asymptotic power-law decay, both the corresponding persistence exponent $θ_{\rm c}$ and the fractal dimension $d_f^{\rm c}$ of the persistence lattice show strong dependence on $p_r$. Combined with the presence of a universal growth exponent $α_{\rm c}\approx 1/2$, this leads to the breakdown of the scaling relation among the characteristic exponents for the composite persistence.

*Alessandro Corso,Daniel M. Busiello*

Abstract: Countless biological and physical systems experience fluctuations that exhibit non-trivial temporal correlations. The Unified Colored-Noise Approximation (UCNA) is a framework providing an approximate description of such stochastic dynamics with colored noise, valid in the limits of vanishing and infinite correlation time of the noise. We first pinpoint and address some criticalities in its original derivation, recasting the result through a time-scale separation procedure. By using our approach, we derive the next-to-leading order correction to the dynamics in both limiting regimes, and highlight the relevant physical scalings of these approximations. Our result helps frame the limits of validity of both the original and the refined formulas, especially in comparison with those derived through different approximation procedures. We show our findings in two paradigmatic examples, a quartic potential and a stochastic logistic growth with multiplicative noise.

</details>


### [184] [Riviera model with egoistical settlers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16791)

TL;DR: 本文研究了Riviera模型（一种沿海岸线致密化定居的晶格模型）中集群的统计特性，推导了空隙-集群-空隙分布的闭式演化方程，给出了堵塞态下集群分布的阶乘衰减形式，并分析了有限系统和连续版本下的统计行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该模型模拟了沿海岸线逐渐致密化的定居过程，其簇分布不满足封闭的演化方程组，需要寻找替代的统计描述方法。

Method: 采用晶格版本和连续版本两个视角：晶格版本中房屋依次建在空位，每栋新房至少有一个空邻居；通过计算空隙-集群-空隙分布间接提取集群分布；对有限系统采用静态方法直接处理堵塞态。

Result: 在堵塞态（所有空隙长度为1，演化停止）下，集群分布具有简洁形式，表现出随簇长度阶乘衰减（factorial decay）；对于有限海岸线段，得到了堵塞态空位数量的统计量（均值、方差和高阶累积量）。

Conclusion: Riviera模型的集群统计可通过空隙-集群-空隙分布间接求解，堵塞态下的阶乘衰减行为以及有限系统和连续版本的解析结果揭示了该模型的统计力学特性。

Abstract: The Riviera model mimics a densifying settlement along the coastline. In the lattice version, houses are built sequentially in empty sites with the constraint that every newly built house has at least one empty neighboring site. The distribution of clusters of adjacent houses does not obey a closed set of evolutionary equations, but the void-cluster-void distribution does. We compute the latter and extract the cluster distribution from it. In the jammed state, when all voids have length one and the evolution ceases, the cluster distribution has a neat form and exhibits a factorial decay with the length of the cluster. To investigate finite systems, we employ a static approach directly treating jammed states. If the coastline is a finite segment, we determine the statistics of the number of empty sites in the jammed state (the average, variance, and higher cumulants). We also study a continuum version in which houses are built along the line so that each newly built house is sufficiently separated from at least one neighboring house.

### [185] [Distributed Acoustic Sensing for Urban Monitoring: Coverage Thresholds and Percolation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17018)
*Khen Cohen,Ariel Lellouch*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文基于图论（Graph Theory）框架，分析了分布式声学传感（Distributed Acoustic Sensing, DAS）在城市监测中的覆盖度临界阈值，定义了低覆盖、逾渗转变和完全覆盖三个不同监测区间，并展示了面向地震预警、交通监测和城市活动追踪的最优传感网络设计框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分布式声学传感（DAS）可将现有光纤网络改造为超密集、长距离的地震阵列用于城市监测，但真实世界光纤基础设施的拓扑和组件约束限制了其在城市尺度上的应用。本文旨在为近未来片上DAS的城市部署提供理论框架和最优设计路线图。

Method: 基于图论（Graph Theory）框架，对城市监测应用的覆盖度进行理论分析，识别出两个关键覆盖度阈值，并定义三个不同监测区间。针对全球多个大都市，通过示例展示了面向地震预警（earthquake early warning）、交通监测和城市活动追踪的最优传感网络设计方法。

Result: 低覆盖度（<10%）在最优设计下可解决地震预警、地下水监测、地质填图和城市活动追踪；覆盖度达到51.6%时发生逾渗转变（percolation transition），城市实际达到全覆盖，可实现统计交通监测；仅当覆盖度达到有效完全覆盖时，基础设施监测、个体车辆追踪和行人运动分析才成为可能。隐私相关风险在此框架下保持极低水平。

Conclusion: 该框架为近未来城市DAS网络部署提供了路线图，将DAS用作智慧城市传感（smart city sensing）的基础骨干网络。

Abstract: Distributed Acoustic Sensing (DAS) enables the repurposing of existing fiber-optic networks as ultra-dense, long-range seismic arrays for urban monitoring. However, constraints imposed by real-world fiber infrastructure topology and components limit its use for city-scale applications. Recent technological developments have paved the way for short-range, on-chip DAS. Assuming their availability, and based on a Graph Theory framework, we show that monitoring applications fall along a coverage spectrum with two critical thresholds that define three distinct regimes. Low coverage (<10%) can, with optimal design, resolve earthquake early warning, groundwater monitoring, geological mapping, and urban activity tracking. A percolation transition occurs at 51.6% coverage, beyond which the city effectively becomes fully covered and statistical traffic monitoring is possible. Only for effectively complete coverage, infrastructure monitoring, individual vehicle tracking, and pedestrian movement analysis become possible. Thus, privacy-related risks remain very low. We show and exemplify how, for metropolises around the world, an optimal sensing network can be designed for earthquake early warning, traffic monitoring, and urban activity tracking. This framework provides a near-future roadmap for deploying urban DAS networks as a backbone of smart city sensing.

</details>


### [186] [Milestoning Markov-jump dynamics: Stationary properties, thermodynamic consistency, kinetic hysteresis, and fluctuation symmetries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17033)
*Tassilo Schwarz,David Hartich,Aljaž Godec*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文推导了将一般马尔可夫跳过程（Markov-jump processes）精确粗粒化为可观测的半马尔可夫动力学（semi-Markov dynamics）的方法，证明了等待时间分布可分解为条件独立的驻留时间（dwell time）和跃迁路径时间（transition-path time），并分析了其热力学一致性及动力学滞后效应（kinetic hysteresis）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为复杂系统中的隐藏耗散循环提供可观测的推断基础，克服马尔可夫近似在粗粒化过程中的局限性。

Method: 从一般马尔可夫跳过程出发，推导了可观测状态之间跃迁的等待时间分布的精确粗粒化公式，证明其可分解为条件独立的驻留时间和跃迁路径时间；通过定义里程碑动力学（milestoned dynamics）并分析其稳态性质、热力学一致性以及对里程碑位置的鲁棒性来验证方法的有效性。

Result: 驻留时间是中观状态（mesostate）的局部属性，仅依赖初始状态；跃迁路径时间依赖初始和最终状态，引发动力学滞后效应，并在隐藏子网络满足适当条件时满足反射对称性（reflection symmetry）。即使观测动力学近似马尔可夫化，动力学滞后对耗散的影响依然存在。

Conclusion: 该方法为从跃迁路径时间的观测数据推断隐藏耗散循环的亲合度（affinity）奠定了理论基础，并通过最小实例验证了其可行性。

Abstract: We derive an exact coarse graining of generic Markov-jump processes into observable semi-Markov dynamics. Exact results for waiting-time distributions for jumps between observable states are derived and proved that these decompose into conditionally independent dwell and transition times. Dwell times are proved to be a local property of mesostates - they depend on the initial but not final state. Conversely, transition-path times depend on both states, trigger kinetic hysteresis, and, under suitable conditions on the hidden sub-network, are shown to obey a reflection symmetry. We characterize the stationary properties of the milestoned dynamics, prove its thermodynamic consistency, and demonstrate robustness to milestone positioning. Surprisingly, even in the limit of a time-scale separation rendering the observed dynamics approximately Markovian, the effect of kinetic hysteresis on the dissipation persists. A minimal example shows how the results lay the foundation for inferring affinities of hidden dissipative cycles from observations of transition-path times.

### [187] [A generalized long-wave limit method with spectral perturbations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15174)
*Tianwei Qiu,Zhen Wang*

Main category: nlin.SI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种广义长波极限方法（generalized long-wave limit method），通过在长波极限框架中引入谱扰动（spectral perturbations），在统一的小参数框架下同时考虑谱参数简并、波数不同消失速率及相位参数高阶调制，从而构造出可控数量的高阶怪波解（higher-order lump solutions），并揭示了从怪波链（lump chain）退化为高阶怪波的机制；该方法能够生成与Yablonskii–Vorob'ev多项式无关的、长期渐近行为独立的高阶怪波解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的改进长波极限方法（improved long-wave limit method）在构造高阶怪波解时，其长期渐近行为受限于Yablonskii–Vorob'ev多项式，需要一种新方法以获得渐近行为独立的高阶怪波解，并统一处理谱参数简并与波数消失速率等复杂因素。

Method: 在长波极限框架中引入谱扰动，构建统一的小参数框架，同时处理谱参数简并（degeneracy of spectral parameters）、波数不同消失速率（vanishing rates of wave numbers）及相位参数高阶调制（higher-order modulations of the phase parameters）；通过调整相位参数，将辅助函数展开的首项推至指定阶数，从而控制怪波数目。

Result: 以Kadomtsev–Petviashvili-I（KP-I）方程为例，系统导出了二阶和三阶怪波解，透明地揭示了怪波链退化为高阶怪波的机制；从M-怪波链可生成最多M(M+1)/2个怪波的退化解；该方法产生的解长期渐近行为与Yablonskii–Vorob'ev多项式无关。

Conclusion: 该广义长波极限方法能生成可控数量的高阶怪波解，且解的长期渐近行为独立于Yablonskii–Vorob'ev多项式，优于改进长波极限方法；该方法还可推广至具有不同谱参数的混合高阶怪波解（hybrid higher-order lump solutions）。

Abstract: A generalized long-wave limit method that introduces spectral perturbations into the long-wave limit framework is proposed for constructing higher-order lump solutions. Within a unified small-parameter framework, the method simultaneously accounts for the degeneracy of spectral parameters, different vanishing rates of wave numbers, and higher-order modulations of the phase parameters. By tuning the phase parameters to push the leading term of the auxiliary function expansion to a prescribed order, the resulting solutions support a controllable number of lump waves and exhibit rich anomalous scattering behavior. Applied to the Kadomtsev--Petviashvili-I equation, second- and third-order lump solutions are systematically derived, and the degeneration of lump chains into higher-order lumps is transparently revealed in the long-wave limit. The method can generate degenerate solutions with up to \(M(M+1)/2\) lumps from an \(M\)-lump chain. Moreover, compared with the previously proposed improved long-wave limit method, the present approach is capable of producing higher-order lump solutions whose long-time asymptotic behavior is independent of the Yablonskii--Vorob'ev polynomials. Its extension to hybrid higher-order lump solutions with distinct spectral parameters is also discussed.

### [188] [Assembly Spaces: Formal Definitions and Fast Methods for Approximating Assembly Indices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15499)
*Gage Siebert,Redwan Chowdhury,Louie Slocombe,Sara Walker*

Main category: cs.FL

TL;DR: 本文提出了组装理论（Assembly Theory）的通用化形式体系，通过定义组装空间（assembly space）和组装指数（assembly index）的与底物无关的形式化定义，并引入统一路径层次框架（path hierarchy framework）与形式语法算法（formal grammar algorithms），以高效近似计算组装指数，从而将组装理论从分子生物标志物检测推广至化学、生物学和复杂性科学等更广泛的领域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有组装理论在分子生物标志物检测中已取得实验验证，但其理论基础——组装空间的形式化定义尚不统一，且组装指数的计算方法在不同底物（substrate）和文献中存在多种表述，缺乏通用性。研究动机在于：提供一个与底物无关的通用形式体系，标准化组装空间与组装指数的定义，并开发高效的近似计算方法，以降低该理论的进入门槛，吸引更多领域的研究者参与。

Method: 首先回顾组装理论在分子、矿物和大气等底物上的应用。然后提出与底物无关的组装空间与组装指数的通用形式化定义。发展统一路径层次框架以澄清文献中各种组装空间与组装路径表示之间的关系。最后展示如何改编形式语法算法来高效界定组装指数的计算范围，并阐明这类近似方法的用途。

Result: 给出了组装空间和组装指数的通用形式化定义；建立了统一路径层次框架；证明了形式语法算法可用于高效计算组装指数的近似边界；实验上验证了高组装指数与高拷贝数（copy number）的组合是生命（life）的非生物（abiotic）生成所无法产生的可靠信号。

Conclusion: 组装理论通过组装指数和拷贝数两个核心可观测量，提供了一种检测生命的计量学方法。本文的通用形式体系统一了理论基础并降低了计算门槛，有望推动该理论在化学、生物学和复杂性科学等跨学科研究中的更广泛应用。

Abstract: Assembly theory is an experimental and theoretical framework that introduces a metrological approach to detecting life, with potential applications across diverse substrates. Its two central observables are assembly index and copy number. The assembly index is the minimum number of joining operations required to construct an object from its elementary parts; for molecules, it can be measured using mass spectrometry, infrared spectroscopy, and NMR. Copy number is the abundance of a given distinguishable object within a sample. A key empirical result of the theory is that high assembly index combined with high copy number constitutes a signature that cannot arise abiotically, and this has been validated experimentally in application to molecular biosignatures. The foundational theoretical concept underlying these results is the assembly space, which encodes the causal possibilities determinable from observed objects, with the assembly index the shortest path to them given the physical constraints of a given substrate. Here, we provide a generalized formalism to describe assembly spaces and tools for assembly index approximations. We begin by reviewing the applications of assembly theory across molecules, minerals and atmospheres, and then introduce a general, substrate-independent formal definition of assembly spaces and assembly indices. We develop a unified path hierarchy framework to clarify relationships among the various representations of assembly spaces and assembly paths that appear in the literature on molecular assembly. Finally, we show how formal grammar algorithms can be adapted to efficiently bound assembly index calculations and provide clarification on the utility of such approximations, with the goal to increase the accessibility of tools to explore this emerging area for a broader group of researchers across chemistry, biology, and complexity science.

### [189] [Painleve XXXIV asymptotics for the defocusing mKdV equation with step-like initial data in transition regions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15747)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用与 mKdV 方程关联的 Riemann-Hilbert 问题（Riemann-Hilbert problem），结合非线性最速下降法（nonlinear steepest descent method）推导解的长时渐近展开。

Result: 在展开中，主项（leading term）与对应的背景常数（background constants）匹配；次项（subleading term）以 $\mathcal{O}(t^{-2/3})$ 阶衰减，其系数由关联的 Painlevé XXXIV 模型（Painlevé XXXIV model）导出。

Abstract: In this paper, we consider the Cauchy problem for the defocusing modified Korteweg-de Vries (mKdV) equation with a step-like initial data. Based on the Riemann-Hilbert problem associated with the mKdV equation, we derive the long-time asymptotic expansion of the solution to the defocusing mKdV equation in two transition regions using the nonlinear steepest descent method. It comes out that the leading term in the expansion is shown to match the corresponding background constants. The subleading term, however, decays at the order $\mathcal{O}(t^{-2/3})$, and its coefficient is derived from the associated Painlevé \uppercase\expandafter{\romannumeral34\relax} model.

### [190] [Asymptotic stability of Bernstein-Greene-Kruskal (BGK) waves, Landau Damping, and scattering theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16194)
*Ricardo Weder*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文针对围绕BGK波线性化的两物种（电子与正离子）Vlasov-Poisson系统，通过将其转化为具有自伴哈密顿量（Hamiltonian）的Schrödinger型Vlasov-Ampère系统，建立了完整的定态散射理论（stationary scattering theory），证明了BGK波的渐近稳定性（asymptotic stability）以及朗道阻尼（Landau damping）的成立。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究对单物种Vlasov-Poisson系统中BGK波的稳定性已有一定认识，但对包含电子与正离子两种带电物种的系统的稳定性及其长时间行为尚缺乏严格的数学分析。本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 本文将两物种Vlasov-Poisson系统线性化为Vlasov-Ampère系统，并在适当的Hilbert空间中将该系统重写为Schrödinger型形式，其中Vlasov-Ampère算子作为自伴哈密顿量。在此基础上，发展完整的定态散射理论：识别算子的绝对连续谱（absolutely continuous spectrum）与奇异谱（singular spectrum），构造广义傅里叶映射（generalized Fourier maps），证明波算子（wave operators）的存在性与完备性及Birman不变性原理（Birman's invariance principle）。

Result: 证明了BGK波渐近稳定；得到了Vlasov-Ampère系统解的长时间行为的精确描述：电子和离子的相空间密度（phase-space densities）渐近趋向于无扰Vlasov-Ampère系统解的相空间密度，即它们沿BGK波势场中Newton方程解的轨迹输运；证明了朗道阻尼成立，即电场在逐点意义上随时间趋于零。

Conclusion: 本文为两物种Vlasov-Poisson系统围绕BGK波的线性稳定性提供了完备的散射理论框架，严格建立了BGK波的渐近稳定性与朗道阻尼，丰富了对等离子体中带电粒子长时间行为的理论理解。

Abstract: We consider the two species (electrons and positive charged ions) Vlasov-Poisson system linearized around BGK waves. We formulate the problem as an equivalent Vlasov-Ampère system, that we write as a system of Schrödinger type in an appropriate Hilbert space, and with a selfadjoint Vlasov-Ampère operator as a Hamiltonian. We develop a complete stationary scattering theory. We identify the absolutely continuous spectrum and the singular spectrum of the Vlasov-Ampère operator, we construct the generalized Fourier maps, we prove that the wave operators exist, are complete, satisfy Birman's invariance principle, and that the stationary formulae hold. Using these results we prove that the BGK waves are asymptotically stable. We obtain a precise description of the large time behaviour of the solutions to the Vlasov-Ampère system Namely,for large times the phase-space densities of electrons and ions are asymptotic to the phase-space densities of solutions of the unperturbed Vlasov-Ampère system. This implies that they follow the trajectories of solutions to Newton's equations for electrons and ions with the potential of the BGK wave, in the sense that they are transported along these trajectories. Furthermore, we prove that Landau damping holds, that is to say, the electric field tends to zero in pointwise sense for large times.

### [191] [Edge modes generated by intersection between 3 energy bands](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16419)
*Clotilde Fermanian Kammerer,Nicolas Frantz*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文研究了三个耦合方程的二维模型问题，探讨了狄拉克型哈密顿量中三个本征值沿曲线对称相交时的边缘模（edge modes）存在性。这些边缘模是半经典关联演化问题的解，渐近于零能量的相干态，并通过在交叉集内部传播而非沿经典轨迹传播，打破了对应原理（correspondence principle）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究在具有质量函数（mass function）沿曲线消失的狄拉克型哈密顿量中，三个本征值对称相交情形下边缘模的存在性及其违反对应原理的传播行为。

Method: 针对三个耦合方程的二维模型问题，假设哈密顿量（Hamiltonian）具有狄拉克型本征值对称相交结构，质量函数沿一条曲线为零；通过分析半经典关联演化问题（semiclassical associated evolution problem）的解，研究零能量相干态（coherent state with zero energy）的渐近行为。

Result: 发现了边缘模的存在，这类解渐近于零能量的相干态，并在交叉集（crossing set）内部传播，而非沿经典轨迹运动，从而破坏了对应原理。

Conclusion: 在三个耦合方程的二维模型中，狄拉克型本征值沿曲线对称相交时存在边缘模，其非经典传播特性表明对应原理在此类系统中失效。

Abstract: In this contribution, we investigate 2-dimensional model problems of three coupled equations. We assume that the underlying Hamiltonian presents a symmetric intersection between three eigenvalues of Dirac's type with a mass function that vanish along a curve. We investigate the existence of edge modes for these models: such functions are solutions of the semiclassical associated evolution problem that are asymptotic to a coherent state with zero energy and break the correspondence principle by propagating inside the crossing set and not along a classical trajectory.

</details>


### [192] [Complete Classification and Nondegeneracy of $N$-Component Cubic Nonlinear Schrödinger System in ${\mathbb R}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16544)
*Yujin Guo,Yong Luo,Juncheng Wei*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文针对任意 N≥2 的一维三次非线性薛定谔系统（cubic nonlinear Schrödinger system），证明了所有非平凡解的完全分类、线性化算子的非退化性以及精确的 L²-质量恒等式（L²-mass identity），从而解决了 Frank–Gontier–Lewin (2021) 和 Guo–Luo–Wei (2026) 针对 N=2 和 N=3 情形提出的猜想。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前的工作仅针对 N=2 和 N=3 的特殊情形研究了该非线性薛定谔系统（nonlinear Schrödinger system），本文旨在将结论推广到任意正整数 N≥2 的一般情形，并解决相关文献中提出的猜想。

Method: 采用泛函分析（functional analysis）与常微分方程（ordinary differential equations）方法，对一维三次非线性薛定谔系统进行严格的理论推导，通过分析系统的对称性与谱性质来证明分类、非退化性和质量恒等式。

Result: (i) 对所有 N≥2，系统的所有非平凡解可被完全分类；(ii) 任意非平凡解对应的线性化算子（linearized operator）是非退化的（non-degenerate）；(iii) 对所有分量 u_i，导出了以 2√|μ_i| 表示的精确 L²-质量恒等式，从而完整刻画了满足 ∫u_i²dx=1 的归一化解（normalized solutions）。

Conclusion: 本文的研究成果将 Frank–Gontier–Lewin (2021) 和 Guo–Luo–Wei (2026) 针对 N=2 和 N=3 的结论完整推广到了任意 N≥2 的一般情形，为更广泛的高维或高阶非线性薛定谔系统研究提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We study the one-dimensional cubic nonlinear Schrödinger system \[ u_i''+2\left(\sum_{k=1}^N u_k^2\right)u_i=-μ_i u_i \quad \mbox{in } \ \mathbb R,\ \ i=1,2,\cdots,N, \] where $u=(u_1,\cdots,u_N)\in \big(H^1(\mathbb{R})\big)^N$, $μ_1\leqμ_2\leq\cdots\leqμ_N<0$, and $N\geq 2$ is arbitrary. In this paper, we prove the following results for any $N\ge 2$: (i). All nontrivial solutions of the system can be completely classified; (ii). The linearized operator at any nontrivial solution of the system is non-degenerate; (iii). For all $i=1, 2,\cdots, N$, the exact $L^2$-mass identity of $u_i$ is derived in terms of $2\sqrt {|μ_i|}$, which yields a complete characterization of normalized solutions satisfying $\int_{\mathbb{R}}u_i^2dx=1$. These settle some conjectures of [R. Frank, D. Gontier and M. Lewin, CMP, 2021] and [Y. Guo, Y. Luo and J. Wei, APDE, 2026], where the system was addressed specially for $N=2$ and $N=3$, respectively.

Motivation: 已有文献中，该系统的局部强解存在性仅能在初始数据足够小的假设下获得，本文旨在取消这一小性限制，在更一般的$L^2$框架下证明局部适定性，从而拓展系统的可解性范围。

Method: 采用能量方法（energy method），揭示非线性项中存在的抵消现象（cancellation phenomena），从而克服非线性耦合带来的困难；再利用压缩论证（contraction argument）证明解的存在性和唯一性。

Result: 在$\mathbb R^N$和$\mathbb R^N_+$（$N=2,3$）中，建立了系统的局部适定性（local well-posedness），无需对初始数据施加小性条件；三维情形下对小初始数据还得到了全局适定性（global well-posedness）。

Conclusion: 能量方法揭示的非线性项抵消现象是突破小性假设的关键，该方法为后续研究更复杂液晶模型或类似耦合系统提供了可行的分析框架。

Abstract: The paper studies the Q-tensor model for nematic liquid crystals, a system that couples a Navier-Stokes equation with an evolution equation for the order parameter tensor Q. The first goal of the paper is to establish the local well-posedness of the system in $\mathbb R^N$ and $\mathbb R^N_+$ for $N=2,3$ in the $L^2$ framework, improving existing results in the literature, where the existence of local strong solutions was obtained only under smallness assumptions on the initial data. Fundamental is the application of the energy method, which shows a cancellation phenomena on the nonlinear terms, allowing the use of a contraction argument to prove existence and uniqueness of solutions. Finally, with the same approach we establish global well-posedness in the three-dimensional case for small initial data.

### [194] [Mathematical Analysis of Subwavelength Resonances and Gradient Blow-up for Two Close-to-Touching Inclusions within the Two-Dimensional Elasticity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17007)
*Hongjie Li,Longjuan Xu,Haolun Yang*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文对二维软基体中两个高对比硬夹杂物构成的二聚体（dimer）进行了严格分析，克服了二维弹性理论的低频频谱奇异性和静态单层势可能不可逆等困难，推导出六个亚波长共振频率及其对材料对比度δ和夹杂间距ε的依赖关系，并定量刻画了窄间隙区域共振场的奇异增强行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 亚波长弹性谐振器（subwavelength elastic resonators）可在远小于入射波长的尺度上集中波能，但当两个谐振器几乎接触时，其行为变得极为精细复杂。二维情形与三维理论存在本质差异：二维弹性基本解（fundamental solution）的对数型低频频谱奇异性（logarithmic low-frequency singularity）以及静态单层势（static single-layer potential）可能不可逆。因此，亟需建立严格的数学分析框架来理解这一系统中的共振机制。

Method: 通过证明正确的频率相关主部算子（frequency-dependent leading-order operator）的可逆性，将共振问题约化到一个有限维系统。利用这一约化框架，对满足自然对称性假设的一般凸谐振器进行分析，推导共振频率并量化窄间隙区域的场集中效应。

Result: 推导出六个亚波长共振频率（subwavelength resonant frequencies），并明确了它们对材料对比度δ和夹杂间距ε的依赖关系。在ε = O(δ^β), 0<β<2的范围内，本征模（eigenmodes）的梯度展现出显著分类的爆破行为：部分模在间隙最近点处达到O(1/ε)的更强增长率，另一些在远离中心线处以O(1/√ε)的速率爆破，剩余一个模则受边界失配机制（boundary mismatch mechanism）控制。

Conclusion: 这些结果揭示了共振诱导的奇异性（resonance-induced singularities）比静态或非共振弹性力学中的情形明显更强且更具结构性，为分析更大规模紧密排列的弹性亚波长谐振器簇提供了理论框架。

Abstract: Subwavelength elastic resonators can concentrate wave energy at length scales far below the incident wavelength, but their behavior becomes especially delicate when two resonators almost touch. In this paper, we give a rigorous analysis of a two-dimensional dimer made of two high-contrast hard inclusions embedded in a soft elastic matrix. The analysis confronts two features that are absent from the corresponding three-dimensional theory: the logarithmic low-frequency singularity of the two-dimensional elastic fundamental solution and the possible non-invertibility of the static single-layer potential. We overcome these difficulties by proving the invertibility of the correct frequency-dependent leading-order operator and then using it to reduce the resonance problem to a finite-dimensional system. For generally convex resonators satisfying natural symmetry assumptions, we derive six subwavelength resonant frequencies and identify their dependence on the material contrast $δ$ and the inter-inclusion distance $\varepsilon$. We further quantify the resonant field concentration in the narrow gap. In the regime $\varepsilon=\Ocal(δ^β)$, $0<β<2$, the gradients of the eigenmodes display sharply classified blow-up behavior: some modes attain the stronger rate $\Ocal(1/\varepsilon)$ at the closest point of the gap, while others blow up at the rate $\Ocal(1/\sqrt{\varepsilon})$ away from the centerline; the remaining mode is governed by a boundary mismatch mechanism. These results uncover resonance-induced singularities that are markedly stronger and more structured than those in static or non-resonant elasticity, and they provide a framework for analyzing larger clusters of closely spaced elastic subwavelength resonators.

### [195] [RepNet: Tackling spectral bias in deep neural networks via parameter reparameterization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16575)
*Yong Wang,Tao Zhou,Xuhui Meng*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出RepNet，一种通过重参数化（reparameterization）第一隐藏层的权重和偏置来克服深度神经网络（DNN）在高频与多尺度问题中的谱偏差（spectral bias）的方法。数值实验表明，RepNet在函数逼近、正反问题求解及算子学习等任务中，以轻微额外计算成本显著提升了预测精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深度神经网络（deep neural networks, DNNs）在科学计算中取得了显著成功，但在捕捉振荡行为和多尺度特征时经常遭受谱偏差（spectral bias）的限制。本文旨在理解并克服这一局限性。

Method: 首先通过分析浅层ReLU网络在高频函数拟合中的失败，识别出两个关键因素：初始斜率尺度（initial slope scale）和网络诱导的分割点分布（distribution of partition points）。基于此，提出RepNet，对第一隐藏层的权重和偏置进行重参数化（reparameterization），从而有效控制初始斜率尺度并提供合适的分割点分布；将重参数化后的参数视为可训练变量，使网络在训练中实现自适应频率缩放（adaptive frequency scaling）。此外，推导了重参数化后网络的输出和斜率幅度的定量估计以指导初始化。

Result: 在多尺度一维和四维函数逼近、结合物理信息神经网络（physics-informed neural networks, PINNs）的正反偏微分方程问题以及算子学习等数值实验中，RepNet以轻微额外计算成本，显著提升了原始DNN在捕获高度振荡特征方面的预测精度。

Conclusion: RepNet提供了一种有效且灵活的方法来克服谱偏差，从而将DNN应用于多尺度问题。

Abstract: Deep neural networks (DNNs) have achieved remarkable success in scientific computing, yet they often suffer from spectral bias in capturing oscillatory and multiscale behaviors. In this study, we investigate this limitation by examining the failure of shallow ReLU neural networks in fitting high-frequency functions. This observation identifies two important factors in resolving rapid oscillations: the initial slope scale and the distribution of partition points induced by the networks. Motivated by this analysis, we propose RepNet, a reparameterized DNN model for ReLU and tanh networks designed for high-frequency and multiscale problems. The key idea is to reparameterize the weights and biases in the first hidden layer, which enables effective control of the initial slope scale and provides an appropriate distribution of the initial partition points. Furthermore, treating the reparameterized weights and biases as trainable parameters allows the DNN to achieve adaptive frequency scaling during training. In addition, we derive quantitative estimates for the output and slope magnitudes of the reparameterized DNN to guide the initialization of the proposed method. Numerical experiments, including multiscale one- and four-dimensional function approximation, forward and inverse PDE problems in combination with physics-informed neural networks (PINNs), and operator learning, demonstrate that RepNet improves the predicted accuracy of vanilla DNNs in capturing highly oscillatory features with slightly additional computational cost. These results indicate that RepNet provides an effective and flexible approach for overcoming spectral bias and applying DNNs to multiscale problems.

</details>

### [197] [The limits of lattice inflation: a cautionary tale](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14853)
*Will Barker,Benjamin Gladwyn,Sebastian Zell*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了宇宙学晶格模拟中忽略度规扰动（metric perturbations）会导致超视界模式（superhorizon modes）无法冻结，从而显著扭曲暴胀（inflation）可观测量的预测；相比之下，再加热（reheating）研究对该近似较不敏感。研究提出了一项基于一阶度规扰动的实用性判据，并在CosmoLattice代码中实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前广泛使用的宇宙学晶格模拟代码近似处理引力背景，采用精确的弗里德曼-勒梅特-罗伯逊-沃尔克（FLRW）时空，忽略了度规扰动。本研究旨在评估这一近似对暴胀与再加热过程模拟的影响，并为该近似的适用范围提供量化判据。

Method: 通过理论分析对比包含与忽略一阶度规扰动的宇宙学晶格模拟，定量考察暴胀期间（包括慢滚（slow roll）与超慢滚（ultra-slow roll）阶段）曲率功率谱（curvature power spectrum）的演化行为，并评估其对再加热过程的影响。提出一项基于一阶度规扰动的有效性判据，并在CosmoLattice代码中实现该判据。

Result: 在暴胀期间，忽略度规扰动会阻止超视界模式的冻结。慢滚阶段曲率功率谱按$H^4$衰减，超慢滚阶段偏差更为显著，从而严重扭曲暴胀可观测量的预测。相比之下，再加热模拟对度规扰动的缺失敏感度较低。

Conclusion: FLRW近似在暴胀模拟中存在严重缺陷，可能导致对观测量的错误预测；而再加热研究对该近似容忍度较高。所提出的有效性判据为未来宇宙学晶格模拟提供了实践指导，有助于提高模拟的可靠性。

Abstract: Cosmological lattice simulations have become important tools for studying non-perturbative dynamics in the early Universe. Many widely used codes, however, approximate the gravitational background by an exact Friedmann-Lemaître-Robertson-Walker (FLRW) spacetime and neglect metric perturbations. We show that, during inflation, this approximation prevents the freezing of superhorizon modes. During slow roll, the curvature power spectrum decays as $H^4$, while the deviation becomes substantially stronger during ultra-slow roll. As a result, inflationary observables can be significantly distorted. In contrast, reheating studies appear to be considerably less sensitive to the omission of metric perturbations. We propose a practical criterion for assessing the validity of FLRW simulations based on the inclusion of first-order metric perturbations, and implement it in CosmoLattice.

</details>


### [198] [Multi-band cross-correlation dark sirens: Enhancing cosmological parameter and gravitational-wave bias constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15844)
*Ji-Yu Song,Ya-Nan Du,Yue-Yan Dong,Jing-Fei Zhang,Xin Zhang*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文首次利用Fisher矩阵预报方法，评估多频段引力波观测（结合空间与地面探测器）在交叉关联暗汽笛宇宙学中的优势。研究表明，多频段配置（BDET2CE）在$Λ$CDM模型下对哈勃常数$h$的测量精度达0.35%，相比纯地面配置提升37%；而其最显著优势在于对引力波成团偏袒因子$b_{\rm GW}(z)$的红移分辨测量，在$z \sim 1-2$处精度达$\sim 3\%$，远超单一频段配置。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多频段引力波观测可大幅提升双致密星源（compact binary sources）的定位精度（sky localization），这对交叉关联暗汽笛（cross-correlation dark siren）分析至关重要——定位不确定度直接决定引力波角功率谱（angular power spectrum）的噪声水平。然而，此前尚无研究对多频段引力波在交叉关联暗汽笛宇宙学中的优势进行定量预测。

Method: 采用Fisher矩阵预报（Fisher forecast）方法，将多频段引力波事件（来自Einstein Telescope、Cosmic Explorer、B-DECIGO）与中国空间站巡天望远镜（Chinese Space-station Survey Telescope）的光度红移星系巡天进行交叉关联。比较三种网络配置：多频段BDET2CE、仅地面ET2CE、以及单B-DECIGO。

Result: 在$Λ$CDM模型中，BDET2CE对$h$的测量精度为$0.35\%$，相较ET2CE（$0.55\%$）提升$37\%$，相较B-DECIGO（$2.45\%$）提升$86\%$；在$w_0w_a$CDM框架中多频段优势更温和。最突出优势在于引力波成团偏袒因子$b_{\rm GW}(z)$的分波段测量：在$z \sim 1-2$时，BDET2CE精度达$\sim 3\%$，而ET2CE为$\sim 8-60\%$，B-DECIGO为$\sim 20-33\%$。

Conclusion: 多频段引力波观测在交叉关联暗汽笛宇宙学中具有显著优势，尤其在高红移处对引力波成团偏袒因子（GW clustering bias）$b_{\rm GW}(z)$的精确、红分辨测量，为探索双致密星并合的天体物理过程（如孤立双星演化isolated binary evolution与动力学组装dynamical assembly）提供了新途径。

Abstract: Multi-band gravitational-wave (GW) observation, combining space-borne and ground-based detectors across different frequency bands, can improve the sky localization of compact binary sources by two to three orders of magnitude compared to single-band detection. This enhancement is crucial for cross-correlation dark siren analyses, since the sky localization uncertainty directly determines the noise level of the GW angular power spectrum. In this work, we present the first Fisher forecast for cross-correlation dark siren cosmology with multi-band GW observations, cross-correlating GW events from the Einstein Telescope (ET), Cosmic Explorer (CE), and B-DECIGO with the Chinese Space-station Survey Telescope photometric galaxy survey. We compare three network configurations: the multi-band B-DECIGO+ET+2CE (BDET2CE), the ground-only ET+2CE (ET2CE), and B-DECIGO alone. In the $Λ$CDM model, BDET2CE achieves $σ(h)/h = 0.35\%$, improving by $37\%$ over the ground-only ET2CE ($0.55\%$) and by $86\%$ over B-DECIGO alone ($2.45\%$). Extending to the $w_0w_a$CDM framework, the multi-band advantage on cosmological parameters becomes more moderate, with BDET2CE improving $σ(h)/h$ by $\sim 4\%$ over ET2CE and $\sim 22\%$ over B-DECIGO. The most striking advantage of multi-band observation lies in the per-bin measurement of the GW clustering bias $b_{\rm GW}(z)$: at $z \sim 1-2$, BDET2CE constrains the bias to $\sim 3\%$ precision, compared to $\sim 8-60\%$ for ET2CE and $\sim 20-33\%$ for B-DECIGO. These precise, redshift-resolved bias measurements open a new avenue for probing the astrophysics of compact binary mergers, enabling constraints on formation channels such as isolated binary evolution and dynamical assembly that predict distinct clustering signatures.

### [199] [Nonlinear Dynamical Regimes of Cosmological Frequency Combs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16227)
*Madhurendra Mishra,Oem Trivedi,Adarsh Ganesan*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文采用动力学系统（dynamical systems）方法，在指数势的quintessence宇宙学中论证了宇宙学频率梳（Cosmological Frequency Combs, CFCs）的自发产生机制：膨胀归一化变量下的自治非线性系统可支持极限环（limit cycles）吸引子，从而在无外部周期驱动的情况下生成梳状谱结构；数值模拟揭示了单频、梳状与混沌（chaotic）三种动力学 regime 之间的转变条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究宇宙学频率梳（CFCs）是否能够作为非线性宇宙动力学的内在涌现现象而自发产生，而非需要外部周期驱动力。

Method: 采用动力学系统（dynamical systems）形式，将指数势quintessence宇宙学的演化方程改写为膨胀归一化变量（expansion-normalized variables），得到一个自治非线性系统，并通过数值模拟分析其吸引子与频谱特征。

Result: 该系统存在时间周期吸引子（极限环），产生梳状谱结构；数值模拟显示系统可在单频、梳状与混沌（chaotic） regime之间转换，转变由基频、背景状态方程参数（equation of state parameter）及初始条件控制；相干梳状结构仅出现在特定动力学窗口内，极低频率与不利初始条件会抑制锁相（phase locking）。

Conclusion: 宇宙学频率梳（CFCs）可自然地源于非线性宇宙动力学，无需外部周期驱动；该发现为探索CFCs的潜在可观测效应提供了理论依据与进一步研究的动机。

Abstract: We study the emergence of Cosmological Frequency Combs (CFCs) in a quintessence cosmology with an exponential potential using a dynamical systems formulation. Expressing the evolution equations in expansion-normalized variables yields an autonomous nonlinear system that supports time-periodic attractors corresponding to limit cycles, producing comb like spectral structures in cosmological observables without external periodic forcing. Numerical simulations reveal transitions between single frequency, comb like and chaotic regimes controlled by the fundamental frequency, background equation of state parameter, and initial conditions. Coherent comb structures arise only within well defined dynamical windows, while very low frequencies and unfavorable initial conditions suppress phase locking. These results show that CFCs naturally emerge from nonlinear cosmological dynamics and motivate further study of their possible observational implications.

</details>


### [200] [Benchmarking Exact, GP-Emulated, and Simulation-Based Inference for Late-Time Cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16248)
*Sai Swagat Mishra*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文系统比较了三种宇宙学推断策略——精确MCMC、高斯过程辅助MCMC和神经模拟推断（SBI），针对晚期ΛCDM宇宙学，利用宇宙计时器、DESI DR2重子声波振荡和Pantheon+超新星数据，检验了它们在统计可靠性与计算可扩展性上的表现。结果表明，加速推断技术能以远低于传统似然方法的计算成本提供可靠的宇宙学约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 即将开展的宇宙学巡天需要统计可靠且计算可扩展的推断管线，但不同加速推断方法在高维参数空间中的系统性能比较尚不充分，因此有必要对三种代表性策略进行统一框架下的定量评估。

Method: 采用基于宇宙计时器（Cosmic Chronometers）、DESI DR2重子声波振荡（baryon acoustic oscillation）测量和Pantheon+ Ia型超新星（Type Ia supernova）汇编数据的共同分析框架，在相同宇宙学假设与先验下，设置两组复杂度递增的数据组合（CC+DESI和CC+DESI+PP），系统比较精确马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（MCMC）、高斯过程（Gaussian Process, GP）辅助MCMC和神经模拟推断（Simulation-Based Inference, SBI）三种策略。

Result: 对于CC+DESI组合，GP仿真和SBI均能以优于0.3σ的精度复现(H₀, Ωₘ,₀)的精确后验约束；对于更具约束力的CC+DESI+PP组合，方法间出现最大约1.5σ的微小偏移。所有方法均恢复出几乎相同的膨胀历史（expansion history），在全红移范围内达到百分位一致性。计算上，GP仿真加速了模型评估但受限于MCMC采样，而SBI通过摊销后验学习（amortized posterior learning）实现总运行时间的量级缩减。

Conclusion: 加速推断技术能够以远低于传统似然分析的计算成本，为现实晚期宇宙学数据集提供可靠的约束。研究还确定了SBI达到稳定后验约束所需的最低模拟次数。

Abstract: Forthcoming cosmological surveys require inference pipelines that are both statistically reliable and computationally scalable. In this work, we perform a systematic comparison of three complementary inference strategies for late-time $Λ$CDM cosmology: exact Markov Chain Monte Carlo (MCMC), Gaussian Process (GP)-assisted MCMC, and neural Simulation-Based Inference (SBI). Using a common analysis framework based on Cosmic Chronometers, DESI DR2 baryon acoustic oscillation measurements, and the Pantheon+ Type Ia supernova compilation, we consider two dataset combinations of increasing complexity, namely CC+DESI and CC+DESI+PP, under identical cosmological assumptions and priors. For CC+DESI, both GP emulation and SBI reproduce the exact posterior constraints on $(H_0,Ω_{m,0})$ to better than $0.3σ$. For the more constraining CC+DESI+PP combination, modest method-dependent shifts emerge, reaching at most $\sim1.5σ$ in a single parameter. Despite these differences, all methods recover a nearly identical expansion history, with percent-level agreement across the full redshift range. From a computational perspective, GP emulation accelerates model evaluations but remains limited by MCMC sampling, whereas SBI achieves order-of-magnitude reductions in total runtime through amortized posterior learning. We further investigate the convergence of SBI as a function of simulation budget and identify the number of simulations required to obtain stable posterior constraints. Overall, our results demonstrate that accelerated inference techniques can deliver reliable cosmological constraints for realistic late-time datasets at a fraction of the computational cost of conventional likelihood-based analyses.

</details>


### [201] [Interactions in the dark sector: intrinsic entropy couplings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16574)
*Elsa M. Teixeira*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一类新的相互作用暗扇区（interacting dark sector）模型，在该模型中，暗物质流体（dark matter fluid）的内禀熵（intrinsic entropy）耦合到描述暗能量（dark energy）的标量场（scalar field）。该模型通过协变拉格朗日框架（covariant Lagrangian framework）构造，包含代数和导数熵耦合，在暗扇区内产生纯动量交换（pure momentum exchange）。背景宇宙学与ΛCDM或未耦合的quintessence模型不可区分，但在线性扰动（linear perturbations）层面，暗物质欧拉方程（Euler equation）出现尺度依赖（scale-dependent）贡献，连续性方程不变。模型与当前宇宙微波背景辐射（CMB）约束兼容，并可能在大尺度结构（large-scale structure）中产生可观测信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有相互作用暗扇区模型通常同时修改背景演化与扰动结构，限制了模型与观测的兼容性并增加了参数简并。本研究旨在构建一类新的相互作用模型，在保持背景宇宙学严格等同于ΛCDM的同时，仅在扰动层面引入暗物质与暗能量之间的纯动量交换，从而产生独特的可观测特征。

Method: 在协变拉格朗日框架下构造暗物质内禀熵与暗能量标量场之间的耦合，引入代数熵耦合（algebraic entropy coupling）和导数熵耦合（derivative entropy coupling）两种形式。该构造确保相互作用仅产生纯动量交换，而不引入能量交换，从而保持背景演化不变。模型在线性扰动理论框架下进行分析，推导修改后的暗物质欧拉方程，并与当前CMB观测数据进行兼容性检验。

Result: 模型在背景宇宙学层面与ΛCDM或未耦合quintessence模型完全不可区分。在线性扰动层面，暗物质的连续性方程保持不变，但欧拉方程出现尺度依赖的修改项。该模型与当前CMB观测约束兼容，并可能在大尺度结构观测中产生可探测的签名信号。

Conclusion: 所提出的熵耦合暗扇区模型为探索暗物质与暗能量相互作用提供了一条新路径，其独特之处在于纯动量交换与背景不变的组合。这类模型为当前的观测约束所允许，并有望通过未来大尺度结构巡天等观测手段在扰动层面检验其尺度依赖的特征，从而区分于标准的ΛCDM宇宙学。

Abstract: We present a new class of interacting dark sector models in which the intrinsic entropy of a dark matter fluid couples to a scalar field describing dark energy. These interactions are constructed within a covariant Lagrangian framework, including algebraic and derivative entropy couplings, effectively leading to pure momentum exchange in the dark sector. A key feature is that the background cosmology remains unchanged and therefore indistinguishable from $Λ$CDM or uncoupled quintessence. However, at the level of the linear perturbations, the dark matter Euler equation exhibits scale-dependent contributions, while the continuity equation is unmodified. We show that these classes of models are compatible with current CMB constraints and can potentially produce observable signatures in large-scale structure.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用ACT DR6最新数据给出的标量谱指数（scalar spectral index）n_s ≈ 0.9743，重新计算Lyth bound对张量-标量比（tensor-to-scalar ratio）r的上限约束，并与原始n_s=1假设下的界限进行对比。

Result: 纳入ACT数据后，对张量-标量比r的上限约束与原始n_s=1下的Lyth bound不同，且更为严格。这一新界限可能排除一些原本在原始Lyth bound下仍然成立的暴胀（inflationary）模型。

Conclusion: 研究结果强调了将理论上的Lyth bound考量与最新的天体物理数据相结合的必要性。

Abstract: The Lyth bound asserts that the field excursion of inflaton must be sub-Planckian, thereby imposing an upper bound on the amplitude of the tensor power spectrum in inflationary scenario. This bound is conventionally derived assuming a scale-invariant curvature power spectrum, i.e., $n_s = 1$. However, astrophysical observations confirm a red-tilted spectrum with $n_s < 1$. In light of recent results from the Atacama Cosmology Telescope (ACT) DR6, we revisit these constraints using the newly implied scalar spectral index of $n_s \simeq 0.9743$. Incorporating the ACT data yields a different upper bound on the tensor-to-scalar ratio $r$, which can potentially exclude inflationary scenarios previously robust under the original Lyth bound with $n_s = 1$. Our result highlights the urgent need to combine theoretical Lyth bound considerations with the most up-to-date astrophysical data.

*Dimitrios Tsimpis,Govind Venugopal*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过解析推导获得标量和张量原初功率谱的模板（analytic templates），并以此框架重新审视曲率辅助的单指数模型（curvature-assisted single-exponential models）。

Result: 在开放宇宙（open universe）情形下，曲率辅助单指数模型的相空间自然包含了从运动主导阶段过渡到参数控制的准德西特（quasi-de Sitter）阶段的宇宙学路径。然而，这些模型不适用于所推导的解析模板，因为其第二个哈勃慢滚参数（second Hubble slow-roll parameter）在准德西特区域保持量级为一（order one）。

Conclusion: 所推导的模板虽能解析恢复标量和张量谱倾斜，但曲率辅助单指数模型因慢滚条件不充分而无法纳入该模板框架，提示此类模型需要更一般的处理方式。

Abstract: We derive analytic templates for the scalar and tensor primordial power spectra describing cosmologies that transition from kinetic dominance to slow-roll inflation in the presence of spatial curvature. Our results extend recent works in the literature, allowing us, in particular, to recover the scalar and tensor tilts analytically. We revisit the case of curvature-assisted single-exponential models in light of this framework. In the case of an open universe, the phase space of such models naturally includes cosmologies that start out in a kinetic-dominance regime followed by a parametrically controlled quasi-de Sitter phase. However, they do not fit in the framework of the templates, as their second Hubble slow-roll parameter remains of order one in the quasi-de Sitter regime.

### [204] [Spectral dimension determines criticality in nonreciprocal phase oscillators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16427)
*Minwoo Bae,Hiroshi Kori*

Main category: nlin.AO

TL;DR: 本文研究了非互易系统中谱维度对临界现象的决定性作用，通过数值相图与动力学重整化群分析，发现当谱维度 d_s 大于临界值 d_s^c=2 时，存在一个随 d_s 单调递增的临界相位滞后 α_c，在该滞后以下系统会出现自发同步。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 谱维度（spectral dimension）是临界现象的关键决定因素，但它在非互易系统（nonreciprocal systems）中的作用此前尚未被探索。

Method: 研究了带有噪声的相同库拉莫托-坂口振子（Kuramoto-Sakaguchi oscillators），其中相位滞后 α∈[0,π/2) 且 α>0 引入了非互易相互作用。在复杂网络（complex networks）的 (d_s, α) 平面上构建了数值相图，并采用动力学重整化群（dynamical renormalization group）方法解析推导了临界行为。

Result: 数值相图揭示了临界相位滞后 α_c 的存在，该临界值仅当谱维度大于临界谱维度 d_s^c=2 时出现，且 α_c 随 d_s 单调递增。

Conclusion: 非互易系统中的自发同步受谱维度调控，临界谱维度 d_s^c=2 是相变发生的分界点，动力学重整化群方法成功解析了该临界性。

Abstract: Spectral dimension is a key determinant of critical phenomena, but its role in nonreciprocal systems remains unexplored. We study noisy identical Kuramoto-Sakaguchi oscillators with phase lag $α\in [0,π/2)$, where $α>0$ induces nonreciprocal interactions. Numerical phase diagrams in the $(d_s,α)$ plane in complex networks, where $d_s$ denotes the spectral dimension, reveal a critical phase lag $α_c$, below which spontaneous synchronization occurs. This critical phase lag appears only for $d_s > d_s^c$, where $d_s^c = 2$ is the critical spectral dimension, and increases monotonically with $d_s$. We analytically derive the criticality using the dynamical renormalization group method.

### [205] [Experimental realization of the complete seven-phase Anderson-localization landscape](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14825)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代局域化理论预测了一个包含扩展态、临界态和局域态及其共存相的完整输运层级结构（七相安德森局域化景观），但这一层级结构从未在单一系统中通过实验实现。

Method: 在一维弗洛凯（Floquet）光子晶格中工程化设计准周期跳跃（hopping）分布，引入非均匀分布的跳跃零点，从而产生临界态并使其与扩展态和局域态共存。

Result: 通过时空动力学（spatiotemporal dynamics）直接分辨不同输运区间的特征：弹道扩展（ballistic expansion）、受限临界振荡（confined critical oscillations）和持续局域化（persistent localization）。观测了全部七个输运相，包括最难实现的三重共存扩展-临界-局域相，并实验追踪了连接各相的相变过程。

Conclusion: 该实验建立了首个完整的安德森局域化景观实验图谱，为研究迁移率边（mobility edges）、多重分形性（multifractality）和可编程相干输运提供了统一平台。

Abstract: Anderson localization has evolved far beyond the conventional dichotomy between extended and localized states. Modern localization theory predicts a complete transport hierarchy comprising extended, critical, and localized phases together with all coexistence phases among them, forming a seven-phase Anderson-localization landscape. Despite its fundamental importance, this hierarchy has never been experimentally realized within a single system. Here we realize the complete seven-phase Anderson-localization landscape in a one-dimensional Floquet photonic lattice. By engineering quasiperiodic hopping profiles containing inhomogeneously distributed hopping zeros, we generate critical states and enable their coexistence with extended and localized sectors. The resulting transport regimes are directly resolved through their distinct spatiotemporal dynamics, including ballistic expansion, confined critical oscillations, and persistent localization. We observe all seven phases, including the elusive triply coexisting extended-critical-localized phase, and experimentally track the phase transitions connecting them. Our results establish the first complete experimental map of the Anderson-localization landscape and provide a unified platform for investigating mobility edges, multifractality, and programmable coherent transport.

### [206] [Identifying Mobility Edge from Finite Temperature Spectral Form Factor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15294)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在无序海森堡自旋1/2模型中，采用有限温度下的谱形因子（SFF）构造典范相图；基于统计力学（statistical mechanics）的简单思路，推导出与临界温度T_MBL对偶的临界能量密度ε_MBL；通过局部扰动的传播和光导率（optical conductivity）数值估计迁移率边（mobility edge, ME），并与ε_MBL进行比较。

Abstract: The spectral form factor (SFF) is a measure of energy correlations and has been widely used to identify the transition from the ergodic to the localized phase in interacting many-body quantum systems. In this work, we show that in a disordered Heisenberg spin-$\frac{1}{2}$ model, the finite temperature SFF can be used to generate a canonical phase diagram exhibiting a critical temperature $T_\mathrm{MBL}$. Using simple ideas of statistical mechanics, we obtain the critical energy density $ε_\mathrm{MBL}$ dual to $T_\mathrm{MBL}$. We show that the mobility edge (ME), numerically estimated from the spread of local perturbations and the optical conductivity, indeed coincides with $ε_\mathrm{MBL}$.

### [207] [Machine Learning Topological Order from Defect Partition Functions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15799)
*Kazem Bitaghsir Fadafan,Wei Cui,Babak Haghighat,Shailesh Lal*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种机器学习框架，通过从环面二维伊辛模型的缺陷配分函数中提取伊辛拓扑序（Ising topological order），利用受限玻尔兹曼机（RBM）学习临界点数据，并通过分量逐点平方根映射构造出(2+1)维伊辛拓扑量子场论（TQFT）的候选波函数，最终从态重叠中提取出模S矩阵（modular S-matrix）并与理论预期一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索如何从经典统计力学（statistical mechanics）的晶格模型数据中，通过神经网络表示自动提取出潜在的拓扑量子场论（TQFT）结构，从而建立从统计力学到拓扑序（topological order）的数据驱动桥梁。

Method: 采用受限玻尔兹曼机（Restricted Boltzmann Machine, RBM）在环面拓扑扇区（topological sectors）上对处于临界点的二维伊辛模型数据进行训练；对学习到的分布进行分量逐点平方根映射（component-wise square-root map），构造出(2+1)维伊辛TQFT的候选波函数；通过计算这些态的重叠来提取模S矩阵。

Result: 从神经网络学习到的波函数中成功提取出了模S矩阵，并得到了与理论预期的伊辛模数据（Ising modular data）一致的结果，验证了该方法的有效性。

Conclusion: 神经网络表示能够同时捕捉临界涨落（critical fluctuations）和涌现的拓扑结构（emergent topological structure），证明了从晶格统计力学数据驱动地走向拓扑量子场论的可行性。

Abstract: We introduce a machine learning framework for extracting Ising topological order from defect partition functions of the two-dimensional Ising model on a torus. Restricted Boltzmann Machines (RBMs) are trained on Ising model data sampled at criticality across topological sectors. We take a component-wise square-root map of the learned distributions which naturally produces candidate wavefunctions for the (2+1)-dimensional Ising TQFT. As a nontrivial consistency check, we extract the modular S-matrix from overlaps of the resulting states and recover the expected Ising modular data. Our results demonstrate that neural network representations can capture both critical fluctuations and emergent topological structure, providing a data-driven route from lattice statistical mechanics to topological quantum field theory.

</details>


### [208] [Generative modelling powered by room-temperature polariton condensates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15344)
*Yuan Wang,Marcin Muszynski,Avinash Dash,Rishabh Kaurav,Vinod M. Menon,Oleksandr Kyriienko*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文实验证明，在强光-物质耦合（strong light-matter coupling）状态下工作的非线性光学系统，可作为条件生成建模（conditional generative modelling）的物理变换层。具体而言，基于有机染料微腔中室温激子-极化激元凝聚体（exciton-polariton condensates）的随机非线性动力学，构建生成对抗网络（generative adversarial network, GAN）实现数字到图像的转换，其性能优于数字注入扰动的基线方法及激光系统，并展现出正则化对抗训练与增强输出多样性的能力。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生成建模（generative modelling）需要高效的随机非线性变换（stochastic nonlinear transformations）以及能够自然实现这些变换的物理平台。现有数字方法依赖人为注入噪声，缺乏物理系统固有的随机性与非线性动力学特性。

Method: 利用有机染料微腔中室温激子-极化激元凝聚体（exciton-polariton condensates）作为生成对抗网络（GAN）中的物理随机变换层（physical stochastic transform），利用极化激元凝聚体的非线性多体动力学（nonlinear many-body dynamics）与内在随机性（intrinsic stochasticity）实现条件数字到图像翻译（conditional digit-to-image translation）。

Result: 基于极化激元的生成对抗网络（Polariton GAN）在初始分数（inception score）、数字保留准确度（digit preservation accuracy）和结构相似性（structural similarity）方面均优于数字采样和激光系统。空间相关的输出变化（spatially correlated output variations）能够自然地正则化对抗训练（regularise adversarial training）并增强输出多样性。

Conclusion: 极化激元凝聚（polariton condensation）可作为一种新的计算资源用于生成建模，开辟了物理增强型机器学习系统（physics-enhanced machine learning systems）的发展路径。

Abstract: Generative modelling requires efficient stochastic nonlinear transformations and physical platforms that can naturally realise them. We experimentally demonstrate that nonlinear optical systems operating in the strong light-matter coupling regime can serve as physical transformation layers for conditional generative modelling. Specifically, we develop a workflow in which room-temperature exciton-polariton condensates formed in organic dye microcavities act as a physical stochastic transform within a generative adversarial network and enable conditional digit-to-image translation. By using the nonlinear many-body dynamics and intrinsic stochasticity of polariton condensates, the workflow outperforms baseline approaches based on digitally injected perturbations. We find that polariton-enabled sampling via generative adversarial network (Polariton GAN) yields improved inception score, digit preservation accuracy and structural similarity compared with both digital sampling and laser-based systems. We further show that spatially correlated output variations can naturally regularise adversarial training and enhance output diversity. Our results establish polariton condensation as a new computational resource for generative modelling, opening a pathway towards physics-enhanced machine learning systems.

### [209] [Cluster-based Message-Passing (CluMP) Optimization for Complex QUBO Problems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15414)
*Paolo Rissone,Stefan Boetcher,Alfonso Amendola,Simone Sala,Federico Ricci-Tersenghi*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文提出CluMP（Cluster-based Message-Passing）算法，利用置信传播（Belief Propagation, BP）的信息对自旋簇进行集体更新，通过控制簇内阻挫（frustration）程度使BP在大子图上收敛，从而在单次操作中实现数百个自旋的非局部重排。在多种图拓扑结构的自旋玻璃模型上，CluMP相比最先进的局部更新启发式方法，能持续绕过局部陷阱并以更少的有效操作达到更低能量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二次无约束布尔优化（QUBO）问题在工业和科学中广泛存在，其对应的伊辛（Ising）系统在包含冲突约束时会产生阻挫，形成复杂的能量景观（energy landscape），使得找到低能构型极为困难，尤其是局部更新启发式方法容易陷入亚稳态（metastable states）。

Method: CluMP算法基于置信传播（Belief Propagation）提供的信息，对连通的伊辛自旋簇（cluster）执行集体更新（collective update）；通过人为控制簇内的阻挫程度，确保BP在大规模子图上能够收敛，从而在一次操作中实现涉及数百个自旋的非局部重排（nonlocal rearrangements）。

Result: 在随机正则图（random regular graphs）以及二维、三维晶格正则图（lattice regular graphs）等多种图拓扑的自旋玻璃模型上，CluMP相比最先进的局部更新启发式方法，始终能绕过局部陷阱，以更少的有效操作达到更低的能量。结果表明，对阻挫具有容忍性的簇更新可以在稀疏图上高效实现。

Conclusion: CluMP框架为大规模组合优化与推断问题提供了一种可扩展的策略，其关键在于利用中程和长程相关性（medium- and long-range correlations）来导航复杂的能量景观。

Abstract: Quadratic Unconstrained Boolean Optimization (QUBO) problems are widespread in both industrial applications and scientific studies. A QUBO problem corresponds to the optimization of a system of Ising spins defined on a generally sparse and heterogeneous graph. When the QUBO problem contains conflicting requests, the corresponding Ising system is frustrated, generating a complex energy landscape, which is hard to explore and optimize. Despite extensive algorithmic and hardware developments, finding low-energy configurations in these systems remains challenging (e.g., local-update heuristics typically become trapped in metastable states), especially when the (possibly frustrated) interactions generate extended correlated domains.
  We introduce CluMP (Cluster-based Message-Passing), an algorithm that performs collective updates on connected clusters of spins using information from Belief Propagation (BP). By controlling the amount of frustration within clusters, CluMP enables BP convergence on large subgraphs and proposes nonlocal rearrangements involving up to hundreds of spins in a single move. We benchmark CluMP against state-of-the-art local-update heuristics on spin-glass models defined on several graph topologies, including random regular graphs and lattice regular graphs in two and three dimensions. Cluster moves consistently bypass local trapping and reach lower energies with fewer effective operations than single-spin dynamics. These results demonstrate that frustration-tolerant cluster updates can be implemented efficiently on sparse graphs. The CluMP framework provides a scalable strategy for large-scale combinatorial optimization and inference problems, where exploiting medium- and long-range correlations is key to navigating complex energy landscapes.

</details>


### [210] [The limits of interpretability in multiple linear regression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16013)
*Anand Sharma,Chen Liu,Daniele Coslovich,Misaki Ozawa*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文揭示了多重共线性（multicollinearity）导致线性回归（linear regression）权重产生大幅波动和振荡模式（oscillatory patterns）的机制，指出这源于特征相关矩阵（feature correlation matrix）的小特征值模式（small-eigenvalue modes）放大权重波动，并验证了Ridge正则化（Ridge regularization）可抑制但不完全消除该问题，从而解释了为何即使在简单线性模型中，物理可解释性（interpretability）仍可能受损。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在物理学研究中，人们不仅希望机器学习模型做出预测，更希望理解其背后的物理机制。线性回归因权重可显式表达为输入特征的加权和，通常被视为可解释的模型。然而，当输入特征高度相关（即存在多重共线性）时，学习到的权重会在不同数据集间大幅波动，并在物理相似特征上呈现振荡行为，使解释变得困难甚至不可能。尽管统计学家已知多重共线性下权重不稳定，但其对物理解释的具体影响——尤其是振荡权重与物理相似特征之间的联系——尚未得到系统阐明。

Method: 本文从理论上分析了特征相关矩阵的特征模式（eigenmodes），指出与多重共线性相关的小特征值模式会放大权重波动，并产生不反映有意义贡献的振荡模式。随后在物理数据集上进行了数值测试，验证了该理论图景，并检验了Ridge正则化对不稳定模式的抑制效果。进一步，通过分析一组多样化的公开非物理数据集，确认了该发现的普适性。

Result: 理论分析表明，多重共线性导致的小特征值模式是权重不稳定和振荡行为的根源。数值实验在物理数据集上证实了这一理论，Ridge正则化虽能抑制不稳定模式，但所得权重仍需谨慎解读。在非物理数据集上的额外测试进一步表明，该结论具有跨领域的一般性。

Conclusion: 即使在看似可解释的线性回归模型中，多重共线性仍可能严重损害物理解释的可靠性。这一发现提醒研究者，在解释线性模型的权重时，必须对特征相关性保持警惕，不可简单地将权重视为特征的独立贡献度量。

Abstract: Interpreting machine-learning models has attracted increasing attention, particularly in the physical sciences, where one often seeks to understand the underlying mechanisms rather than merely make predictions. Multiple linear regression is often regarded as an interpretable alternative to more complex models, such as deep neural networks, because its predictions are expressed as explicit weighted sums of input features. However, when input features are strongly correlated, namely in the presence of multicollinearity, the learned weights can exhibit large dataset-to-dataset fluctuations and oscillatory behavior across physically similar features, making their interpretation difficult or even impossible. Although the instability of the weights under multicollinearity is well known in statistics, its consequences for physical interpretation, in particular its connection to oscillatory weights across physically similar features, have not been systematically clarified. Here, we theoretically discuss the mechanism behind this loss of interpretability by analyzing the eigenmodes of the feature correlation matrix. We show that small-eigenvalue modes associated with multicollinearity amplify fluctuations in the weights and generate oscillatory patterns that do not necessarily reflect meaningful contributions. We test this theoretical picture numerically on physics datasets and show that Ridge regularization suppresses these unstable modes, although the resulting weights must still be interpreted with caution. We further confirm the generality of our findings beyond physics by analyzing a diverse collection of publicly available datasets. Our results clarify why, in the presence of multicollinearity, physical interpretation can remain difficult even for linear regression models.

</details>

Method: 开发了一种几何精确（geometrically exact）方法，该方法计算复杂度与系统体积呈线性关系（linearly in the system volume），用于识别连续空隙的形状和尺寸。

Result: 计算了柏拉图立体（Platonic solids）及截角二十面体（truncated icosahedra）形状内含物在有序和随机取向下的颗粒簇渗流与空隙渗流临界浓度。对于空隙渗流，结果精度显著优于先前基准。此外，在立方体内含物经历随机放置和取向的断裂面破碎后，空隙渗流的临界孔隙率趋向于5%。
