This critical density for void percolation can be difficult to calculate due to the irregular shape of the void regions. We develop and implement a geometrically exact method, scaling only linearly in the system volume, for identifying the shape and size of contiguous voids. In this manner, we calculate percolation thresholds for both grain cluster percolation (where system spanning networks of overlapping grains begin to appear with increasing density) and void percolation at much higher grain concentrations where networks of interstitial volumes no longer exist on macroscopic scales. For both the former and the latter, we calculate critical concentrations for inclusions in the shape of the Platonic solids (as well as truncated icosahedra) for both aligned and randomly oriented grains. In the case of critical densities for void percolation, the accuracy of our results is significantly improved relative to prior benchmarks. We also incorporate structural disorder of inclusions by considering impermeable grains in the form of cubes subject to a series of randomly placed and oriented fracture planes to mimic aggressively fractured inclusions found in nature. As the number of sustained slices becomes large, we find that the critical porosity for void percolation tends to 5%

*Masayuki Ohzeki*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Information criteria such as WAIC and WBIC extend model selection to singular learning machines, but they are usually derived for equilibrium posteriors. The resulting estimator gives a computable thermodynamic contribution to time-bounded MDL and identifies the finite-time singular complexity relevant to the structural information measured by epiplexity.

### [214] [Kinematic Inconsistencies and Initial-Value Boundary Paradoxes in Rate-Dependent Viscoelastic Yield Stress Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14751)
*Lalit Kumar*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该论文严格分析了一个用于统一屈服应力流体（yield-stress fluids）屈服前与屈服后动力学的速率相关松弛时间框架，发现其存在不可避免的边界悖论（boundary paradox），为避免数学奇异性需引入非物理的瞬时速度或应变率阶跃（instantaneous velocity/strain-rate step），该阶跃显式违反动量守恒（momentum conservation）与流体惯性（fluid inertia），最终导致该框架保留了经典黏塑性模型（viscoplastic models）的分段不连续缺陷。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分析一个近期提出的、旨在统一屈服应力流体屈服前与屈服后动力学的速率相关松弛时间框架（rate-dependent relaxation time framework），揭示其在数学边界与运动学一致性（kinematic consistency）方面的根本性问题。

Method: 通过在一个理想化的瞬态蠕变协议（transient creep protocol）下，从物理静止（physical rest）状态出发评估该框架的本构方程（governing constitutive equations），检验其在屈服阈值以下恒定应力（$σ\le σ_y$）条件下的数学行为。

Result: 该框架在屈服阈值以下会面临边界悖论：为避免预测完美刚性固体行为（perfectly rigid solid behavior）或遭遇除零数学奇异性（division-by-zero mathematical singularity），必须引入一个非物理的瞬时速度或应变率阶跃，该阶跃显式违反动量守恒与流体惯性。

Conclusion: 该速率相关松弛时间框架无法克服经典黏塑性模型的分段不连续（piecewise, discontinuous）缺陷，其在运动学一致性上存在根本性局限。

Abstract: We present a rigorous analysis of the mathematical boundaries and kinematic consistency of a recently proposed rate-dependent relaxation time framework intended to unify pre- and post-yield dynamics in yield-stress fluids. By evaluating the governing constitutive equations under an idealized transient creep protocol from a state of physical rest, we show that the model encounters an unavoidable boundary paradox. To avoid predicting perfectly rigid solid behavior or falling into a division-by-zero mathematical singularity under a constant applied stress below the yield threshold ($σ\le σ_y$), the framework requires an unphysical, instantaneous velocity or strain-rate step at $t = 0^+$. We show that assuming a non-zero initial strain rate explicitly violates momentum conservation and fluid inertia. Consequently, the framework preserves the piecewise, discontinuous drawbacks of classic viscoplastic models.

</details>


### [215] [Inverse Laplace Transform for Dynamic Light Scattering: Impact of Regularization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14761)
*Pierre Pajuelo,Stéphane G. Roux,Adrien Meynard,François Liénard,Éric Freyssingeas,Pierre Borgnat*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出一种改进的CONTIN方法，通过基于物理的正则化、数据驱动的L-曲线准则和方差缩减策略，从含噪动态光散射（DLS）数据中稳健地恢复弛豫时间分布，在模拟与实验数据上均优于传统参数化方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 动态光散射（Dynamic Light Scattering, DLS）通过散射光强的自相关函数（autocorrelation function）分析粒子动力学，但从含噪数据中精确提取弛豫时间分布（relaxation time distribution）非常困难。

Method: 将分布恢复问题建模为带物理正则化（physics-based regularization）的拉普拉斯变换（Laplace transform）反演问题，即CONTIN方法；引入数据驱动的L-曲线准则（L-curve criterion）选择正则化强度；采用对数离散化（logarithmic discretization）和方差缩减的相关估计（variance-reduced correlation estimation）提升算法性能。

Result: 在模拟数据上对比了Cramér-Rao下界（Cramér-Rao bound）和参数化方法，并在Carbopol微凝胶的实验数据上验证；改进方法在高噪声下表现出更强的鲁棒性，能够揭示复杂系统中的多尺度动力学（multi-scale dynamics），尤其在宽时间分布情形下显著优于参数化方法。

Conclusion: 该算法为DLS分析提供了一种强大的非参数化（non-parametric）工具，能够在高噪声和宽时间尺度条件下稳健恢复弛豫时间分布，有助于深入理解软物质（soft matter）动力学。

Abstract: Dynamic Light Scattering (DLS) analyzes particle dynamics from the autocorrelation functions of scattered light intensity, yet extracting accurate relaxation time distributions from noisy data is challenging. We develop an inverse problem approach to recover this distribution by inverting the Laplace transform with physics-based regularization, called the CONTIN method. We improve it to use it on noisy data, across a wide range of time scales, with a selection of the regularization strength through a data-driven L-curve criterion. Our approach enhances robustness under high noise and reveals multi-scale dynamics in complex systems. Validation is performed on simulated data, compared to the Cramér-Rao bound and to parametric methods, and on experimental data from Carbopol microgels. It demonstrates superior accuracy over parametric methods, especially for broad time distributions. The algorithm's logarithmic discretization and variance-reduced correlation estimation enhance performance, offering a powerful tool for non-parametric DLS analysis and deeper insights into soft matter dynamics.

</details>


### [216] [Kinetics of coagulation phenomena from a granular matter perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14768)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本文采用综述方法，整合颗粒物理、气溶胶科学（aerosol science）和天体物理学（astrophysics）的见解，分析聚集过程中的相互作用、结构与集体动力学之间的相互影响，以及分凝（segregation）、堵塞（jamming）和阻塞（clogging）等力学约束现象。

Result: 研究表明，平均场假设因颗粒物理效应而失效，聚集应被理解为受相互作用、结构与集体动力学共同塑造的多尺度过程；力学约束与空间组织在限制或改变聚集增长方向中发挥关键作用。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种关于非平衡颗粒系统（non-equilibrium particulate systems）中凝固过程的统一视角，并将其置于“沙子、筒仓与小行星：颗粒材料研究中的聚集挑战”这一专题背景下。

Abstract: Aggregation processes play a central role in systems ranging from aerosol coagulation and cloud formation to dust growth in protoplanetary disks and granular materials. These processes are traditionally described by Smoluchowski's coagulation equation, which provides a mean-field account of growth through binary collisions. However, incorporation of granular physics-dissipative interactions, spatial heterogeneity, and force transmission through contact networks-reveals important limitations of this framework.

Phenomena such as segregation, jamming, and clogging further highlight the role of mechanical constraints and spatial organization in limiting or redirecting growth. By integrating insights from granular physics, aerosol science, and astrophysics, we outline a unified perspective on coagulation in non-equilibrium particulate systems.

### [217] [Many-body activity emerging in a monolayer of air-fluidized hollow pentagons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14904)
*Wan-Jung Lin,Bohan Wu-Zhang,Rodrigo Fernández-Quevedo García,C. Miguel Barriuso G.,Aayush Agarwal,Yue Fan,Miguel Ruiz-García,Chantal Valeriani,Hongyi Xiao*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过实验和Langevin动力学模拟，研究了在多体空气动力学相互作用下五边形颗粒单层的集体运动行为，揭示了由局域堆积密度调控的“涌现活性”（emergent activity）现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多体相互作用（many-body interactions）支配下的颗粒系统可以表现出高度复杂的结构与动力学，但如何在无外部驱动的情况下自发产生类活性物质（active matter）行为，仍需深入探索。

Method: 实验采用受向上气流驱动的单层五边形颗粒（pentagon particles），通过改变颗粒几何形状（空心 vs. 实心）和气流强度，观测其运动行为；同时结合二维吸引性活性五边形颗粒的Langevin动力学模拟（Langevin dynamics simulations），将活性视为局域堆积密度的有效结果。

Result: 空心五边形颗粒表现出有效吸引（effective attraction），实心颗粒相互排斥；在强气流下稀疏分布的空心五边形呈现长时间扩散运动；在弱气流下观察到孤立静态五边形与密堆积“活性”团簇共存，后者中的颗粒呈现超扩散（super-diffusivity），此涌现活性源于局域无序结构与气流的耦合，产生跨时空尺度的关联运动。

Conclusion: 颗粒的几何形状通过影响空气动力学相互作用决定其有效力类型（吸引或排斥）；涌现活性可由局域堆积密度自然诱导，无需引入显式的主动驱动机制，为理解集体运动提供了新途径。

Abstract: Particles governed by many-body interactions exhibit remarkably complex structures and dynamics. We experimentally investigate a monolayer of pentagon particles subjected to an up-lifting air flow which induces many-body aerodynamic interactions and stochastic motion akin to a thermal bath. To minimize air flow resistance, particles move collectively with interactions dictated by their geometry: hollow particles exhibit effective attraction, whereas solid particles repel each other. Under sufficiently large air flow, sparsely packed hollow pentagons overcome substrate friction and undergo long-time diffusive motion. Under lower air flow, we see a coexistence of isolated, static pentagons and densely packed, "active" clusters, whose particles display super-diffusivity. This "emergent activity" arises collectively when locally disordered structures interact with the air flow, resulting in correlated motion across broad temporal and spatial scales. Using Langevin dynamics simulations of two-dimensional attractive active pentagons, whose activity is an effective result of the local packing density, we further unravel the basic features of this emergent activity.

### [218] [Controlling Porosity in Supraparticles Composed of Colloidal Rods and Spheres](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14928)
*Kritika Kritika,Michael P. Howard,Arash Nikoubashman*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文利用介观尺度粒子模拟（mesoscale particle-based simulation）研究由棒状和球形胶体粒子构成的超粒子（supraparticle, SP）在液滴干燥过程中的自组装行为。通过对干燥后选择性移除某类粒子，分析所得多孔超粒子的结构特征，发现剩余粒子大多形成连通网络，且孔隙表面积与剩余组分总表面积高度相关，而孔径分布则强烈依赖于球体尺寸和被移除组分的类型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超粒子（SP）的内部孔隙率（porosity）在催化、光子学和吸附等领域具有重要应用价值。干燥过程的非平衡特性可能成为调控超粒子内部粒子排列的额外手段，因此有必要深入理解粒子形状、尺寸及加工条件如何影响多孔超粒子的最终结构。

Method: 采用介观尺度粒子模拟方法，模拟由棒状（rod-shaped）和球形（spherical）胶体粒子构成的超粒子在液滴干燥过程中的组装行为。干燥完成后，选择性移除其中一类粒子，并对所得多孔超粒子的结构进行表征，包括连通性、孔隙表面积和孔径分布（pore-size distribution）等。

Result: 在大多数组成条件下，剩余粒子形成连通网络，其中棒状粒子在较低体积分数下即可发生渗流（percolation）。大部分孔隙体积构成单一连通空间，其表面积与剩余组分的总表面积高度吻合。然而，孔径分布强烈依赖于球体尺寸和被移除组分的类型，反映了移除前球体团聚（sphere-clustering）和棒体成束（rod-bundling）行为的差异。

Conclusion: 该工作为如何利用粒子尺寸、形状以及加工条件来调控超粒子的孔隙率提供了新的认识。

Abstract: Supraparticles (SPs) are assemblies of colloidal particles whose properties can be tuned by modifying the chemistry, shape, and size of the colloidal particles as well as their arrangement in the SP. SPs with internal porosity are of particular interest for catalysis, photonics, and adsorption applications because of their high surface area and tunable pore size distribution. SPs are often fabricated by droplet drying, and the nonequilibrium nature of drying processes may provide an additional handle to control particle arrangement within the SP. Here, we use mesoscale particle-based simulations to explore the drying-induced assembly of SPs made from rod-shaped and spherical colloidal particles. We selectively remove one type of particle after drying and characterize the structure of the resulting porous SP. We find that the remaining particles form connected networks for most compositions, with rods percolating at lower volume fractions than spheres. Most of the resulting void volume forms a single contiguous space whose surface area closely follows the total surface area of the remaining component. The pore-size distribution, however, depends strongly on sphere size and on the removed component, reflecting differences in sphere-clustering and rod-bundling before removal. This work provides new insight into how particle size and shape, as well as processing conditions, might be used to manipulate porosity in SPs.

### [219] [Kinetic Criticality in Linker-Mediated Colloidal Aggregation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15415)
*Alexei V. Tkachenko,Soojung Lee,Zohar A. Arnon,Oleg Gang*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 链接子介导的聚集（linker-mediated aggregation）动力学与经典斯莫卢霍夫斯基动力学（Smoluchowski kinetics）存在显著偏差，其核心在于团簇反应性（cluster reactivity）在生长过程中持续演化。通过理论结合DNA连接金纳米粒子实验，研究确立了由链接子丰度（linker abundance）控制的动力学临界点（kinetic critical point）。低于阈值时，活性链接子耗尽，生长停滞；高于阈值时，团簇不断积累反应位点，实现自加速并过渡到扩散受限粗化（diffusion-limited coarsening）。实验结果验证了所预测的停滞、加速生长以及缩放塌缩（scaling collapse）现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 链接子介导的聚集在现代纳米科学中具有重要作用，但经典斯莫卢霍夫斯基动力学无法描述其关键特征——团簇反应性在生长过程中的演化。本研究旨在揭示此类聚集体系的动力学临界行为及其内在机制。

Method: 采用理论分析（theory）与DNA连接金纳米粒子实验（DNA-linked gold-nanoparticle experiments）相结合的方法，研究链接子介导聚集过程中团簇反应性的演化及其对整体动力学的影响。

Result: 发现一个由链接子丰度控制的动力学临界点：低于阈值时，活性链接子耗尽，生长停滞；高于阈值时，团簇积累反应位点，实现自加速，并最终过渡到扩散受限粗化。实验数据验证了所预测的停滞、加速生长及缩放塌缩行为。

Conclusion: 链接子介导的聚集动力学显著偏离经典斯莫卢霍夫斯基框架，其核心差异在于团簇反应性的演化。该发现为理解并调控纳米尺度聚集过程提供了新的动力学临界视角。

Abstract: Linker-mediated aggregation plays an important role in modern nanoscience. We demonstrate that it departs sharply from classical Smoluchowski kinetics because cluster reactivity evolves during growth. Combining theory with DNA-linked gold-nanoparticle experiments, we establish kinetic critical point controlled by linker abundance. Below threshold, active linkers are depleted and growth arrests; above threshold, clusters accumulate reactive sites, self-accelerate, and cross over to diffusion-limited coarsening. Experiments verify the predicted arrest, accelerated growth, and scaling collapse.

### [220] [Universal scaling in the rheology of dense cellular systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15100)
*Helen S. Ansell,Daniel M. Sussman*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过模型细胞单层在恒定应力下的实验，揭示了汇合组织（confluent tissues）具有从固态到流体态的丰富非线性流变学（nonlinear rheology）相图，包括屈服、剪切变稀、连续/不连续剪切增稠以及剪切堵塞（shear jamming）转变。研究发现，不同流变状态下的宏观黏度受同一物理参数控制的普适标度行为（universal scaling behavior）支配，表明汇合组织通过形状驱动的拓扑约束（topological constraints）实现堵塞现象，从而构成一类独特的无序物质（disordered matter）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生物组织在形态发生（morphogenesis）和集体迁移（collective migration）等过程中需要在刚性态与类流动态之间动态转换，同时还要抵抗生理剪切应力。目前尚不清楚这些组织动力学是否受与非平衡临界现象（non-equilibrium critical phenomena）相同的机制所支配。

Method: 该研究对模型细胞单层施加恒定应力，系统观测其在不同应力条件下的非线性流变学行为，并分析其结构变化特征，包括力链（force chains）的形成和取向有序化（orientational ordering）。

Result: 模型细胞单层在恒定应力下展示出丰富的非线性流变学相图：刚性状态下，小内部涨落维持类固态直至有限屈服应力（yield stress），超过则发生剪切变稀（shear-thinning）；类流动态则表现出稳健的连续和不连续剪切增稠（shear thickening），最终通过剪切堵塞（shear jamming）导致结构失稳。该剪切堵塞转变伴随着系统尺度力链的形成和取向有序的出现。不同流变状态下的宏观黏度由同一底层物理参数控制，遵循普适标度行为。

Conclusion: 该研究证明汇合组织是一类独特的无序物质，表明普适的堵塞现象（jamming phenomena）可以完全通过形状驱动的拓扑约束来产生，从而调节生物力学过程。

Abstract: Biological tissues must dynamically transition between rigid and fluid-like states during processes like morphogenesis and collective migration, often while simultaneously resisting physiological shear stresses. It remains unclear whether these tissue dynamics are governed by the same non-equilibrium critical phenomena that control conventional disordered matter. Here we show that model cell monolayers under constant stress display a rich phase diagram of nonlinear rheology. In rigid regimes, small internal fluctuations maintain a solid-like state up to a finite yield stress, above which the tissue shear-thins; conversely, fluid-like regimes exhibit robust continuous and discontinuous shear thickening, culminating in structural arrest via shear jamming. This space-filling shear-jamming transition is accompanied by structural changes including the formation of system-spanning force chains and the emergence of orientational ordering. We demonstrate that the macroscopic viscosity across these disparate regimes is described by universal scaling behavior controlled by the same underlying physical parameters. These results establish confluent tissues as a distinct class of disordered matter, demonstrating that universal jamming phenomena can emerge entirely through shape-driven topological constraints to regulate biological mechanics.

### [221] [On the flow of electrically charged particles in an elastic solid](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15279)
*Jiashi Yang*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于三连续介质混合物模型（three-continuum mixture model）推导理论框架，该模型包含带电晶格连续介质（charged lattice continuum）、用于描述电极化的束缚电荷连续介质（bound charge continuum），以及用于描述可移动电荷流动的理想流体（ideal fluid）。基本电机械定律被系统性地应用于该模型，电场采用准静态（quasistatic）近似，并使用国际单位制（SI units）。

Result: 得到了一个可描述软固体电解质与弹性半导体行为的连续介质理论，该理论具有非线性（nonlinear）特性，适用于大变形（large deformation）与强场（strong fields）条件。

Conclusion: 该专精化理论在保持原始理论严谨性的同时，降低了阅读与应用的复杂度，为后续研究软固体电解质与弹性半导体中的电-力耦合行为提供了一个更友好的理论工具。

Abstract: This paper is a specialization of a broad and complicated continuum theory [arXiv:2403.07582] to a relatively simple and useful case so that it is more reader friendly. A continuum theory of the flow of charged particles in an elastic solid is presented. It can describe the behavior of soft solid electrolytes and elastic semiconductors. It is nonlinear and is valid for large deformation and strong fields. The theory is derived from a three-continuum mixture model including a charged lattice continuum, a bound charge continuum for electric polarization, and an ideal fluid for the flow of mobile charges. The basic electromechanical laws are applied systematically to the model. The electric fields are quasistatic and are in SI units.

### [222] [Intrinsic decay length in elastic localization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15312)
*Xiang Yu*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文揭示有限弹性结构中局部化（localization）现象能否用无限域解近似，取决于一个内在衰减长度（intrinsic decay length）。当结构长度超过该衰减长度时，有限域局部化解以指数方式收敛于无限域解，该长度还决定了弱非线性近似的有效性区间及数值计算的可区分性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 有限弹性结构中的局部化问题常借用无限域解来简化分析，但有限域解何时能准确用无限域解近似并不清楚。作者旨在建立判断这一近似有效性的统一准则。

Method: 使用一个原型局部化模型（prototypical localization model）进行理论分析，并通过两个代表性的弹性局部化问题——膜管鼓胀（bulging in membrane tubes）和扭杆局部螺旋屈曲（localized helical buckling in twisted rods）——进行数值验证。

Result: 有限域局部化解在结构长度超过内在衰减长度后，与无限域解之间的差异呈指数级衰减；该衰减长度也决定了有限域与无限域弱非线性近似的有效性区间存在显著差异；在数值计算中，不同域长的局部化解在结构长度超过衰减长度后难以区分。

Conclusion: 本文为弹性局部化中的局部化转变（localization transition）、渐近有效性（asymptotic validity）和数值计算（numerical computation）提供一个统一的几何框架。

Abstract: Localization in finite elastic structures is often studied using infinite-domain solutions, which avoid the explicit treatment of boundaries and admit simpler analytical descriptions. Yet it remains poorly understood when finite-domain localized states can be accurately approximated by their infinite-domain counterparts. In this work, we show that the accuracy is controlled by an intrinsic decay length. Using a prototypical localization model, we show that finite-domain localized solutions converge exponentially to the corresponding infinite-domain localized solution once the structural length exceeds the intrinsic decay length. The intrinsic decay length also explains the markedly different validity regimes of finite- and infinite-domain weakly nonlinear approximations. It further has important implications for numerical computation, since once the structural length exceeds the intrinsic decay length, localized solutions corresponding to different domain lengths differ only by exponentially small quantities, making them increasingly difficult to distinguish numerically. The theoretical predictions are validated using two representative localization problems: bulging in membrane tubes and localized helical buckling in twisted rods. The present work provides a unified geometric framework for understanding localization transition, asymptotic validity, and numerical computation in elastic localization.

### [223] [Cobalt-Catalysed Chain Transfer Polymerisation Enables Soft Methacrylate Nematic Elastomers for Switchable Pressure-Sensitive Adhesion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15403)
*Noboru Koshimizu,Mohand O. Saed*

TL;DR: 本文通过催化链转移聚合（catalytic chain-transfer polymerization）策略，利用CoBF催化剂调控甲基丙烯酸酯类液晶弹性体（LCE）的网络结构，降低了玻璃化转变温度（T_g）和储能模量（E'），实现了兼具高粘附性与可逆热脱粘的压敏粘合剂（PSA）性能。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在光聚合过程中引入百万分浓度级别的双(二氟硼二甲基乙二肟)钴(II)（CoBF）作为催化链转移剂，降低有效交联密度并增大交联间分子量；进一步加入单官能甲基丙烯酸酯和柔性聚乙二醇二甲基丙烯酸酯（PEGDMA）以优化流变学性能。

Result: CoBF浓度的增加降低了T_g和E'并保留了向列有序性，同时增强了粘弹性耗散并拓宽了向列相温度窗口。优化配方的T_g接近0 °C，室温储能模量约0.3 MPa，表现出高阻尼行为，接近Dahlquist判据（Dahlquist criterion）。所得向列弹性体在向列态具有强粘附性（ tack、剥离和搭接剪切），并在加热至向列-各向同性转变温度以上时实现快速、可逆、无残留脱粘。

Conclusion: 催化链转移聚合是一种调控软性甲基丙烯酸酯向列弹性体网络结构的有效策略，能够在保持液晶有序性的同时显著降低模量和玻璃化转变温度，实现可逆切换的压敏粘附性能。

Abstract: Liquid crystal elastomers (LCEs) exhibit unique viscoelastic behavior arising from reversible liquid-crystalline ordering, making them attractive candidates for switchable pressure-sensitive adhesives (PSAs). However, methacrylate-based LCEs are typically highly crosslinked, leading to elevated glass-transition temperatures ($T_g$) and storage moduli ($E'$) that limit adhesive performance. Here, we demonstrate that catalytic chain-transfer polymerization provides an effective strategy for engineering soft methacrylate nematic elastomers through systematic control of network architecture. Incorporation of parts-per-million concentrations of bis(boron difluorodimethylglyoximate)cobalt(II) (CoBF) during photopolymerization reduced the effective crosslink density and increased the molecular weight between crosslinks, producing substantial decreases in $T_g$ and $E'$ while preserving nematic order. Dynamic mechanical analysis revealed that increasing CoBF concentration enhanced viscoelastic dissipation and broadened the accessible nematic temperature window. To further optimize rheological properties for pressure-sensitive adhesion, monofunctional methacrylates and flexible poly(ethylene glycol) dimethacrylate (PEGDMA) were incorporated into the network. The optimized formulation exhibited a $T_g$ near 0~$^\circ$C, a room-temperature storage modulus of approximately 0.3 MPa, and high damping behavior, approaching the Dahlquist criterion for pressure-sensitive adhesion. As a result, the resulting nematic elastomers displayed strong tack, peel, and lap-shear adhesion in the nematic state, together with rapid, reversible, and residue-free debonding upon heating above the nematic-to-isotropic transition temperature.

</details>


### [224] [Underscreening and related phenomena in strong electrolytes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15492)
*Diana Shvydka,Victor Karpov*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出一个启发式模型，用于解释高密度库仑系统（如强电解质和超高通量辐射下生物组织中的电子-空穴聚集体）中的欠屏蔽（underscreening）现象。该模型揭示了屏蔽长度随带电粒子浓度增加而增大的机制，并阐明其对浓缩电解质电导率与还原电位的影响，同时验证了FLASH放射治疗（FLASH-RT）中观察到的组织保护效应（sparing effect）与欠屏蔽现象的类比关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高密度库仑系统中欠屏蔽现象的机制尚未明确，尤其是在超高通量辐射（UHDR）生物组织的背景下，屏蔽长度随浓度反常增加的现象缺乏统一理论解释。

Method: 提出一个基于粒子间相互结合（mutual binding）产生扩散屏障（diffusion barriers）的启发式模型，用以描述高密度库仑系统中屏蔽长度的变化规律。

Result: 模型成功解释了屏蔽长度随带电粒子浓度增加而增加的数据，并为浓缩电解质的电导率和还原电位提供了额外见解；同时，该模型验证了FLASH放射治疗中观察到的组织保护效应与UHDR体系中欠屏蔽现象的物理一致性。

Conclusion: 粒子间的相互结合通过抑制移动粒子浓度来增大屏蔽长度，并减缓生物活性自由基生成的化学反应速率，从而解释了UHDR条件下观察到的保护效应。

Abstract: We propose a heuristic model of underscreening phenomenon in high density Coulomb systems, such as strong electrolytes and electron hole conglomerates under ultra high dose rate (UHDR) radiation in biological tissues. It explains the data on screening length $L$ increasing with charge particle concentration and offers additional insights in understanding the conductivity and reduction potential of concentrated electrolytes. Also, it validates our current understanding of the FLASH radiation treatment of tumors (FLASH-RT) perceived as an analogous system. The underlying physics is that mutual binding creates diffusion barriers which suppress the concentration of mobile particles thus increasing the screening length. Also, they slow down the rates of chemical reactions responsible for generation of biologically active radicals which explains the sparing effect observed under UHDR.

### [225] [End-Functionalized Ions Promote Stability of Highly Frustrated Phases in Diblock Copolymers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15580)
*Chao Duan,Zhen-Gang Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出并论证了一种通过端基功能化离子引入强离子关联（strong ion correlations）来稳定嵌段共聚物（block copolymer）中拓扑复杂且不易获得的高沮豫相（frustrated phase）——立方单网络相（primitive cubic $Im\bar{3}m$ network）的新机制，揭示了曲率选择性链端缔合作为一类通用设计原则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 嵌段共聚物自组装形成的经典有序纳米结构受界面能与链构象熵的竞争调控，但拓扑复杂的“沮豫”相（如$Im\bar{3}m$立方网络）因严重的堆积惩罚在中性体系中难以获得。为此，作者探索利用离子功能化引入新的稳定机制。

Method: 在AB双嵌段共聚物（AB diblock copolymer）熔体中，对其中一种嵌段的末端进行离子功能化，利用强离子关联驱动链端缔合，产生朝向带电域的曲率偏好。通过自由能分解和超越平均场（beyond-mean-field）的离子关联计算，分析静电能量随界面曲率的变化趋势。

Result: 该离子功能化策略选择性地稳定了高度沮豫的$Im\bar{3}m$单网络相，使其出现在中性体系有序-无序转变以下的参数空间区域。自由能分解表明，静电能量几乎完全来自超越平均场的离子关联，且随界面曲率增大而负向增强。在$Im\bar{3}m$相中，离子被局部富集于圆柱支柱（cylindrical struts）中形成致密弯曲簇（compact curved clusters），其关联能增益超过堆积沮豫的惩罚。增大离子尺寸会削弱关联并抑制$Im\bar{3}m$相，与实验观察一致。

Conclusion: 曲率选择性的端基缔合（curvature-selective end-group association）为在嵌段共聚物体系中获取沮豫拓扑结构提供了通用设计原则。离子尺寸是调控该效应的关键参数。

Abstract: Block copolymers self-assemble into ordered nanostructures whose geometry is governed by a competition between interfacial energy and chain conformational entropy. While this competition produces a rich sequence of morphologies, topologically complex ``frustrated'' phases such as the primitive cubic ($Im\bar{3}m$) network incur severe packing penalties and are difficult to access in neutral systems. Here we show that ions functionalized at the termini of one block in an AB diblock copolymer melt introduce a qualitatively new stabilization mechanism. Strong ion correlations drive chain-end association and generate a curvature preference toward the charged domain; the resulting tendency of end-localized ion clusters to adopt compact, curved geometries selectively favors the highly frustrated $Im\bar{3}m$ single-network over the classical phases, in a region of parameter space lying below the order-disorder transition of the neutral system. Free energy decomposition reveals that the electrostatic energy, arising almost entirely from beyond-mean-field ion correlations, becomes increasingly negative with increasing interfacial curvature. In the primitive cubic network, pronounced local segregation of ions into the cylindrical struts generates compact curved clusters whose correlation energy gain more than offsets the enhanced packing frustration, so the very geometry that is the source of packing frustration in neutral systems becomes the source of its stability here. Increasing ion size weakens correlations and suppresses the $Im\bar{3}m$ phase, consistent with experimental observations. Our results establish curvature-selective end-group association as a general principle for accessing frustrated topologies in block copolymer systems.

</details>


### [226] [Phase Behavior of Unilamellar Hybrid Lipid-Diblock Copolymer Membranes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16156)
*James F. Tallman,Junyu Wu,Antonia Statt*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出一个物理信息框架，将化学不互溶性（chemical immiscibility）、疏水厚度错配（hydrophobic thickness mismatch）和几何约束（geometric constraints）相结合，预测杂化膜（hybrid membrane）的形态，并通过粗粒化分子动力学（coarse-grained molecular dynamics）在广泛的参数空间内验证理论，将观测结果统一为相图。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 杂化脂质-嵌段共聚物膜（hybrid lipid block copolymer membranes）在药物递送、单分子检测、膜内蛋白质折叠和合成细胞等领域具有广阔应用前景，但由于决定其纳米至微米尺度形态与性质的设计参数繁多，理性设计十分困难。

Method: 本文扩展了现有两亲性单层（amphiphilic monolayers）理论，用以建模二嵌段共聚物双层（diblock copolymer bilayers）的厚度，表明疏水段和亲水段长度共同决定厚度；在此基础上，构建了一个融合化学不互溶性、疏水厚度错配和几何约束的物理信息框架来预测形态。

Result: 识别并解释了四种主要的膜形态：混合（mixed）、横向相分离（laterally phase-separated）、解拉链（unzipped, thick-thin coexistence）和聚合物富集（polymer-rich）。化学不互溶性区分混合和横向相分离膜；疏水错配驱动向解拉链或聚合物富集形态的转变；面密度（areal density）决定解拉链与聚合物富集状态之间的交叉。理论预测通过涵盖多种脂质物种（DOPC, DPPC）、聚合物物种（1,4 PBD-b-PEO, 1,2 PBD-b-PEO, PE-b-PEO）、嵌段长度、温度和组分的粗粒化分子动力学得到验证。

Conclusion: 所得相图（phase maps）统一了已有的实验与模拟观测，实现了对系统参数如何影响纳米尺度形态的通用且机理性（mechanistic）理解。

Abstract: Hybrid lipid block copolymer membranes are promising for many applications in drug delivery, single molecule detection, in-membrane protein folding, and synthetic cells. However, rational design is difficult due to the many design parameters which determine the nano- and micron-scale morphology and properties. In this work, we propose a physically-informed framework which incorporates chemical immiscibility, hydrophobic thickness mismatch and geometric constraints to predict the morphology of hybrid membranes. For this purpose, we extend existing theory for amphiphilic monolayers to model the thickness of diblock copolymer bilayers, demonstrating that both the hydrophobic and hydrophilic block lengths determine the thickness. We identify and rationalize the four primary membrane morphologies observed: mixed, laterally phase-separated, unzipped (thick-thin coexistence), and polymer-rich. Specifically, chemical immiscibility differentiates mixed membranes from laterally phase separated membranes, and hydrophobic mismatch drives transitions to unzipped or polymer-rich morphologies. Areal density, finally, determines the crossover between unzipped and polymer-rich states. We validate our theoretical predictions using coarse-grained molecular dynamics across a broad parameter space, including multiple lipid species (DOPC, DPPC), polymer species (1,4 PBD-b-PEO, 1,2 PBD-b-PEO, PE-b-PEO), block lengths, temperatures, and compositions. The resulting phase maps unify previously reported experimental and simulation observations and enable a generic and mechanistic understanding for the effect of system parameters on the nanoscale morphology.

</details>


### [227] [Effect of a Cone Shape on the Motion of Active Janus Colloids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16391)
*Zhiyuan Zhao,Teun W. J. Verouden,Dillip K. Mohapatra,Evert M. E. Simons,Janne-Mieke Meijer*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过双光子聚合3D打印结合交流电场实验，系统研究了不同锥形形状对Janus微游泳者推进速度的影响，发现球形颗粒运动最快，且在低频诱导电荷电泳（ICEP）与高频自介电泳（sDEP）之间可触发运动方向反转，其中大锥形凸起结构在sDEP模式下速度提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 活性胶体（active colloids）的推进由其对称性和形状决定，但目前缺乏对微小几何效应如何影响各向异性（anisotropic）活性胶体运动的系统研究。本文旨在填补这一空白，探究锥形形状对Janus微游泳者推进速度的具体影响。

Method: 采用高分辨率双光子聚合3D打印（two-photon polymerization 3D printing）技术制备一系列不同形状（从球体到带有锥形凸起的半球体）但具有相似半球形金涂层的Janus胶体（Janus colloids），并在外加交流电场（AC electric field）下开展实验研究。

Result: 在交流电场下所有颗粒均表现出活性弹道运动（active, ballistic motion）。推进速度呈形状与尺寸依赖性：球形Janus颗粒运动最快，其次是小锥形和大锥形凸起结构，而带平边的打印球体运动最慢。所有形状均可触发运动方向反转，该现象由低频下的诱导电荷电泳（induced-charge electrophoresis, ICEP）向高频下的自介电泳（self-dielectrophoresis, sDEP）转变所致。大锥形凸起在sDEP模式下速度显著提升。

Conclusion: 研究结果揭示了活性粒子几何形状与推进速度之间的内在联系，对理解生物微游泳者（biological micro swimmers）以及设计优化微机器人（microrobots）具有重要意义。

Abstract: The propulsion of active colloids is governed by their symmetry and shape, yet a systematic investigation of how small geometric effects influence the locomotion of anisotropic active colloids is lacking. In this paper, we study the effect of a cone shape by combining high-resolution two-photon polymerization 3D printing with AC electric field experiments to study anisotropic Janus micro swimmers. We fabricate a series of Janus colloids with different shapes, ranging from a sphere to a hemisphere with a cone-protrusion, but containing similar hemispherical gold-coatings. Under an applied alternating current (AC) electric field, all particles exhibit active, ballistic motion. We find a shape and size dependence on the propulsion velocity, with the spherical Janus particle moving fastest, followed by a small cone and a large cone protrusion, while surprisingly a printed sphere with a flat side moves slowest. In addition, a reversal in the direction of motion for all shapes was triggered, a phenomenon governed by a transition from induced-charge electrophoresis (ICEP) at low frequencies to self-dielectrophoresis (sDEP) at high frequencies. We reveal a distinct shape influence, with the large cone-protrusion increasing their velocity in the sDEP regime. Our results provide insight into the link between active particle geometry and their propulsion velocity that are important for understanding biological micro swimmers and designing optimized microrobots.

### [228] [Progress toward a better BOCS: Systematic coarse-graining with local density potentials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16998)
*Maria C. Lesniewski,Michael R. DeLyser,W. G. Noid*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文介绍了Bottom-up Open-source Coarse-graining Software (BOCS) 软件包5.0版本及其配套仿真包PKG-BOCS，该版本新增了依赖局部密度（local density）及其平方梯度（square gradient）的势函数，并通过数值计算验证了这些势函数在提升粗粒化模型结构忠实度、热力学性质与可迁移性方面的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有粗粒化（coarse-grained, CG）模型在描述复杂分子体系时，缺乏对局部环境信息的有效编码，导致结构忠实度（structural fidelity）和热力学性质的准确性有限。BOCS 5.0旨在通过引入依赖局部密度及其平方梯度的势函数来弥补这一不足。

Method: BOCS 5.0基于力匹配变分原理（force-matching variational principle），直接从全原子模拟数据参数化粗粒化势函数。新版本扩展了势函数形式，使其可依赖每个粒子周围的局部密度（local density, LD）以及该局部密度的平方梯度（square gradient, SG）。同时开发了新软件包PKG-BOCS，用于在LAMMPS中模拟这些势函数，支持复杂分子拓扑结构并允许灵活定义局部密度。

Result: 数值计算结果表明，所实现的LD和SG势函数具有物理合理性且计算精度良好。对水模型的粗粒化模拟显示，引入局部密度依赖势函数能够显著提升模型的结构忠实度（structural fidelity）、热力学性质（thermodynamic properties）以及可迁移性（transferability）。

Conclusion: BOCS 5.0版本通过引入局部密度及其平方梯度依赖的势函数，拓展了自下而上粗粒化方法的能力边界。结合PKG-BOCS仿真包，该软件为构建具有更高准确性和可迁移性的粗粒化模型提供了完整的技术方案。

Abstract: We describe version 5.0 of the Bottom-up Open-source Coarse-graining Software (BOCS) package. BOCS employs the force-matching variational principle to parameterize potentials for coarse-grained (CG) models directly from atomically detailed simulations. BOCS version 5.0 significantly extends previous versions by treating potentials that depend upon the local density (LD) around each particle, as well as potentials that depend upon the square gradient (SG) of this local density. We also describe a new package, PKG-BOCS, for simulating these potentials in LAMMPS. This software treats complex molecular topologies and provides considerable flexibility for defining the local density, as well as the LD and SG potentials. We present numerical calculations that provide physical insight into these potentials and demonstrate the accuracy of our implementation. Finally, we demonstrate that LD potentials can significantly improve the structural fidelity, thermodynamic properties, and transferability of CG models for water.

</details>

### [229] [The Winner Takes It All](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16885)
*P. L. Krapivsky*

Main category: physics.soc-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了任意图上进行的“胜者通吃（winner-takes-all, WTA）”过程，分析了在一维格点、线段以及无限正则树（Bethe晶格）上最终胜者比例等相关统计性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解在一般图结构上进行的竞争淘汰过程的最终稳态统计行为，特别是不同图拓扑（如线段、树）对胜者比例和分布的影响。

Method: 采用概率论与统计力学方法，对WTA过程进行建模：每个顶点上的智能体（agent）与邻居随机进行游戏，每次游戏中随机一方获胜，败者被淘汰，直到所有活跃智能体的邻居均为败者为止。分别在一维格点、线段和无限正则树（Bethe晶格）上解析求解相关统计量。

Result: 在一维格点上，最终胜者比例为 $e^{-1}$，并给出了胜者获胜次数 $j=0,1,2$ 的比例 $w_j$。在线段上，得到了胜者总数的平均值、方差及所有高阶累积量，以及达到最小或最大胜者数状态的概率与边界附近行为。在度为 $d$ 的无限正则树（Bethe晶格）上，胜者比例为 $(2/d)^{d/(d-2)}$。

Conclusion: WTA过程的最终胜者统计性质高度依赖于底层图的结构：一维格点给出普适常数 $e^{-1}$，而正则树上则呈现与度数 $d$ 相关的幂律形式。线段上的边界效应显著影响胜者分布的高阶矩。

Abstract: The winner-takes-all (WTA) process takes place on an arbitrary graph. There is an agent on each vertex of the graph, and active agents at neighboring vertices play games. In each game, a randomly chosen agent wins, while the loser is eliminated from subsequent games. The games are played at random times; each game finishes instantaneously, and the games cease when each active agent has only losers among its neighbors. On the one-dimensional lattice, the fraction of winners in the final state is $e^{-1}$, and we also determine the fractions $w_j$ of winners who won $j=0, 1, 2$ games. For the WTA process on a segment, we determine statistics of the total number of winners (the average, the variance, and all higher cumulants), the probabilities of reaching the final state with the minimum or maximum number of winners, and establish the behavior near the boundaries. For infinite regular trees with vertices of degree $d$, i.e., Bethe lattices with coordination number $d$, the fraction of winners is $(2/d)^{d/(d-2)}$.

</details>


### [230] [q-Exponential Random Graphs: higher-order networks from simple constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.31209)
*David Dobáš,Diego Garlaschelli,Petr Jizba*

Main category: physics.soc-ph

TL;DR: 本文在非香农（Shannon）熵框架下，将指数随机图（ERGs）推广为高阶q-指数随机图。通过最大化Uffink熵族（而非香农熵），得到的图分布从指数型（Boltzmann-Gibbs）变为q-指数型，从而引入边之间的依赖关系。在该框架下，经典的Erdos-Renyi模型和配置模型在保持原有约束（边数和度序列）不变的情况下，展现出原始ERGs所不具备的稀疏-稠密相变、更丰富的同配性与聚类结构等高阶网络特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期研究表明，在缺乏额外信息时，最无偏的推断构造应最大化更广义的Uffink熵族，而非香农熵。然而，最大化香农熵可能导致自由度之间产生不合理的独立性假设。因此，本文旨在探究在非香农情况下，最流行的具有独立边的ERGs如何推广为具有依赖边的q-指数随机图，同时保持其定义性约束不变。

Method: 本文将最大化香农熵得到的指数分布（Boltzmann-Gibbs）替换为最大化Uffink熵族得到的q-指数分布，从而构建高阶q-指数随机图（q-Exponential Random Graphs）。具体以Erdos-Renyi模型和配置模型（configuration model）为例，在保持边数与度序列约束不变的条件下，引入边的依赖关系，推导出相应的非香农分布形式。

Result: 研究发现，高阶q-指数随机图展现了原始ERGs中不存在的稀疏-稠密相变（phase transition）、更丰富的同配性（assortativity）与聚类（clustering）特征，使得边的稀疏性（sparsity）与三元闭包（triadic closure）可以共存。

Conclusion: 高阶网络特征并不一定需要高阶约束；在比香农框架更无偏的推断框架下，简单的低阶约束即可自然产生高阶网络现象。

Abstract: Exponential Random Graphs (ERGs) are among the most widely used network models, derived as principled least-bias graph ensembles that maximize Shannon entropy under constraints on the expected values of given structural properties. However, it has been recently (re)discovered that, in the absence of additional information privileging Shannon entropy, the most agnostic inferential construction should maximize the broader class of Uffink entropies. The resulting entropy-maximizing distribution changes from the exponential (Boltzmann-Gibbs) to the so-called q-exponential one. Since maximizing Shannon entropy may produce an unjustified independence between degrees of freedom, here we investigate how the most popular ERGs with independent edges (namely, the Erdos-Renyi and configuration models) generalize to higher-order q-Exponential Random Graphs with dependent edges in the non-Shannon case, while keeping their defining constraints (number of links and degree sequence, respectively) unchanged. We find features, such as a phase transition between sparse and dense regimes, that are absent in the original ERGs but typical of higher-order networks, plus novel phenomena such as richer assortativity and clustering profiles, which allow for the coexistence of link sparsity and triadic closure. These results show that higher-order networks do not necessarily require higher-order constraints, as they naturally arise from simpler ones in a framework that is even more agnostic than Shannon's.

</details>


### [231] [Physics of anticipatory active matter, with application to crowd dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14818)
*Alexis Raulin-Foissac,Alexandre Nicolas*

Main category: physics.soc-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一个统计物理（statistical physics）框架，用于描述“预期型智能体（anticipatory agents）”的动力学行为，将其映射为d+1维非预期链的涨落问题，并成功应用于行人动力学（pedestrian dynamics），以最小成本函数复现了多种实验场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统统计物理学主要处理仅依赖当前（或过去）构型进行交互的实体，这种被动反应式（reactive）框架在涉及捕食者-猎物追逐、行人或机器人等具有预期能力的行为体时效率低下，因此需要建立能刻画预期行为的新统计物理框架。

Method: 将预期型智能体（anticipatory agent）的当前动力学表达为基于观测构建的成本函数（cost function），并将其在d维空间中的动力学映射为d+1维非预期链（non-anticipatory chain）的动力学，其中涨落（fluctuation）横向作用于链以表征对未来状态的不确定性。借助高分子物理（polymer physics）的洞见来表征链的动力学，并定义预期视界（anticipation horizon），超出该视界的模糊未来可用平均场（mean-field）方式处理。

Result: 该框架成功应用于行人动力学，实现了代理模型（agent-based model）中操作层（operational level）与战术层（tactical level）的无缝整合。即使采用极简形式的成本函数，模型仍能复现多种对现有模型具有挑战性的实验场景，例如穿越杂乱环境（crossing cluttered environments）或从拥挤列车下车（alighting from a crowded train）。

Conclusion: 该模型具有透明且灵活的基底，可便捷地纳入额外机制，为统计物理学处理具有前瞻性行为的复杂系统提供了一种新的途径。

Abstract: Statistical Physics has traditionally dealt with entities that interact merely based on the present, and possibly past, configurations. This reactive framework is inefficient in many situations involving living beings, such as predators chasing a prey, pedestrians, or even robots. This paper introduces a statistical physical framework for the dynamics of anticipatory agents, whose present-time dynamics depend on the prospective system state that they anticipate. We clarify how these dynamics can be expressed in terms of a cost function constructed based on observations and we show that the dynamics of an anticipatory agent in d dimensions can be mapped onto the dynamics of a (non-anticipatory) chain in d + 1 dimensions, with fluctuations acting transversely on the chain to account for the uncertainty about the future state. Insights from polymer Physics help us characterize the dynamics of these chains and delineate an anticipation horizon beyond which the blurry future can be handled in a mean-field way. The foregoing framework is successfully applied to pedestrian dynamics, leading to a seamless integration of operational and tactical levels in an agent-based model. Even with a minimal expression of the cost, the model succeeds in reproducing various experimental scenarios which are challenging for state-of-the-art models, such as crossing cluttered environments or alighting from a crowded train. The transparent and flexible basis of the model allows the straightforward incorporation of additional mechanisms.

</details>

### [232] [O(N) BCFT: new data from conformal partial wave expansions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14733)
*Jozef Csipes,Petr Vaško*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在大$N$展开框架下分析了$\mathsf{O}(N)$边界共形场论（$\mathsf{BCFT}$），聚焦于普通跃迁边界条件，利用体-边界共形分波展开谱函数，证明了先前关于边界谱函数的猜想，推导了新的体展开结果，并提取出未知OPE系数$C_{\sigma\sigma\sigma^3}$的领头阶大$N$表达式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在大$N$展开下系统分析$\mathsf{O}(N)$边界共形场论（$\mathsf{BCFT}$）中的体两点关联函数，以揭示边界共形场论数据（$\mathsf{BCFT}$ data）并验证或推导相关猜想与展开结果。

Method: 采用大$N$展开（large $N$ expansion）方法，在体维度$2<d+1<4$下研究普通跃迁（ordinary transition）对应的边界条件；将体两点关联函数$\langle φφ\rangle$、$\langle φ^2 φ^2\rangle$和$\langle σσ\rangle$（$σ$为 Hubbard–Stratonovich 场）展开为体/边界共形分波（bulk/boundary conformal partial waves），并分析其谱函数（spectral functions）。

Result: 证明了Dujava等人[arXiv:2503.16345]中关于边界谱函数（boundary spectral functions）的猜想；复现了Giombi等人[arXiv:2007.04955]中$\langle φφ\rangle$的体展开结果；首次给出$\langle σσ\rangle$的体展开，并从中提取出未知OPE系数$C_{\sigma\sigma\sigma^3}$的领头阶大$N$表达式；作为副产品导出的混合系数（mixing coefficient）与Derkachov等人[arXiv:hep-th/9705020]的结果一致，支持了主要结果的正确性。

Conclusion: 本文方法可推广至特殊跃迁（special transition）或超常跃迁（extraordinary transition）；除已导出的数据外，还产生了无穷多个约束条件，但由于算子混合（operator mixing）随简并度增加而趋于复杂，若无额外输入则无法进一步解耦。

Abstract: The $\mathsf{O}(N)$ $\mathsf{BCFT}$ is analyzed in the large $N$ expansion in a generic bulk dimension $2<d+1<4$. Focus is on boundary conditions corresponding to the ordinary transition, however techniques used can be generalized to special or extraordinary transitions. We study the system of bulk $2$-pt functions $\langle φφ\rangle$, $\langle φ^2 φ^2\rangle$ and $\langle σσ\rangle$, where $σ$ is the Hubbard--Stratonovich field. They are expanded in bulk/boundary conformal partial waves. The coefficient functions of this expansion -- the spectral functions -- encode $\mathsf{BCFT}$ data and determine bulk/boundary conformal block expansions. We prove conjectures about boundary spectral functions in Dujava et al. [arXiv:2503.16345] and reproduce the bulk expansion of $\langle φφ\rangle$ in Giombi et al. [arXiv:2007.04955]. The bulk expansion of $\langleσσ\rangle$ is new and allows to extract the leading large $N$ expression for an unknown OPE coefficient $C_{σσσ^3}$ (the computation outputs as a byproduct also a mixing coefficient, which matches an existing result by Derkachov et al. [arXiv:hep-th/9705020], providing further support for the main result). Besides these derived data infinitely many constraints are produced, though due to operator mixing growing in complexity as degeneracy increases, they cannot be disentangled without further input.

### [233] [Entropy Quantization and Quasi-normal Modes of Dyonic Kerr-Sen Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14834)
*Muhammad Fitrah Alfian Rangga Sakti,Piyabut Burikham*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了双电荷Kerr-Sen黑洞内外视界的热力学性质，发现熵（面积）乘积与中心荷仅依赖角动量；通过热力学方法推导出对偶CFT的中心荷，并与Kerr-Newman黑洞对比，揭示了右移扇区的本质差异；进一步从CFT与多视界热力学的关系中，导出准正则模谱的解析表达式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索双电荷Kerr-Sen黑洞（dyonic Kerr-Sen black hole）内外视界热力学（thermodynamics）的基本性质，并利用Kerr/CFT对应（Kerr/CFT correspondence）研究其对偶共形场论（conformal field theory），以揭示黑洞微观自由度与全息对偶的普适性结构。

Method: 利用热力学关系（thermodynamic relations）分析内外视界的熵（entropy）与面积（area）乘积；基于二维共形场论（2D CFT）计算中心荷（central charge）；通过对比Kerr-Newman黑洞以及双电荷伸缩子黑洞（dyonic dilaton BH）的静态解，识别不同黑洞的CFT扇区差异；从CFT与多视界热力学的关系出发，推导准正则模（quasi-normal modes, QNM）谱的解析表达式。

Result: 熵（面积）乘积是普适的（universal），仅依赖黑洞的角动量（angular momentum）；中心荷同样仅由角动量决定；与Kerr-Newman黑洞对比，关键差异出现在CFT的右移扇区（right-moving sector）；双电荷伸缩子黑洞的静态解在热力学方法下也可产生非零中心荷；准正则模谱获得了以黑洞参数表示的解析形式。

Conclusion: 双电荷Kerr-Sen黑洞的热力学与CFT对偶表现出与角动量相关的普适性，不同黑洞类型在CFT右移扇区存在本质区别；热力学方法可有效衔接黑洞多视界热力学与全息对偶，并为准正则模谱提供解析构造。

Abstract: We explore the properties of inner and outer horizon thermodynamics of dyonic Kerr-Sen black hole (DKSBH). It is observed that the entropy (or area) product is universal, depending only on the angular momentum of the BH. We then proceed to study the dual conformal field theory~(CFT) in the Kerr/CFT correspondence using thermodynamic relations and compute the central charges from 2D CFT. The central charges are found to be universal with only angular momentum dependence. By comparing to Kerr-Newman BH, it is found that the essential difference is in the right-moving sector of the CFT. Interestingly, we can then explicitly produce the non-vanishing central charges related to its static solution, the dyonic dilaton BH, using the thermodynamic method. Moreover, from the CFT relations to multi-horizon thermodynamics, we find the analytical expression of the quasi-normal modes~(QNM) spectra in terms of BH parameters.

*Tuan Q. Do*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 考察de Sitter解在Einstein-Grisaru-Zanon引力（一种新近提出的四阶引力模型）中的稳定性。

Method: 基于Euler-Lagrange方程（Euler-Lagrange equations）的有效方法推导Einstein-Grisaru-Zanon引力对应的场方程；采用动力学系统方法（dynamical system method）进行稳定性分析。

Result: 推导所得的场方程中有一项与原始论文结果不一致，原因在于高阶导数项（higher-order derivative terms）之间存在差异；但de Sitter解（de Sitter solution）与原始论文一致，因为差异项在该解下为零。稳定性分析表明，无论de Sitter解代表宇宙暴胀相（inflationary phase）还是膨胀相（expanding phase），该解始终不稳定。

Conclusion: 本文的稳定性分析结果验证了原始论文中关于Einstein-Grisaru-Zanon引力de Sitter解稳定性的结论。

Abstract: In this paper, we would like to investigate the stability of de Sitter solution in the Einstein-Grisaru-Zanon gravity, which is a novel fourth-order gravity model considered recently in a paper [Phys. Lett. B {\bf 855} (2024) 138811]. As a result, we are able to derive the corresponding field equations for the Einstein-Grisaru-Zanon gravity by using an effective method based on the Euler-Lagrange equations. Unfortunately, one of the obtained field equations does not coincide with that derived in the original paper of the Einstein-Grisaru-Zanon gravity due to a gap between higher-order derivative terms. However, our de Sitter solution is still identical to one solved in the original paper of the Einstein-Grisaru-Zanon gravity due to the vanishing of the gap. Furthermore, a stability analysis based on the dynamical system method is performed to indicate that the obtained de Sitter solution is always unstable, no matter it presents an inflationary phase or expanding phase of universe. This result confirms the validity of stability investigation carried out in the original paper of the Einstein-Grisaru-Zanon gravity.

### [235] [The Holographic Multi-Entropy Cone](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15173)
*Xin-Xiang Ju,Yang Zhao*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文将全息熵锥（HEC）推广到全息多熵锥（HMEC），通过引入多熵坐标，证明了全息态在多熵空间中形成一个有理多面体锥，并确定了 n=3 和 n=4（含纯化器）HMEC 的所有 facet，得到七个基本全息多熵不等式轨道，同时提出了两个结构猜想。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准全息熵锥仅基于二分熵坐标描述全息态的熵约束，未涵盖多体纠缠（multi-partite entanglement）的高阶信息。本文通过引入多熵（multi-entropy）坐标，将框架推广至全息多熵锥，以更完整地刻画全息态的多体纠缠结构。

Method: 在全息熵锥的基础上添加多熵坐标，构造全息多熵锥；利用多收缩映射（multicontraction maps）作为全息多熵不等式（HMEI）的精确证书；通过分析有理多面体锥的 facet 结构，枚举并分类 n=3 和 n=4（含纯化器）情形下的基本不等式轨道。

Result: 全息态的多熵向量在多熵空间中构成一个有理多面体锥；多收缩映射可精确证明全息多熵不等式；确定了 n=3 和 n=4 HMEC 的所有 facet，获得七个基本全息多熵不等式轨道（n=3 两个，n=4 五个）。

Conclusion: 提出两个结构猜想：HEC 的 facet 不等式是 HMEC facet 不等式的凸组合；HMEC 的 facet 满足“平衡但不过度平衡”原则。这些结果为理解全息多体纠缠的几何约束提供了系统框架。

Abstract: We generalize the holographic entropy cone (HEC) to the holographic multi-entropy cone (HMEC) by adjoining multi-entropy coordinates to the standard bipartition entropy coordinates. We show that holographic states, through their multi-entropy vectors, form a rational polyhedral cone in multi-entropy space, and multicontraction maps provide exact certificates for holographic multi-entropy inequalities (HMEIs). We determine all facets of the $n=3,4$ HMECs, where $n$ includes the purifier, and obtain seven fundamental HMEI orbits: two for $n=3$ and five for $n=4$. We further propose two structural conjectures: HEC facet inequalities are convex combinations of HMEC facet inequalities, and HMEC facets obey a balanced-but-not-too-balanced principle.

### [236] [On the Schubert calculus of the quantum K-theory for partial flag manifolds: a 3d A-model perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15261)
*Zhihao Duan,Osama Khlaif,Hao Zou*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文进一步研究了部分旗流形（partial flag manifolds）$X \equiv {\rm Fl}(\boldsymbol{k};n)$ 的三维规范线性西格玛模型（3d gauged linear sigma model, 3d GLSM）与量子K-理论（quantum K-theory）之间的对应关系。作者利用舒伯特线缺陷（Schubert line defects）计算了2-点和3-点关联函数，将其解释为属-0 K-理论Gromov-Witten不变量，并推导了量子K-理论环中的K-理论Littlewood-Richardson系数。通过小$\beta$极限，还关联到二维GLSM与量子上同调（quantum cohomology）结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在将二维GLSM与量子上同调的对应关系提升到三维情形，探索三维GLSM与部分旗流形上量子K-理论之间的精确对偶，并验证最近构造的舒伯特线缺陷能否正确重现K-理论环结构。

Method: 理论框架采用三维GLSM，在$\mathbb{R}^2\times S^1_β$上紧化，利用半BPS线算子（Schubert line defects）对应K-理论环中的舒伯特类（Schubert classes）。使用代数几何算法计算2-点和3-点关联函数，并取小$\beta$极限过渡到二维GLSM。

Result: 计算得到的关联函数被解释为属-0 K-理论Gromov-Witten不变量，从而提取出量子K-理论环的K-理论Littlewood-Richardson系数。通过具体实例展示了这一对应关系，并在小$\beta$极限下计算了部分旗流形的量子上同调环关系，与文献已有结果一致。

Conclusion: 三维GLSM与量子K-理论之间的对应关系在部分旗流形情形下得到验证，舒伯特线缺陷提供了计算K-理论Gromov-Witten不变量的有效工具。该框架可通过小$\beta$极限一致地退化为二维量子上同调结果。

Abstract: We further investigate the 3d gauged linear sigma model (GLSM)/quantum K-theory correspondence for partial flag manifolds $X \equiv {\rm Fl}(\boldsymbol{k};n)$. This is a 3d uplift of the 2d GLSM/quantum cohomology correspondence with the 3d theory compactified on $\mathbb{R}^2\times S^1_β$. Recently, a set of half-BPS line operators, called Schubert line defects, were constructed that correspond to the Schubert classes in the K-theory ring of $X$. Utilizing algebro-geometric algorithms, we compute $2$-point and $3$-point correlation functions of these line operators in the 3d A-model regime of the theory. These are interpreted as genus-$0$ K-theoretic Gromov--Witten invariants, and they produce the K-theoretic Littlewood--Richardson coefficients of the quantum K-theory ring of $X$. We show how this works explicitly in examples. Taking the small $β$ limit, we apply these techniques to the resulting 2d GLSM. We explicitly compute the quantum cohomology ring relations of $X$ for some cases and match with existing results in the literature in examples.

### [237] [Generalized Schwarzian Dynamics from a Bulk-First BF Perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15270)
*H. T. Özer,Aytül Filiz*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文从一个体优先的BF理论视角出发，研究广义Schwarzian动力学的涌现机制。通过对二维BF引力的边界相空间及其Drinfeld-Sokolov约化进行分析，在sl(2,R)情形中恢复了标准Schwarzian作用量，并在sl(3,R)情形中通过第二和第三Wilczynski不变量获得了广义Schwarzian导数的高秩推广。该框架将广义Schwarzian动力学与Casimir荷、单值性数据和热力学结构直接联系起来。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究中广义Schwarzian动力学通常被当作独立的边界理论引入，缺乏从体理论出发的统一描述。本文旨在从二维BF引力出发，通过边界相空间的Drinfeld-Sokolov约化（Drinfeld-Sokolov reductions），建立广义Schwarzian动力学与体理论（BF理论）之间的直接联系。

Method: 从二维BF引力出发，分析其边界相空间并进行Drinfeld-Sokolov约化。对于sl(2,R)和sl(3,R)李代数情形，分别研究约化后的边界动力学，并利用Wilczynski不变量（Wilczynski invariants）构造广义Schwarzian导数的推广。进一步将射影不变量（projective invariants）与Casimir荷（Casimir charges）、单值性数据（monodromy data）及热力学性质联系起来。

Result: 在sl(2,R)情形下恢复了标准Schwarzian作用量；在sl(3,R)情形下得到了由第二和第三Wilczynski不变量控制的广义动力学，实现了Schwarzian导数的高秩推广。常数射影不变量决定了对应的Casimir扇区和单值性数据，进而组织整个理论的热力学结构。

Conclusion: 本文提供了一个统一的、体优先的描述框架，揭示了BF引力、渐近对称性约化（asymptotic symmetry reductions）、射影几何（projective geometry）与边界热力学（boundary thermodynamics）之间的直接联系。广义Schwarzian动力学来源于平坦BF联络及其伴随形式，而非作为独立的边界理论引入。

Abstract: We investigate the emergence of generalized Schwarzian dynamics from a bulk-first BF perspective. Starting from two-dimensional BF gravity, we analyze the associated boundary phase space and its Drinfeld-Sokolov reductions. For the sl(2,R) theory, we recover the ordinary Schwarzian action as the reduced boundary dynamics arising from a particular sector of the BF asymptotic phase space. We then extend this construction to sl(3,R), where the reduced dynamics is governed by the second and third Wilczynski invariants, providing a natural higher-rank generalization of the Schwarzian derivative. In this framework, generalized Schwarzian dynamics emerges directly from flat BF connections and their companion forms rather than being introduced as an independent boundary theory. We further relate the resulting projective invariants to Casimir charges, monodromy data, and generalized Schwarzian thermodynamics, including monodromy spectra and semiclassical thermodynamics. In particular, constant projective invariants determine the corresponding Casimir sectors and monodromy data, which in turn organize the thermodynamic structure of the theory. Our results provide a unified bulk-first description of Schwarzian and generalized Schwarzian dynamics and reveal a direct link between BF gravity, asymptotic symmetry reductions, projective geometry, and boundary thermodynamics.

We average the boundary energy and the outgoing flux over these two soft modes and obtain corrected balance equations for the temperature and chemical potential. We then use the corrected background to calculate the no-island and island entropies and the Page time shifts. We also study the possibility of black hole formation and gravitational wave background in this scenario. Result: 电荷通过增强有效整体张力（effective global tension）增加膜上自由度，从而提高饱和熵（saturation entropy）；标量源则通过降低红外区域附近的局域张力（effective local tension）减少自由度，抑制纠缠熵。饱和前的纠缠动力学表现出先二次增长（预局域热化阶段）后线性增长的行为。Page时间由热激发与膜自由度竞争决定：高温加速Page时间，丰富自由度则延迟Page时间。

Abstract: We investigate the entanglement dynamics and Page curve of a 2D brane Maxwell-Scalar (MS) black hole coupled to thermal baths in double holography. Computing the entanglement entropy via the island formula, we find that injecting electric charge and scalar source into the system produce opposite effects: the former increases the degrees of freedom (DOF) on the brane by enhancing the effective global tension, thereby raising the saturation entropy of the system; conversely, the latter reduces the DOF on the brane by lowering the effective local tension near the IR geometry, ultimately suppressing the entanglement. Despite the non-trivial backreaction from the matter fields, the pre-saturation entanglement dynamics remain robust. We identify an early-time quadratic growth corresponding to the pre-local-thermalization phase, which smoothly transitions into a late-time linear growth. Furthermore, the scale of the Page time is governed by a competition between thermal excitations and the brane DOF. Method: 通过构造Lax联络和经典r-矩阵的方式建立模型的可积性；底层代数被识别为sl(2,ℝ)李代数的直和（具有共享的嘉当（Cartan）子代数），构成一个Z-分次的非李马尔采夫代数（Malcev algebra）。

It is a direct sum of $sl(2, {\rm I\!R})$ Lie algebras with a shared common Cartan. A Malcev algebra is the tangent space at the identity of an analytic Moufang loop as a Lie algebra is the tangent space at the identity of a Lie group. We expect the model to be integrable at the quantum level. We also give a family of classically integrable models which are related to the Poisson-Boltzmann equation in two dimensions.

### [243] [Dressed Fock Spaces in Gauge Theory and Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15988)
*Sangmin Choi,Prahar Mitra*

TL;DR: 本文证明，四维规范理论（gauge theory）与引力理论（gravitational theory）中，Faddeev-Kulish dressing导致的多粒子态无法分解为张量积的问题，并非根本性缺陷，而是源于红外变量选取不当。通过引入辐射场的新零模（zero modes）并分离出渐近对称性（asymptotic symmetries）的Goldstone模（Goldstone modes），红外有限的多粒子态可以恢复标准的Fock空间分解（Fock-space factorisation）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者重新分析了红外发散（infrared divergence）的来源：真实的软发散由渐近对称性的Goldstone模复制；而库仑相（Coulomb phase）则由本文新引入的辐射场零模（zero modes of the radiative fields）复制。基于这些新的红外变量，对多粒子态进行重新构造。

Result: 在新变量下，红外有限（infrared-finite）的穿戴多粒子态恢复了标准的Fock空间分解，即可分解为穿戴单粒子态（dressed single-particle states）的张量积。

Conclusion: Faddeev-Kulish dressing导致的多粒子态Fock空间分解失效并非本质问题，而是源于红外变量选取不当。合适的红外变量（渐近对称性的Goldstone模与辐射场新零模）可以恢复该分解。

Abstract: Four-dimensional gauge and gravitational theories exhibit long-range interactions that require asymptotic particles to be dressed by clouds of soft photons and gravitons. Faddeev-Kulish dressings render scattering amplitudes infrared-finite, but the resulting multi-particle states do not factorise into tensor products of dressed one-particle states. We show that this loss of Fock-space factorisation is not fundamental, but reflects an inappropriate choice of infrared variables. The real soft divergence is reproduced by the Goldstone modes of asymptotic symmetries, while the Coulomb phase is reproduced by new zero modes of the radiative fields that we introduce here. In these variables, infrared-finite dressed multi-particle states admit the usual Fock-space factorisation into single-particle dressed states.

### [244] [The O(4)-breaking bubble](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16024)
*Guy Avraham,Kfir Blum,Omri Rosner,Isaac G. Smith*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在标量场论（scalar field theory）中，假真空衰变（false vacuum decay）长期被认为由Coleman的O(4)对称反弹解（bounce）主导；尽管数学上存在O(4)破缺解的非构造性存在证明（non-constructive existence proofs），但这些解的具体形式及其物理内涵一直未知。本文旨在填补这一空白，显式构造一个非径向（nonradial）的O(4)破缺解。

Method: 采用一个下方有界（bounded-below）的标量场势能 $V(φ)=\frac{m^2}{2}φ^2-\fracλ{4}φ^4+\frac{g}{6}φ^6$，构造了一个非径向解：两个符号相反的气泡管（bubble-tubes）分别缠绕在正交环（orthogonal rings）上，该解在O(2)×O(2)旋转与一个交换两环的宇称变换（parity）组合下保持不变。

Result: 成功构造了该O(4)破缺的假真空衰变解；该解在$t=0$切片上为现实时间演化（real time evolution）提供了合法的柯西数据（Cauchy data），并且支持奇数个不稳定形变模（unstable deformation modes）。

Conclusion: 该构造表明，在标量场理论的假真空衰变中，存在有别于传统O(4)对称反弹解的新型非径向解，其动力学性质（由柯西数据和奇数不稳定模表征）值得进一步研究。

Abstract: False vacuum decay in field theory is thought to be dominated by Coleman's O(4)-symmetric bounce, the minimum action nontrivial solution of the imaginary time equations of motion. Beyond the bounce, non-constructive existence proofs of O(4)-breaking solutions are available in the mathematics literature, but the solutions themselves, and their physics, have remained unknown. Considering the simple, bounded-below, scalar field potential $V(φ)=\frac{m^2}{2}φ^2-\fracλ{4}φ^4+\frac{g}{6}φ^6$, we construct a nonradial solution explicitly: two bubble-tubes of opposite sign wrapping orthogonal rings, invariant under ${\rm O}(2)\times{\rm O}(2)$ rotations combined with a parity that exchanges the rings. The solution admits valid Cauchy data for real time evolution from a $t=0$ slice, and supports an odd number of unstable deformation modes.

### [245] [Effect of $ξRφ^2$ non-minimal coupling on gravitational light bending](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16406)
*Ayan Kumar Naskar,Avijit Sen Majumder,Sourav Bhattacharya*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文利用微扰量子引力（perturbative quantum gravity）计算到单圈阶，研究了有质量物体在曲率-标量非最小耦合（curvature-scalar non-minimal coupling）$\sqrt{-g}\xi R \phi^2$ 存在时对无质量场的弯曲效应。在eikonal近似下，发现弯曲角出现在${\cal O}(\xi G^2)$阶，且与碰撞参数$b$的-7次方成正比，与标准最小耦合情形存在定性差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将质量物体建模为非相对论性有质量标量场$\phi$（例如恒星），通过引力子（graviton）交换计算无质量标量与光子对该物体的2-2散射过程。假设耦合参数$\xi$和弯曲角都很小，采用eikonal近似（eikonal approximation）计算弯曲角至${\cal O}(\xi G^2)$阶。树图阶${\cal O}(\xi G)$未产生弯曲，因此${\cal O}(\xi G^2)$结果成为领头阶。

Result: 非最小耦合顶点在结构上定性不同于标准最小耦合顶点（如$\sqrt{G} h_{\mu\nu} T^{\mu\nu}$）：前者包含引力子的显式动量而非标量的动量，与后者形成互补。计算得到的弯曲角行为约为$\sim b^{-7}$，其中$b$为碰撞参数（impact parameter）。

Conclusion: 非最小耦合情形下的弯曲角定性区别于标准最小耦合情形，表明该耦合机制在引力散射中可产生显著不同的物理效应。该结果有助于进一步理解非最小耦合在量子引力理论中的角色。

Abstract: We investigate the bending of massless fields by a massive object in the presence of a curvature-scalar $\sqrt{-g}ξR φ^2$ non-minimal coupling up to one loop, using the perturbative quantum gravity computations. It is well known that without such coupling a self interacting scalar field theory cannot be renormalised in the presence of gravity. The massive object is modelled by a massive scalar $φ$, and it is assumed to be non-relativistic, e.g., a star. We compute the 2-2 scattering of massless scalar and photons off this object via graviton exchanges. Assuming both $ξ$ and the bending angle to be small, we use the eikonal approximation to compute the angle up to ${\cal O}(ξG^2)$. At tree level $({\cal O}(ξG))$ we find no bending, and hence the ${\cal O}(ξG^2)$ result happens to be leading in this case. The non-minimal vertices are qualitatively different from that of the standard minimal ones, e.g. $ \sqrt{G} h_{μν} T^{μν}$, as the former contains explicit momenta of the gravitons instead of the scalar, complementing the second. The bending angle is found to behave like $\sim b^{-7}$, where $b$ is the impact parameter. We have emphasised the qualitative differences of our results from that of the well studied minimal case.

### [246] [Complexified Virasoro Flow and the Logarithmic Graviton at the Chiral Point](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16444)
*Yannick Mvondo-She*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过复化Virasoro演化（complexified Virasoro evolution）为拓扑质量引力（topologically massive gravity）在手征点（chiral point）出现的对数引力子（logarithmic graviton）及其对应的Jordan结构提供了几何解释，揭示了径向演化、时间演化、Jordan混合（Jordan mixing）与对数单值性（logarithmic monodromy）可统一理解为单一复化Virasoro流的不同表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拓扑质量引力在手征点处出现简并对数模式，其与AdS₃/LCFT₂对偶中边界对数共形场论（logarithmic conformal field theory, LCFT）的对数伙伴对应，但该Jordan结构的几何起源尚不清晰，需要发展一种几何解释。

Method: 基于Grumiller–Johansson给出的对数引力子，分析其对应对数系数在AdS₃边界附近的渐近形式；引入复化参数s=ρ+iτ，并利用Virasoro生成元L₀作用于秩二Jordan胞腔（rank-two Jordan cell）的指数化形式e^{sL₀}=e^{sh}(1+sN)，展示其如何重现对数扇区（logarithmic sector）的特征性对数混合（logarithmic mixing）与单值性。

Result: 对数引力子的对数系数渐近为y(τ,ρ)=−s+ln2+O(e^{−2ρ})；Jordan演化e^{sL₀}=e^{sh}(1+sN)准确再现对数混合行为；解析延拓s→s+2πi生成相应的对数单值性；径向演化、时间演化、Jordan混合与对数单值性可视为单一复化Virasoro流的不同侧面。

Conclusion: 该分析为对数共形场论中不可分解结构（indecomposable structures）提供了几何解读，为AdS₃/LCFT₂框架下的对数引力子提供了新的理论视角。

Abstract: At the chiral point of topologically massive gravity, the massive graviton becomes degenerate with the left-moving graviton, leading to the appearance of a logarithmic mode and a corresponding rank-two Jordan structure. This logarithmic graviton plays a central role in the conjectured AdS$_3$/LCFT$_2$ correspondence, where it has been widely interpreted as the bulk counterpart of a logarithmic partner in the putative boundary logarithmic conformal field theory. In this work, we develop a geometric interpretation of this Jordan structure based on complexified Virasoro evolution. Starting from the logarithmic graviton of Grumiller and Johansson, we show that its logarithmic coefficient \[ y(τ,ρ) =
-iτ-\ln\coshρ\] admits, near the AdS$_3$ boundary, the asymptotic form \[ y(τ,ρ) =
-s+\ln2+\mathcal O(e^{-2ρ}), \qquad s=ρ+iτ. \] The same complex parameter naturally appears in the exponentiation of the Virasoro generator $L_0$ acting on a rank-two Jordan cell, \[ L_0=h\mathbf1+N, \qquad N^2=0, \] for which \[ e^{sL_0} =
e^{sh}(1+sN). \] We show that the resulting Jordan evolution reproduces the characteristic logarithmic mixing of the logarithmic sector, while analytic continuation $s\rightarrow s+2πi$ generates the corresponding logarithmic monodromy. From this perspective, radial evolution, temporal evolution, Jordan mixing, and logarithmic monodromy may be viewed as different manifestations of a single complexified Virasoro flow. The analysis suggests a geometric interpretation of the indecomposable structures characteristic of logarithmic conformal field theory and offers a new perspective on the logarithmic graviton within the conjectural AdS$_3$/LCFT$_2$ framework.

</details>

The setup is realised by gluing two AdS5 pp-wave spacetimes across a three-brane. As an application, we analyse localised beams of light and their gravitational backreaction. Abstract: This proceedings contribution summarizes the main results of the original paper arXiv:2506.18988. In this work, we explore a related setup where the addition of an orientifold plane modifies the cascade structure: the RG flow now consists of a finite number of steps, originating from a UV fixed point with a finite number of degrees of freedom. ### [249] [Holographic study of heavy quark potential, free energy, and running coupling in backgrounds with broken translational symmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16640)
*Wenxing Cheng,Zi-qiang Zhang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过五维渐近AdS时空（含平移对称性破缺）研究重夸克观测量，发现化学势和动量弛豫参数均会削弱色相互作用并促进夸克偶素解离，但作用机制不同：化学势主导色屏蔽，β主要影响等离子体熵。有限重子密度对束缚的抑制强于动量耗散。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用五维渐近反德西特（asymptotically AdS）时空中的爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-轴子（Einstein-Maxwell-axion）引力模型，引入两个尺度参数：化学势μ（对应有限重子数密度）和平移对称性破缺参数β（对应动量弛豫）。通过有限温度和零温度下的数值模拟，计算静态夸克间势能、热自由能和跑动耦合。经重整化处理后提取色屏蔽长度和解离尺度。

Result: μ和β均会削弱色相互作用并促进夸克偶素解离，但机制不同：μ主导色屏蔽并显著修改重夸克势能和跑动耦合；β主要影响等离子体熵并修正热自由能。零温度下热贡献消失，重整化自由能退化为类库仑形式的介质修正静态势。在所有温度区间，有限重子密度对Q\bar{Q}束缚的抑制作用远强于动量耗散。

Conclusion: 本文厘清了色相互作用与热力学性质的介质修正机制，在稠密耗散等离子体中为重夸克探针建立了自洽的图像，并给出了夸克偶素在重离子碰撞中的现象学含义。

Abstract: We study heavy-quark observables including static interquark potential, thermal free energy and running coupling via a five-dimensional asymptotically AdS spacetime with translational symmetry breaking (TSB). The Einstein-Maxwell-axion geometry involves two scales: chemical potential $μ$ for finite baryon density, and TSB parameter $β$ for momentum relaxation. Numerical simulations at finite and zero temperature reveal that both $μ$ and $β$ weaken color interactions and facilitate quarkonium dissociation in strongly coupled quark-gluon plasmas through different mechanisms. The chemical potential dominates color screening and modifies the heavy-quark potential and running coupling, while $β$ mainly affects plasma entropy and corrects thermal free energy. At zero temperature, thermal contributions vanish, and the renormalized free energy becomes a medium-modified static potential with an approximate Coulombic form. Finite baryon density suppresses $Q\bar{Q}$ binding much more strongly than momentum dissipation at all temperatures. We extract the color screening length and dissociation scale, and discuss phenomenological implications for quarkonium in heavy-ion collisions. This work clarifies medium correction mechanisms for color interactions and thermodynamics, and presents a consistent picture for heavy-quark probes in dense dissipative plasmas.

Method: 利用斜率为$\nu=u/m$的广义仿射Springer纤维$Sp_ν(\tilde{g},f)$的几何结构；每个非空$C^*$-不动点集由双陪集（double coset）$\tilde w\in W_ν\backslash\tilde{W}/W_f$标记，给出单模（simple modules）的最高权，而不动点簇的维数编码额外的非半单结构（对数模，logarithmic modules）。

The central proposal is that each non-empty $C^*$-fixed locus, labeled by a double coset $\tilde w\in W_ν\backslash\tilde{W}/W_f$, gives rise to simple modules whose highest weight is determined by the map $\tilde w\mapsto\tilde w(kΛ_0+\tildeρ)-\tildeρ$, while the dimension of the fixed variety encodes additional non-semisimple structure (logarithmic modules). We verify this correspondence in numerous examples, including $D_4$, $E_6$, $E_8$, and twisted theories of type $^3D_4$ and $^2A_3$, where our geometric counting reproduces known results for both admissible and non-admissible $W$-algebras.

*Davide Cassani,Enrico Turetta*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种高效方法，通过等变积分与环形图分解，计算五维超引力中具有环面U(1)³对称性和一般拓扑的超对称黑鞍解（black saddle solutions）的在壳作用量，包括高阶导数修正，并推导了黑鞍作用量与极值解Wald熵的新结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超对称黑鞍解的在壳作用量（on-shell action）计算对于理解超引力中的黑洞热力学和熵公式至关重要，但现有方法在处理一般拓扑和高阶导数修正时效率较低，亟需一个更系统的计算框架。

Method: 该方法将异常多项式六形式（anomaly polynomial six-form）的等变积分（equivariant integration）分解为环形图（toric diagram）的单纯锥（simplicial cones），并将在壳作用量表示为各锥顶点的局域贡献之和。

Result: 该框架不仅简化了近期文献中已有表达式的推导，还给出了黑鞍解在壳作用量和极值解（extremal solutions）Wald熵（Wald entropy）的新预测，涵盖渐近AdS₅与渐近平直两种情形，并成功应用于黑洞、黑环（black rings）和黑透镜（black lenses）等例子。

Conclusion: 该方法为五维超引力中多种拓扑黑鞍解的在壳作用量和Wald熵提供统一、高效的计算方案，并衍生出新的理论预测。

Abstract: We consider five-dimensional supergravity coupled to vector multiplets, gauged or ungauged, and propose an efficient method to evaluate the on-shell action of supersymmetric black saddle solutions with toric ${\rm U}(1)^3$ symmetry and general topology, explicitly known or just assumed to exist, including higher-derivative corrections. This is equivalent to equivariant integration of the anomaly polynomial six-form over simplicial cones obtained by decomposing the toric diagram of the solution. The on-shell action is then expressed as a sum over contributions localized at the tip of each cone. We obtain a simple derivation of recently calculated expressions as well as new predictions, both for the on-shell action of the black saddles and the Wald entropy of the related extremal solutions. These may be asymptotically AdS$_5$ or asymptotically flat. As examples, we discuss black holes, black rings and black lenses, including a black hole in the background of a topological soliton.

</details>


### [256] [Solutions in Liouville theory on dS and AdS backgrounds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17025)
*Damir Sadekov*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文在非动态背景（non-dynamical background）下，利用嵌入空间形式（embedding-space formalism）与辅助零向量（auxiliary null vector），导出了$D$维德西特（de Sitter）和反德西特（anti-de Sitter）时空上刘维尔型标量场理论（Liouville-type scalar field theory）的一阶可积方程，并获得了两种解析解类。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在弯曲时空背景下精确求解非线性标量场理论（nonlinear scalar field theory）是理论物理中的重要问题；作者希望找到刘维尔型标量场在德西特和反德西特几何上的精确解析解，并比较两类时空中的物理性质差异。

Method: 采用嵌入空间形式，引入辅助零向量，将刘维尔方程转化为一阶Bäcklund型方程（Bäcklund-like equations），通过可积性条件（integrability condition）获得标量场的解。

Result: 得到两类解析解类；这些解在德西特和反德西特时空中表现出不同的物理性质。

Conclusion: 嵌入空间形式可以有效地求解德西特和反德西特背景上的刘维尔型标量场理论，且其解在两种几何背景下的物理行为存在显著差异。

Abstract: We find exact solutions of a Liouville-type scalar field theory on $D$-dimensional de Sitter and anti-de Sitter backgrounds, treating the geometry as nondynamical. Using the embedding-space formalism with an auxiliary null vector, we derive first-order (Bäcklund-like) equations whose integrability yields the solution of the Liouville equation for the scalar field. This method produces two classes of analytic solutions, whose physical properties are different for de Sitter and anti-de Sitter spacetimes.

</details>
