### [257] [Interlayer pairing mechanism for bilayer nickelate superconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15298)
*Jiangfan Wang,Yi-feng Yang*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文综述了双层镍氧化物超导体（bilayer nickelate superconductors）的理论研究进展，涵盖关键的电子结构特征、理论模型、强关联层间配对机制以及正常态与超导态的多重物理行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Ruddlesden-Popper 双层镍氧化物在高压及常压条件下超导电性的发现开启了非常规超导研究的新范式，亟需对相关理论进展进行系统性梳理。

Method: 基于关键实验观测，归纳了杂化电子结构、轨道依赖电子关联、Hund耦合与强层间磁耦合等物理要素；引入了双层双轨道Hubbard模型及其最小t-J变体；从原子极限层间价键图像出发，阐述了基于不同极限考虑的强关联层间配对机制，并重点分析了杂化机制（hybridization mechanism）。

Result: 分析了配对对称性、超导临界温度Tc对内外参数的依赖、正常态中的费米液体（Fermi liquid）、非费米液体（non-Fermi liquid）、弱绝缘体及赝能隙（pseudogap）行为；讨论了压力调控、氧含量和氧空位诱导的Kondo散射效应；简要覆盖了基于费米面嵌套（Fermi surface nesting）的自旋涨落弱关联理论。

Conclusion: 双层镍氧化物超导体展现出丰富的强关联物理图景，杂化机制为理解其层间配对提供了重要理论框架，同时弱关联理论亦具有参考意义。

Abstract: The discovery of superconductivity in Ruddlesden-Popper bilayer nickelates under both high pressure and ambient conditions has opened a new paradigm for exploring unconventional superconductivity. This review provides a brief survey of theoretical progress on bilayer nickelate superconductors. Drawing from the key experimental observations, we summarize essential physical ingredients including the hybridized Ni-3$d_{x^2-y^2}$ and 3$d_{z^2}$ electronic structure, orbital-dependent electronic correlation, Hund's coupling, and strong interlayer magnetic coupling. The fundamental theoretical models including the bilayer two-orbital Hubbard model and its minimal $t$-$J$ variants are introduced. Starting from the atomic-limit interlayer valence bond picture of the half-filled $d_{z^2}$ orbital, we elaborate on strong correlation interlayer pairing mechanisms based on different limiting considerations. Specific emphasis is placed on the hybridization mechanism, where the $d_{z^2}$ local singlet pairs provide the pairing energy and their hybridization with itinerant $d_{x^2-y^2}$ promotes superconducting phase coherence. We further analyze the pairing symmetry, the dependence of $T_c$ on various internal and external parameters, the nontrivial normal state properties including the Fermi liquid, non-Fermi liquid, weakly insulating and pseudogap behaviors. Effects of pressure tuning, oxygen content, and Kondo scattering induced by oxygen vacancies are also discussed. Finally, weak correlation theories based on spin fluctuations associated with Fermi surface nesting are briefly covered.

</details>


### [258] [Electronic structure trends in La$_{2}R$Ni$_2$O$_7$ ($R=$ Pr, Nd, Sm) from first-principles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16195)
*Yi-Feng Zhao,Antia S. Botana*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理计算，系统研究了不同稀土元素（Pr、Nd、Sm）掺杂对La₃Ni₂O₇晶体结构和电子性质的影响，发现化学压力导致晶格体积减小、压力诱导的结构相变与超导电性出现大致同步，并揭示了面内与面外跳跃积分的不同变化趋势，为理解RP型镍基超导体中掺杂效应与超导转变温度（T_c）的关系提供了微观见解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期在Sm掺杂La₃Ni₂O₇单晶中报道了高达96 K的超导转变温度，这一实验发现促使研究者系统探索不同稀土元素掺杂对该体系晶体结构与电子性质的影响，以期理解掺杂效应与超导电性之间的关联。

Method: 采用第一性原理（first-principles）计算方法，系统比较了未掺杂与不同稀土元素（R = Pr, Nd, Sm）掺杂的La₃Ni₂O₇的晶体结构和电子性质，分析了晶格参数、能带结构以及跳跃积分（hopping integrals）的变化。

Result: 从Pr到Sm掺杂，晶格体积（volume）逐渐减小，体现了化学压力（chemical pressure）效应。所有掺杂体系中均发现了压力诱导的四方对称性结构相变，该相变与超导电性的出现大致同步，并伴随费米能级处平坦的d_{z^2}能带出现。随着稀土离子半径减小，面内主导跳跃积分增大，而面外跳跃积分却因顶角Ni-O_{\rm rocksalt}键长缩短而减小。

Conclusion: 稀土掺杂通过化学压力调控晶格和电子结构，对RP型镍基超导体的超导转变温度（T_c）产生重要影响；面内与面外跳跃积分的不同变化趋势为理解掺杂效应提供了微观层面的关键信息。

Abstract: The discovery of superconductivity in bilayer La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$ under pressure has sparked tremendous attention on Ruddlesden-Popper (RP) nickelates. Recently, a higher superconducting transition temperature of 96 K was reported in Sm-doped La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$ single crystals at $\sim$ 22 GPa. Motivated by this experimental observation, we systematically explore the crystal structure and electronic properties of La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$ doped with different rare-earth elements in comparison to the undoped counterpart. As expected due to the effect of chemical pressure, we find that the volume of La$_{2}$$R$Ni$_2$O$_7$ ($R=$ Pr, Nd, Sm) progressively decreases with doping from Pr to Sm. We further find a pressure-induced structural transition to tetragonal symmetry that approximately coincides with the emergence of superconductivity in all cases. This transition is characterized by the emergence of flat $d_{z^2}$ bands at the Fermi level in the electronic structure. Despite subtle distinctions in the electronic structure between undoped and $R$-doped La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$, an increase in the dominant planar hopping is obtained as the $R$ size decreases. In contrast, the out-of-plane hopping decreases (in spite of the $c$ lattice constant compression), due to the decrease in the apical Ni-O$_{\rm rocksalt}$ bond length. Our findings provide further microscopic insights into the effects of $R$-doping in the electronic structure of RP nickelate superconductors in connection to $T_c$.

</details>


### [259] [Tuning superconductivity and charge density wave order by next-nearest-neighbor hopping integral in honeycomb Holstein model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16260)
*Hongxing Liu,Lufeng Zhang,Tianxing Ma*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该论文利用无偏行列式量子蒙特卡洛（determinant quantum Monte Carlo）模拟，研究了蜂窝晶格Holstein模型中超导（superconductivity）与电荷密度波（charge density wave）序之间的竞争关系，发现次近邻跳跃（\(t^{\prime}\)）通过调节电子-声子耦合强度与填充依赖效应，可分别增强或抑制这两类有序相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在蜂窝晶格（honeycomb lattice）Holstein模型中，超导配对与电荷密度波序之间的相互竞争机制，并揭示次近邻跳跃参数（\(t^{\prime}\)）对该竞争关系的调控作用。

Method: 采用无偏行列式量子蒙特卡洛（determinant quantum Monte Carlo）方法，对包含次近邻跳跃（\(t^{\prime}\)）的蜂窝晶格Holstein模型进行数值模拟。

Result: 在弱电子-声子耦合（weak electron-phonon coupling）区域，有限的负\(t^{\prime}\)增强了范霍夫填充（van Hove fillings）附近的\(s\)-波超导配对磁化率（\(s\)-wave superconducting pairing susceptibility）；在中等电子-声子耦合强度下，\(t^{\prime}\)抑制超导并促进电荷密度波序。\(t^{\prime}\)对电荷密度波的影响具有填充依赖性：在半填充（half filling）时抑制电荷密度波，在范霍夫奇点（van Hove singularities）附近则增强该有序相。

Conclusion: 光谱分析（spectral analysis）显示低温下能隙（gap）打开，表明超导序与电荷密度波序之间存在竞争关系，该竞争由电子-声子耦合介导，并可通过\(t^{\prime}\)进行调控。

Abstract: By using unbiased determinant quantum Monte Carlo simulations, we investigate the interplay between superconductivity and charge density wave order in the Holstein model on a honeycomb lattice with next-nearest-neighbor hopping \(t^{\prime}\).
  We find that a finite negative \(t^{\prime}\) enhances \(s\)-wave superconducting pairing susceptibility near the van Hove fillings in the weak electron-phonon coupling regime, while it suppresses superconductivity and promotes charge density wave order at intermediate electron-phonon coupling strengths.
  The effect of \(t^{\prime}\) on a charge density wave is filling-dependent: It suppresses the charge density wave at half filling but enhances it near the van Hove singularities.
  A spectral analysis reveals the opening of a gap at low temperatures, highlighting the competitive relationship between superconducting and charge density wave orders mediated by electron-phonon coupling and tuned by \(t^{\prime}\).

</details>


### [260] [Non-stationary longitudinal Josephson effect in electron-hole bilayers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16338)
*O. M. Konstantynov,S. I. Shevchenko*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文研究了双层系统中空间分离的电子-空穴配对导致的非稳态纵向约瑟夫森效应（non-stationary longitudinal Josephson effect），分析了高密度（类超导体）和低密度（激子玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚）两种极限下的隧穿电流特性，揭示了不同密度区间内准粒子、超流和干涉贡献的差异行为，以及非正弦电流-相位关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索电子-空穴双层系统中空间分离配对下的非稳态约瑟夫森效应，特别是沿层方向施加外电压时，弱耦合电子-空穴凝聚体之间的隧穿电流行为。

Method: 采用隧穿哈密顿方法（tunneling Hamiltonian approach）推导隧穿电流的准粒子（quasiparticle）、超导（superconducting）和干涉（interference）贡献表达式，并分别分析高密度与低密度两种极限情形。

Result: 在高密度极限下，零温时准粒子和干涉电流在阈值电压以下消失，仅剩超流（supercurrent）；在低密度极限下，集体激发的无能隙（gapless）谱导致即使零温也存在有限耗散贡献，使约瑟夫森振荡（Josephson oscillations）出现阻尼。当空间分离隧穿势垒间距超过相干长度（coherence length）时，各势垒处发生相位跳跃，导致电子和空穴势垒两端的电压振荡及非正弦的电流-相位关系。

Conclusion: 高密度与低密度区域在约瑟夫森效应上表现出本质不同的行为：前者类似传统超导体，后者因无能隙激发谱而产生耗散与振荡阻尼。空间分离势垒结构引入额外的相位跳跃，导致电压振荡和非正弦电流-相位关系，为理解电子-空穴配对系统的非平衡输运提供了理论基础。

Abstract: The non-stationary longitudinal Josephson effect in bilayer systems with pairing of spatially separated electrons and holes is investigated. The tunneling current between two (right and left) weakly coupled electron-hole condensates is analyzed in the presence of an external voltage applied along the layers. Two limiting regimes are considered: the high-density regime, where pairing occurs in momentum space similarly to conventional superconductors, and the low-density regime corresponding to a Bose-Einstein condensate of spatially indirect excitons. Using the tunneling Hamiltonian approach, expressions for the quasiparticle, superconducting and interference contributions to the tunneling current are derived. It is shown that in the high-density limit the quasiparticle and interference currents vanish at zero temperature below a threshold voltage determined by the energy gap, so that only the supercurrent remains. In contrast, in the low-density regime the gapless spectrum of collective excitations leads to finite dissipative contributions even at zero temperature, resulting in damping of Josephson oscillations. For spatially separated tunneling barriers with distance exceeding the coherence length, phase jumps occur at each barrier, resulting in voltage oscillations across the electron and hole barriers and a non-sinusoidal current-phase relation governed by the critical currents of the two barriers.

</details>


### [261] [Vortex-core size and quantum geometry in flat-band superconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16536)
*M. Özkurt,M. Iskin*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文研究Mielke棋盘晶格上吸引Hubbard模型的平带超导体实空间涡旋结构，通过量子度量（quantum metric）推导出相干长度（coherence length）的闭式表达式，发现涡旋核心尺寸由平带量子几何主导，且在半满时最小，与传统BCS图像定性不同。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解平带超导体中涡旋结构的形成机制，特别是传统BCS理论中依赖费米面（Fermi surface）和动能机制的相干长度描述在平带系统中是否仍然适用，探索量子几何（quantum geometry）在其中的作用。

Method: 采用动量空间平均场分析（mean-field analysis）推导相干长度的闭式表达式，该表达式依赖于布洛赫态（Bloch states）的量子度量和粒子-空穴对称配对密度（particle-hole-symmetric pair density）；在有限圆盘上通过自洽Bogoliubov-de Gennes（BdG）计算验证该预测。

Result: 相干长度在半满时最小，向能带边缘方向随配对密度消失而发散，且仅对数依赖于相互作用强度；这些特征与依赖费米面和动能配对输运机制的传统BCS图像存在本质差异，涡旋核心尺寸由量子度量编码的虚带间过程（virtual interband processes）产生的几何配对质量（geometric pair mass）主导。

Conclusion: 涡旋核心是平带量子几何在实空间中的直接体现，揭示了平带超导体中量子几何而非费米面决定涡旋结构这一全新物理图像。

Abstract: We investigate the real-space vortex structure of a flat-band superconductor described by the attractive Hubbard model on the Mielke checkerboard lattice. Using a momentum-space mean-field analysis, we derive a closed-form expression for the coherence length in terms of the quantum metric of the Bloch states and a particle-hole-symmetric pair density. Self-consistent Bogoliubov-de Gennes calculations on a finite disk confirm this prediction across a wide range of fillings and interaction strengths. The coherence length is minimized at half filling, diverges toward both band edges as the pair density vanishes, and depends only logarithmically on the interaction strength. These features differ qualitatively from the conventional BCS picture, which relies on a well-defined Fermi surface and a kinetic mechanism for pair transport. Instead, the vortex-core size is governed by a geometric pair mass arising from virtual interband processes encoded in the quantum metric. Our results establish the vortex core as a direct real-space manifestation of flat-band quantum geometry.

</details>


### [262] [Effect of the hyperbolic photon mode on the metal insulator transition in a proximate material](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16665)
*Patrick A. Lee*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文研究了六方氮化硼(hBN)中双曲模式(HM)的特性，发现其零点涨落电场可达MV/cm量级，并探讨了将该模式应用于Mott相变材料时对金属-绝缘体相变的调控效应，指出该效应随距离迅速衰减，仅影响数个原子层。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究双曲模式(HM)是否能够通过其巨大的零点涨落电场来调控邻近材料的物性，特别是对处于Mott转变附近材料的金属-绝缘体相变产生显著影响。

Method: 首先计算了双曲模式(HM)的光子态密度(photon density of states)，并由此得到均方根电场(RMS electric field)的零点涨落(zero point fluctuation)。随后，将处于Mott转变(Mott transition)附近的材料直接放置在具有双曲模式的六方氮化硼(hBN)基底上，通过解析或数值手段计算相变位移。

Result: 双曲模式(HM)中零点涨落的均方根电场可达到MV/cm量级，与太赫兹(THz)泵浦-探测实验中使用的最大电场相当。将材料置于hBN上后，金属-绝缘体相变(metal-insulator transition)会出现显著位移，但该效应随距离急剧衰减，仅能影响少数几个原子层(monolayers)。

Conclusion: 双曲模式(HM)提供的强电场确实能够调控邻近材料的量子相变，但由于作用距离极短，仅适用于超薄层材料体系。文中给出了若干相关候选材料的具体估算与建议。

Abstract: The hyperbolic mode (HM) refers to a polariton mode where the dielectric function is negative in some direction of propagation. Within a frequency window the light occupies a greatly expanded region in momentum space. We compute the photon density of states and find that the zero point fluctuation in the RMS electric field can reach $MV/cm$, comparable to the largest field used in pump probe experiments in the THz scale. The HM in hexagonal Boron Nitride (hBN) has been under intense study and we consider placing a material that is near the Mott transition directly on top hBN. We find that a substantial shift in the metal-insulator transition is possible, but the effect decays rapidly with distance, so that only a few monolayers are affected. We provide estimates and suggestions for a number of materials of interest.

</details>


### [263] [Possible high temperature superconductivity induced by coupling to proximate hyperbolic photon modes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16674)
*Zhiyu Dong,Patrick A. Lee*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文研究了六方氮化硼（hBN）中双曲模式（hyperbolic mode, HM）与金属直接接触时的物理效应，发现该模式导致波函数和速度的显著重整化，并通过类似Anderson-Morel机制的能量空间配对过程实现高温超导，即使在小耦合常数下也能获得很高的超导转变温度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 六方氮化硼（hexagonal Boron Nitride, hBN）中的双曲模式（hyperbolic mode, HM）近年来受到广泛关注，但将金属直接置于其顶部后物理性质是否受到强烈影响尚不清楚，本文旨在探索这一耦合体系的独特物理效应。

Method: 通过类比电子-声子耦合问题，但聚焦于HM模式的纵向（longitudinal）特性，考虑由时间依赖的电荷涨落（time dependent charge fluctuations）驱动的耦合机制，引入无量纲耦合常数（dimensionless coupling constant）λ₀来控制效应，并采用类似Anderson-Morel机制但在能量空间（energy space）而非频率空间（frequency space）的配对过程进行理论分析。

Result: 发现HM模式导致波函数和速度的显著重整化（velocity renormalization）；虚拟交换（virtual exchange）HM产生排斥相互作用，但由于其强烈的能量依赖性，可以通过能量空间中的Anderson-Morel类似机制实现配对；有效配对相互作用估算表明，即使在小λ₀（理论可控区域）下，也能实现非常高的超导转变温度（T_c）。

Conclusion: 基于实际参数估算，该体系具有实现高温超导的潜力，为极化绝缘体（polar insulator）与金属界面的超导研究提供了新方向。

Abstract: The hyperbolic mode (HM) refers to a polariton mode in a polar insulator where the dielectric function is negative in some direction of propagation. Within a frequency window the light occupies a greatly expanded region in momentum space. The HM in hexagonal Boron Nitride (hBN) has been under intense study and we consider placing a metal directly on top hBN and ask whether its physical properties can be strongly affected. While the problem resembles superficially the electron phonon coupling problem, there are important differences. Due to the longitudinal nature of the HM mode the coupling is driven by time dependent charge fluctuations which results in a coupling that strongly increases with the energy difference of the initial and final states. We find a significant modification of the wavefunction and velocity renormalization and we identify the dimensionless coupling constant $λ_0$ that controls this effect. The virtual exchange of HM leads to a repulsive interaction. However, due to its strong energy dependence, pairing is possible by a process analogous to the Anderson-Morel mechanism, but in energy space instead of frequency space. We estimate the effective pairing interaction and find that very high $T_c$ is possible, even for small $λ_0$ where the theory is controlled. We provide estimates using realistic parameters.

</details>


### [264] [Dynamical Steering and Unambiguous Signature of Majorana Corner Modes in Altermagnetic Josephson Junctions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16931)
*Yu-Xuan Li,Tao Zhou*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文提出一种相位偏置的交变磁约瑟夫森结（phase-biased altermagnetic Josephson junction）作为生成和控制马约拉纳角态（Majorana corner modes, MCMs）的通用平台。通过超导相位差和奈尔矢量（Néel-vector）取向两个独立控制旋钮动态重塑边界质量，实现MCMs在固定器件几何中的确定性空间重新定位。该空间重构产生一种控制关联的电导开关效应，可排除平庸安德烈夫束缚态（Andreev bound states）的假阳性，为马约拉纳编织架构提供可行路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 马约拉纳零模（Majorana zero modes）的动态操控及其与拓扑平庸态（topologically trivial states）的明确区分，仍是拓扑量子计算（topological quantum computation）中悬而未决的关键挑战。

Method: 该平台利用超导宏观相位差（macroscopic superconducting phase difference）和奈尔矢量取向作为两个独立控制旋钮，动态重塑边界质量（boundary mass），并将交变磁约瑟夫森结（altermagnetic Josephson junction）置于相位偏置下运行，从而实现超越传统全局参数调节的操控能力。

Result: 该方案实现了马约拉纳角态（MCMs）在固定器件几何中选定角之间的确定性空间重新定位。这种重新配置产生一种控制关联的电导开关效应（control-correlated conductance switching）：当MCMs被重新定位时，量化零偏峰（quantized zero-bias peak）在目标角完美显现，同时在初始角同步消失。

Conclusion: 这种宏观相位锁定的空间关联（macroscopically phase-locked spatial correlation）有效排除了来自平庸安德烈夫束缚态的假阳性信号，建立了一种控制关联的诊断方法，并为未来马约拉纳编织架构（Majorana braiding architectures）提供了有前景的路线。

Abstract: Dynamical manipulation of Majorana zero modes and their unambiguous distinction from topologically trivial states remain paramount challenges in topological quantum computation. Here, we propose a phase-biased altermagnetic Josephson junction as a versatile platform for generating and controlling Majorana corner configurations. Moving beyond conventional global parameter tuning that merely toggles the topological phase in situ, our platform utilizes the macroscopic superconducting phase difference and the Néel-vector orientation as independent control knobs to dynamically reshape the boundary mass. This synergistically enables the deterministic spatial relocation of Majorana corner modes (MCMs) among selected corners of a fixed device geometry. Crucially, this spatial reconfiguration yields a definitive experimental fingerprint: a control-correlated conductance switching. As the MCMs are relocated, the quantized zero-bias peak perfectly emerges at the target corner while simultaneously vanishing at the initial one. This macroscopically phase-locked spatial correlation effectively eliminates false positives from trivial Andreev bound states, establishing a control-correlated diagnostic and a promising route toward future Majorana braiding architectures.

</details>

### [265] [Quantum uniformity norms are pullbacks of matrix-valued uniformity norms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16862)
*Asgar Jamneshan*

Main category: math.GR

TL;DR: 本文证明 Bu、Gu 和 Jaffe 近期引入的量子均匀性范数（quantum uniformity norms）是 Gowers 与 Hatami 的矩阵值均匀性范数（matrix-valued uniformity norms）在 Weyl 轨道嵌入（Weyl orbit embedding）下的拉回（pullback）。这一识别推导出量子均匀性范数的 Gowers-Cauchy-Schwarz 不等式和三角不等式，从而回答了 Bu、Gu 和 Jaffe 提出的一个问题。在极值情形下，该结果将 Gottesman 与 Chuang 的 Clifford 层级（Clifford levels）描述为有限向量空间上某些酉值 Leibman 多项式映射（unitary-valued Leibman polynomial maps）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Bu、Gu 和 Jaffe 提出了量子均匀性范数，但该范数的基本不等式性质（如 Cauchy-Schwarz 不等式与三角不等式）以及其与已有范数理论的关系尚不明确。本文旨在通过建立量子均匀性范数与 Gowers-Hatami 矩阵值均匀性范数之间的精确联系，填补这一理论空白。

Method: 本文采用的方法是识别（identification），具体而言，证明量子均匀性范数是矩阵值均匀性范数在 Weyl 轨道嵌入下的拉回。该识别将量子信息论中的对象（Weyl 算符的轨道）映射到 Gowers-Hatami 的加性组合学框架中。

Result: 推导出量子均匀性范数满足 Gowers-Cauchy-Schwarz 不等式和三角不等式，从而回答了 Bu、Gu 和 Jaffe 的公开问题。在极值情形下，将 Clifford 层级刻画为有限向量空间上的酉值 Leibman 多项式映射。

Conclusion: 量子均匀性范数与矩阵值均匀性范数之间的等价关系不仅确立了其基本不等式性质，还建立了量子信息论（Clifford 层级）与加性组合学（Leibman 多项式映射）之间的深层联系，为后续交叉研究提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We show that the quantum uniformity norms recently introduced by Bu, Gu, and Jaffe are the pullbacks, under the Weyl orbit embedding, of the matrix-valued uniformity norms of Gowers and Hatami. This identification yields the Gowers-Cauchy-Schwarz inequality and the triangle inequality for the quantum uniformity norms, answering a question of Bu, Gu, and Jaffe. In the extremal regime, it describes the Clifford levels of Gottesman and Chuang in terms of certain unitary-valued Leibman polynomial maps on finite vector spaces.

</details>

### [266] [Jahn-Teller effect in $j = 3/2$ Mott insulators: Ground states and thermal fluctuations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14851)
*Kathleen Hart,Ruairidh Sutcliffe,Arun Paramekanti*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过SU(4)自旋蒙特卡洛方法耦合杨-泰勒声子，系统研究了Mott绝缘体中j=3/2多重态与晶格畸变相互作用下的多极基态、热相图及温度依赖谱分裂，揭示了声子耦合导致的多极共存序、热涨落效应及耦合系统的熵特性，并讨论了在双钙钛矿和缺位尖晶石等材料中的广泛意义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强原子自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）与杨-泰勒（Jahn-Teller, JT）晶格畸变之间的相互作用是含重原子量子材料中的一个重要课题，而简并的j=3/2多重态耦合局域声子模式是该类系统的典型范例。本文旨在系统研究该体系在Mott绝缘体中的多极基态、热相图及温度依赖的谱分裂，以理解声子耦合如何影响多极序的共存与竞争。

Method: 采用基于SU(4)自旋蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）方法，将自旋自由度与JT声子模式耦合，对j=3/2多重态系统进行数值模拟，计算其热力学相图及温度依赖的多重态分裂，相关结果可用于光谱学探针的分析。

Result: 发现了由声子耦合引发的共存且可区分的多极序（multipolar orders），阐明了热JT涨落（thermal JT fluctuations）的作用以及耦合的多极-声子系统的熵（entropy）行为，并给出了温度依赖的j=3/2多重态分裂特征。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了JT声子耦合在多极序共存中的关键角色，为理解重原子量子材料中的自旋-轨道耦合与晶格畸变相互作用提供了理论框架，并对双钙钛矿（double perovskites）Ba₂MgReO₆、Ba₂NaOsO₆以及缺位尖晶石（lacunar spinels）GaTa₄Se₈、GaNb₄Se₈等实际材料体系具有广泛指导意义。

Abstract: The interplay of strong atomic spin-orbit coupling with Jahn-Teller (JT) lattice distortions is an important theme in quantum materials hosting heavy atoms. A prototypical example of such a system is a degenerate $j = 3/2$ multiplet coupled to local phonon modes. Here, we study the multipolar ground states of this system as realized in Mott insulators, explore its thermal phase diagram via an $SU(4)$ spin Monte Carlo approach coupled to JT phonons, and study the temperature dependent splittings of the $j = 3/2$ multiplet as relevant to spectroscopic probes. Our work sheds light on coexisting distinct multipolar orders engendered by phonon coupling, role of thermal JT fluctuations, and the entropy of the coupled multipole-phonon system. We discuss broad implications for double perovskites $\rm Ba_2MgReO_6$, $\rm Ba_2NaOsO_6$ and lacunar spinels such as $\rm GaTa_4Se_8$ and $\rm GaNb_4Se_8$.

</details>


### [267] [Topological Tricritical Ising Universality Class in One Dimension](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15588)
*Sheng Yang,Hai-Qing Lin,Xue-Jia Yu*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文发现一维cluster O'Brien-Fendley模型的三临界点实现了拓扑非平凡的三临界伊辛（TCI*）普适类，该普适类在保持体共形数据的同时具有对称性增强的拓扑结构，表现为开边界条件下的两重简并，且拓扑简并的能级劈裂呈指数行为，与Ising*的代数劈裂形成鲜明对比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子临界普遍性（quantum critical universality）可被非平凡拓扑所丰富，但已有的研究尚不充分。本文旨在探究拓扑如何影响三临界点（tricritical point）的普适类结构。

Method: 以一维cluster O'Brien-Fendley模型为研究对象，通过分析其在开边界条件下的边界简并性、边界重整化群流（boundary renormalization-group flow）以及Z_2^T荷等性质，刻画TCI*临界性的拓扑结构。

Result: TCI*临界点具有与普通TCI临界性相同的局域体共形数据（local bulk conformal data），但拥有不同的对称性增强拓扑扇区（symmetry-enriched topological sector），并在开边界条件下表现为受保护的两重简并（twofold degeneracy）。拓扑两重简并的能级劈裂呈指数形式（exponential energy splitting），而Ising*临界点的简并劈裂为代数形式（algebraic splitting）。

Conclusion: 本文揭示了一种对称性增强的TCI临界性，发现了超出普通TCI理论的拓扑上不同的边界结构，表明拓扑能级劈裂行为可作为区分不同拓扑临界相的标志。

Abstract: Recent advances have revealed that quantum critical universality can be enriched by nontrivial topology. Here we study the tricritical point of the one-dimensional cluster O Brien-Fendley model and show that it realizes a topologically nontrivial tricritical Ising ($\text{TCI}^*$) universality class. The transition shares the local bulk conformal data of ordinary TCI criticality, while realizing a distinct symmetry-enriched topological sector, manifested through a protected twofold degeneracy under open boundary conditions. We further show that TCI criticality admits two spontaneously fixed boundary conditions, realized respectively through symmetry enrichment and boundary renormalization-group flow, which are distinguished by the $\mathbb{Z}_2^T$ charge of the disorder field. Remarkably, we find that the topological twofold degeneracy at the $\text{TCI}^*$ critical point exhibits an exponential energy splitting, in stark contrast to the algebraic splitting at the $\text{Ising}^*$ critical point. These results reveal a symmetry-enriched form of TCI criticality and uncover topologically distinct boundary structures beyond those of the ordinary TCI theory.

### [268] [Coupled-cluster study of dynamic Jahn-Teller effect in a $5d^2$ W antifluorite](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15697)
*Teruki Matsuzaki,Liviu F. Chibotaru,Maristella Alessio,Naoya Iwahara*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该论文运用运动方程耦合簇（EOM-CC）理论，对关联绝缘体Cs₂WCl₆中5d² W位点的振动耦合（vibronic coupling）与磁性进行定量分析，发现弱Jahn-Teller效应虽不引起明显晶格畸变，但动态Jahn-Teller效应会调制共振非弹性X射线散射（RIXS）谱峰形并影响有效磁矩，验证了EOM-CC方法在关联绝缘材料中金属位点物性预测方面的适用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在关联绝缘体（correlated insulators）中，电荷、自旋、轨道和晶格等多自由度共存并相互耦合，产生丰富的量子现象，但解耦其相互作用并不直接。在立方5d²双钙钛矿体系中，5d金属位点的自旋-轨道耦合基态简并，并与Jahn-Teller活性振动耦合，然而低温有序相中是否存在对称性降低尚无实验证据。因此，定量揭示5d²中心的振动耦合与磁性本质成为研究动机。

Method: 应用运动方程耦合簇（EOM-CC）理论分析Cs₂WCl₆中5d² W位点的振动耦合与磁性。推导了电子和振动耦合模型哈密顿量，计算了W L₃边共振非弹性X射线散射（RIXS）谱，并确定了有效磁矩（effective magnetic moment）。

Result: 模拟的RIXS谱显示振动耦合导致若干峰不对称。有效磁矩的温度依赖性与实验观测一致，验证了低能级分布计算的有效性。计算表明Cs₂WCl₆中Jahn-Teller效应处于弱耦合区域，不会发生明显晶格变形，但动态Jahn-Teller效应会调制RIXS谱形并影响磁矩。

Conclusion: 该工作证明了运动方程耦合簇（EOM-CC）理论在预测关联绝缘材料中金属位点物理现象方面的实用价值。

Abstract: In correlated insulators, the interplay among coexisting charge, spin, orbital, and lattice degrees of freedom gives rise to rich quantum phenomena, while unraveling the interplay is not straightforward. In the family of cubic $5d^2$ double perovskites, the ground spin-orbit coupled electronic states of $5d$ metal sites are degenerate and couple to the Jahn-Teller active vibrations, whereas no experimental evidence of the symmetry-lowering in the low-temperature ordered phases has been reported. To quantitatively unravel the nature of $5d^2$ centers, we apply equation-of-motion coupled cluster (EOM-CC) theory to analyze the vibronic and magnetic properties of $5d^2$ W sites of Cs$_2$WCl$_6$. We derive the electronic and vibronic model Hamiltonians, calculate the W $L_3$ edge resonant inelastic x-ray scattering (RIXS) spectra, and determine the effective magnetic moment. The simulated RIXS spectra show that vibronic coupling makes several peaks asymmetric. The effective magnetic moments exhibit a temperature dependence similar to that observed experimentally, confirming the validity of the calculated distribution of low-energy levels. Our calculations indicate that the Jahn-Teller effect in Cs$_2$WCl$_6$ is in a weak regime, and noticeable deformation would not occur, whereas the dynamic Jahn-Teller effect modulates the shapes of the RIXS spectra and affects the magnetic moment. This work demonstrates the usefulness of the EOM-CC method for predicting physical phenomena on metal sites in correlated insulating materials.

</details>


### [269] [Stabilizing Itinerant Electrons in a Corner-Sharing Kagomé Oxide Nd4Os3ZnO14](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15774)
*Ryutaro Okuma,Yuita Fujisawa,Chia-Hsiu Hsu,Keita Kojima,Daisuke Nishio-Hamane,Kazuki Sumida,Akio Kimura,Akira Yasui,Kohei Yamagami,Jun-ichi Yamaura,Yoshihiko Okamoto*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本研究报告了一种通过高温高压水热合成法制备的5d过渡金属Kagome氧化物Nd4Os3ZnO14。该材料具有由OsO6八面体共角连接形成的二维Kagome网络，标称锇价态为+4.67。面内电阻率和硬X射线光电子能谱测量表明，其室温半金属电子结构在冷却过程中演变为半导体基态，并伴随空穴迁移率的显著增强。磁化率测量显示局域化的Nd3+磁矩在2K以下不存在长程磁有序。金属性Kagome平面、5d电子固有的强自旋-轨道耦合与稀土磁性的共存，使该材料成为研究巡游体系中Kagome氧化物关联电子现象的理想平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Kagome氧化物因其几何阻挫（geometrical frustration）和特征能带拓扑（band topology）而产生的奇异电子态，是凝聚态物理的重要研究对象。然而，现有研究多集中于3d或4d过渡金属体系，5d过渡金属Kagome氧化物因其强自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）与关联效应的耦合尚未被充分探索。本文旨在合成并表征一种新型5d Kagome氧化物，以拓展该材料家族并探究其奇异物性。

Method: 采用高温高压水热合成法（high-temperature, high-pressure hydrothermal synthesis）制备了单晶样品Nd4Os3ZnO14。利用单晶X射线衍射（single-crystal X-ray diffraction）解析晶体结构，通过面内电阻率（in-plane resistivity）和硬X射线光电子能谱（hard X-ray photoelectron spectroscopy, HAXPES）测量电子输运和能带结构，并使用磁化率测量（magnetic susceptibility measurements）表征磁性行为。

Result: 该材料具有由共角OsO6八面体构成的二维Kagome网络，Os的平均价态为+4.67。电阻率和HAXPES测量表明，室温下呈现半金属（semimetallic）电子结构，随温度降低演变为半导体（semiconducting）基态，且空穴迁移率（hole mobility）在降温过程中显著增强。磁化率测量显示磁矩来源于局域化的Nd3+离子，在2K以下未观察到长程磁有序（long-range magnetic order）。

Conclusion: Nd4Os3ZnO14中金属性Kagome平面、5d电子强自旋-轨道耦合与稀土局域磁性的共存，使其成为研究巡游（itinerant）体系中Kagome氧化物关联电子现象（correlated electron phenomena）的一个有前景的平台。

Abstract: Kagome oxides provide a fertile platform for exploring exotic electronic states arising from geometrical frustration and characteristic band topology. Here, we report the synthesis of a 5d transition-metal kagome oxide, Nd4Os3ZnO14, obtained via high-temperature, high-pressure hydrothermal synthesis. Single-crystal X-ray diffraction reveals a two-dimensional kagome network formed by corner-sharing OsO6 octahedra, with a nominal osmium valence of +4.67. In-plane resistivity and hard X-ray photoelectron spectroscopy measurements indicate that the semimetallic electronic structure at room temperature evolves into a semiconducting ground state upon cooling, accompanied by a pronounced enhancement of hole mobility. Magnetic susceptibility measurements demonstrate localized Nd3+ moments without long-range magnetic order down to 2 K. The coexistence of a metallic kagome plane, strong spin-orbit coupling inherent to 5d electrons, and rare-earth magnetism establishes Nd4Os3ZnO14 as a promising platform for investigating correlated electron phenomena in kagome oxides within the itinerant regime.

### [270] [Probing Interfacial Magnetic Anisotropy in \texorpdfstring{CoV$_{2}$O$_{4}$}{CoV2O4} using Spin Hall Magnetoresistance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15865)
*Sairam Ithineni,Krishna Jha,Aditya A. Wagh,Shwetha G. Bhat,Debashree Nayak,K. Senapati,P. S. Anil Kumar,D. Samal*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过角度依赖的磁输运测量，利用自旋霍尔磁电阻（SMR）揭示了Pt/CVO异质结中与体相截然不同的界面磁各向异性，发现双轴各向异性并在120 K以下保持，表明SMR对界面磁性的高灵敏度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自旋霍尔磁电阻（spin Hall magnetoresistance, SMR）已被用于探测复杂氧化物异质结中的界面自旋输运和磁各向异性，但体相与界面磁性行为可能存在显著差异，需要高灵敏度的界面探测手段来揭示界面磁性。

Method: 对Pt/CVO异质结进行了角度依赖的磁输运测量（angle-dependent magnetotransport measurements），包括面内横向SMR旋转扫描和面外旋转测量，并与体相敏感的磁性测量结果进行对比。

Result: 体相测量显示CVO和Pt/CVO薄膜在$T_{C} \approx 150$ K发生亚铁磁转变，面外各向异性在90 K以下重取向为面内各向异性；而SMR在20 K显示沿[100]方向存在显著滞回，沿[110]和[1$\bar{1}$0]则无滞回，表明双轴各向异性（biaxial anisotropy）且易轴沿[110]和[1$\bar{1}$0]方向。面内纵向和横向SMR均无尖锐不连续，但面外旋转时在[010]方向附近出现明显不连续，证实面内各向异性存在至120 K。自旋混合电导（spin mixing conductance）约为$10^{14}$ $Ω^{-1}\mathrm{m}^{-2}$，与其他氧化物自旋电子学系统相当。

Conclusion: Pt/CVO界面保留了与体相不同的磁各向异性，证实了SMR对界面磁性的高灵敏度；界面效应在自旋输运中起关键作用，Pt/CVO可作为自旋电子学应用的有前景平台。

Abstract: Spin Hall magnetoresistance (SMR) has emerged as a powerful probe for investigating interfacial spin transport and magnetic anisotropy in complex oxide heterostructures. In this work, we investigate the interfacial magnetic anisotropy in Pt/CVO through angle-dependent magnetotransport measurements. Unlike the bulk-sensitive magnetic measurements on both strained CVO and Pt/CVO films, which exhibit a ferrimagnetic transition at $T_{C} \approx 150$ K accompanied by out-of-plane anisotropy that reorients toward in-plane anisotropy below 90 K, SMR reveals a distinct interfacial magnetic anisotropy. The rotational scans of the in-plane transverse SMR at 20 K exhibit substantial hysteresis about [100], while no hysteresis is observed along [110] and [1$\bar{1}$0], indicating a biaxial anisotropy with easy axes along [110] and [1$\bar{1}$0]. Furthermore, the absence of sharp discontinuities in both the in-plane longitudinal and transverse SMR, together with pronounced discontinuities near the in-plane [010] direction during out-of-plane rotation, strongly indicates the presence of in-plane anisotropy. This behavior persists up to 120 K. The discrepancy between the bulk-sensitive magnetic measurements and the SMR response suggests that the Pt/CVO interface retains a magnetic anisotropy distinct from the bulk, highlighting the interfacial sensitivity of SMR. Additionally, the spin mixing conductance is found to be of the order of $10^{14}$ $Ω^{-1}\mathrm{m}^{-2}$, comparable to other oxide-based spintronic systems. These findings highlight the crucial role of interfacial effects in spin transport and establish Pt/CVO as a promising platform for spintronic applications.

</details>


### [271] [Staggered Virtual-Loop-Current Order in Pseudospin-1 Dirac Flat Bands](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16155)
*Yi-Chun Hung,Arun Bansil*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文证明在骰子晶格（dice lattice）的部分填充赝自旋-1（pseudospin-1）狄拉克平带（Dirac flat band）中，短程相互作用（short-range interactions）可以驱动交错虚环流（staggered virtual-loop-current, SVLC）序与√3×√3电荷序。该序态自发破缺时间反演对称性（time-reversal symmetry），产生有限的内禀反常霍尔电导（intrinsic anomalous Hall conductivity）和轨道磁化（orbital magnetization），且不依赖于电子能谱中明确定义的低能谷（valleys）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管已知相互作用可在赝自旋-1/2平带狄拉克材料（pseudospin-1/2 flat-band Dirac materials）中产生奇异相，但更高赝自旋系统能否实现全新类型的序、以及此类序如何受底层狄拉克态（Dirac states）性质的调控，仍是未解决的问题。

Method: 采用受限实空间哈特里-福克（restricted real-space Hartree-Fock）计算，在弱相互作用区间求解短程相互作用下的骰子晶格部分填充赝自旋-1狄拉克平带系统的最低能量解。

Result: 研究表明，SVLC序与√3×√3电荷序同时出现，虚环流源于相互作用驱动的电荷密度量子涨落（quantum fluctuations），并在相邻三角形元胞（triangular plaquettes）之间交替循环。该序态在弱相互作用区间是能量最低的解，且通过平带波函数（flat-band wavefunctions）的等价性进入，不依赖明确定义的低能谷。

Conclusion: 本研究建立了更高赝自旋狄拉克系统（higher-pseudospin Dirac systems）作为探索平带物理中新兴奇异序的新平台，揭示了此类序与赝自旋-1/2狄拉克系统在底层机制上的本质差异。

Abstract: Although interactions are known to generate exotic phases in pseudospin-1/2 flat-band Dirac materials, it remains an open question whether the higher-pseudospin systems could realize entirely new types of orders and, if so, how such orders are governed by the nature of the underlying Dirac states. Here, we demonstrate that short-range interactions can drive a staggered virtual-loop-current (SVLC) order together with a $\sqrt{3}\times\sqrt{3}$ charge order in a partially filled pseudospin-1 Dirac flat band of the dice lattice. The virtual loop currents are shown to originate from interaction-driven quantum fluctuations of charge densities and exhibit alternating circulation between the neighboring triangular plaquettes. The resulting spontaneous time-reversal symmetry breaking is found to induce finite intrinsic anomalous Hall conductivity and orbital magnetization. The SVLC state is shown to be the lowest energy solution in restricted real-space Hartree-Fock calculations in the weakly interacting regime. The pseudospin-1 Dirac cones enter the SVLC order through the equivalence of their flat-band wavefunctions, and unlike the pseudospin-1/2 Dirac systems, do not rely on the presence of well-defined low-energy valleys in the electronic spectrum. Our study establishes higher-pseudospin Dirac systems as a new platform for investigating exotic emergent orders in flat-band physics.

Abstract: The interplay between polar and altermagnetic orders remains largely unexplored in the broader landscape of correlated electron systems. No diffraction signature of the $Pn2_{1}a$ structure is detected down to 20 K within experimental limits of $\sim$60-200 fm atomic displacements, significantly smaller than the DFT prediction of $\sim$1 pm. Combined with recent nonlinear transport measurements, our structural study suggests Ca$_{3}$Ru$_{2}$O$_{7}$ as a unique system where strong electron correlations drive an electronic phase transition without any measurable lattice symmetry change. With Ti substitution exceeding $\sim$3%, a chemically tunable altermagnetic phase with $Bb2_{1}m$ structure emerges. The study highlights the importance of sub-picometer metrology towards de-convolving structural versus electronic origins of altermagnets.

### [273] [symveig: Verified eigenvalue enclosures for symmetry-decomposed Hermitian matrices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16217)
*Sarang Vehale,Ritu Goel*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文介绍 symveig，一个纯 NumPy/SciPy 包，可计算厄米矩阵所有特征值的严格可机器验证区间（enclosure），并利用阿贝尔对称性分解加速，提供比全矩阵验证更紧密（3–9 倍）且更快（最高 130 倍）的保证上界，已在多种海森堡晶格模型上验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子晶格哈密顿量的精确对角化（exact diagonalization）返回的浮点特征值缺乏精度认证，舍入误差、求解器行为及病态性（ill-conditioning）可能无预警地破坏结果，因此需要一种能提供严格、可验证特征值区间的方法。

Method: 设计纯 NumPy/SciPy 包 symveig，利用显式浮点误差分析（floating-point error analysis）在 IEEE 754 最近舍入算术下计算特征值的严格上界；对与对角阿贝尔守恒量（abelian conserved quantity）对易的矩阵，独立验证各对称性扇区（symmetry sector），避免构造和对角化全矩阵。

Result: 在系统尺寸 L = 4–12 时，对称性分解所得区间半宽度比全矩阵验证紧 3–9 倍；在 L = 12 时实现最高 130 倍的墙钟加速（wall-clock speedup）。在 1D 海森堡、J1–J2 海森堡及 2D 海森堡晶格上的所有测试中，每个计算出的特征值均被其区间包含。

Conclusion: symveig 将严格验证的特征值区间方法引入标准科学 Python 栈，无需 INTLAB 或 MATLAB，为计算物理学中量子晶格哈密顿量的特征值计算提供了可认证的精度保障。

Abstract: Exact diagonalization of quantum lattice Hamiltonians returns floating-point eigenvalues whose accuracy is not certified: rounding error, eigensolver behaviour, and ill-conditioning can corrupt a result without warning. We present \texttt{symveig}, a pure NumPy/SciPy package that computes rigorous, machine-checkable enclosures of all eigenvalues of a Hermitian matrix, with an optional symmetry-sector decomposition. For a matrix that commutes with an abelian conserved quantity diagonal in the working basis (for example the total magnetization of a spin model), the package verifies each symmetry sector independently. Because each sector block is much smaller than the full matrix, this yields enclosures that are both tighter (by a factor of $3$-$9$ across system sizes $L = 4$-$12$) and dramatically faster (a wall-clock speedup of up to $130\times$ at $L = 12$) than verifying the full matrix, while never forming or diagonalizing it. Every enclosure half-width is a guaranteed upper bound on the distance from a computed eigenvalue to the nearest true eigenvalue under IEEE~754 round-to-nearest arithmetic, obtained by explicit floating-point error analysis with no heuristic slack. The implementation requires neither INTLAB nor MATLAB, bringing rigorously verified eigenvalue enclosure into the standard scientific-Python stack used in computational physics. We validate the package on $1$D Heisenberg (open and periodic), $J_1$-$J_2$ Heisenberg, and $2$D Heisenberg lattices, confirming that every computed eigenvalue is contained in its enclosure across all tested configurations.

</details>

Abstract: Heterointerfaces between structurally dissimilar oxides provide a platform to exploit the interfacial mismatch in the lattice and electronic degrees of freedom to realize emergent functionalities and tunable physical properties with potential applications in oxide electronics. Interestingly, the low-temperature resistivity upturn below 5 K arising from disorder-induced quantum corrections in bare SRO is strongly suppressed in SRO/SCO, and it exhibits Fermi-liquid-like transport ($ρ\propto T^2$) down to 2 K. Analysis of the anomalous Hall effect (AHE) reveals dominant intrinsic Berry-curvature driven electron transport in both samples, with enhanced intrinsic and skew-scattering contributions in the SRO/SCO bilayer, indicating the critical role of the interface in modifying the electronic band structure near the Fermi level. Our results demonstrate that the interface acts as an effective control knob, concurrently enhancing the magnetization, PMA, and intrinsic scattering contribution to the AHE in the SRO/SCO heterostructure, while suppressing the disorder-driven quantum corrections to transport behavior observed in the bare SRO film.

Abstract: In strongly correlated materials such as high-temperature superconductors, the relation between charge density wave (CDW) order and magnetism remains an important unresolved problem. ### [276] [Multiband transport hierarchy and large Nernst effect in EuAuBi: Establishing a Nernst scaling for asymmetric multiband systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16249)
*Weimin Quan,Xiaodong Guo,Lingxiao Zhao,Shengwei Chi,Gang Xu,Zengwei Zhu,Xiaokang Li*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文研究极性半金属EuAuBi中稀电子与稠空穴共存时的输运性质，发现Nernst效应完全由超高迁移率电子口袋主导，并推导出多带体系下的Nernst标度律ν/T ∝ μ_e/E_F,tot，证明该效应源于半经典多带补偿而非拓扑Berry曲率贡献。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在关联材料（correlated materials）中，载流子密度差异巨大的共存口袋带来了两个基础问题：哪个口袋主导各种输运系数？以及最初针对单带体系推导的经典Nernst标度律（Nernst scaling）ν/T ∝ μ/E_F是否仍然成立？本工作旨在回答这两个问题。

Method: 实验测量极性半金属EuAuBi的纵向电阻率、Hall效应、Seebeck系数和Nernst效应，并结合两带热电导率（two-band thermoelectric conductivity）模型进行分析。

Result: 空穴口袋主导纵向电阻率；Hall效应随磁场增强从电子主导转变为空穴主导；Seebeck系数在低温下由电子口袋主导、高温下由两者共同主导。Nernst效应完全由超高迁移率电子口袋（n_e ∼ 10^16 cm⁻³）主导，在202 K、约1 T下产生约5 μV/K的大信号。Nernst系数遵循标度律ν/T ∝ μ_e/E_F,tot，该标度源于电子-空穴电导率比与费米能（Fermi energy）比之间的补偿。

Conclusion: 多带体系中的大Nernst效应是半经典的多带补偿现象，而非拓扑Berry曲率贡献。这一认识推进了多带电子系统的热电输运物理理解，并为低场横向热电（transverse thermoelectric）设计提供了指导性原则。

Abstract: In correlated materials, coexisting pockets of vastly different carrier densities raise two fundamental questions: which pocket governs the various transport coefficients, and does the conventional Nernst scaling $ν/T \propto μ/E_F$, originally derived for single-band systems, still hold? We address both questions in the polar semimetal EuAuBi, where a dilute electron pocket ($n_e \sim 10^{16}~\mathrm{cm}^{-3}$) coexists with a dense hole pocket ($n_h \sim 10^{21}~\mathrm{cm}^{-3}$). We find a clear hierarchy: the hole pocket dominates the longitudinal resistivity; the Hall effect crosses from electron- to hole-dominance with increasing field; the Seebeck coefficient is dominated by the electron pocket at low temperature and by both pockets at high temperature. Remarkably, the Nernst effect is governed entirely by the ultrahigh-mobility electron pocket, yielding a large low-field signal of $\sim 5~μ\mathrm{V/K}$ near 1~T at 202~K, comparable to anomalous Nernst signals in magnetic Weyl semimetals. By analyzing the two-band thermoelectric conductivity, we show that the Nernst coefficient follows a scaling $ν/T \propto μ_e/{E_{F, tot}}$. This scaling originates from a compensation between the electron-to-hole conductivity ratio and the Fermi-energy ratio, establishing that the large Nernst effect is a semiclassical multiband phenomenon rather than a topological Berry-curvature contribution. This understanding advances the thermoelectric transport physics of multiband electronic systems and offers a guiding principle for low-field transverse thermoelectric design.

### [277] [Quantum oscillations in proximity to high-angular-momentum band inversion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16397)
*Jiahao Yang,Gang v. Chen*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过研究高角动量能带反转（high-angular-momentum band inversion）的最小模型，揭示了手性双带模型和时间反演不变四带模型中的量子振荡（quantum oscillations）行为，指出振荡信号可作为该能带反转的实验可观测特征，并为其他离散对称相关的杂化与激子配对提供了分析框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子振荡是探测磁场中电子结构和费米面拓扑（Fermi surface topology）的基本手段，但高角动量（HAM）能带反转体系中的振荡行为尚不明确。本文旨在建立最小模型并分析其振荡特征，以识别HAM能带反转的可实验观测信号。

Method: 采用两类最小模型：手性双带模型（chiral two-band model）和时间反演不变四带模型（time-reversal-invariant four-band model）。通过解析和数值方法分析两类模型在磁场下的量子振荡行为，重点关注杂化Chern绝缘体和时间反演对称性导致的干涉效应。

Result: 在手性双带模型中，杂化Chern绝缘体区域（Chern-insulating regime）因热激活激子（thermal-activated excitations）可出现有限振荡。在时间反演不变四带模型中，两个时间反演相关块（time-reversal-related blocks）之间的干涉导致振荡振幅偏离Lifshitz-Kosevich形式，产生非单调温度依赖性，且特征抑制温度数目等于角动量量子数$l$。

Conclusion: 上述振荡特征为HAM能带反转提供了实验可观测的签名，并为其他由离散对称性（discrete symmetry）驱动的杂化机制和激子配对（excitonic pairings）体系建立了通用的分析框架。

Abstract: Quantum oscillations provide a fundamental probe of electronic structure in magnetic fields, revealing the Fermi surface topology in metals, and/or the quasiparticle properties even in the insulating regimes. Here we study quantum oscillations in minimal models of high-angular-momentum (HAM) band inversion for both a chiral two-band model and a time-reversal-invariant four-band model. In the former case, finite oscillations can appear at the hybridized Chern-insulating regime due to thermal-activated excitations. In the latter case, interference between the two time-reversal-related blocks drives a strong deviation from the Lifshitz-Kosevich form, producing a non-monotonic temperature dependence of the oscillation amplitude and characteristic suppression temperatures whose number follows the angular momentum $l$. These results identify experimentally accessible signatures of HAM band inversion and provide a framework for other discrete-symmetry-related hybridizations and excitonic pairings.

</details>


### [278] [Intervalley coherence and flavor polarization in three-valley moiré systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16622)
*Jeyong Park,Laura Classen,Mathias S. Scheurer*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文研究了扭转M点材料莫尔超晶格中相互作用诱导的对称性破缺，识别并分类了包括谷间相干（IVC）序在内的多种候选不稳定性，并通过强耦合框架和无限制哈特里-福克（Hartree-Fock）方法分析了其能量学。研究表明，IVC不稳定性不仅出现在中等带宽的超交换机制中，也出现在强耦合区间，且依赖于堆叠方式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索扭转M点材料中相互作用诱导的对称性破缺机制，并分类可能的候选不稳定性，特别是与三谷结构相关的谷间相干（IVC）序，以揭示该体系与扭转多层石墨烯的异同。

Method: 基于一般对称性论证识别和分类不稳定性；采用解析强耦合框架（strong-coupling framework）和无限制哈特里-福克（unrestricted Hartree-Fock）方法对完整连续模型进行能量学分析。

Result: 识别出除味极化态（flavor polarized states）外的多种IVC序；两种方法（强耦合与Hartree-Fock）结果高度一致；发现IVC不稳定性在中等带宽下由超交换（superexchange）驱动，在强耦合区间则因偏离平带度量条件（flat-metric condition）而产生。

Conclusion: 扭转M点材料为复杂关联物理提供了丰富的研究平台，其IVC序的多样性源于三谷结构；研究结果揭示了该体系与扭转多层石墨烯的差异与相似性。

Abstract: We investigate interaction-induced symmetry breaking in moiré superlattices created by twisting two identical materials where the electronic low-energy degrees of freedom reside in the vicinity of the $M$ points. Based on general symmetry arguments, we identify and classify the possible candidate instabilities that, besides flavor polarized states, also involve a variety of intervalley-coherent (IVC) orders. This complexity is related primarily to the presence of three valleys, instead of the well-studied scenario of two, e.g., in graphene: IVC states can couple all three valleys identically, with a non-trivial sign structure, or even with different magnitudes. We study the energetics using an analytical strong-coupling framework and unrestricted Hartree-Fock applied to the full continuum model, with very good agreement between the two approaches. Interestingly, depending on stacking, IVC instabilities not only appear due to superexchange at moderate bandwidths, but also deep in the strong-coupling regime as a result of deviations from the flat-metric condition. Our work demonstrates that twisted $M$-point materials provide a rich playground for complex correlated physics and highlights differences and similarities to twisted multilayer graphene.

### [279] [Field-selected seven-site topological magnons in a classical frustrated triangular-lattice K-$Γ$-$Γ'$ magnet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16704)
*Bin Xi,Jie Lu,Shun-Li Yu,Yafang Xu*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过经典自旋基态搜索和线性自旋波理论（linear spin-wave theory, LSWT），证明三角晶格K-Γ-Γ'模型在强Γ交换区中，面内磁场可选出一种紧凑的非共面七位序，该序为磁子拓扑（magnon topology）提供了可控的半经典基准，并展示了场可调的陈数和拓扑相变如何改变热霍尔电导率（thermal Hall conductivity）的温度依赖性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在强阻挫磁体中，零场下缺乏简单的简谐磁子真空（harmonic magnon vacuum），使得定义磁子拓扑（magnon topology）变得困难。本文旨在通过外加磁场选择一种可控的经典参考态，从而为强阻挫体系中磁子拓扑相的研究建立半经典框架。

Method: 采用经典自旋基态搜索（classical-spin ground-state search）结合线性自旋波理论（linear spin-wave theory, LSWT），研究三角晶格上以Γ交换为主的K-Γ-Γ'模型，并通过面内磁场选择非共面七位序作为参考态。

Result: 磁场选定的七位序具有可调陈数（Chern numbers）；增大磁场会驱动狄拉克型能带接触（Dirac-like band touching），使得贝里曲率（Berry curvature）在第五和第六能带之间转移，陈向量从(0,1,0,-2,1,0,0)转变为(0,1,0,-2,-1,2,0)。该拓扑转变重新组织能带分辨的热霍尔电导率，导致总κ_{xy}(T)在上能带热激发后出现接近零的穿越。动力学结构因子（dynamical structure factor）将约一半的相干谱权重分布在陈活性支路上。

Conclusion: 本文在纯最近邻交换模型中为磁子拓扑建立了可控的半经典基准（controlled semiclassical benchmark），并指出动力学结构因子可作为识别拓扑支路的光谱学途径。

Abstract: Defining magnon topology in strongly frustrated magnets is often hindered by the absence of a simple harmonic magnon vacuum at zero field. Within a classical-spin ground-state search followed by linear spin-wave theory (LSWT), we demonstrate that a representative triangular-lattice K-Gamma-Gamma' model in a dominant-Gamma exchange regime has an in-plane-field-selected compact, noncoplanar seven-site order. This field-selected state provides a controlled classical reference state and hosts magnon bands with field-tunable Chern numbers. Increasing the field drives a Dirac-like band touching that transfers Berry curvature between the fifth and sixth bands, altering the Chern vector from (0, 1, 0, -2, 1, 0, 0) to (0, 1, 0, -2, -1, 2, 0). This topological transition reorganizes the band-resolved thermal Hall conductivity, driving the total $κ_{xy}(T)$ through a near-zero crossing once the upper bands are thermally populated. The dynamical structure factor places roughly half of the coherent spectral weight on the Chern-active branches, offering a spectroscopic route to identify the topological branches. These results define a controlled semiclassical benchmark for magnon topology in this pure nearest-neighbor exchange model.

</details>


### [280] [Spin-orbit-entangled $J_{\rm eff}=\frac{1}{2}$ magnetism and unconventional spin freezing in the bond-disordered pyrochlore antiferromagnet NaCdCo$_2$F$_7$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16875)
*Andrej Kancko,Hironori Sakai,Javier Herrero-Martín,Adam Berlie,Marc Uhlarz,Tetiana Haidamak,Yo Tokunaga,Ross H. Colman*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过实验表明，受挫烧绿石（pyrochlore）反铁磁体中的键无序（bond disorder）与自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）共同作用，导致NaCdCo₂F₇展现出一种非传统的持续动态自旋玻璃态（spin-glass-like state），与同构的S=1/2体系NaCdCu₂F₇实现的随机单态（random-singlet state）形成鲜明对比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用高场磁化测量、Co L₂,₃边X射线吸收光谱（XAS）与X射线磁圆二色性（XMCD）确定Co²⁺的自旋-轨道纠缠态；利用μSR和²³Na NMR测量追踪自旋涨落的动力学行为；并与同构的键无序烧绿石NaCdCu₂F₇进行对比。

Result: 实验确认Co²⁺具有J_eff=1/2矩和显著的未猝灭轨道贡献，符合局域XY各向异性（local XY anisotropy）。μSR和NMR显示自旋涨落在~10 K以下逐渐减速，最终形成部分冻结态（partially frozen state）并保持低温持续动态，偏离经典自旋玻璃（canonical spin glass）。

Conclusion: 自旋-轨道耦合是决定键无序受挫烧绿石磁体量子基态的关键因素，Co²⁺与Cu²⁺体系对键无序的响应截然不同。

Abstract: Bond disorder in frustrated pyrochlore antiferromagnets can give rise to fundamentally different quantum ground states depending on the nature of the local magnetic moments. Here, we show that the bond-disordered pyrochlore NaCdCo$_2$F$_7$ realizes an unconventional spin-glass-like state with continued dynamics, in stark contrast to its isostructural $S=\frac{1}{2}$ NaCdCu$_2$F$_7$ counterpart. High-field magnetization and Co $L_{2,3}$-edge XAS/XMCD establish spin-orbit-entangled $J_{\rm eff}=\frac{1}{2}$ Co$^{2+}$ moments with a substantial unquenched orbital contribution, consistent with local $XY$ anisotropy seen in the isostructural Na$A''$Co$_2$F$_7$ ($A''$ = Ca, Sr) analogues. $μ$SR and $^{23}$Na NMR measurements reveal progressive slowing of spin fluctuations below $\sim10$ K, culminating in a partially frozen state with persistent low-temperature dynamics that deviates from a canonical spin glass. Comparison with the isostructural bond-disordered pyrochlore NaCdCu$_2$F$_7$, which realizes a random-singlet state, reveals a fundamentally different response of spin-orbit-entangled Co$^{2+}$ moments to bond disorder. These results identify spin-orbit coupling as a key ingredient governing the fate of bond-disordered frustrated pyrochlore magnets.

</details>


### [281] [Electronic Green's function across the pseudogap to stripe transition in the $t$-$t'$-$J$ model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16968)
*Martin Ulaga,Aritra Sinha,Alexander Wietek*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文利用张量网络算法研究欠掺杂t-t'-J模型，发现赝能隙（pseudogap）的动量区分特征强烈依赖于次近邻跳跃参数t'，在降温过程中出现动量依赖的能隙打开，形成费米弧（Fermi arc），同时节线能隙随温度升高而闭合，对应条带序（stripe order）熔化为涨落电荷团簇。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用张量网络算法（tensor network algorithms），针对宽度为4的圆柱几何上的欠掺杂t-t'-J模型（underdoped t-t'-J model）进行有限温度动力学计算，研究电子格林函数（Green's function）。

Result: 赝能隙的标志性特征——动量区分（momentum differentiation）强烈依赖于次近邻跳跃参数t'。随着温度降低，系统出现动量依赖的能隙打开，与中等温度下费米弧（Fermi arc）的形成一致。在k=(π/2,π/2)附近的节线能隙（nodal gap）随温度升高而闭合并填充，同时相干条带序（coherent stripe order）熔化为涨落电荷团簇（fluctuating charge clusters）区域。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了赝能隙的动量结构对t'的敏感性，以及条带序熔化与节线能隙关闭之间的关联，为理解铜氧化物超导体中赝能隙与电荷序的关系提供了新的微观认识。

Abstract: Superconducting domes in strongly correlated electronic systems are often accompanied by charge density waves and peculiar features in the electronic structure. The appearance of a pseudogap, in particular, and its relation to charge density waves remains insufficiently understood. Here, we investigate the electronic Green's function of the underdoped $t$-$t'$-$J$ model of the cuprate superconductors using tensor network algorithms for finite temperature dynamics on cylinders of width $4$. We find the prominent momentum differentiation, the hallmark of the pseudogap, to be strongly dependent on $t'$, which develops into a momentum-dependent opening of a gap upon decreasing temperature, consistent with the formation of a Fermi arc at intermediate temperatures. The nodal gap around ${\bf k}=(π/2,π/2)$ closes and fills with increasing temperature as coherent stripe order melts into a regime of fluctuating charge clusters.

### [282] [Disentangling multi-spin dynamic correlations in the Heisenberg spin-$\frac{1}{2}$ chain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16992)
*V. K . Bhartiya,U. Kumar,T. Kim,S. Fan,S. Okamoto,M. Mitrano,M. P. M. Dean,J. Pelliciari,I. A. Zaliznyak,S. Johnston,V. Bisogni*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究展示如何通过共振非弹性X射线散射（RIXS）中的能量失谐技术，选择性地探测海森堡自旋-1/2链中的多自旋动力学关联，并通过理论建模分离出两自旋与多自旋响应，揭示了二者的共振能量分离、谱形差异（洛伦兹型 vs 高斯型）及其物理来源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超越两粒子关联的高阶关联（higher-order correlations）对于理解新奇物相和量子动力学的普适方面至关重要，但现有手段（如非弹性中子散射）主要局限于两粒子关联测量，多粒子关联的实验探测仍面临重大挑战。

Method: 以海森堡自旋-1/2链（Heisenberg spin-1/2 chain）中的磁激发为研究对象，利用共振非弹性X射线散射（resonant inelastic X-ray scattering, RIXS）通过能量失谐（energy detuning）激发不同中间态，从而选择性地探测多自旋动力学关联；辅以t-J哈密顿量的精确对角化（exact diagonalization）进行理论建模与验证。

Result: (i) 两自旋与多自旋动力学关联的共振能量分离约3/4 J，表明多自旋截面源于包含自旋翻转的中间态；(ii) 两自旋通道谱重呈洛伦兹型（Lorentzian）共振能量轮廓，对应单一主导电子组态；多自旋通道呈高斯型（Gaussian-like）轮廓，反映多个中间自旋组态的贡献；(iii) 轮廓宽度分别主要取决于芯空穴寿命Γ/2和2J/Γ。

Conclusion: 通过RIXS能量失谐作为调控手段，可实现对多自旋动力学的可控探测，为探索量子材料中的多体动力学（many-body dynamics）开辟新途径。

Abstract: Higher-order correlations are essential for understanding exotic phases and uncovering universal aspects of quantum dynamics. While inelastic neutron scattering provides well-established access to two-particle correlations, measuring correlations in solids involving more than two particles remains a major challenge. Focusing on magnetic excitations in the Heisenberg spin-$\frac{1}{2}$ chain, we demonstrate that resonant inelastic X-ray scattering (RIXS) can selectively probe multi-spin dynamical correlations by exciting distinct intermediate states through energy detuning. Through theoretical modeling, we isolate the two- and multi- spin responses, and establish that: (i) The resonant energies of the two- and multi- spin dynamical correlations are separated by $\approx \frac{3}{4}J$; implying that the multi-spin part of the cross-section comes from intermediate states that contain spin flips; (ii) The spectral weight of the two-spin channel exhibits a Lorentzian resonant energy profile consistent with a single dominant electronic configuration, whereas the multi-spin channel response shows a Gaussian-like profile, implying contributions from multiple intermediate spin configurations. These characteristics are reproduced by exact diagonalization of the $t-J$ Hamiltonian, which further reveals that the widths of Lorentzian and Gaussian resonant energy profiles depend primarily on core-hole lifetime ($Γ/2$) and $\frac{2J}Γ$, respectively. Controlled access to multi-spin dynamics, using RIXS energy detuning as a knob, can open new pathways to explore many-body dynamics in quantum materials.

</details>


### [283] [Compact Spin-Charge Separated Neural Quantum States for Valence-Bond States](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17045)
*Ang-Kun Wu,Louis Primeau,Yixin Zhang,Jingtao Zhang,Adrian Del Maestro,Yang Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于可解点引导的策略来设计神经网络量子态（NQS）架构，通过四个物理驱动的设计组件在价键固体（VBS）及其掺杂变体（sVBS）上实现了高保真度和参数效率，展现了约 L² 的参数缩放，优于全连接、卷积和Transformer基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 神经网络量子态（neural-network quantum states, NQS）的性能高度依赖于网络架构是否匹配目标量子态的符号结构（sign structure）和约束希尔伯特空间（constrained Hilbert space），但缺乏系统性的架构设计原则。

Method: 提出可解点引导策略：在精确可解点处读取正确的局域规则（local rules），然后仅通过增大卷积核大小（kernel size）和隐藏维度（hidden dimension）将架构推广到非精确区域。具体包含四个物理驱动设计：步长匹配的局域规则卷积、几何池化（geometric pooling）、符号分辨激活函数 tanh(x^{2k+1})，以及显式的自旋-空穴扇区分离（spin-hole sector separation）。

Result: 在准一维价键固体（VBS）及其掺杂孤子变体（sVBS）的有限尺寸基准测试中，该架构在参数更少的情况下达到高保真度；自旋扇区的局域规则从小系统迁移到大系统无需重训练；在非可解点附近，增大卷积核大小和隐藏维度系统性地提升精度；在无间隙区（gapless regime）参数缩放约为 L²，而矩阵乘积态（matrix-product states）在同一区域约为 L⁴。

Conclusion: 该工作为具有符号结构和约束希尔伯特空间的系统建立了一种紧凑NQS的设计方案，并为更广泛的 t-J 模型和 Hubbard 模型家族的物理启发的架构设计铺平了道路。

Abstract: Neural-network quantum states (NQS) provide a flexible nonlinear representation of quantum many-body wavefunctions, but their efficiency depends sensitively on whether the architecture reflects the sign structure and constrained Hilbert space of the target state. In this work, we propose a solvable-point-guided strategy: design the architecture at an exactly solvable point where the correct local rules can be read off, then refine to the non-exact regime by enlarging only the kernel size and hidden dimension. The strategy is built from four physics-motivated designs: a stride-matched local-rule convolution, geometric pooling, a sign-resolving $\tanh(x^{2k+1})$ activation, and explicit spin-hole sector separation. We test this approach on quasi-one-dimensional valence-bond-solid (VBS) states and their doped soliton variants (sVBS), the exact ground states of a $t$-$J$-like model with a single mobile hole. In finite-size benchmarks, this architecture reaches high fidelity for the exact sVBS state with substantially fewer parameters than generic fully connected, convolutional, and transformer baselines tested under the same setup. For the spin sector, the learned local rule transfers from small to larger systems without retraining. Away from the solvable point, increasing kernel size and hidden dimension systematically improves accuracy, and the model shows approximately $L^2$ parameter scaling in the gapless regime for system size $L$, compared with approximately $L^4$ for matrix-product states in the same regime. Our work establishes a recipe for compact NQS in sign-structured, constrained Hilbert spaces and paves the pathway to physics-informed architectures for the broader $t$-$J$ and Hubbard families.

</details>

### [284] [Resolvent estimates for one-dimensional Dirac operators with imaginary potentials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16049)
*Antonio Arnal,Tho Nguyen Duc,Petr Siegl*

Main category: math.SP

TL;DR: 本文研究了一类受对角矩阵势 iV 扰动的一维大质量 Dirac 算子，其中 V 为实值无界函数。利用广义强制性和 Schur 补优势技巧构造了具有非空预解集的 L² 实现，并在 Airy-Dirac 原型情形 V(x)=x 下推导了预解式的渐近行为，进而推广至一般势函数，给出了 ε-伪谱曲线的渐近形态并证明了伪谱区域的最优性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 一类受无界实值势扰动的大质量一维 Dirac 算子的谱分析尚未充分展开，特别是在预解集非空性、预解式渐近行为以及伪谱（pseudospectrum）区域最优性等方面缺乏系统性结果。

Method: 采用广义强制性（generalized coercivity）和 Schur 补优势（Schur complement dominance）技巧构造 L² 实现并确保预解集非空；在 Airy-Dirac 原型情形 V(x)=x 下解析推导预解式在谱参数趋于无穷和质量 m 趋于 0 时的渐近行为；利用 Airy-Dirac 预解式表征一般势函数下的预解式范数渐近。

Result: 获得了 Airy-Dirac 情形下预解式在谱参数趋于无穷及质量趋于 0 时的精确渐近行为；建立了以 Airy-Dirac 预解式描述的一般势函数预解式范数渐近式，进而导出了 ε-伪谱曲线（ε-pseudospectral curves）的渐近形状，并证明了文献[32]中伪谱区域的最优性。

Conclusion: 所提出的广义强制性和 Schur 补优势方法可有效处理无界势扰动下的 Dirac 算子 L² 实现问题；Airy-Dirac 预解式在伪谱渐近分析中起到核心作用，其给出的伪谱区域是最优的。

Abstract: We investigate massive one-dimensional Dirac operators perturbed by diagonal matrix potentials of the form $i V$ where the function $V$ is real-valued and unbounded at infinity. For such operators we find an $L^2$-realization with non-empty resolvent set using generalized coercivity and Schur complement dominance techniques. In the prototypical Airy-Dirac case $V(x)=x$, $x \in \mathbb{R}$, we derive the precise asymptotic behavior of the resolvent as the spectral parameter tends to infinity and also as the mass $m$ tends to $0$. Finally, we find the asymptotics of the resolvent norm for general potentials $V$ in terms of the Airy-Dirac resolvent, which in particular yields an asymptotic shape of $\varepsilon$-pseudospectral curves and establishes the optimality of the pseudospectral region found in [32].

</details>


### [285] [$m$-sectorial discrete Laplacians and recurrence of complex-weighted graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16554)
*Anna Muranova*

Main category: math.SP

TL;DR: 本文研究了边权位于复平面扇区内的复加权图（complex-weighted graphs），证明了其狄利克雷拉普拉斯算子（Dirichlet Laplacian）是 m-扇形的（m-sectorial），从而生成一个收缩的全纯 C₀-半群（contractive holomorphic C₀-semigroup）。进一步表明每个扇形复加权图均可扩展为以全纯函数为边权的电网络（electrical network），并基于此建立了无穷复加权图的收敛性结果，最后定义了复加权图的常返性（recurrence）并给出了多个等价刻画。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将经典图论和网络理论中的正实边权（如电阻网络）推广到复值边权情形，并建立复加权图在泛函分析和复分析框架下的理论基础，特别是其与电网络的联系。

Method: 采用扇形算子（sectorial operator）理论和 m-扇形算子方法分析复加权图的狄利克雷拉普拉斯算子；通过将扇形复加权图扩展为电网络（边权为源于物理导纳的全纯函数），建立收敛性结果（包括狄利克雷问题的解收敛和复值容量收敛）；利用这些收敛性定义并刻画复加权图的常返性。

Result: 证明了复加权图的狄利克雷拉普拉斯算子是 m-扇形的，因而生成收缩的全纯 C₀-半群；证明了每个扇形复加权图可扩展为电网络；建立了无穷复加权图在有限穷竭（finite exhaustion）上的收敛性；给出了复加权图常返性的多种刻画。

Conclusion: 复加权图的扇形结构保证了其拉普拉斯算子的良好算子性质，且与电网络理论的联系使得复分析方法和物理直觉得以应用于无穷复加权图的渐近分析；常返性的多种刻画表明该框架具有与经典正加权图理论相平行的丰富结构。

Abstract: We consider complex-weighted graphs, whose edge weights belong to a sector in the complex plane. We show that the corresponding Dirichlet Laplacian is $m$-sectorial, and, hence, generates a contractive holomorphic $C_0$-semigroup. Further, it is shown that every sectorial complex-weighted graph can be extended to an electrical network, where by electrical networks we mean graphs, whose edge weights are holomorphic functions, arising from physical admittances. This result allows us to establish convergence results for the infinite complex-weighted graphs, e.g. convergence of solutions of Dirichlet problems and convergence of complex-valued capacities on a finite exhaustion. Finally, we define a recurrence for complex-weighted graphs, and, using the convergence results, give its characterizations in terms of functional spaces, capacity, Green's function, resolvents of the Dirichlet Laplacian and properties of the Neumann Laplacian.

</details>

### [286] [Polarization Signatures of Rotating Black Holes in Perfect Fluid Dark Matter Spacetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.14736)
*Yu-Xiang Huang,Sen Guo,En-Wei Liang,Kuan Liu,Kai Lin*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文通过全相对论性射线追踪（ray tracing）模拟，研究了沉浸于完美流体暗物质（PFDM）背景中的旋转黑洞（Kerr BH）的偏振辐射特征，发现PFDM强度参数k会系统性地改变事件视界尺度上的偏振结构，包括电矢量位置角（EVPA）的偏转、偏振强度分布以及净线偏振分数，表明暗物质可在黑洞偏振信号中留下可观测印记。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受M87*视界尺度偏振观测的启发，旨在量化完美流体暗物质（PFDM）背景对旋转黑洞偏振辐射结构的影响，探讨暗物质是否会在黑洞偏振信号中产生可观测的印记。

Method: 采用完全相对论性射线追踪（ray tracing）方法，模拟旋转黑洞在完美流体暗物质（PFDM）背景下的偏振辐射传输，系统分析偏振结构对磁场几何、高阶成像以及PFDM强度参数k的联合依赖关系。

Result: 含极向分量的磁场构型会产生连续螺旋状的电矢量位置角（EVPA）模式；PFDM参数k的变化会影响近视界光传播与偏振输运，引起EVPA偏转和光子环附近偏振强度的相应变化。高阶图像在环附近提供局域但不可忽略的修正。与M87*的偏振特征相比，PFDM使净线偏振分数|m|_{\rm net}降低、大尺度偏振相位\argβ_2发生系统性偏移。

Conclusion: 完美流体暗物质（PFDM）作为一种额外的强引力成分，会系统性地重组视界尺度的偏振结构，表明周围暗物质可以在黑洞偏振信号中留下可观测的印记。

Abstract: Motivated by horizon-scale polarization observations of M87^{*}, we investigate polarized emission from rotating black holes (BHs) immersed in a perfect fluid dark matter (PFDM) background. Fully relativistic ray tracing is utilized to examine how the polarization structure jointly depends on magnetic-field geometry, higher-order imaging, and the PFDM intensity parameter k. We show that, for a given k value, magnetic configurations with a polar component naturally produce a continuous spiral pattern in the electric vector position angle (EVPA), while the large-scale EVPA morphology remains primarily controlled by the magnetic-field topology. Variations in k affect light propagation and polarization transport near the horizon, leading to corresponding changes in EVPA deflection and polarized intensity around the photon ring. A decomposition of the total polarized image further reveals that higher-order images provide localized yet non-negligible corrections near the ring. Compared with the polarization characteristics of M87^{*} inferred by the EHT, image-domain quantities such as |m|_{\rm net} and \argβ_2 indicate that PFDM induces systematic shifts relative to the pure Kerr BH case, lowering the net linear polarization fraction and modifying the large-scale polarization phase. Overall, PFDM acts as an additional strong-gravity ingredient that systematically reorganizes the horizon-scale polarization structure, suggesting that surrounding dark matter can leave observable imprints on black hole polarization signatures.

</details>


### [287] [Relativistic Accretion Flow in a Generic Class of Spherically Symmetric Static Spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15143)
*Pradeepkumar Yadav,Sayan Chakrabarti,Santabrata Das*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 该论文在包含高阶（最高四阶）1/r修正的静态球对称时空中，自洽求解相对论流体动力学方程，获得了低角动量、无黏、平流主导的全局跨声速吸积流解族（O、A、W、I型），分析了时空参数与流体参数对临界点个数及参数空间的影响，并计算了热初致辐射谱能量分布（SED），发现时空高阶修正会增强SED且含内临界点的I型解辐射光度更高。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在广义相对论框架下，标准史瓦西（Schwarzschild）时空假设了最简单的静态球对称黑洞解，但更高阶的引力修正（如弦理论或量子引力效应）可能改变吸积流的结构与辐射特性。该研究旨在利用包含四阶1/r修正的广义静态球对称度规，系统探索高阶时空修正对低角动量吸积流动力学及可观测信号的影响。

Method: 采用一个包含直至1/r^4阶修正项的静态球对称度规，其中引入三个时空参数（δ, η, β）；在此度规下自洽求解相对论流体动力学（relativistic hydrodynamical）方程，通过对特定能量（specific energy，ℰ）和角动量（angular momentum，λ）的控制，得到全局跨声速（global transonic）吸积流解族；利用热初致辐射（thermal bremsstrahlung）模型计算谱能量分布（SED），对比不同时空参数下的辐射差异。

Result: 吸积流解的类型及临界点数目由时空参数（δ, η, β）和流体参数（ℰ, λ）共同决定，存在单临界点和多临界点两类解；绘制了δ-λ和λ-ℰ参数空间中支持多临界点解的区域，并揭示这些区域随δ增大而演化的规律；增大δ会显著增强SED（相对于史瓦西情形）；含内临界点的I型全局跨声速解比仅含外临界点的O型、A型解具有更高的辐射光度。

Conclusion: 高阶时空修正对低角动量吸积流的动力学和辐射特性有可观测影响，I型解在辐射效率上占据优势，这为未来利用吸积流观测区分不同引力理论提供了理论依据。

Abstract: We investigate the properties of low angular momentum, inviscid, advective accretion flows in a generic static and spherically symmetric spacetime that incorporates higher-order corrections up to the fourth order in $1/r$. Employing this metric, we self-consistently solve the relativistic hydrodynamical equations and obtain the family of global transonic accretion solutions ($O$, $A$, $W$ and $I$-types) by means of the spacetime parameters ($δ$, $η$, $β$) and the flow parameters (specific energy $\mathscr{E}$ and angular momentum $λ$). Our analysis reveals that the accretion flow possesses either single or multiple critical points depending on these input parameters. We delineate the regions of the $δ-λ$ and $λ-\mathscr{E}$ parameter spaces that admits solutions with multiple critical points and demonstrate how these regions evolve with increasing spacetime parameter $δ$. Furthermore, while connecting the spacetime geometry with observable signatures, we compute the spectral energy distribution (SED) from thermal bremsstrahlung emission and observe that increasing $δ$ enhances the SED relative to the Schwarzschild case. Finally, we find that global transonic solutions harbouring inner critical points ($I$-types) yields more luminous power than those with only outer critical points ($O$ and $A$ types).

</details>


### [288] [Mapping Domain-Wall Bayesian Reconstruction with LISA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.15387)
*Satyabrata Datta,Rome Samanta*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文利用嵌套采样（nested sampling）和 Clough–Tocher 插值方法，在考虑天体物理前景和 LISA 仪器噪声的条件下，系统构建了尖峰型畴壁引力波信号（peaked domain-wall gravitational-wave signals）在 LISA 频段上的贝叶斯重建图（Bayesian reconstruction maps），确定了信号可被有效重建的参数区间（湮灭温度约在 10³–10⁶ GeV，信噪比 SNR ≳ 50），并给出了弱信号区域对应的峰值振幅和频率约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 评估 LISA 对尖峰型畴壁引力波信号（peaked domain-wall gravitational-wave signals）的贝叶斯重建能力，并量化信号参数（湮灭温度 T_* 等）的可辨识区域，为粒子物理中预言毫赫兹（mHz）频段引力波谱的畴壁模型提供重建预报。

Method: 采用两参数畴壁谱模板（two-parameter domain-wall spectral template），加入银河系双白矮星双星（Galactic double white-dwarf binaries）和河外致密双星（extra-galactic compact binaries）的各向同性、未调制天体物理前景以及 LISA 仪器噪声；在等距网格的 64 个注入点（injection points）上使用嵌套采样（nested sampling）进行贝叶斯推断，并通过 Clough–Tocher 方法对后验量进行插值，生成全覆盖参数平面的光滑重建图。

Result: LISA 在湮灭温度约 10³–10⁶ GeV 范围内对畴壁信号重建最有效，此时后验分布更窄且简并性更低，实现真正的两参数重建；最有利区域的信噪比 SNR ≳ 50，而 SNR ∼ 10 的信号仅在 T_* ≲ 10⁵ GeV 的较窄区域内有效重建，对应峰值振幅 Ω_GW^peak h² ≳ 4×10⁻¹¹ 且峰值频率 f_p ≲ 10–20 mHz。

Conclusion: 本文结果为 LISA 频段内的尖峰型畴壁信号提供了定量的重建预报，并为预言毫赫兹频段尖峰引力波谱的畴壁粒子物理模型提供了实用指导。

Abstract: We study the Bayesian reconstruction of peaked domain-wall gravitational-wave signals at LISA and construct reconstruction maps over the signal-parameter plane. These maps identify the regions in which the signal can be probed with minimal posterior uncertainty and parameter degeneracy. Our analysis employs a two-parameter domain-wall spectral template and includes isotropic, unmodulated astrophysical foregrounds from Galactic double white-dwarf binaries and extra-galactic compact binaries, together with LISA instrumental noise. The inference is performed for 64 injection points distributed on an equidistant grid using nested sampling, and the resulting posterior quantities are interpolated with the Clough--Tocher method to generate smooth maps over the full parameter plane. We find that LISA reconstructs domain-wall signals most effectively when the annihilation temperature lies approximately in the range $10^3\text{--}10^6\,\mathrm{GeV}$. In this regime, the posterior becomes both tighter and less degenerate, enabling genuine two-parameter reconstruction. The most favorable region corresponds to signals with ${\rm SNR}\gtrsim 50$, while signals with ${\rm SNR}\sim 10$ can still be reconstructed effectively only in a narrower part of parameter space concentrated near $T_*\lesssim 10^5\,\mathrm{GeV}$. In terms of the observable spectrum, this weaker-signal region corresponds approximately to peak amplitudes $Ω_{\rm GW}^{\rm peak}h^2 \gtrsim 4\times10^{-11}$ and peak frequencies typically satisfying $f_p\lesssim 10\text{--}20\,{\rm mHz}$. Our results provide a quantitative reconstruction forecast for peaked domain-wall signals in the LISA band and a useful guide for particle-physics realizations of domain walls that predict peaked gravitational-wave spectra in the milli-Hz range.

</details>


### [289] [On the transformation of the Maxwell-Boltzmann Distribution to a Power-Law](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.04659)
*Ari Laor,Igor Gitelman*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文通过直接蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）模拟研究碰撞硬球系统中能量分布函数（distribution function, DF）的演化，发现幂律（power-law, PL）分布形成的三个关键条件：初始远离平衡态、系统动力学无标度（scale-free）以及无标度边界条件；这些条件在自然界中普遍存在，从而解释了幂律分布为何如此广泛。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 幂律分布函数（PL DF）在从纳米尺度到兆光年尺度、从尘埃颗粒到生物体等高度多样化的系统中普遍存在，作者希望探究这种普遍性背后的机制，理解幂律分布在自然和人类活动中为何如此常见。

Method: 采用直接蒙特卡洛（direct Monte Carlo）模拟方法，追踪碰撞硬球系统中能量分布函数（DF）的时间演化过程，系统性地考察从非平衡初始状态到统计平衡态的转变。

Result: 在统计平衡态下，分布函数演化为麦克斯韦-玻尔兹曼分布（Maxwell-Boltzmann DF）。当满足以下三个条件时，分布函数转变为幂律（PL）分布：（1）系统初始远离平衡态（如轻、重粒子以相同速度混合）；（2）系统动力学无标度（scale-free），发生在远离初始态和最终平衡态的中间渐近区域；（3）系统为开放系统且具有无标度边界条件（如持续注入远离平衡的粒子）。幂律指数由自相似DF的时间依赖性和边界条件共同决定，与自相似DF的具体形式无关。

Conclusion: 所识别的三个条件（初始非平衡、无标度动力学、无标度边界条件）在大量不同系统中普遍存在，这为幂律分布函数（PL DF）在自然界中如此普遍提供了可能的解释机制。

Abstract: Power-law (PL) distribution functions (DF) are prevalent in highly diverse systems. The systems range in size from nanometer to mega light years, in complexity from dust grains to living organisms, and characterize the distribution of various events in nature and in various human activities. To gain some insight on why PL DF are so prevalent, we explore the conditions leading to the formation of a PL DF in a simple system of colliding hard sphere. We follow the time evolution of the energy DF through direct Monte Carlo simulations. In statistical equilibrium, the DF evolves into the Maxwell-Boltzmann (MB) DF. A transition to a PL DF occurs when: 1. The system is initially far from equilibrium. For example, a mix of light and heavy particles with the same velocity. 2. The system dynamics is scale-free, which holds in the intermediate asymptotic regime, far from the initial and the final equilibrium states. The scale-free dynamics leads to a DF which evolves in a self-similar form. 3. The system is open with a scale-free boundary condition. For example, a constant injection of particles far from equilibrium. The DF PL index is set by the time dependence of the self-similar DF and by the boundary condition. The PL index is independent of the self-similar DF form. Conditions 1-3 are common in a great variety of systems, which may explain why PL DF are so prevalent in nature.

</details>

# math.GT [[Back]](#toc)

### [290] [Quantization of Contact 3-Manifolds and the Reeb Gravitational Field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.16529)
*Ali M. Elgindi*

Main category: math.GT

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种针对闭接触3-流形（closed contact 3-manifolds）的规范几何量子化方案，通过将流形嵌入C³并利用复切向链环（link of complex tangents）构造有限维量子希尔伯特空间（quantum Hilbert space），在Sasakian条件下Reeb向量场（Reeb vector field）可编码爱因斯坦引力（Einstein gravity），从而统一了量子力学与引力在接触几何框架下的描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在为闭接触3-流形建立一个统一的规范几何量子化（canonical geometric quantization）框架，使得接触结构（contact structure）编码量子力学，而其Reeb向量场在Sasakian条件下编码引力，并区分不同紧接触结构（tight contact structures）。

Method: 利用前期工作中构造的显式嵌入$M \hookrightarrow \mathbb{C}^3$，使得接触结构沿复切向链环$L$变为全纯（holomorphic），并将该链环视为支撑开书（supporting open book）的装订（binding）。通过Stein延拓（Stein extension）得到唯一全纯线丛$L_\xi \to \mathbb{C}^3$，其在$L$上的限制与半典范线丛（canonical bundle）的平方根$\kappa^{1/2}$张量积后定义量子希尔伯特空间$\mathcal{H}_\xi = H^0(L, L_\xi|_L \otimes \kappa^{1/2})$。

Result: 所构造的量子希尔伯特空间是有限维的（finite-dimensional）。在流形为Sasakian的附加假设下，Reeb向量场$R_\alpha$是测地线（geodesic）且具有时间型Killing Reeb场，进而可对$M$上的爱因斯坦引力进行建模。由此得到的不变量$\mu_M(\xi) = [L_\xi] \in \operatorname{Pic}_\mathbb{C}(M)$能够以新颖方式区分$\mathbb{T}^3$上的不同紧接触结构。

Conclusion: 该构造仅依赖于$(M,\xi,\alpha)$及支撑开书的选择，建立了一个统一的几何框架，其中接触结构编码量子力学，Sasakian条件下的Reeb场编码引力。该框架对量子模型具有启示意义，并可作为量子不变量（quantum invariant）使用。

Abstract: We present a canonical geometric quantization scheme for closed contact 3-manifolds $(M,ξ)$ using the corresponding explicit embedding $M \hookrightarrow \C^3$ as we constructed in our earlier papers. The contact structure becomes holomorphic along the chosen link $L \subset M$ of complex tangents, of which we may also consider this link as the binding of a supporting open book for $ξ$. Stein extension yields a unique holomorphic line bundle $L_ξ\to \C^3$ whose restriction to $L$ will define the quantum Hilbert space $\Hilb_ξ= H^0(L, L_ξ|_L \otimes κ^{1/2})$, which we find will be finite-dimensional. The Reeb vector field $R_α$ of a chosen compatible contact form $α$ is shown to be geodesic with a time Killing Reeb field under further assumption that the manifold is Sasakian, and under this assumption will model Einstein gravity over $M$. This construction depends only on $(M,ξ,α)$ and a choice of supporting open book for $ξ$. This establishes a unified geometric framework in which the contact structure encodes quantum mechanics and whose Reeb field will encode gravity assuming that the manifold is Sasakian. In addition, we use my previous paper in which we get a related invariant $μ_M(ξ) = [L_ξ] \in \Pic_\C(M)$ which is useful in that it distinguishes between different tight contact structures on $\T^3$ in a novel way. We also show how this will have implications for the quantum model and serve as a quantum invariant there-in.

</details>
